
 
 

     sūtrasthānanam || caturtho ' dhyāyaḥ || 

      1.4.1  pippalyo dīpyakaś caiva tathā mūṣikakarṇikāḥ |
       
       bilvasya pallavāḥ śvetā haridrā madhukaṃ tathā ||  
 1.4.2  ete kuṣṭhaṃ pratighnanti yuktāḥ pānapralepanaiḥ |
       
       gavāṃ pittaṃ śunaḥ pittamalāvūṃ kaṭukāṃ tathā ||  
 1.4.3 nimbaṃ nataṃ śarkarāṃ ca dadyāt tadvat pralepanam |
       
       yātuṇḍamaṇḍalīdvīpāt mūlānyeḍagajasya ca(?) ||  
 1.4.4  surādanīṃ(?) sugandhāṃ ca dadyāt tadvat pralepanam |
       
 suvarṇapuṣpīṃ kaṭukāṃ śyāmāṃ tejovatīṃ tathā ||  
 1.4.5  trivṛtsañjātakaṃ? caiva kuṣṭhe saṃśodhanaṃ viduḥ |
       
       āragvadhaṃ ca bhārgīṃ ca sāśvagandhāṃ gavādanīm ||  
 1.4.6  śvetāṃ jyotiṣmatīṃ caiva sūkṣmacūrṇāni kārayet |
       
       gavāṃ pittena taccūrṇaṃ saptakṛtvaḥ subhāvitam ||  
 1.4.7 yojyaṃ sarṣapatailena saindhavena ca yuktitaḥ
      |
       
       etadvai hṛtadoṣasya mitadadhyannabhojinaḥ ||  
 1.4.8  tanulepanamuddiṣṭaṃ kṛmikuṣṭhavināśanam |
       
 gavedhukamakuṣṭhau ca khadirakvāthapācitau ||  
 1.4.9  tāvapyubhau prayuñjīta kuṣṭhināṃ kuṣṭhaśāntaye |
       
       atha kaṇḍūghnavṛkṣāṇāṃ rasāḥ syuḥ kuṣṭhināṃ hitāḥ ||  
 1.4.10  pralepapariṣekeṣu khadiras tu praśasyate |
       
       khadirodaka pāyī syāt khadirodakabhojanaḥ ||  
 1.4.11  bhūyiṣṭhamudakārthe ca kurvīta khadirodaram |
       
       sāravantau mahāvṛkṣau dhavarohita kāvubhau ||  
 1.4.12  śiṃśupā cāśvakarṇaś ca khadiro bilvamāśritaḥ |
       
       kadalīmuṣkakau hiṃsrā bhadrodumbarikāphalam ||  
 1.4.13  etairapyuṣitaṃ kuṣṭhe gomūtraṃ pariṣecanam |
       
       sālāśvakarṇaniryāso niryāsaḥ kuliśasya ca ||  
 1.4.14  ete kuṣṭhanimittānāṃ vraṇānāṃ syuḥ prapīḍakāḥ |
       
       puṇḍarīkasya vakṣyāmi kriyāṃ rogavināśinīm ||  
 1.4.15  āvartāṃ śālmalīmūlaṃ malayūkāṃ sudhāṃ varīm |
       
       bhadrodumbarikāmūlaṃ phalānyāvalgujāni ca ||  
 1.4.16  rātrau yantreṇa niṣpīḍya danticitrakam eva ca |
       
       pāṭhāṃ haridre ca tathā gavāṃ mūtreṇa yojayet ||  
 1.4.17  aṣṭabhāgāvaśiṣṭaṃ tatsādhitaṃ supariṣkṛtam |
       
       pibetkālyaṃ samutthāya śvitrī śītodakaṃ pibet ||  
 1.4.18 sarvataḥ parirakṣet tu sthāpayeccainamātape |
       
       bhaiṣajyapīḍitā doṣās tv acamasyānusaṃśritāḥ ||  
 1.4.19  maṇḍaleṣu tapasphoṭaṃ janayantyarkaraśmibhiḥ |
       
       sphoṭeṣv atha tu jāteṣu chāyāyām upaveśayet ||  
 1.4.20  śītābhir adbhiḥ prakṣālya bhojayed rasabhojanam |
       
 saṃkṣubhyante ' tha vai toyaparipūrṇā ivāmbudāḥ ||  
 1.4.21  sūcyagreṇātha tīkṣṇena vyathayetkaṇṭakena vā |
       
       candanasya ca yatsāraṃ badarāt khadirasya ca ||  
 1.4.22  etaiḥ pānīyapiṣṭais tu sarpiḥkṣaudrasamanvitaiḥ |
       
       patreṣu puṣkariṇyās tu saṃviṣṭasyātha dehinaḥ ||  
 1.4.23  tatas tv ālepayetsphoṭān śītodakapariplutān |
       
       kṣīriṇāṃ cāpi vṛkṣāṇāṃ tvacassaṃkṣodayed bhiṣak ||  
 1.4.24  taiḥ kaṣāyeiś ca kalkaiś ca siñcayel lepayec ca tam |
       
       kharjūrasya ca bījāni śaṅkhanābhiḥ ca dāpayet ||  
 1.4.25 añjanaṃ tagaraṃ patraṃ gairikaṃ nīlamutpalam |
       
       eṣāṃ sūkṣmeṇa cūrṇena sravantamavacūrṇayet ||  
 1.4.26  śakṛddrākṣākṣaudrayukto dātavyaḥ paripoṭane |
       
       āhārotsādanābhyaṅgaṃ pūrveṇa vidhinā bhiṣak ||  
 1.4.27  kārayetkuṣṭhināmevaṃ tataḥ sampadyate sukhī |
       
       na ca vyādhimupekṣeta śarīraṃ patitaṃ budhaḥ |
       
       tvareta śamane tasya pradīptasyeva veśmanaḥ ||  
 1.4.28  yathā hyekāntato vṛkṣo vardhate sukhataśśanaiḥ |
       
       tathā śarīramāsādya rogo vardhata eva tu ||  
 1.4.29 tasmād rakṣanmahāvegādakṣīṇasyaiva dehinaḥ |
       
       prāgevopacayādrogānhanyādvaidyo vicakṣaṇaḥ ||  
 1.4.30  tryahāttryahāccāvapīḍaḥ pakṣānmāsādvamettathā |
       
 recayed ayane pūrṇe sirāmokṣo vidhīyate ||  
 1.4.31 śyāmākāś ca makuṣṭhāni caṇakāḥ kuṣṭhināṃ hitāḥ |
       
       evaṃ hi vartamānānāṃ kuṣṭhaṃ praśamameti vai || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele caturtho ' dhyāyaḥ || || pañcamo ' dhyāyaḥ || athātyāśitīyaṃ
      vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 1.5.1  athāśitena pītena khāditena ca yuktitaḥ |
       
       balamāpyāyate jantoḥ sadyo vahnirivendhanaiḥ ||  
 1.5.2  tenaivātyādṛteneha bhojanena śarīrajāḥ |
       
       vyādhayassaṃpravardhante kāyāgnāvapi dūṣite ||  
 1.5.3  dvividhaṃ tu bhiṣagvidyādāhārasyaiva lāghavam |
       
 dvividhaṃ gauravaṃ bhukte procyamānaṃ nibodhata ||  
 1.5.4  mātrālaghussyādāhāraḥ kaściddravyalaghuḥ smṛtaḥ |
       
       mātrāgurus tathaiva syād dravyataś ca tathā guruḥ ||  
 1.5.5  purāṇaśālayo mudgāḥ śaśatittirilāvukāḥ |
       
 evaṃprakāraṃ yaccānyat taddravyaṃ laghu saṃsmṛtam ||  
 1.5.6 grāmyānūpaudakaṃ māṃsaṃ dadhi
      piṣṭaṃ tilāhvayam |
       
       evaṃprakāraṃ yaccānyattaddravyaṃ gurviti smṛtam ||  
 1.5.7  tatra yo mātrayā bhuṅkte dravyaṃ gurvapi mānavaḥ |
       
       āhāraṃ tasya paśyanti laghum eva cikitsakāḥ ||  
 1.5.8 śālyādīny api yo ' tyarthamaśnāti sulaghūny api |
       
       āhārassa tathārūpo vyaktaṃ sampadyate guruḥ ||  
 1.5.9  dravyasya laghuno yuktyā sauhity aṃ yo ' dhigacchati |
       
       ekāntapathyaṃ taṃ vidyādāhāraṃ kuśalo laghum ||  
 1.5.10 yadi yuktyāpi sauhityaṃ dravyasyālaghuno vrajet |
       
       tathāvidhamihāhāraṃ gurum eva bravīmyaham ||  
 1.5.11 tasmāt tribhāgasasauhityam ardhasauhityam eva vā |
       
       āhāraṃ laghumanvicchet gurūṇāṃ sevitaṃ sadā ||  
 1.5.12 laghu vāpi samāsādya dravyaṃ yo hy atisevate |
       
       tallaghvapyatisaṃyuktaṃ koṣṭhe sampadyate guru ||  
 1.5.13  gurulāghavavidvaidyo narāṇāṃ vardhayaty asūn |
       
       tasmād evaṃ vijānīyāddravyāṇāṃ gurulāghavam ||  
 1.5.14  evam eva ca bhojyena pathyenāpyāyate naraḥ |
       
       hīyate cāpy apathyena praduṣṭairmārutādibhiḥ ||  
 1.5.15 svasthasyānnena vardhante dhātavaḥ śoṇitādayaḥ |
       
       vyādhitasyāpi doṣāya bhojyaṃ pariṇamaty atha ||  
 1.5.16  yathā hy akālavṛṣṭyā ca bhūmau bījaṃ vipadyate |
       
       vardhate kālavṛṣṭyā ca dehino ' pi tathā rasaiḥ ||  
 1.5.17  yaś ca nityam udāraḥ syāt sukhaniścalamānasaḥ |
       
 laghupānarataḥ sātmye ' pi yathāgasi dūragaḥ ||  
 1.5.18  snāto ' nuliptaḥ sragvī syāddhautadantassvalaṃkṛtaḥ |
       
 dharmassatyamahiṃsā ca prāyo hyannaṃ samāśritam ||  
 1.5.19  vamayecchaleṣmarogāṃś ca  paittikāṃś ca virecayet |
       
       nirūhayed vātarogān raktajāṃś cāvasecayet ||  
 1.5.20 raktaśālīn samudgān vā ṣaṣṭikānathavā punaḥ |
       
       susvinnānmātrayāśnīyāt ghṛtasaindhavasaṃyutān ||  
 1.5.21  īṣatpippalikaṃ yūṣamīṣac ca madhunānvitam |
       
       īṣatsalavaṇaṃ cāpi payaś cārdhakṛtaṃ pibet ||  
 1.5.22  viṣkirānpratudāṃś cājān jāṅgalāṃś ca mṛgadvijān |
       
       yac cānyatkaṭukaṃ pāke bhojyaṃ tan nityam ācaret ||  
 1.5.23  pādābhyāṃ na caretkṛṣṭe viṣame kaṇṭakeṣu ca |
       
       gahanaṃ paradārāṃś ca nadīḥ pūrṇāś ca na vrajet ||  
 1.5.24  kalahaṃ cāpi kopaṃ ca rātricaryāṃ vivarjayet |
       
       gajasya na syādāsannaḥ  toyārdrasya ca vājinaḥ ||  
 1.5.25  janavādāṃś ca śauṇḍāṃś ca dviṣataś cāpi mānavān |
       
 mlecchānnikṛtibuddhīṃś ca na seveta kadācana ||  
 1.5.26  sarvān sarīsṛpāṃś caiva kṣudrapādāṃś ca na spṛśet |
       
       mahiṣān gavayān khaḍgān vyāghrān siṃhāṃś ca varjayet ||  
 1.5.27  nārohetpādapān veśma na dhāvedvarṣadurjale |
       
       na gavāṃ pratilomaṃ ca na madhye nāgrato vrajet ||  
 1.5.28 sadyaḥ pravṛṣṭau nāroheddhimavantaṃ ca parvatam |
       
       ghṛtamuṣṇāmbu ca bhajedetadārogyam uttamam || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele pañcamo ' dhyāyaḥ || || ṣaṣṭho ' dhyāyaḥ || atha na vegāndhāraṇīyaṃ
       vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 1.6.1  na vegāndhārayed dhīraḥ prāptānmūtrapurīṣayoḥ |
       
       na vātasya na pittasya na śuklasya kaphasya ca ||  
 1.6.2  udgāracchardijṛmbhāṇāṃ tathā ca kṣavathorapi |
       
       na bāṣpasya na nidrādeḥ prāptaṃ vegaṃ vidhārayet ||  
 1.6.3  rogasañjanakā hyete hiṃsyurāyurvidhāritāḥ |
       
       etāneva prakuryuś ca tathā ' prāptāssamīritāḥ ||  
 1.6.4  vātamūtrapurīṣāṇāṃ dhāraṇādanilādayaḥ |
       
       kupyanti retasaś cāpi śarkarā sāśmarī tathā ||  
 1.6.5  tvagdoṣo vā jvaro vā syāt gātre śophādi vā punaḥ |
       
       chardipittakaphānāṃ tu dhāraṇena samīraṇāt ||  
 1.6.6  jṛmbhādidhāraṇādāndhyaṃ timiraṃ bāṣpadhāraṇāt |
       
 kṣavathūdgāranidrādeḥ dhāraṇātsyācchirorujā ||  
 1.6.7  tasmānmūtrapurīṣaṃ vai visṛjetkālyamutthitaḥ |
       
       uktā hy adhāraṇīyās tu dhāraṇīyānnibodhata ||  
 1.6.8  lobhamohabhiyāṃ tṛṣṇācintayor madamānayoḥ |
       
       śauryasya ca tathā vidvān prāptaṃ vegaṃ vidhārayet ||  
 1.6.9  etaddhārayato hy asya balamāyuś ca vardhate |
       
       udaṅmukhaśśucau deśe prāṅmukhaś cā ' vakuṇṭhitaḥ ||  
 1.6.10  āvaśyakamupāsīta kṛte cādbhir upaspṛśet |
       
       kṛtaśaucastato janturbhakṣayed dantadhāvanam ||  
 1.6.11  dhavaṃ palāśaw nyagrodhaw naktamālamathāpi vā || śirīṣaṃ
      karavīraṃ ca jātivṛkṣamathārjunam ||  
 1.6.12  eteṣāṃ dantadhavanaṃ śreṣṭhamāha punarvasuḥ |
       
       āpāṭya vidalīkṛtya dantamāṃsamabādhayan ||  
 1.6.13  tadasya śodhayed vaktraṃ pittasya ca kaphasya ca |
       
 śamanaṃ vātaraktādeḥ kurute dantadhāvanam ||  
 1.6.14  mustakalkaṃ satriphalaṃ madhu tailaṃ sukhodakam |
       
       pratyekaṃ kabalagrāhaṃ dhārayed anupūrvaśaḥ ||  
 1.6.15  vātapittakaphā duṣṭāḥ śāmyanti kabalagrahāt |
       
 mādhūkaṃ copadehaghnaṃ svararaktaprasādanam ||  
 1.6.16  tailaṃ dantyaṃ surabhikṛttadabhiṣyandanāśanam |
       
       kṣataṃ saṃrohayed vaktraṃ śīryamāṇaṃ niyacchati ||  
 1.6.17  indriyāṇāṃ mato ' bhyaṅgo gurudoṣavimokṣaṇaḥ |
       
       tvagdoṣaśamano balyo vātaraktaprasādanaḥ ||  
 1.6.18 grāmyadharmātigatyā ca rathāśvagajapātanāt |
       
       daṇḍamuṣṭihatānāṃ ca rujāśramavināśanaḥ ||  
 1.6.19  tvacaḥ prasādano+ abhyaṅgaḥ
      śāmyatyutsādanātklamaḥ  |
       
       praharṣaṃ kurute sthairyaṃ malaghnaṃ cāvasecanam ||  
 1.6.20  vilepanaṃ hlādayati kaṇḍūṃ hanti prasādanam |
       
       śiśiraṃ hyañjanaṃ dṛṣṭeḥ timiraṃ ca praṇaśyati ||  
 1.6.21  tanūruhendriyabalaṃ nasyatailādupāgatāt |
       
       svararaktaprasādaś ca naśyanti palitāni ca ||  
 1.6.22  svaktaḥ sūtsāditaś caiva praghṛṣṭaś ca yathābalam |
       
       yathartuvāriṇā snātas tv anuliptastataḥ param ||  
 1.6.23  prasādhitottamāṅgaś ca tato nasyaṃ pradāpayet |
       
       tatassaṃśuddhadoṣasya dhūmamasya prakalpayet ||  
 1.6.24  kuṭannaṭailāhrīberaṃ dhyāmakāgarucandanam |
       
       kālānusāryāṃ naladaṃ pṛthvīkām atha guggulam ||  
 1.6.25  tālīsaṃ padmakaṃ mustaṃ priyaṃguṃ sahareṇukām |
       
       haridrāṃ ca sugandhāṃ ca saralāṃ devadāru ca ||  
 1.6.26  śrīveṣṭakaṃ sarjarasaṃ corakaṃ ceti saṃharet |
       
       vaktraṃ ca sarpiṣāktaṃ syād dhūmametaṃ tataḥ pibet ||  
 1.6.27  aṣṭāṃgulapramāṇā vāpy athavā dvādaśāṃgulā |
       
       ṣaḍaṃgulapramāṇā vā dhūmavartiḥ praśasyate ||  
 1.6.28  sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ tāmraṃ gajadantasya vā punaḥ |
       
       vṛkṣasāramayaṃ vāpi dhūmanetraṃ praśasyate ||  
 1.6.29 caturvā pañcakṛtvo vā dhūmaṃ srotasyavācaret |
       
       vātānulomanaṃ kuryāc chleṣmāṇaṃ cāpakarṣati |
       
       balaṃ dadāti dṛṣṭeś ca samyagdhūmo niṣevitaḥ ||  
 1.6.30  aṣṭau dhūmasya kālāḥ  syur yeṣām ante praśasyate |
       
       utthitasyaiva śayanād dantaprakṣālane kṛte ||  
 1.6.31  jalakrīḍānivṛttasya tathā bhuktavato ' śanam |
       
       kṣutoccāravyavāyānte bhuktavāntavatas tathā ||  
 1.6.32  guṇāṃś caikaikaśas teṣāṃ dhūmapānakṛtān śṛṇu |
       
       tatra śayyotthitasyaiva vakṣyāmyatha yathākramam ||  
 1.6.33  hantyutsannaṃ kaphaṃ jantoṣṣaḍindriyavibodhanaḥ |
       
       pratibuddhasya ceddhūmo mārutasyānulomanaḥ ||  
 1.6.34  dantaprakṣālanādūrdhvaṃ rogānsamyagvyapohati |
       
       cyutaśleṣmāpanayanaḥ sugandhiviśadāsyakṛt ||  
 1.6.35  dantamāṃsakṣayakṛtavyādhayo vadaneṣu ye |
       
       doṣāḥ kāsaprabhṛtayastāṃś ca dhūmo vyapohati ||  
 1.6.36  śirogatā yāś ca rujāḥ salilakrīḍanodbhavāḥ |
       
       karṇaśūlaṃ pratiśyāyaṃ cāśu dhūmo vyapohati ||  
 1.6.37  vātapittakaphān dhūmaḥ śamayed bhojanodgatān  |
       
       śiroviśuddhiṃ kurute bhuktaṃ ca sthāpayaty api ||  
 1.6.38  dhamanipratipannas tu vāyuḥ kṣavathuneritaḥ |
       
       vyāpnoti sarvasrotāṃsi sa dhūmenānulomyate ||  
 1.6.39  varcaḥkarmoddhato vāyurgalamūrdhaśirogataḥ |
       
       prāṇānādhmāpayati vā sa dhūmenānulomyate ||  
 1.6.40  śuklasrotogato vāyurūrdhvam eva prapadyate |
       
       sa ghorān hi sṛjedrogāṃstaṃ  dhūmenānulomayet ||  
 1.6.41  rogādhipataye chardyā sthānebhyo ' bhis amīritāḥ |
       
       anārogyāya kalpante teṣāṃ dhūmaḥ praśasyate ||  
 1.6.42  hṛteṣu doṣeṣv anilaḥ śūnyasthānāni saṃcaran |
       
 sammūrcchati śiro gatvā taṃ dhūmenānulomayet ||  
 1.6.43  pūrvaṃ pītodako bhuktvā labhate kṛśatāṃ naraḥ |
       
       madhye bhaktasya pibato bhojanaṃ nāpakṛṣyate ||  
 1.6.44  bhuktavānatha pānīyaṃ paścād anupibec ca yaḥ |
       
       tadāpyānugataṃ bhuktaṃ samatvāyopapadyate ||  
 1.6.45  agnau pratāpayet pāṇī syātāṃ yāvat tu nirjalau |
       
       tataḥ padaśataṃ gacchedbhaktaṃ hyevaṃ prayātyadhaḥ ||  
 1.6.46  na rātrau dadhi bhuñjīta nāghṛtaṃ nāpy amākṣikam |
       
       kuṣṭhau patepi vāṃchaṃ kiṃ kaṇṭharogāc ca buddhimān(?) ||  
 1.6.47 toyakṣiptaṃ spṛśennānnaṃ na ca paryuṣitāśanaḥ |
       
       na cājīrṇāśano janturjighāṃsurvyādhisaṃbhavam ||  
 1.6.48 sopānatkas tathā daṇḍī chatreṇa vyajanena ca |
       
 ābādhān varjayetsarvānvicaredāpariśramāt ||  
 1.6.49  tapasvinaḥ pitṝndevānbrāhmaṇāṃś ca samāhitaḥ |
       
       arcayanvidhivannityaṃ jīvedvarṣaśataṃ naraḥ ||  
 1.6.50  vāto hi śūlaṃ vihataḥ karoti mūtrapradoṣaṃ janayec ca
      mūtram |
       
 kāsaḥ pratiśyāyamatho kṣayaṃ ca śvāsaṃ ca kuryād vihate tu vege ||  
 1.6.51  purīṣamānāhamatīva kuryād reto ' varodhaḥ kurute ' tha
      ṣāṇḍyam |
       
       tasmād dhi vegaṃ na vidhārayeta naro ya icchediha dīrghamāyuḥ || ity āha
      bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele ṣaṣṭho ' dhyāyaḥ || || saptamo ' dhyāyaḥ || athāta
      indriyopakramaṇīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 1.7.1  indriyāṇi hi sarvāṇi parijīryanti jīryataḥ |
       
       tasmāt sarvatra vayasi yathākālaṃ striyaṃ vrajet ||  
 1.7.2  na tvanāpyāyitabalaḥ samāgacchet tu yoṣitaḥ |
       
       nāyoniṣu prayuñjīta tiryagyonīś ca varjayet ||  
 1.7.3  na prāptaṃ dhārayed vegaṃ gatvā śītodakaṃ spṛśet |
       
       na tu śrānto na vā bhukto na kliṣṭo ' pyāvilo na ca ||  
 1.7.4  kṛśo nātyaśito vāpi dīno vā maithunaṃ vrajet |
       
       mitavāk satataṃ yaḥ syāt snigdhānnāśī  yuvā++ācaret ||  
 1.7.5 subahusnigdharetāś ca yathartuśayanāśanaḥ |
       
       jīrṇāmāsannasatvāṃ ca vyādhitāṃ malināṃ kṛśām ||  
 1.7.6  vyaṅginīṃ parakāmāṃ ca pūtikoṣṭhāṃ ca varjayet |
       
       balamārogyamāyuś ca vapustejaś ca dehinām ||  
 1.7.7  hīyate hīdṛśīṃ gatvā prāpyākālajarāmiva  |
       
       ṛtāvṛtau yathākālaṃ maithunaṃ nā samācaret ||  
 1.7.8  varṣāsu navarātrāt tu daśarātrāccharady api |
       
       pañcāhāddhemasamaye saptāhācchiśire tathā ||  
 1.7.9  pakṣādvasante grīṣme tu māsi māsi samācaret |
       
       nidāghe paścime māse maithunaṃ caiva varjayet ||  
 1.7.10  athavā yauvanotsāhabalasnehasamanvitaḥ  |
       
       śiśirāmbukṛtasnāno hṛdyasraganulepanaḥ ||  
 1.7.11  nātivyāyāmanirataḥ kṣīramāṃsaghṛtāśanaḥ |
       
       hṛdyamālyāmbaradharā hṛdyābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ ||  
 1.7.12  hṛdyayauvanasaṃpannāḥ priyāḥ priyakathānugāḥ |
       
       hṛṣṭāḥ sarvatra kāle a śaktyardhena vrajetstriyaḥ ||  
 1.7.13  caturdaśīṃ pañcadaśīmaṣṭamīṃ ca vivarjayet |
       
       pibetkṣīraṃ ghṛtaṃ nityam āyuṣyakaraṇaṃ hitam ||  
 1.7.14  balavarṇakaraṃ hyetadārogyakaraṇaṃ tathā |
       
       saṃhārayed romanakhaṃ trirmāsasya ca mānavaḥ ||  
 1.7.15  oṣadhīś ca maṇīṃś caiva maṅgalyān dhārayetsadā |
       
       mantrānāvartayec cāpi brahmaproktaṃ sanātanam ||  
 1.7.16  sa me mādyāpagāddehādvāyuḥ prāṇāś ca ye sadā |
       
       indro me balamādadyād śivaṃ cāpo diśantu naḥ ||  
 1.7.17  ity evaṃ mantramārṣaṃ vai bhuktvā gatvāt havā striyaḥ |
       
       saṃjapanvai spṛśan vāri tathā ' syāyurna hīyate || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele saptamo ' dhyāyaḥ || || aṣṭamo ' dhyāyaḥ || athāto mātrāśitīyaṃ
      vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 1.8.1  mātrāśī syādvipakvāśī daṇḍapāṇirmitādhvagaḥ |
       
       yathartubhojanaṃ kṛtvā janturdhūmamimaṃ pibet ||  
 1.8.2  kaiḍaryaśśatapuṣpā ca tālīsāguruguggulu |
       
       priyaṅgavaś ca kṣaumaṃ ca sarpiṣā snehitaṃ pibet ||  
 1.8.3  bhojanenerito vāyuḥ koṣṭhācchirasi tiṣṭhati |
       
       prasidhyati sa dhūmena kaphaś cāpaiti cakṣuṣaḥ ||  
 1.8.4  taṇḍulān pṛthukāṃś cāpi sarvān piṣṭamayāṃstilān |
       
       na khāded bhuktavān janturmātrāṃ khādedbubhukṣitaḥ ||  
 1.8.5  adhvanā na śramaṃ gacchetsarvānvegānna dhārayet |
       
 hitvāpi sarvakāryāṇi tathāsyāyurna hīyate ||  
 1.8.6  varjayed viṣamaṃ duḥkhamāsanaṃ pādalambanam |
       
       rakṣeccharīraṃ vātebhyo nityam eva durāsanāt ||  
 1.8.7  atyāsanamatisthānamaticaṅkramaṇāni ca |
       
       atisvapnamaśayyāṃ ca tathā  cāpy atibhāṣaṇam ||  
 1.8.8  yac ca kiṃcidviceṣṭābhir atyarthaṃ kurute naraḥ |
       
       sarvametadanāyuṣyaṃ bhiṣajaḥ paricakṣate ||  
 1.8.9  samasthānāsanagatissamaśayyāśanastathā  |
       
       samajalpaviceṣṭaś ca ciraṃ jīvati mānavaḥ ||  
 1.8.10  nivātam upaseveta sukhavātaṃ kadācana |
       
       nivātamāyuṣaḥ pathyamārogyāya ca sarvadā ||  
 1.8.11  ātape nācaretkarma śirastrāṇamṛte tathā |
       
       nidāghavarjaṃ ca sadā nāvaśyā ye samācaret ||  
 1.8.12  śaradvasantaprāvṛṭsu kārayec cānuvāsanam  |
       
       rogāś ca vastidāpyāḥ syuryasya nityaṃ  ca dāpayet ||  
 1.8.13  svapnāntasandhyayoś cāpi na khādenna ca saṃviśet |
       
       na rātrau vicaredeko nāgāraṃ śūnyamāviśet ||  
 1.8.14  catuṣpathaṃ pariharetparvate na ciraṃ vaset |
       
       rātrau ca vṛkṣamūlāni paradārāṃtathaiva ca ||  
 1.8.15  rājāniṣṭaṃ prajābhaṅgaṃ dāvāgniṃ  kalahaṃ nṛṇām |
       
       mattonmattāṃś ca saṃlakṣya dūrād eva vivarjayet ||  
 1.8.16  vairiṇo nopaseveta bāhubhyāṃ na nadīṃ taret |
       
       hastyaśvagāś ca sarpaṃ ca dūrataḥ parivarjayet ||  
 1.8.17  madhumehaś ca śoṣaś ca tṛṣṇā vātādyupadrutiḥ |
       
       madyapānāt tu na bhavettasmāt tadvidhivatpibet ||  
 1.8.18 ākvāthitajalaṃ māsāṃś caturo  mātrayā pibet |
       
 śrāvaṇaprabhṛtīneva śeṣānaṣṭa yathāsukham ||  
 1.8.19  abhuktvāmalakaṃ khāded bhuktvā cāpi harītakīm |
       
       pariṇāme ca bhaktasya khādec cāpi vibhītakam ||  
 1.8.20  kaṣāyabhāvācchaleṣmāṇamamlabhāvāc ca mārutam |
       
       pittaṃ madhurabhāvāc ca samyagāmalakaṃ jayet ||  
 1.8.21 uṣṇabhāvātkṣaṇādeti pittaṃ cāśayamūrcchitam |
       
 samyaṅnayatyataḥ khādedabhayāṃ bhuktavān naraḥ ||  
 1.8.22  āhārapariṇāmas tu pittaśleṣmavivardhakaḥ |
       
       tasmāt sāmyaṃ tayor icchannādadīta  vibhītakam ||  
 1.8.23  kālyaṃ vidhiṃ vai kṛtvā ca snāyādṛtusukhairjalaiḥ |
       
 susthaśśucisamācāraḥ sadācārapade sthitaḥ ||  
 1.8.24  mūtramapsu na kurvīta purīṣaṃ ca kadācana |
       
 na niṣṭhīvettathā prājño rakṣañjīvitamātmanaḥ ||  
 1.8.25  na haredviṣamaṃ grīvāṃ na vāpi viṣamaṃ kṣuyāt |
       
       ṛjvāsīno naraḥ khādyamādadīta vicakṣaṇaḥ ||  
 1.8.26  mātaraṃ pitaraṃ bhāryāmācāryaṃ vānupālayet |
       
       abhivādanayogāc ca vardhayed āyurātmanaḥ ||  
 1.8.27  rājāpathyacarā ye vai ye ca taddrohiṇo narāḥ |
       
       vidharmiṇaś cānṛtāś ca na tairekībhavetkvacit ||  
 1.8.28  etadapyāhurārogyaṃ dhanyaṃ pūjyaṃ yaśaskaram |
       
       sadbhir ācaritaṃ pūrvaṃ vṛttamātreyasammatam || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele aṣṭamo ' dhyāyaḥ || || navamo ' dhyāyaḥ || athātaś
      catuṣpādabhiṣagjitīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 1.9.1  bheṣajaṃ hi catuṣpādamāturaṃ kurute ' gadam |
       
       yunakti yaśasā vaidyamarthamapyasya yacchati ||  
 1.9.2  tasmād auṣadhayogasya  vaidyasyāpy āturasya 
      ca |
       
 upasthātuś ca vakṣyāmi sampadaṃ siddhikārikām ||  
 1.9.3  prativātaṃ yathākṣiptaḥ  pāṃsumuṣṭirvinaśyati |
       
       tathā hi nāśamāgacchedṛte  karma bhiṣakkṛtāt ||  
 1.9.4 nadyāṃ prasyandamānāyāṃ śvabhrasthāne sthaleṣu ca |
       
       praṇaśyati yathā vṛṣṭaṃ tathā duryojitāḥ kriyāḥ ||  
 1.9.5 iṣvāsas tu yathā yukto dharmātmā khaḍgapāṇidhṛt |
       
       parebhyaḥ kṣobham ādhatte pātyātmīyāṃś ca hantyarīn ||  
 1.9.6  evaṃ cikitsakaḥ pādair bheṣajaiś copabṛṃhitaḥ |
       
       rakṣatyakīrterātmānaṃ vyādhiṃ cāpi niyacchati ||  
 1.9.7  sidhyati pratikurvāṇa ity ātreyasya śāsanam |
       
       api cāpratikurvāṇa ity ākhyadbhadraśaunakaḥ ||  
 1.9.8 guṇayuktāturadravyabhiṣakparicarānvitā  |
       
 dṛśyate viphalā yasmānnāphalā tu viparyaye ||  
 1.9.9  tasmānnaikāntikī siddhiś catuṣpāde cikitsite |
       
       na tvetāṃ buddhimātreyaśśaunakasyānumanyate ||  
 1.9.10  pratikurvati siddhirhi varṇotsāhabalānvitā |
       
       na ca syādvyādhibahutā na tvevāpratikurvati ||  
 1.9.11  durvarṇo durbalaś ca syād vyādhibhiś cāpy upadrutaḥ |
       
       vikalo vā bhavatyajñair upakrānta ivāturaḥ ||  
 1.9.12  na sā siddhirasiddhiḥ syādyāṃ dṛṣṭvā nābhipadyate |
       
       tasmāt jñānavatāṃ siddhiṃ vindeta matimān bhiṣak ||  
 1.9.13  tatra prathamataḥ pādamauṣadhaṃ tu nibodha me |
       
       khaṃ vāyuranalastoyaṃ bhūmiś caiveha pañcamī ||  
 1.9.14 guṇottarāṇi sarvāṇi yathāsaṃkhyaṃ vibhāvayet |
       
       teṣāntu ye bhūtaguṇāḥ pṛthagbhāvanidarśakāḥ ||  
 1.9.15  parasparasamāyogāddravyeṣveva bhavanti te |
       
       lakṣaṇaṃ khasya sauṣiryaṃ raukṣyaṃ cāpy anilātmakam ||  
 1.9.16  auṣṇyamagnerapāṃ śaity aṃ kharatvaṃ pārthivo guṇaḥ |
       
       yasminyasmin bhavelliṅgametaddravye viśeṣataḥ ||  
 1.9.17  yasya bhūtasya taddravyaṃ tattadātmakamiṣyate |
       
       sauṣiryaṃ lāghavaṃ yatra bhaiṣajyaṃ cāpi khātmakam ||  
 1.9.18  kharatvaṃ ca vivekaś ca raukṣyaṃ cāpy anilātmakam |
       
       snehaḥ kledaś ca śaity aṃ ca mṛdutvaṃ cāpi vārijam ||  
 1.9.19  paicchilyaṃ gauravaṃ mūrtisthairyaṃ gandhaś ca pārthivam
      |
       
       etairbhūtaguṇairyuktaṃ yaddravyaṃ tattadātmakam ||  
 1.9.20  pañcabhūtātmakaissarvairguṇais tatra samanvitam |
       
 (prativāsaṃ raso gandhastadā praduvanāni ca ||  
 1.9.21  śitamuṣṇodakaṃ caiva raidya cedipriyaṃ rathāḥ |
       
       sajjopakaraṇatvaṃ ca mūlatvakphalasañcayaḥ) ||  
 1.9.22  mūlādīnāṃ sugandhitvaṃ kalyāṇasparśavattathā  |
       
 anyūnānatiriktatvarūpavac ca praśasyate ||  
 1.9.23 sthalātmatākanimneṣu saikateṣūpaleṣu ca |
       
       suṣiraṃ nātiviṣṭaṃ ca tiryagyātaṃ ca garhitam ||  
 1.9.24  yenauṣadhārthassadyassyāttena cāpratibadhnatā |
       
       bheṣajaṃ prathamaḥ pādaḥ iti jñeyaṃ cikitsite ||  
 1.9.25  pratiśrāvī dvitīyaḥ syāttasya pratyekaśo guṇāḥ |
       
       balavān dakṣiṇo dakṣaḥ priyavāgajugupsakaḥ ||  
 1.9.26  vīraś cāpratikūlaś ca raktaścitrakathas tathā |
       
       prajñāvāṃś cāpy upasthāyī tathā śāstrānusārataḥ ||  
 1.9.27  na cātipratibadhnīyātsarveṣv auṣadhakarmasu |
       
       praśasyate kleśasahaḥ pratiśrāvī yathāguṇaḥ ||  
 1.9.28  tṛtīyaś cāturaḥ pādaḥ satyāśaṃsī praśasyate |
       
       lakṣaṇaś cātmavāṃś caiva kṛtajñassumanāś ca yaḥ ||  
 1.9.29  auṣadhasya pratigrāhī na ca rogānnigūhayet |
       
       dṛḍhabhakto ' nasūyaś ca yaś cāpi na viṣīdati ||  
 1.9.30  sarvatrāpratikūlaś ca na kriyāmativartate |
       
       ebhir guṇaissamāyuktaṃ jānīyātsādhyamāturam ||  
 1.9.31  bhiṣak caturthaḥ pādas tu sasūtrārthaviśāradaḥ |
       
       arogo dṛṣṭakarmā ca kṛtakṛtyeṣu kovidaḥ ||  
 1.9.32  prayoktā ca pragalbhaś ca kṣamāvānpratibhānavān |
       
       buddhimāṃstarkakuśalo vīryaudāryabalānvitaḥ ||  
 1.9.33  astabdhaś cāpramattaś ca satataṃ saṃyatendriyaḥ |
       
       ojasvī cauṣadhajñaś ca deśakālaprayogavit ||  
 1.9.34  bhiṣak caturthapādaḥ syādevaṃguṇasamanvitaḥ |
       
       bheṣajaṃ ca pratiśrāvī bhiṣagātura eva ca ||  
 1.9.35  anyonyaguṇasaṃyogād ete syus siddhikārakāḥ |
       
       eta eva ca vauguṇyāttasya vyādhivivardhanāḥ  ||  
 1.9.36  tasmāc caturṣu pādeṣu cikitsāsiddhiriṣyate |
       
       paktaye kāraṇaṃ pakturyathā pātrendhanānalāḥ ||  
 1.9.37  vijeturvijaye  bhūmiś camūḥ praharaṇāni ca |
       
       āturādyās tathā pādāḥ siddhau kāraṇasaṃjñitāḥ ||  
 1.9.38  mṛddaṇḍacakrasūtrādyāḥ kumbhakārādṛte yathā |
       
       nāvahanti guṇān vaidyādṛte pādatrayaṃ tathā |
       
       vidyāt tasmāc cikitsāyāṃ pradhānaṃ kāraṇaṃ bhiṣak || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ
      iti bhele navamo ' dhyāyaḥ || || daśamo ' dhyāyaḥ || athāta āmapradoṣīyaṃ
      vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 1.10.1  athāha tailātpiṣṭānnāt kṛsarāt pāyasād api |
       
       viruddhādhyaśanādāmācchālūkācchuṣkaśākataḥ ||  
 1.10.2  hrīśokakrodhakāmerṣyā lobhodvegādbhayād api |
       
       anyasmādīdṛśādvāpi rātrau jāgaraṇena vā ||  
 1.10.3  jantośśāmyati kāyāgnirathavā duṣṭaśayyayā |
       
 udveṣṭyante ' sya gātrāṇi kaṭipṛṣṭhaṃ ca dūyate ||  
 1.10.4  jaṅghe śūlāyataś cāsya jvaraś cāsyopajāyate |
       
       śiro guru bhavatyasya tathā netre śarīriṇaḥ ||  
 1.10.5  sodgāraṃ  savidāhaṃ  ca kaphapittaṃ
      prasicyate |
       
 stimitaṃ cāsya hṛdayamādhmātamiva codaram ||  
 1.10.6  dṛtiḥ pūrṇaṃ ivānaddhaḥ kṣubhyate doṣasaṃcayāt |
       
       saṃchardayati cābhīkṣṇaṃ mūrchāṃ cāpi niyacchati ||  
 1.10.7  api tṛṣyatyayaṃ gāḍhamāsyaṃ hyasyopaśuṣyati |
       
       svarabhedo ' sya bhavati kaṇṭhaśśuṣka  ivodgataḥ ||  
 1.10.8  manye ca paridahyete śraddhā cāsya na jāyate |
       
       yadāsya vāyuḥ pittaṃ ca śleṣmā cāpi samudgataḥ ||  
 1.10.9 āmena saṃyutaś caiva sāvaśeṣaḥ pravartate |
       
       sa ubhābhyāṃ tathābhīkṣṇaṃ srotobhyāmatirecitaḥ ||  
 1.10.10  kaphapitte kṣayaṃ prāpte vāte hi kila mūrcchite |
       
       śuddhakoṣṭhe hṛte doṣe śūnyakāye ca mārutaḥ ||  
 1.10.11  ekasthāne  tvanāsakto vidhāvati tatastataḥ |
       
       vaṅkṣaṇaṃ hṛdayaṃ nābhivastimarmāṇi cāviśan ||  
 1.10.12 saṃjñāṃ hṛtvaiva kurute muhurmuhuracetanam |
       
       ity etadrūpamāmasya yathāvadupalakṣayet ||  
 1.10.13 ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi jīrṇasyānnasya lakṣaṇam |
       
       madhuraḥ pūrvamudgāro madhye cāmlo yadā bhavet ||  
 1.10.14 paścātsakaṭukaś cāpi nirvidāho bhavatyatha |
       
       lāghavaṃ vīkṣyate kāye viśuddhaṃ viśadaṃ mukham ||  
 1.10.15  praguṇaṃ kurute vātamūrdhvaṃ vā yadi vāpy adhaḥ |
       
       bhoktuṃ śrāddhā bhavatyasya rujā cānyopaśāmyati ||  
 1.10.16  ity ebhir lakṣaṇairjīrṇaṃ vidyādannaṃ śarīriṇām |
       
       ajīrṇaṃ laṅghayed āme pācanīyastato bhavet ||  
 1.10.17  yavāgvādibhir āhāraissaṃsṛjedvā tamuttaram |
       
       śuṇṭhīprativiṣāmustākvāthaḥ syādāmapācanaḥ ||  
 1.10.18 śuṇṭhīnīrakadhānyākaistulyaiḥ kvātho rucipradaḥ |
       
       mustaṃ hiṅgu trikaṭukaṃ pāṭhā vatsā harītakī ||  
 1.10.19 cūrṇaḥ prativiṣā ceti citrakaś cāmanāśanaḥ |
       
 pippalīnāgarakṣārassukhodakasamāyutaḥ  ||  
 1.10.20  svedanaṃ kaphavartiś ca śūleṣu stimiteṣu ca
      |
       
       agāradhūmaḥ pippalyo madanaṃ rājasarṣapāḥ |
       
 gomūtrapiṣṭāssaguḍāḥ phalavartiḥ praśasyate || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ
      iti bhele daśamo ' dhyāyaḥ || || ekādaśo ' dhyāyaḥ ||
       athātassamaśayanaparighanīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān
      ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 1.11.1  āhāraṃ praghasaṃ nẏṇām upayuktaṃ caturvidham |
       
       pacyamānaṃ dvidhā kāye koṣṭhe rasamalākhyayā ||  
 1.11.2  svedamūtraśakṛdrūpairniṣkrāmati  malaḥ punaḥ |
       
       annasya pākatastejo raso nirvartyate nṛṇām ||  
 1.11.3  rasādraktaṃ tato māṃsaṃ māṃsānmedastato ' sthi ca |
       
       asthno majjā tataḥ śuklaṃ śuklād garbhasya saṃbhavaḥ ||  
 1.11.4  evaṃ pūrvātparaṃ yāti dhātuṃ dhāturyathākramam |
       
       mātrāpathyaṃ yadā bhuktaṃ rasarūpaṃ gataṃ punaḥ ||  
 1.11.5  kuryānna rogān dīptāgneḥ rasavyāpattisambhavān |
       
       śoṇitādyātmatāṃ gacchet pariṇāmavaśāṃ tadā ||  
 1.11.6  yasmin vyāpadyate dhātau tasmin vyādhīn karotyatha |
       
       viṣūcikāṃ sālasakāṃ pittadāhaṃ vilambikām ||  
 1.11.7  anyedyuṣkaṃ satatakaṃ tṛtīyakacaturthakam |
       
       pittaṃ lohitapittaṃ ca raktārśāṃsi pralepakam ||  
 1.11.8  vipāṭikāṃś ca tān vyādhīn rasavyāpattijān viduḥ |
       
 kacchūṃ carmadalaṃ pāmāṃ carmakīlaṃ vicarcikām ||  
 1.11.9 vyaṅgavīsarpakuṣṭhāni raktavyāpattijānviduḥ |
       
       māṃsakīlārbudaṃ gaṇḍamajakāṃ jātulāni(?) ca ||  
 1.11.10 pūtimāṃsālajīś caiva māṃsavyāpattijān viduḥ |
       
       daurgandhyaṃ svedanaṃ sthaulyaṃ pipāsāṃ bahunidratām ||  
 1.11.11  pramehān viṃśatiṃ cāpi medovyāpattijānviduḥ |
       
       dantarogo nakhaśmaśrukeśaromābhipātanam ||  
 1.11.12  ativṛddhis tathā vāsthnāmasthivyāpattijān viduḥ |
       
       vidāhaṃ ca madaṃ caiva sonmādaṃ cāpatānakam ||  
 1.11.13  tamodarśanamūrchāyau majjāvyāpattijān viduḥ |
       
       retaḥ kṣārāgnimañjiṣṭhānīlahāridrakaṃ pṛthak ||  
 1.11.14  mehane bhasmavarṇaṃ ca śuklavyāpattijānviduḥ |
       
       narasya strīsvaratvaṃ vā strī vāpi puruṣasvarā ||  
 1.11.15  āmagarbhacyutirvāpi garbhavyāpattijānviduḥ |
       
       ity ete āmajā nẏṇāṃ viruddhādhyaśanātmakāḥ |
       
       viruddhāśanavarjī syādetadārogyam uttamam || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ iti
      bhele ekādaśo ' dhyāyaḥ || || dvādaśo ' dhyāyaḥ || athātaḥ
      ātreyakhaṇḍakāpyīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 1.12.1 ātreyaḥ khaṇḍakāpyaś ca maitreyo ' nye ca tadvidhāḥ
      |
       
       rasasaṃkhyākathāṃ cakrurvane caitrarathe dvijāḥ ||  
 1.12.2  tatra kaścidrasaikatvaṃ rasasāmānyato ' bravīt |
       
       sātmyāsātmyāttathā dvitvaṃ traividhyaṃ sthānato ' pare ||  
 1.12.3 svādurasvāduramṛdurmṛduśceti  catuṣṭayam |
       
       mahābhūtavibhāgena pañcetyāhustathāpare ||  
 1.12.4  tadetad evaṃ jānīyādyathoktādeva kāraṇāt |
       
       ṣaṭtvaṃ saptatvamathavā brūyustadrucibhedataḥ ||  
 1.12.5  madhuro lavaṇāmlau ca kaṣāyakaṭutiktakāḥ |
       
       kṣāraś ca tān rasān sapta nātirekaṃ samācaret ||  
 1.12.6  rasātisevanājjantussadyo mṛtyumavāpnuyāt |
       
       bhaveyurvyādhayaś cāsya rasavyāsaṅgasaṃbhavāḥ ||  
 1.12.7  vṛttarohitarājībhiḥ vṛttākṣaśśakalī tathā |
       
       matsyaścilicimo nāma kūle carati vāriṇaḥ ||  
 1.12.8  taṃ matsyaṃ varjayed ekaṃ dugdhenānyāṃs tu bhakṣayet |
       
       payasā bhakṣyamāṇas tu nararaktaṃ pradūṣayan ||  
 1.12.9  raktavyāpattijānvyādhīn mṛtyuṃ cāpi sa yacchati |
       
       śvāvidvarāhaṃ caikatra payasā parivarjayet ||  
 1.12.10  vanyamūlaphalāhārastadvidhena  viruddhyate |
       
       aśnīyātpayasā yas tu sadyo mṛtyumavāpnuyāt ||  
 1.12.11  bhaveyurvyādhayaś cāsya śaṅkharogagalagrahāḥ |
       
       madhunā gorasenāpi likucaṃ na ca bhakṣayet ||  
 1.12.12  bādhiryaṃ vā ' pyathāndhyaṃ vā mṛtyuṃ vā bhakṣayan
      vrajet |
       
       kapotān sarṣapairbhṛṣṭān payasā na tu bhakṣayet ||  
 1.12.13  majjāvyāpattijān vyādhīnprāpnuyāddhi tathā param |
       
       payasā sarpadaṣṭassan khādyaissiddhyati tādṛśaiḥ ||  
 1.12.14  krimijā vyādhayaś cāsya dṛśyante yadi jīvati |
       
       iha yā strī pumāṃś caiva hitajīrṇamitāśanau ||  
 1.12.15  anudāvartinau caiva syātāṃ garbhastayoḥ khalu |
       
       balavān varṇavāṃś caiva cakṣuṣmāṃś ca bhavatyatha ||  
 1.12.16  viparyaye vartamānau  viparītamiharcchataḥ |
       
       ajīrṇe tvaśanaṃ yasya jīrṇe cānaśanaṃ bhavet ||  
 1.12.17  sa tathobhayathā rogān dāruṇān prāpyān naraḥ |
       
       tasmājjīrṇe ca pathyāś ca mātrāvanto ' virodhinaḥ |
       
       sarva eva rasā bhojyāḥ yuktyā saṃvṛtadhātubhiḥ || ity āha
      bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele dvādaśo ' dhyāyaḥ || |
       
       |trayodaśo ' dhyāyaḥ || athāto janapadavibhaktīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha
      bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 1.13.1  kasmin janapade rogāḥ ke bhavantyadhikā iti |
       
       gurdālubhekinā pṛṣṭo vyācacakṣe punarvasuḥ ||  
 1.13.2  matsyānnabhojino nityaṃ prācyāḥ syuḥ kaphapittanaḥ |
       
       ślīpadaṃ galagaṇḍaṃ ca prāyaśasteṣu dṛśyate ||  
 1.13.3  nadītoyagatān matsyān bhakṣayanti samudrajān |
       
       prāyaśaḥ kuṣṭhikāstena manuṣyā dakṣiṇādiśi ||  
 1.13.4  masūrayavagodhūmatilakoddālasevinaḥ |
       
       bhūyiṣṭhamarśasāstena kāmbhojādantajāḥ smṛtāḥ ||  
 1.13.5  māṃsakāmāḥ surākāmāḥ strīkāmāssāhasapriyāḥ |
       
       prīcyāstena bhūyiṣṭhaṃ dṛśyante rājayakṣmiṇaḥ ||  
 1.13.6  tīkṣṇoṣṇāni hi bāhlīkāḥ prāyeṇānnāni bhuñjate |
       
       abhiṣyandīni māṃsāni pānakāny audakāni ca ||  
 1.13.7  prakṛtyā cāpy abhiṣyaṇṇāḥ  pārvatopatyakāssadā |
       
       tena bāhlīkadeśeṣu prāyo vyādhirbalāsakaḥ ||  
 1.13.8 meghe ' varṣati varṣāsu hemante yatra varṣati |
       
       ṛtuvyāpattisamaye janamāraḥ pravartate ||  
 1.13.9  tatropavāsī dhṛtimān rato viprābhivādane |
       
       mantrauṣadharataś cāpi janamārāt pramucyate ||  
 1.13.10  sūryopatāpātsahasā varṣānte pittamīryate |
       
       śaradi prāyaśastena jvaro bhavati dehinām ||  
 1.13.11  gavāṃ ca cāraṇākhyaś ca catuṣpācchvāpadeṣu ca |
       
       indrajālaś ca matsyeṣu śakunānāṃ pramīlakaḥ ||  
 1.13.12  citrakassarvadhānyeṣu davo mūlaphaleṣu ca |
       
       hastināṃ pākalaś caiva jvara ity abhidhīyate ||  
 1.13.13  utkarṇakastathāśveṣu tejassarvāmayeṣu ca |
       
       sarvatra vasati hyeṣa eṣa cāntaka ucyate ||  
 1.13.14  taṃ dhūmaketuṃ pratyakṣaṃ kṣipraṃ praśamayejjvaram
      |
       
       asātmyaṃ gandhamādāya vāto yatrātivījyate  ||  
 1.13.15  tatra martyeṣu sāmānyaḥ pratiśyāyaḥ pravartate |
       
       tathā batālikā nāma piṭakā cāsya jāyate ||  
 1.13.16  kakṣāyāmūrumūle ca pāṇipādataleṣu ca |
       
       kaṇṭhe vā śrotramāśrity a vastau vā hṛdaye ' pi vā ||  
 1.13.17  tvaramāṇaścikitseta pravṛddhā mārayennaram |
       
       pittaśleṣmasamutthānā vātaśoṇitmūrcchitā ||  
 1.13.18  batāliketi tāmāhuryatnavāṃs tatra jīvati |
       
       ity etatsamyaguddiṣṭaṃ sarvaṃ yadyac ca coditam |
       
       ṛṣibhyaḥ paripṛcchadbhyaḥ praśnajātaṃ yathākramam || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ
      |
       
       iti bhele trayodaśo ' dhyāyaḥ || || caturdaśo ' dhyāyaḥ || athātaḥ
      cikitsāprābhṛtīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 1.14.1  cikitsāprābhṛto vidvān vidyāt saṃśodhane vidhim |
       
       na ca dhāmārgavaṃ dadyāt snehasvedānupaskṛte ||  
 1.14.2  yo hi saṃśodhanaṃ pītvā sakaṣāyāṇi sevate |
       
       tasya tāni tadā jīvaṃ harantyanu hutāśanam ||  
 1.14.3  dāru śuṣkamivāsvinnaṃ nāmyamānaṃ yathā bhevet |
       
       tathā virecanaṃ hanyāt snehasvedānupaskṛte ||  
 1.14.4  snehasvedopapannaṃ tu charditaṃ bhāvitaṃ punaḥ |
       
       virecanasya siddhyarthaṃ pūrvamāsthāpayed bhiṣak ||  
 1.14.5  ajīryadatha rūkṣaṃ hi virecanamathollikhet |
       
       oṣadhīrhīnavīryāś ca mātrāhīnāś ca varjayet ||  
 1.14.6 atimātraṃ hi bhaiṣajyaṃ jīvaṃ harati dehinām |
       
       tasmāt kālaṃ balaṃ mātrāmṛtuṃ vidyādvirecane ||  
 1.14.7  yathā vṛkṣasya puṣpeṣu palāśeṣu phaleṣu ca |
       
 śīrṇeṣv anyāni rohanti tathā vyādhiranirhṛtaḥ ||  
 1.14.8  yathā mūle tarośchanne mlāyatyagraṃ na saṃśayaḥ |
       
       evaṃ virecite vyādhirupaśāmyati dehinām ||  
 1.14.9 udakaṃ codamanthaṃ ca matsyānmāṃsatilānapi |
       
       guru cānnaṃ na bhuñjīta snehasantarpaṇāni ca ||  
 1.14.10  virecanaṃ tu yaḥ pītvā dāruṇaṃ  rūkṣite gude |
       
       dāruṇaṃ bhaktamaśnāti tamāmiṣarasena vai ||  
 1.14.11  tad yathā hyudakaṃ nimnaṃ sthalādadhyavarohati |
       
       snehitasya tathā doṣāḥ kukṣimāyānti sarvaśaḥ ||  
 1.14.12  snehanairvyādhitasthānādrasaiś cābhyadhikīkṛtāḥ |
       
       svedairmṛdūkṛtāssantaḥ srotasā ca samāgatāḥ ||  
 1.14.13  mṛdusarvāṅgakoṣṭhasya bheṣajaiśśucibhis tadā |
       
       doṣāssunirharā jantorbhavantīti viniścayaḥ ||  
 1.14.14  eṣa heturvirekeṣu chardaneṣveṣa eva tu |
       
       eṣa heturnirūheṣu śirasaś ca virecane ||  
 1.14.15  bahusnigdho viriktaś ca yo rasairnopapādyate |
       
       bheṣajairapyupastabdhaḥ so ' timātraṃ vipadyate ||  
 1.14.16  vakṣyāmi ca kriyāmanyāmajātavyādhināśinīm |
       
       madhu seveta varṣāsu sarpiḥ śaradi cācaret ||  
 1.14.17  sammiśraṃ gaṇḍakenaiva vāruṇīṃ śiśire pibet |
       
       mārdvīkaṃ tu vasante vai nidāghe kṣīramācaret ||  
 1.14.18  kalmāṣā vātalā rūkṣā guravo bhinnavarcasaḥ |
       
 śiraso ' ntastarpayantaḥ śleṣmaṇaś ca viśoṣaṇāḥ ||  
 1.14.19  udāvartāñjayantyete snigdhatvād gauravād api |
       
       raukṣyāt tridhā sā jananāt śleṣmannākalāstathā(?) ||  
 1.14.20  evaṃ tu vartamānānām āyurvṛddhim avāpnuyāt |
       
       nẏṇāṃ samādhipūrṇānāmadīnamanasāṃ tathā || ity āha bhgavānātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele caturdaśo ' dhyāyaḥ || || pañcadaśo ' dhyāyaḥ ||
      athātastisraiṣaṇīyamadhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 1.15.1  prāṇaiṣaṇā syāt prathamā dvitīyā
      tu dhanaiṣaṇā |
       
       dharmaiṣaṇā tṛtīyā tu puruṣasya bhavatyatha ||  
 1.15.2  tatra prāṇaiṣaṇāṃ  pūrvaṃ samāpadyeta mānavaḥ |
       
       dharmārthakāmaprāptirhi sadbhiḥ prāṇaiḥ prapadyate ||  
 1.15.3  dharmadīnāmavāptiś ca puruṣārthaḥ paraḥ smṛtaḥ |
       
       tasmāccharīraṃ prayataḥ parirakṣeddhi śāstrataḥ ||  
 1.15.4 dhanaiṣaṇāṃ dvitīyāṃ tu samāpadyeta mānavaḥ |
       
 pāpīyo nāstyataḥ kiñcidyathā jīvannṛte dhanāt ||  
 1.15.5  dharmakāmau na saṃpīḍya tasmād vittamupārjayet |
       
       jvararogādikā yena nirasyedāpado budhaḥ ||  
 1.15.6  dharmaiṣaṇāṃ tṛtīyāṃ tu samāpadyeta mānavaḥ |
       
 avaśyamādhigantavyā dehabhede varā gatiḥ ||  
 1.15.7 prāṇādyanuparodhena tasmād dharmaṃ caredbudhaḥ |
       
       trivargānuparodhena tatprāptirhi nare hitā ||  
 1.15.8  ity etāssammatā loke vyākhyātāstisra eṣaṇāḥ |
       
       yathoktāstāḥ prayuñjānaḥ paratreha ca modate ||  
 1.15.9 upastambhās tu catvāro yadāhāraś caturvidhaḥ
      |
       
       śarīre ca balaṃ caiva malaṃ tebhyaḥ prajāyate ||  
 1.15.10  śarīramātmano marma malamātmabalaṃ punaḥ |
       
 rogās tasyātivṛddhyāṃ ca vātapittakaphātmakāḥ ||  
 1.15.11  malaṃ tu rogo bhavati vaiṣamyaṃ dhātubhir gataiḥ |
       
       malāc cāpy eti vaiṣamyaṃ tasmāt tamabhinirharet || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele pañcadaśo ' dhyāyaḥ || || ṣoḍaśo ' dhyāyaḥ || athāto
      vātakalākalīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 1.16.1 katamo ' bhyadhiko doṣo nyūnaś
      caiveti tatvataḥ |
       
       kṛṣṇātreyaṃ puraskṛtya kathāś cakrurmaharṣayaḥ ||  
 1.16.2 vātaṃ tatrādhikaṃ kaścitprāhānyam upahanti 
      yaḥ |
       
       yāvattiṣṭhati vāto hi dehī tāvat tu jīvati ||  
 1.16.3  sa hi garbhāśaye śuklaṃ visraṃsayati yoṣitaḥ |
       
       vātaḥ striyā rajo hanti vandhyā bhavati tena sā ||  
 1.16.4  na striyaḥ puruṣā vāpi vandhyāssantīha janmanā |
       
       āśaye śītalo vāpi vātaśśuṣkendriyas tathā ||  
 1.16.5  vātaḥ sadindriyo vāpi vāto hīnendriyas tathā |
       
       ālokitaṃ nimiṣitaṃ yac ca kiṃcidviceṣṭitam ||  
 1.16.6  aśītiś cāmayā nẏṇāṃ nāvātātsaṃbhavanti hi |
       
       vātāddhi kubjāḥ kuṇinaḥ khaṃjā gṛdhrasinas tathā ||  
 1.16.7  hīnāṅgā hy adhikāṅgāś ca bhavantyanye  ca tadvidhā
      |
       
       sthitiḥ prāṇabhṛtāṃ caiva saritāṃ caiva niḥsvanāḥ ||  
 1.16.8  pṛthivyāś calanaṃ caiva vātādeva pravartate |
       
       vātena dhūmo bhavati dhūmādabhraṃ prajāyate ||  
 1.16.9  abhrādvimucyte vāri bījānāṃ sambhavastataḥ |
       
       ulkānipātaḥ stanitaṃ vidhutārāgaṇasya ca ||  
 1.16.10  vidyutāṃ ca balaṃ caiva vātādeva pravartate |
       
       agnirjvalati vātena puṇyānāṃ haviṣāṃ patiḥ ||  
 1.16.11  sravanti cāpagāstena pṛthivīṃ plāvayanti ca |
       
       vāyustatrādhiko devaḥ prabhavassarvadehinām ||  
 1.16.12  yonyāṃ retaḥ prasiktaṃ ca vāyunā yujyate guṇaiḥ |
       
 eṣa pittaṃ kaphaṃ caiva hanyādanyataraṃ tayoḥ ||  
 1.16.13  ādāya kupito vāyuḥ dehe vipratipadyate |
       
       evaṃ vyānamudānaṃ ca samānaṃ ca pracakṣate ||  
 1.16.14 dehe bahuviśeṣitvād apānaṃ  prāṇam eva ca |
       
 ūrdhvago ' trāpyudānaḥ syād vyānastiryagvivṛddhikṛt ||  
 1.16.15  prāṇo nyasyatyapānaṃ tu pravartayati dehinām |
       
       samāno dhāraṇaś caiva saṃgṛhṇāti sa dehinām ||  
 1.16.16  indriyāṇi manaś caiva bhūtātmānaṃ ca sammataḥ |
       
       viśeṣas tv aparo vāyurapāna iti saṃjñitaḥ ||  
 1.16.17  śoṣaṇaś caraṇaś caiva tathā vicaraṇaḥ smṛtaḥ |
       
       vāyuḥ pañcasu bhūteṣu bhūtaṃ paramamucyate ||  
 1.16.18  tāni vāyunibaddhāni vāyussarvatra sarvadā |
       
 mūtrendriyapurīṣāṇāṃ vāyor utsarga eva ca ||  
 1.16.19  pācanāccaiva bhuktasya karmāpānasya śiṣyate |
       
       prāṇaḥ prīṇāti bhūtāni prāṇo jīva iti smṛtaḥ ||  
 1.16.20  vyānāccharīraceṣṭā ca nimeṣonmeṣaṇāni ca |
       
       yaccānyadūrdhvagaṃ jantostadudānasya ceṣṭitam ||  
 1.16.21 kṣavathuṃ hikkitaṃ kāsamucchvāsaṃ bhāṣaṇaṃ tathā |
       
       gudamādhmāpayatyeṣa dehaṃ yassa ca sarvaśaḥ ||  
 1.16.22  eṣu pratiṣṭhito vāyurapāna iti saṃjñitaḥ |
       
       ity ebhir īdṛśaiś cānyairhetubhis tattvadarśibhiḥ |
       
       bhūtebhyo ' bhyadhikaṃ vātaṃ lakṣayāma śarīriṇām  || ity āha bhagavān
      ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele ṣoḍaśo ' dhyāyaḥ || |
       
       |saptadaśo ' dhyāyaḥ || athāto daśaprāṇāyatanīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha
      bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 1.17.1  caturvidhamatho bhuktaṃ daśadhā prāṇamṛcchati |
       
       ūṣmasvedaśakṛnmūtrais tathā vātādibhis tribhiḥ ||  
 1.17.2  striyāḥ stanyena śuklena śoṇitena  ca vāpy atha |
       
       ity ebhir daśabhiḥ prāṇaḥ sthirībhavati dehinām ||  
 1.17.3 īhate ' mṛtavadvṛttiṃ vātapittakaphaistribhiḥ |
       
       āhārasāmyayogād dhi vaiṣamye vyādhayaḥ smṛtāḥ ||  
 1.17.4  iha dvau bhiṣajau vidyāt jñaś caivājñaś ca dehinām |
       
       tatra jñaḥ sūtravānyaḥ syāt sūtrārthena vicakṣaṇaḥ ||  
 1.17.5  pañcāśrayānkaṣāyāṃś ca bhojanaṃ caturāśrayam |
       
       catuḥśreṣṭhāṃs tathā snehānāmayāṃś cāturāśrayān ||  
 1.17.6  cūrṇapradehānvividhān yavāgūś cāṣṭadhā smṛtāḥ |
       
       dvādaśānnāni pathyāni prāyaścittadvayaṃ tathā ||  
 1.17.7  triṃśataṃ copanāhānāṃ sthāneṣv aṣṭāsu tattvataḥ |
       
       sūtrasthānaṃ cikitsā  ca triṃśatriṃśadihocyate ||  
 1.17.8  aṣṭau nidānānyuktāni vimānāni tathaiva ca |
       
 śārīrāṇyaṣṭa gātrāṅgapratyaṅgaṃ yatra varṇitam ||  
 1.17.9  siddhayo dvādaśa proktās tathā kalpendriyāṇi ca |
       
       etadviṃśaśataṃ proktaṃ mūlinyo yatra ṣoḍaśa ||  
 1.17.10  ekonaviṃśatirjñeyāḥ phalinyaḥ kṣīriṇītrayam |
       
       āyurjñānamariṣṭibhyaḥ sādhyāsādhyacikitsitāḥ ||  
 1.17.11 rogajñānaṃ nidānebhyo deśakālau vimānataḥ |
       
       śārīrāddhātusaṃghātaṃ prakṛtiṃ dhātusātmyatām ||  
 1.17.12  anyadevaṃvidhaṃ yac ca śāstre kiṃcidapi śrutam |
       
       bhiṣagyo vai  vijānāti sajñaḥ ajñaṃ tu nibodhata ||  
 1.17.13  yo ' nnakāle yavāgūṃ tu sūpakāle tathā rasam |
       
       yūṣakāle ' tha māṃsaṃ tu śodhyeṣu stambhanāni ca ||  
 1.17.14  virecanīye vamanaṃ nirūhye cānuvāsanam |
       
       viparyayeṇa yo ' nyadvā kurute so ' jña ucyate ||  
 1.17.15  yogena vidyām ādadyāt tasmāt tattvadidṛkṣayā |
       
       yathā tamasi dīpaḥ syāt tatrarahā śāstraṃ prakāśakṛt || ity āha bhagavān
      ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele saptadaśo ' dhyāyaḥ || || aṣṭādaśo ' dhyāyaḥ || athāto '
      nnarakṣīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 1.18.1  gāndhārabhūmau rājarṣirnagnajitsvargamārgadaḥ |
       
       saṃgṛhya pādau papraccha cāndrabhāgaṃ punarvasum ||  
 1.18.2  na ca strībhyo na cāstrebhyo na bhṛtyebhyo ' sti me
      bhayam |
       
       anyatra viṣayogebhyaḥ so ' tra me śaraṇaṃ bhavān ||  
 1.18.3  evamuktas tathā tasmai maharṣiḥ pārthivarṣaye |
       
       viṣayogeṣu vijñānaṃ provāca vadatāṃ varaḥ ||  
 1.18.4  viṣeṇa saha saṃsṛṣṭamannapānaṃ caturvidham |
       
       yāni duṣṭāni rūpāṇi tāni me gadataḥ śṛṇu ||  
 1.18.5 pratikūlamivābhāti phenilaṃ viplutākṛti  |
       
 śuklaṃ bhavati yatkṣipraṃ nainaṃ śliṣyanti makṣikāḥ ||  
 1.18.6  dhūmaś cāsya gataḥ śyāmo raktaḥ kṛṣṇo ' tha pītakaḥ
      |
       
       prādur bhavati tadvidyād duṣṭamannaṃ pracakṣaṇaḥ ||  
 1.18.7  nīlapītāsitā rājyo bhantīndrāyudhopamāḥ |
       
       madhye madyeṣu sarveṣu ye cānye pānasaṃśrayāḥ ||  
 1.18.8  anulepanadoṣe tu tvagasya bahulībhavet |
       
       sarvavyāpattimāpnoti klidyate māṃsam eva ca ||  
 1.18.9  mālyaṃ tu śyāvapuṣpaṃ syānmlānaṃ kālaṃ ca dṛśyate |
       
       cūrṇayogāvakīrṇaṃ tu reṇunevāvṛtaṃ bhavet ||  
 1.18.10  romāṇi pariśīryante keśabhūmiś ca dhūpyate |
       
       kūrcasparśaś ca duḥkhaḥ syājjaṭilācāsya mūrdhajāḥ ||  
 1.18.11  vedanāṃ caiva kaṇḍūṃ ca kurute duṣṭamañjanam  |
       
       aśru sravati nātyarthamandhakāraṃ ca paśyati ||  
 1.18.12  dhūmadoṣe  virekaḥ syādatyarthaṃ śirasaś ca ruk |
       
       paridāhaś ca bhedaś ca gandhajñānamasādhu ca ||  
 1.18.13  na samyagvetti ca rasānaraṇīva ca mathyate |
       
       iti dhūmasya rūpāṇi sarvāṇy etāni lakṣayet ||  
 1.18.14  duṣṭe vāsasi liṅgāni sūcībhir iva tudyate |
       
       dahyate muñcati svedaṃ mūrchatyapyavalīyate ||  
 1.18.15  duṣṭe tvābharaṇe  dāhaḥ svedaḥ kaṇḍūś ca jāyate |
       
       kurute gātravaivarṇyaṃ svayaṃ cābhāti niṣprabhaḥ ||  
 1.18.16  duṣṭamāsanamāsthāyī vimūḍho vipaten naraḥ |
       
       sīdatyucchūnavṛṣaṇo na cotthātuṃ sahī bhavet ||  
 1.18.17  ūrū cāsya pravepete sadoṣāsanasevayā |
       
       duṣṭe tu śayane rūpaṃ suptiḥ kaṇḍūyate bhṛśam ||  
 1.18.18  svedaś ca  viṣamatyeti romakūpaiḥ samantataḥ |
       
       tudyamānaḥ punaḥ śayyāṃ manyate jantubhir vṛtām ||  
 1.18.19  sudine durdine cāpi durdine sudinaṃ tathā |
       
       syād bhūś ca duṣṭaparyantā  duṣṭacchatraniṣevaṇāt ||  
 1.18.20  kurute rūpavaivarṇyaṃ praduṣṭaśmaśruvardhakaḥ |
       
       śiśire muñcati svedaṃ grīṣme śītāturo bhavet ||  
 1.18.21  pravepate pravyathate gadgadā ca sarasvatī |
       
       syandanau ca vivarṇau ca paruṣau daśanacchadau ||  
 1.18.22  upānahau yadā duṣṭau tadā kaṇḍūḥ prajāyate |
       
       prasvidyate pādatalaṃ tathā cimacimāyate ||  
 1.18.23  atheha viṣapītasya viṣadagdhasya vā punaḥ |
       
       digdhaviddhasya vā rājan rūpāṇīmāni lakṣayet ||  
 1.18.24  gātrodveṣṭanamāpnoti vepate vyathate naraḥ |
       
       kampate cāpi kaṇṭho ' sya niḥsvanaṃ ṣṭhīvate muhuḥ ||  
 1.18.25  jihvā cāsya jaḍībhūtā śūlair iva ca tudyate |
       
       vyāhartuṃ ca na śaknoti śarma caiva na vindati ||  
 1.18.26  keśāntaṃ śīryate cāsya nakhāḥ śyāmībhavanti ca |
       
       aṅguṣṭhāṅgulayaḥ kṛṣṇāḥ hastapādatalaiḥ saha ||  
 1.18.27  śarīraṃ pāṇḍutāmeti viṣārtasyaiva dehinaḥ |
       
       so ' kṛtyakaratāmeti bhagno ratha ivāhave ||  
 1.18.28  tasmāt kuryāt kriyāṃ vaidyaḥ ṣoḍaśāgadakovidaḥ |
       
       hriyā yuktaḥ kulīnaś ca dharmajño dīrghadarśanaḥ ||  
 1.18.29  arthāś cāsya pratiṣṭheyā vidhivatsaṃbhṛtā gṛhe |
       
       cikitsiteṣu  yā proktā viṣapraśamane hitā || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele ' ṣṭādaśodhyāyaḥ || || ekonaviṃśo ' dhyāyaḥ || athāto
      vidhiśoṇitīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 1.19.1  vidhinā śoṇitaṃ jātaṃ sevamānasya vāruṇīm |
       
       praduṣyati vidāhena tato rogāya kalpate ||  
 1.19.2  sarvaṃ madyamacakṣuṣyamapauruṣyaṃ tathaiva ca |
       
       upahanti balaṃ nẏṇāmanāyuṣyaṃ ca kīrtyate ||  
 1.19.3  yas tu tadbhajate yuktyā na taṃ vyādhiḥ prasajjate
      |
       
 atipītaṃ ca tadviddhi  tatrāhṛdyaṃ  balāya na ||  
 1.19.4  na naktaṃ tu, pibedyuktyā pānaṃ tasmād vicakṣaṇaḥ |
       
       balavarṇakaraṃ hyetadārogyakaraṇaṃ param ||  
 1.19.5  snehapāne tathā mātrāvastikarmaṇi cāpy atha |
       
       kṣāre ca lavaṇe caiva na surā prātiṣidhyate ||  
 1.19.6  bṛṃhaṇaṃ nedṛśaṃ kijcidyathānnasahitā surā |
       
       tāṃ tu rūkṣāṃ viśeṣeṇa nātimātraṃ samācaret ||  
 1.19.7  vātena śleṣmaṇā caiva sampraduṣṭāṃ suśītalā |
       
       viśoṣya dīpayatyeṣā grahaṇīṃ vai śarīriṇām ||  
 1.19.8  yasya koṣṭhagato vāyurduḥkhamutpādayed  bhṛśam |
       
       udāvartaṃ sahṛdrogaṃ vātagulmamathāpi ca ||  
 1.19.9  athavā sarvagātreṣu mārutaḥ pratyavasthitaḥ |
       
       yuktāṃ prasannāṃ pibataḥ sa kṣipram upaśāmyati ||  
 1.19.10  hantyāsavaḥ kaphaṃ pittaṃ purīṣaṃ ca bhinattyatha
      |
       
       madhu pittamariṣṭas tu vātārtiṃ  śamayatyatha ||  
 1.19.11  vastiḥ śuddhyati pānena śarkarā cāpi bhidyate |
       
       tejo balaṃ ca harṣaś ca yuktyā pānena vardhate ||  
 1.19.12 kāmaṃ dīpayate svādurbṛṃhaṇo na vipadyate |
       
       tasmāt pānaguṇān buddhvā yathāyogaṃ samācaret || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele ekonaviṃśo ' dhyāyaḥ || || viṃśo ' dhyāyaḥ || athāto '
      rthedaśamūlīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 1.20.1  artha ity āha hṛdayaṃ tasmin dhamanayo daśa |
       
       ūrdhvaṃ catasro dve tiryak catasraś cāpy adhaḥ kramāt ||  
 1.20.2  tābhyo mūlasirāstiryagbhidyante naikadhā sirāḥ |
       
       tasmāt tadarthavijñānaṃ smṛtiyogaṃ ca mānasam ||  
 1.20.3  hṛdo raso niḥsarati tasmād eti  ca sarvaśaḥ |
       
 sirābhir hṛdayaṃ vaiti tasmāt tatprabhavāḥ sirāḥ ||  
 1.20.4  hṛdi prāṇāś ca cakrasthāḥ vimāne karṇikā yathā |
       
       marmābhighātaṃ tenātra sahate hṛdaye na tu ||  
 1.20.5  puṇḍarīkasya saṃsthānaṃ kumbhikāyāḥ phalasya ca |
       
       etayor eva varṇaṃ ca vibharti hṛdayaṃ nṛṇām ||  
 1.20.6  yathā hi saṃvṛtaṃ padmaṃ rātrāvahani  puṣyati |
       
       hṛttathā saṃvṛtaṃ svapne vivṛtaṃ jāgrataḥ smṛtam ||  
 1.20.7  āpo mahārasā vidyādannaṃ caiva mahauṣadham |
       
       mahāpralepanaṃ tatra tejaś caiva mahatparam ||  
 1.20.8  rasānāmudakaṃ yonirannaṃ vṛttiḥ parā smṛtā |
       
 viklinnam upasandhatte punaḥ kāyaṃ śarīriṇām ||  
 1.20.9  sūryāṃśaṃ dhūmam ity āhuryato ' bhraprabhavaḥ smṛtaḥ |
       
       abhrādvarṣaṃ tato ' nnāni, tasmāt tejo mahatparam ||  
 1.20.10  svedaś cāsraṃ ca mūtraṃ ca phenaṃ cāmyantaraṃ malam |
       
       avaśyāyahimāmbūni bāhmāni paricakṣate || hṛdayo  |.. |.. |.. |.. |..
      |.. |.. |.. |
       
       |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. iti bhele viṃśo ' dhyāyaḥ || |
       
       |ekaviṃśo ' dhyāyaḥ || |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |..
      |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |..
      |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |..
      |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. virecyāṃś caiva mānavān |
       
       āsthāpyānanuvāsyāṃś ca vātavyādhīṃś ca sarvaśaḥ ||  
 
 
 1.21.1  virūkṣayed atisnigdhaṃ kṛmikoṣṭhinam eva ca |
       
       rūkṣastambhyān pramehāṃś ca kapharogāṃś ca sarvaśaḥ ||  
 1.21.2  vāmayecchaleṣmakāse ca pratiśyāye ca mānavān |
       
       hṛdroge caiva kuṣṭhe ca sarvaśleṣmāmayeṣu ca ||  
 1.21.3  vorecayed dhi kuṣṭhāni jvarānvisphoṭakāni ca |
       
       dāhaṃ vicarcikāṃ caiva vātavyādhīṃś ca sarvaśaḥ ||  
 1.21.4  anvāsayetkaṭīpṛṣṭhapārśvarogān vicakṣaṇaḥ |
       
       udveṣṭanaṃ ca gulmaṃ ca vātavyādhīṃś ca sarvaśaḥ ||  
 1.21.5  āsthāpayed dhi gulmāṃś ca mūtrāghātodarāṇi ca |
       
       apasmārāṃś ca kuṣṭhaṃ ca vātavyādhīṃś ca sarvaśaḥ ||  
 1.21.6  svedayeta hanustambhamāyāmam api cārditam |
       
       pārśvarogaṃ ca gulmaṃ ca vātavyādhīṃś ca sarvaśaḥ ||  
 1.21.7  stambhayed raktapittaṃ ca visarpaṃ ca vicakṣaṇaḥ |
       
       dāhaṃ visphoṭakāṃś caiva pittavyādhīṃś ca sarvaśaḥ ||  
 1.21.8  iti pittakaphotthānvai  vidyād āmāśayātmakān |
       
       pakvāśayasamutthāṃś ca vātarogānvinirdiśet ||  
 1.21.9  vāmayed vamanīyāṃs tu samīkṣyāmāśayānnarān  |
       
       virecayed virecyāṃs tu tathā pakvāśayāśrayān || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele ekaviṃśo ' dhyāyaḥ || || dvāviṃśo ' dhyāyaḥ || athātaḥ svedādhyāyaṃ
      vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 1.22.1  saṃkaraṃ prastaraṃ sekaṃ nāḍīṃ droṇiṃ jalāni ca |
       
       udakoṣṭhaṃ kuṭiṃ caiva svedamaṣṭavidhaṃ viduḥ ||  
 1.22.2  pāṣāṇabhasmasikatātuṣapāṃsubusāni ca |
       
       ajāvigopurīṣāṇi prāvārāṇi pravātikāḥ ||  
 1.22.3  payāṃsyamlāni dhānyāni girisādhāraṇānica |
       
       sarvāṇi madyamāṃsāni lavaṇāni tathaiva ca ||  
 1.22.4  vidhivadyojayetsvede kāleyāgarurūṣitān |
       
       bhiṣag balābalaṃ dṛṣṭvā balino durbalānapi ||  
 1.22.5 kuthakambalakauśeyaiḥ praveṇyajinakādibhiḥ |
       
       kiṭijairāvijairvastraiḥ pracchādya svedayennarān  ||  
 1.22.6  sparśasaukhyamavaivarṇyaṃ svedo ' ṅgeṣu ca mārdavam |
       
       śītābhinirgamaś caiva samyak svinnasya lakṣaṇam ||  
 1.22.7  pittaprakopo dāhaś ca tṛṣṇā mūrchā vilāyanam |
       
       svedadveṣo ' ṅgarāgaścetyatisvinnasya lakṣaṇam ||  
 1.22.8  udveṣṭanaṃ dāruṇatā gurutvaṃ stabdhagātratā |
       
       marutaś cāprasiddhiś ca na tatsvinnasya lakṣaṇam ||  
 1.22.9  asvinne snehanaṃ kṛtvā tataḥ svedair upācaret  |
       
       snehapūrvaprayukto hi svedo jayati mārutam ||  
 1.22.10  śuṣkāṇy api hi kāṣṭhāni snehasvedopapādanaiḥ |
       
       namayanti yathānyāyaṃ kiṃ punarjīvato narān ||  
 1.22.11  atisvinne viśeṣeṇa kārayecchītalāṃ kriyām |
       
       athavā śītalair vātha kṣīraiḥ siṃced ghṛtena vā ||  
 1.22.12  pipāsuṃ vā na śaktaṃ ca garbhiṇīṃ kukṣirogiṇīm |
       
       sarvāṃś ca pittajān vyādhīn kaḥ svedaiḥ samupācaret ||  
 1.22.13  ye svedāḥ pūrvamuddiṣṭāstānapyekaikaśaḥ śṛṇu |
       
       bilvāgnimanthaśyonākaṃ kāśmarīṃ pāṭalāṃ tathā ||  
 1.22.14  yavān kulutthān kolāni sthālyāmāsicya sādhayet |
       
       yavapākāni vijñāya sukhoṣmāṇyavatārayet ||  
 1.22.15  tato ' bhyaktasya vidhivatsvedanīyasya dehinaḥ |
       
       gātraṃ gātraikadeśaṃ vā sukhoṣṇaiśchādayecchanaiḥ ||  
 1.22.16  tataḥ pracchādayed bhūyaḥ kauśeyājinakāmbalaiḥ  |
       
       saṅkaras tv eṣa vijñeyaḥ svedānāmagrya ucyate ||  
 1.22.17  etānyanyāni ca bhiṣak svedadravyāṇi saṃharet ||  
 1.22.18  prakīrya tāni śayane kalbalenāvaguṇṭhitam  |
       
       svabhyaktaṃ śāyayejjantuṃ  svedaṃ prastaramādiśet ||  
 1.22.19  vasātailaghṛtakṣīramūtramastvamlakāñjikaiḥ |
       
       sukhauṣṇaiḥ secayetsvedyaṃ sekaḥ sa parikīrtitaḥ ||  
 1.22.20  nāḍīṃ gajakarākārāṃ trihastāṃ tādṛśīṃ tathā |
       
       dhānyāmladravapūrṇāyāṃ dhānyāṃ sandhāya lepayet ||  
 1.22.21  tāṃ trihastāṃ samāhṛtya svabhyaktāṅgasya dehinaḥ |
       
       pracchannagātrasya tu tāṃ nāḍīmudghāṭayed bhiṣak ||  
 1.22.22  nāḍīsvedaḥ samākhyātaḥ yāvatprasvedanāditi |
       
       kaṇṭhāvagāhāmacchidrāṃ tāvadevāyatāṃ samām ||  
 1.22.23  droṇiṃ pāyasaniṣkvāthakṛsarakṣīrapūritām |
       
       kṛtvā tasyāṃ sukhoṣṇāyāṃ svabhyaktaṃ vātarogiṇam ||  
 1.22.24  jñātvāvagāhayet tāvad yāvat svedodgamo bhavet |
       
       taptaiḥ pātrayutair vāpi śuddhair vā salilairbhiṣak ||  
 1.22.25  svamyaktagātrasya tataḥ salilasvedamācaret |
       
       īdṛśair eva salilaiḥ kaṭāhe cārdhapūrite ||  
 1.22.26  praveśya svedayetsvedyamudakoṣṭhaḥ prakīrtitaḥ |
       
       suliptāṃ saṃvṛtadvārāṃ yantritāṃ kārayetkuṭim ||  
 1.22.27  hrasvāgāramitāṃ hṛdyāṃ śilāstīrṇatalāṃ dṛḍhām |
       
       tāsyāścullyau ca kartavye adhastātpārśvasaṃvṛte ||  
 1.22.28  tatra sthālyau pratiṣṭhāpya sarvataḥ paribṛṃhayet |
       
       sthālyau tapte kuṭiś cāpi yadā tenoṣmaṇā tadā ||  
 1.22.29  sarvāṅgarogipuruṣaḥ praviśetsa kuṭiṃ tataḥ |
       
       svabhyaktagātraḥ susvinnaḥ kṣaumaprāvṛtalocanaḥ ||  
 1.22.30  tataḥ praveśayet tatra śītāmbumaṇikāṃ śubhām |
       
       klāntaḥ śītāmvunā tatra sparśasaukhyam avāpnuyāt ||  
 1.22.31  kuṭisveda iti jñeyaḥ sadyo roganivartakaḥ |
       
       svedo ' gnihīnaḥ kṣuttṛṣṇābhayaṃ krodhastathāhavaḥ  ||  
 1.22.32  nivātamadhvasantāpau  guruprāvaraṇaṃ tathā |
       
       svedyās tu vātakaphajā vātajāḥ kaphajās tathā ||  
 1.22.33 rogāstatroṣṇalavaṇasnigdhāmlair eva vātajāḥ |
       
       karīṣabusapāṣāṇabāṣpāṅgāraiḥ kaphātmakāḥ |
       
 svedyās tu snigdharūkṣābhyāṃ jñātvā vyādhibalābalam || ity āha bhagavān
      ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele dvāviṃśo ' dhyāyaḥ || || trayoviṃśo ' dhyāyaḥ || athāto
      gāḍhapurīṣīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 1.23.1  gāḍhaṃ purīṣaṃ grathitaṃ śuskaṃ vātasamīritam |
       
       tenāsyāpihitaṃ srotaḥ śvayathuṃ kurute gude ||  
 1.23.2  tasyaiva kupito vāyurūrdhvaṃ jantoḥ prapadyate |
       
       pārśve śroṇyāṃ ca pṛṣṭhe ca hṛdaye cāvatiṣṭhate ||  
 1.23.3  śiraś cāpy avasaṃgṛhya vikārān kurute bahūn |
       
       bādhiryaṃ timiraṃ cāpi pratiśyāyamathāpi ca ||  
 1.23.4  atha pittaṃ kaphaṃ vā svātsthānāccyāvayate ' nilaḥ
      |
       
       tato ' sya dhāvato doṣairduṣyanti ca rasādayaḥ ||  
 1.23.5  tato jvaro ' sya balavān pāṇḍutvaṃ cāpi jāyate |
       
       śvayathuś ca bhaved asya grahaṇī ca praduṣyati ||  
 1.23.6  tasmād dāruṇakoṣṭhas tu gāḍhavarcāś ca yo bhavet |
       
       rūkṣamannaṃ pariharenna cainamavasraṃsayet ||  
 1.23.7  snigdhānyannāni hṛdyāni māṃsāni vividhāni ca |
       
       kuluttharasayuktāni pradadyāddehine sadā ||  
 1.23.8  āsthāpanaṃ vātaharaṃ tailaṃ cāpy anuvāsanam |
       
       na bhavanti vikārā hi narasya pratikāriṇaḥ ||  
 1.23.9 atha yaḥ kalilaś ca syāt prajākāmaś ca mānavaḥ |
       
       utkṛṣṭatāradāriś ca karmahinas tathaiva ca ||  
 1.23.10  atha sthūlakṛśaś caiva vaidyamāni ca yo bhavet |
       
       tathaikalokoyatikāṃ motriyānna ca tadvijān ||  
 1.23.11  sabhaṃgān sukumārāṃś ca garbhiṇīṃ taruṇi tadā |
       
       durdilāṃś ca yadu prāptān kāsinaḥ sāti nāriṇaḥ ||  
 1.23.12  pāṇḍurājaiva karṇaṃ ca satataṃ yaś ca kāsati |
       
       pāyayec ca bhiṣaktāpairvamanaṃ savirecanam || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele trayoviṃśo ' dhyāyaḥ || || pañcaviṃśo ' dhyāyaḥ || athātaḥ
      ṛtuvibhāgīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 1.25.1  suśrotā nāma medhāvī cāndrabhāgamuvāca ha |
       
       na pātavyamarogeṇa sukhakāmena recanam ||  
 1.25.2  anīritānāṃ doṣāṇāṃ haraṇaṃ na praśasyate |
       
       avasthitānāṃ cyavanaṃ prāṇāpāyāya me matam ||  
 1.25.3  yathā vyālāgniśastrāṇāṃ sparśaḥ svasthe tathauṣadham |
       
       tasmānna pāyayetsvasthaṃ prakṛtyarthaṃ hi dhīyate ||  
 1.25.4  acākṣuṣatvāt koṣṭhasya pītaṃ svasthena cauṣadham |
       
       yāti naikāntataḥ siddhiṃ tasmāt svasthaṃ na payayet ||  
 1.25.5  ity etadvacanaṃ śrutvā pratyuvāca punarvasuḥ |
       
       iha doṣaviśeṣeṇa naro bhaiṣajyamācaret ||  
 1.25.6  vāte tu bṛṃhaṇaṃ kuryāt pitte tu pariśodhanam |
       
       kaphe prarcchadanaṃ sādhu sannipāte virecanam ||  
 1.25.7  vātātapaviśuṣkāś ca ye ca karmaparā narāḥ |
       
       adhvayānaviśuṣkāś ca tānna saṃśodhayed bhiṣak ||  
 1.25.8  tailamāṣāṃstilaghṛtaṃ phāṇitaṃ piṣṭamodakān |
       
       ājaṃ gavyamathauramraṃ matsyānmāṃāsavaṃ dadhi ||  
 1.25.9  atyaśnano ' tipibataḥ sadā ca svapato divā |
       
       doṣā ghorāḥ prakupyanti teṣāṃ sādhu virecanam ||  
 1.25.10  kiñcānyadvidhivatkāle snigdhasvinnena  bheṣajam |
       
       mātrāvallaghu  pītaṃ hi na kadācidvipadyate ||  
 1.25.11  nācaredatimātraṃ hi bahuśo ' pi pibenmṛdu  |
       
       kaṣāyeṇa tu dātavyaṃ kaṣāyaiḥ  sādhu sidhyati ||  
 1.25.12  yathā hy annamakāle syādviṣaṃ kāle ' mṛtaṃ bhavet |
       
       tathauṣadhamakāle syāt viṣaṃ kāle ' mṛtaṃ bhavet ||  
 1.25.13  tasmād yadā  vai vasudhā tṛptā puṣpavatī bhavet |
       
 tadā prāvṛṣi saṃprāptavamanādīni kārayet ||  
 1.25.14  madhyacārī yadā sūryo dhātūnutkleśayenmṛṇām |
       
 tadā vasante saṃprāpte vamanādīni kārayet ||  
 1.25.15 tadā varṣāsu dātavyaṃ yadā hyeṣa ṛtuḥ sukhaḥ
      |
       
       ṛtavo yuktaśītoṣṇāḥ praśasyante  hi karmasu ||  
 1.25.16  haimantepyanyathā kāryo grīṣme bhavati cānyathā |
       
       varṣāsu cāpy anyathā ca durdine cāpy ato ' nyathā ||  
 1.25.17  tasmiṃstasmiṃś ca kāle vai bhavetkāryo ' nyathānyathā |
       
       sātmyāsātmyaṃ manuṣyāṇāmanyathā parivartate ||  
 1.25.18  tryahaṃ tu dāpayet snehaṃ deye
      snehavirecane  |
       
       nātiśīte na cātyuṣṇe peyaṃ snehavirecanam ||  
 1.25.19  tṛṣṇābādhā bhavatyuṣṇe śīte tu vyapalīyate |
       
       atha grīṣme tu santaptairdhātubhir dehino bhavet ||  
 1.25.20  atiyogaḥ pipāsā ca tadā tasmānna dāpayet |
       
       hemante cāpi tadvīryāddoṣā dāruṇatāṃ gatāḥ ||  
 1.25.21  bhavantyakāle snehasya tadāpyatha na dāpayet |
       
       iha bhaiṣajyamuṣṇaṃ hi vikriyāmeti kālataḥ ||  
 1.25.22 mandī bhavati vaitat tu grīṣme taikṣṇyaṃ
      niyacchati |
       
 yanmaithunācchuklavāhā vastisakthitrikādi ca ||  
 1.25.23  hṛdayaṃ durbalaṃ cāsya samudīrṇaś ca mārutaḥ |
       
       brahmacārī bhavettasmāt paittikān bhajate ' nyathā ||  
 1.25.24  mukhapākaṃ madaṃ mūrchāṃ pralāpaṃ pākavibhramau |
       
       dāhaṃ pipāsāṃ santāpaṃ vaktrasyākṣṇoś ca pītatām ||  
 1.25.25 dhūmābhidūṣite pittavikārā ye prakīrtitāḥ |
       
       bhramaḥ klamaḥ pramohaś ca mado mūrcchā vikampanam ||  
 1.25.26  santāpo ' bhyantare caiva rasasthānagate smṛtāḥ |
       
       aruṣāṃ vivṛtānāṃ vā sphoṭānāṃ vā prapācanam ||  
 1.25.27  raktasthānagate vidyāt pitte vaivarṇyam eva ca |
       
       māṃsasthānagate svedaḥ sadanaṃ copajāyate ||  
 1.25.28  medodhātugate vidyāt plāvanaṃ pītamūtratā |
       
       asthimajjagate śoṣo nakhadantavivarṇate ||  
 1.25.29  meḍhremuṣkaparītāpaḥ klaibyaṃ vāpy atha śuklage |
       
       balavadvigrahād bhārāt pīḍanāllaṅghanād api ||  
 1.25.30  maithunasyātiyogāc ca jāyate manasaḥ klamaḥ |
       
       trāsodvegātpratīghātādrūkṣapānānnasevanāt ||  
 1.25.31  ity ebhir īdṛśaiś cānyairhetubhiḥ  kupito ' nilaḥ
      |
       
       vikārāñjanayecchavāsakāsaviṣṭambhasaṃjñakān ||  
 1.25.32  śūlavepanamādhmānaṃ nistodaṃ suptatāṃ tathā |
       
       sphoṭanaṃ cālanaṃ raukṣyaṃ veṣṭanotkṣepaṇāni ca ||  
 1.25.33  śoṣaṇaṃ kārṣṇyaviṣyandau viśleṣas tu paraḥ smṛtaḥ
      |
       
       dvividhā vyādhayaḥ proktāḥ śarīre vātasaṃbhavāḥ ||  
 1.25.34  koṣṭhānusāriṇas tatra jñeyāḥ sarvāṅgarogiṇaḥ |
       
       pakṣāṅgarogiṇaś caiva jñeyāḥ sarvāṅgasāriṇaḥ ||  
 1.25.35  śūlavepanasaṃkocagātrastambhaiś ca pīḍitāḥ |
       
 asthigrahagṛhītāś ca sarve sarvāṅgarogiṇaḥ ||  
 1.25.36  tatra pādatalāṅguṣṭhajaṅghājānūruvaṃkṣaṇaiḥ  |
       
       gudameḍhrakaṭīpṛṣṭhayonigarbhāśayair api ||  
 1.25.37  yakṛtplīhāṃsahṛdayapārśvavakṣobhujāntaraiḥ |
       
 grīvāgaṇḍaharūśaṅkhanāsākṣidaśanacchadaiḥ ||  
 1.25.38  lalāṭakarṇasīmantaiḥ pratyekamanilārditaiḥ |
       
       dūyadbhir vikalaiś cāpi jñeyās tv ekāṅgarogiṇaḥ ||  
 1.25.39  ity etanmūlamuddiṣṭaṃ rogāṇāṃ ca yathāvidhi |
       
 bhūyas tv idam adhiṣṭhānaṃ pratirogaṃ pratīkṣata || ity āha bhagavān
      ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele pañcaviṃśo ' dhyāyaḥ || || ṣaḍviṃśo ' dhyāyaḥ || athātaḥ
      aṣṭodarīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 1.26.1  athāṣṭāvudarāṇīha mūtrāghātāṃś ca nirdiśet |
       
       ṣaṭ kācāṃlliṅganāśāṃś ca jānīyāt timirāṇi ca ||  
 1.26.2  hikkāśvāsāṃś ca kāsāṃś ca khālity aṃ palitāni
      ca |
       
       śirorogārbudān gulmān chardīnatha bhagandarān ||  
 1.26.3  unmādānmukharogāṃś ca sthānānyanaśanasya ca |
       
       granthīṃś ca pañca pañcaiva kuṣṭhānyaṣṭau vinirdiśet ||  
 1.26.4  hṛdrogān pāṇḍurogāṃś ca sāsrāvān  śvayathūṃs tathā
      |
       
 abhiṣyandānadhīmanthānklībasthānāni cāpy atha ||  
 1.26.5  akṣirogānapasmārān raktarohiṇikāṃ tathā |
       
       pipāsāścopadaṃśāṃś ca catuṣkāṇi vinirdiśet ||  
 1.26.6 pṛṣṭharogajvarārśāṃsi raktapittavraṇau tathā |
       
       dvau dvau tisras tu vidradhyas tv alajyaḥ śoṇitāni ca ||  
 1.26.7  retasāṃ ślīpadaṃ cārma sapta sapta vinirdiśet |
       
       pramehān kṛmijātīś ca yonidoṣāṃś ca viṃśatim  ||  
 1.26.8  tatrodarāṇyathāṣṭau tu vyākhyātāni cikitsite |
       
       nidānenaiva rogās tu ye noktāstānnibodha me ||  
 1.26.9  aruṇā nīlapītāś ca haritaśvetalohitāḥ |
       
       kācaṃ ca liṅganāśaṃ ca timirāṇi ca nirdiśet ||  
 1.26.10  vātaḥ pittaṃ kapho vāpi yasya śīrṣaṃ vidhāvati |
       
       vidahanneṣa  mūlāni srotāṃsi samabhidrutaḥ ||  
 1.26.11 adhvanā vātibhārādvā dehināṃ vārdhakena vā |
       
 khālity aṃ palitaṃ vāpi pañcadhaiva  bhavatyatha ||  
 1.26.12  vātajaṃ pittajaṃ caiva śleṣmajaṃ māṃsajaṃ tathā |
       
       arbudaṃ medasā caiva pañcamaṃ nirdiśetpṛthak ||  
 1.26.13  vātajaṃ pittajaṃ caiva śleṣmajaṃ sannipātajam |
       
       āgantukaṃ pañcamaṃ ca mukharogaṃ pracakṣate ||  
 1.26.14  uṣṭragrīvaṃ parisrāvi śambūkāvartam eva ca |
       
       unmārgaṃ śatayoniṃ ca tadvadvidyādbhagandaram ||  
 1.26.15  chardayatyatha  vātena pittena ca kaphena ca |
       
       āhārādamanojñācca  sannipātāc ca pañcamam ||  
 1.26.16 praticchanne tu hṛdaye vātapittakaphairnaraḥ |
       
 arasādamanojñāc ca bhojyamannaṃ na sevate ||  
 1.26.17  vātajaṃ pittajaṃ caiva śleṣmajaṃ sannipātajam |
       
 sirāgranthiṃ vijānīyāt pañcamaṃ snāyuto bhiṣak ||  
 1.26.18  vātajaṃ pittajaṃ caiv kaphajaṃ sannipātajam |
       
       abhiṣyandaṃ vijānīyādadhimanthaṃ  ca buddhimān ||  
 1.26.19  śukloparodhāddaurbalyād dhvajabhaṅgāttathaiva ca |
       
       śukrakṣayāc ca catvāri klaibyasthānāni nirdiśet ||  
 1.26.20  vātajaṃ pittjaṃ caiva śleṣmajaṃ sannipātajam |
       
       akṣirogaṃ vijānīyānmānavānāṃ caturvidham ||  
 1.26.21  pūyānmūtrāc ca śuklāc ca sandhānāc cāpi dehinām |
       
       upadaṃśaṃ vijānīyādbhiṣagevaṃ caturvidham ||  
 1.26.22  raktāsrāvaṃ kaphasrāvaṃ pūyāsrāvaṃ tathaiva ca |
       
       toyāsrāvaṃ ca jānīyādbhiṣagevaṃ caturvidham ||  
 1.26.23  vātajāṃ pittajāṃ caiva śleṣmajāṃ sannipātajām |
       
       pipāsām api jānīyādbhiṣagevaṃ caturvidhām ||  
 1.26.24  vātajāṃ pittajāṃ caiva śleṣmajāṃ sannpātajām |
       
       vidyādrohiṇikāṃ caiva bhiṣagevaṃ caturvidhām ||  
 1.26.25  māṃsārma tvatha medo ' rma prastāryarma tathaiva
      ca |
       
 snāyavarma pravijānīyād bhiṣagevaṃ caturvidham ||  
 1.26.26  dvau jvarau dāhaśītau tu śārīrāgantujavraṇau |
       
       śuṣkārśaḥ śoṇitārśaś ca tathā dve cārśasī viduḥ ||  
 1.26.27  pṛṣṭharogāvupakṣārikṣāriṇau ca vinirdiśet |
       
       bāhyāyāmāntarāyāmau vidyādākṣepakau tathā ||  
 1.26.28  medasaḥ snāyuto māṃsādalajyastisra eva ca |
       
       vātātpittātkaphāccaiva tisro vidradhayaḥ smṛtāḥ ||  
 1.26.29  varāhākāraṇaṃ caiva raktaṃ kāṃsyavakaṃ tathā(?) |
       
       vātātpittātkaphānmāṃsānmedasaḥ snāyuto+ api ca ||  
 1.26.30  sirājamarma jānīyāt saptamaṃ dehināṃ bhiṣak |
       
       sapta sātmyāni jānīyāt tatra ṣaṭ syuryathā rasaiḥ ||  
 1.26.31 sarvasātmyaṃ yadeva syādvaraṃ  sātmyaṃ
      taducyate |
       
       mṛjjā jarāyujā levā rūpakā bahurūpakāḥ ||  
 1.26.32  parisarpā visarpāś ca gātrajā netrajās tathā |
       
 romadā rohitāś caiva kaṣṭā dāruṇakās tathā ||  
 1.26.33  śirojā dantajāś caiva śleṣmajāḥ śakṛdāśrayāḥ |
       
       lohitāḥ kālakāś caiva tathaiva śatamātṛkāḥ ||  
 1.26.34  vidyādviṃśatirity etāḥ kṛmijātīś ca dehinām |
       
       yathā patatriḥ śīghro ' pi svāṃ chāyāṃ nātivartate |
       
       vātādernātivartante bahavo ' pi tathā++āmayāḥ || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele ṣaḍviṃśo ' dhyāyaḥ || |
       
       |saptaviṃśo ' dhyāyaḥ || athāto ' nnapānavidhīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha
      bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 1.27.1  athodakaṃ kledayati lavaṇaṃ syandayaty api |
       
       atha pācayati kṣāraḥ kṣīraṃ vai jīvayaty api ||  
 1.27.2  snehayatyatha sarpiś ca piśitaṃ bṛṃhayaty api |
       
       māṣā bahumalāś cāpi ślīpadaṃ janayed dadhi ||  
 1.27.3  tvacaṃ prasādayet tailaṃ snehanāya ca kalpate |
       
       piṇyākaḥ kurute glāniṃ takraṃ ca kṣapayaty api ||  
 1.27.4  madhu cāpy atha sandhatte jarjarīkurute surā |
       
       hareṇubhir masūraiś ca bhṛśaṃ vāyuḥ prakupyati ||  
 1.27.5  kaphakṛnmūlakaṃ vidyāt sarṣapaṃ vātakopanam |
       
       laśunaṃ vātaśamanaṃ pittaśleṣmakaraṃ ca tat ||  
 1.27.6  nātiśleṣmakaraṃ hiṅgu ṣaṇḍyaṃ kṣāraḥ karoti ca |
       
       sarvaṃ tiktamavṛṣyaṃ tu vidyādanyatra kūlakāt ||  
 1.27.7  avṛṣyaṃ paiṣṭikaṃ sarvaṃ yavagodhūmavarjitam |
       
       dāḍimāmalakādanyatsarvamamlaṃ tu pittalam ||  
 1.27.8  yavakān dāruṇān vidyāt pṛthukānśāliṣaṣṭikān |
       
       nirdiśenmṛgatulyāṃs tu tathānūpānmṛgadvijān ||  
 1.27.9 tathaikāntahitāṃś cāpi jāṃgalānmṛgapakṣiṇaḥ |
       
       ity etatsaṃgraheṇoktaṃ bhojyaṃ vistarataḥ śṛṇu ||  
 1.27.10  pippalī śṛṅgiberaṃ ca palāṇḍulaśunāni ca |
       
       mūlakaṃ kṛśṇagandhā ca parṇāsaṃ kālamānakam ||  
 1.27.11  surasaṃ sumukhaṃ caiva caṭakaṃ ca phaṇijjakam |
       
       rasena kaṭukaṃ vidyāt vipāke madhuraṃ tathā ||  
 1.27.12  kirātatikto nimbaś ca ketukāśakaṭhillakāḥ |
       
       kūlakaṃ ca savetrāgraṃ tiktaṃ madhuvipāki ca ||  
 1.27.13  plakṣakāśmaryamadhukaṃ svādu pāke parūṣakam |
       
       kharjūraṃ nālikeraṃ ca priyālaṃ tadvidhāni ca ||  
 1.27.14  madhukaṃ ca bisaṃ caiva jīvanīyāni yāni ca |
       
       rase pāke ca madhuraṃ tadvidyād vividhaṃ ca yat ||  
 1.27.15  basāni kaṭukā bimbī sarvaṃ caivekṣuvaikṛtam |
       
       rase pāke ca madhuraṃ tad vidyāt trividhaṃ ca yat ||  
 1.27.16  nyaṅkuṃ carasamudrāṃś ca sṛmarānkhaḍgasūkarān |
       
 anyāṃś cānūpajān vidyānmadhurān rasapākataḥ ||  
 1.27.17  kādambānsaindhavānhaṃsānsārasāñścetavāraṇam  |
       
       kācākṣānmallikākṣāṃś ca tathā puṣkarasāyakān ||  
 1.27.18  dipavepni(?) śarārīṃś ca vikramān sumanāmukhān |
       
       nandimaudgalyakāṃś cāpi kālakān kṛṣṇapucchakān ||  
 1.27.19  ājñātān ḍuṇḍubhāṃś caiva maṇḍūkān chuṭumallikān |
       
       harṣyāt tu saptavārādi tathā garbhabhatāsakān(?) ||  
 1.27.20  sarvāṃś ca vārijānvidyānmadhurān rasapākataḥ |
       
       priyaṅguś ca plāṅgaś ca balākāś ca khagās tathā ||  
 1.27.21  ye cānye ' pyaudakā bhaumyāḥ khecarāś ca khagāḥ smṛtāḥ |
       
       nakrāṃś ca śiśumārāṃś ca vallakīmatsyakacchapān  ||  
 1.27.22  anyāṃś ca vārijānvidyānmadhurānrasapākataḥ |
       
       priyaṅguś ca vinaktāś ca nīlikāśāliṣaṣṭikāḥ ||  
 1.27.23  parūṣakāś ca nīvārāḥ kodravā brahmabhūtikāḥ |
       
       ity etaddhānyajātaṃ vai yaccānyadapi tadvidham ||  
 1.27.24  rasena madhuraṃ tadvai vipāke kaṭukaṃ viduḥ |
       
       mudgān masūrāṃś caṇakān kulutthāṃś ca kalāyakān ||  
 1.27.25  rasena madhurāṃstānvai vipāke kaṭukānviduḥ |
       
       rohīṃ śvadaṃṣṭrānuṣṭrāṃś ca śarabhānmṛgamātṛkān ||  
 1.27.26  athānyānmadhurāsvādānvipāke  kaṭukānviduḥ |
       
       kharāś cāścatarāmeṣā  ye cānye tādṛśā mṛgāḥ ||  
 1.27.27  rasena madhurāṃstānvai vipāke kaṭukānviduḥ |
       
       harītān stokakāṃś caiva kapotān śukaśārikāḥ ||  
 1.27.28  caṭakān bhṛṅgarājāṃś ca tathā pippalakānapi |
       
       godhāputrāṃstailapākānye cānye pratudāḥ khagāḥ ||  
 1.27.29  ye cānye madhurāstānvai vipāke kaṭukānviduḥ |
       
       anupānāni vakṣyāmi yeṣu yāni hitāni vai ||  
 1.27.30  āje kaṣāyaśītas tu hāyane codakaṃ tathā |
       
       anupānaṃ vidhātavyaṃ vārāhe khadirodaram ||  
 1.27.31  dadhi cukraṃ ca dhānyānām anupānaṃ pradāpayet |
       
       śīrodakaṃ bisagranthisevanānāṃ tathāsavān ||  
 1.27.32  tadvārijānāṃ satvānām anupānaṃ pradāpayet |
       
       triphalāṃ śīdhumārdvīkaṃ kadambapanasodakam ||  
 1.27.33  suradrujambūplakṣāṇāṃ phalaskandhāsavānpṛthak |
       
       mudgādisūpadhānyānām anupānaṃ pradāpayet ||  
 1.27.34  bilvapiṇḍakakalkānāṃ kapitthasyāthavāsavān |
       
       guhāśayānāṃ satvānām anupānaṃ pradāpayet ||  
 1.27.35  nyagrodhādigaṇasyātha skandhaśākhāphalāsavān |
       
       viṣkirāṇāṃ vihaṅgānām anupānaṃ pradāpayet ||  
 1.27.36  kakubhasyānupānaṃ tu snigdhānāṃ cāpi vāruṇīm |
       
       caturvidhasya snehasya toyamuṣṇaṃ pradāpayet ||  
 1.27.37  drākṣākāśmaryakharjūrayavavāṭyāṃstathāsavān  |
       
       aśvagandhakaṣāyaṃ tu vāruṇīmaṇḍam eva ca ||  
 1.27.38  sukhena pācayaty annaṃ rocayaty apakarṣati |
       
       anupānaṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ sātmyatāṃ ca prayacchati || ity āha bhagavān
      ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele saptaviṃśo ' dhyāyaḥ || || aṣṭāviṃśo ' dhyāyaḥ || athāto
      bhojanavidhīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 1.28.1  yad bhakṣayati bhuṅkte vā vidhivac cāpi mānavaḥ |
       
 anyac ca kiñcit pibati tat sarvaṃ ṣaḍrasānvitam ||  
 1.28.2  pathyāpathyam abodhāryaṃ, tasmād bhojyaṃ śarīriṇām |
       
 rasato vīryataś caiva pravakṣyāmy ata uttaram ||  
 1.28.3  śālayo madhurāḥ sarve vipāke kaṭukāḥ smṛtāḥ |
       
       raktaśālirvaras teṣāmaraukṣyāl lekhano  na ca ||  
 1.28.4  dīrghaśūko  mahā śāliḥ sugandhiḥ śālikāmukhaḥ
      |
       
       kṛṣṇavrīhiḥ kāñcanakaḥ lopārkṣaḥ śītabhīrukaḥ ||  
 1.28.5  hāyano lodhraśāliś ca raktaśāliguṇānvitaḥ |
       
       pūrvapūrvo laghutaraḥ pathyaḥ kiṃca bhavatyataḥ ||  
 1.28.6  sugandhakā gandhavanto gandhena madayantyatha |
       
       raukṣyāc ca kalamaṃ vidyādadhikaṃ vai viśeṣataḥ ||  
 1.28.7  kaṣāyas tv adhikaḥ kiṃcit ṣaṣṭikāḥ śālibhiḥ samāḥ |
       
       mahādoṣāḥ suguravaḥ pāṭalāvrīhayas tathā ||  
 1.28.8  yavakā nityam ahitāḥ  kṛṣṇavrīhipramodakāḥ |
       
 vīryoṣṇā madhurāste vai sakaṣāyāś ca kīrtitāḥ ||  
 1.28.9  bahūrūkṣāḥ kaṣāyāś ca koradūṣāḥ savāruṇāḥ |
       
       prasādhikāḥ kaṃ gavaś ca śyāmākāś ca samā rasaiḥ ||  
 1.28.10 uddālakās tu saṃkhyā tāḥ kaṣāyā madhurā rase
      |
       
       grīṣme tu sevitāste vai kopayanty āśu mārutān ||  
 1.28.11  yavās tv atiyavāś caiva godhūmāś ca samā rase |
       
       madhurāḥ sakaṣāyāś ca śleṣmalā lohitā nṛṇām ||  
 1.28.12  atha veṇuyavā nātikaṣāyā madhurā rase |
       
       kaphaṃ pittaṃ ca medaś ca kopayantyatisevitāḥ ||  
 1.28.13  kṛṣṇā mudgā mahāmudgāḥ haritāścirajīvinaḥ |
       
       makuṣṭhakāś ca te ' pyuktāḥ kaṣāyā madhurā rase ||  
 1.28.14  hareṇavo masūrāś ca satīnāś ca tathāḍhakī |
       
       kulutthāś ca viseṣeṇa kaṣāyamadhurā rase ||  
 1.28.15  sarve tu lavaṇakṣārā dīpanīyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ |
       
 avṛṣyāś ca viśeṣeṇa durbalānāṃ hitā na ca ||  
 1.28.16  śvadaṃṣṭrā yāvanālaś ca dvau kṣārau śītalau(?) smṛtau |
       
       śuklaṃ vinihatastau tu dṛṣṭiṃ cāpi śarīriṇām ||  
 1.28.17  navanītaṃ tathāmlaṃ tu ghṛtaṃ vai madhuraṃ smṛtam |
       
       sarvaṃ dugdhamabhiṣyandi gavyaṃ tebhyo viśiṣyate ||  
 1.28.18  vājī bhavati dugdhena balaṃ cātyupajāyate |
       
       sañjīvanaṃ sambhavati sarvaṃ kṣīramudāhṛtam ||  
 1.28.19  rase pāke ca madhuraṃ tailaṃ sarvaṃ prakīrtītam |
       
       yasminyasminviśeṣas tu yo yastasminnibodha tam ||  
 1.28.20  tailameraṇḍabilvānāmuṣṇaṃ vātaharaṃ smṛtam |
       
       ity uktānyuṣṇavīryāṇi ya danyacchītam eva tat ||  
 1.28.21  vibhītakānāṃ tailaṃ tu kaṣāyamadhuraṃ rase |
       
       kaphapittaharaṃ proktaṃ keśyaṃ caiva śarīriṇām ||  
 1.28.22  ataḥ karañjabījānāṃ vijñeyāni tathaiva ca |
       
       tailāni rasato vidyāt tiktāni madhurāṇi ca ||  
 1.28.23 pittaśleṣmakaraṃ tiktamiṅgudītailamucyate |
       
       sakaṣāyaṃ madhūkānāṃ kaphapittānilāpaham ||  
 1.28.24 kaulakaṃ madhurasparśaṃ rasato ' tha vipākataḥ |
       
       yasminyasminviśeṣas tu yo yastaṃ me nibodhata ||  
 1.28.25  palālajātaṃ chvākamatīva guru sammatam |
       
       mahādoṣamabhiṣyandi  sukhaṃ bāhyopaghātakam(?) ||  
 1.28.26  chatrākaṃ gomayodbhūtaṃ kaṣāyamadhuraṃ rase |
       
       kaṣāyaṃ veṇucchatrākaṃ mārutaṃ kopayennṛṇām ||  
 1.28.27  sarvaṃ tu śākaṃ madhuraṃ rasato ' tha vipākataḥ |
       
       yasminyasminviśeṣas tu yo yastasminnibodha tam ||  
 1.28.28  mārutaṃ kopayennṝṇāṃ viṣṭambhitvād alāvukam |
       
       śleṣmāṇaṃ vardhayec cāpi vipākena balīyasā ||  
 1.28.29  kūṣmāṇḍaṃ śleṣmalaṃ vidyānnavaṃ śaradi bhakṣitam |
       
       tadalpadoṣaṃ bhavati parisaṃvatsaroṣitam ||  
 1.28.30  kaṣāyamadhuraṃ vidyāt khādiraṃ cātisāri ca |
       
 tiktaṃ dīpanasaṃsṛṣṭaṃ nirdoṣaṃ taccharīriṇām ||  
 1.28.31  kośātakī karīrāṇāṃ śatāvaryāś ca tiktakam |
       
       kaṣāyaṃ nālikāyāś ca tiktaḥ puṣkaravartakaḥ ||  
 1.28.32  vetrāgraṃ tiktakaṃ nimbaṃ tilaśākaṃ ca śītikā |
       
       kurūṭikā kunaṭikā tathā gandharvahastakaḥ ||  
 1.28.33  tathā nāḍīkalāyaś ca pañcāṅgulyas tathaiva ca |
       
       etāni vidyācchākāni tiktāni rasapākataḥ ||  
 1.28.34  sa tīnaśākaṃ madhuramīṣatiktopasaṃhitam |
       
       kovidārasya śākaṃ tu pūrveṇaiva samaṃ matam ||  
 1.28.35  vārtākīnāṃ phalaṃ tiktaṃ kaṭukenopasaṃhitam |
       
       grahaṇīṃ dīpayatyetacchaleṣmāṇaṃ vinihanti ca ||  
 1.28.36 kaṭhillabakulau caiva madhurau
      śukraśo dhanau |
       
       hatastandrāṃ ca vātaṃ ca nityam eva viṣūcikām ||  
 1.28.37  alambusaḥ sakaṭukastiktako vātakopanaḥ |
       
       bhinatti kaphasaṅghātaṃ viṣṭabhyātha vipacyate ||  
 1.28.38  lāṅgaśākaṃ tu madhuraṃ lavaṇenopasaṃhitam |
       
       kaṭukaṃ bahudoṣaṃ ca tathā pakṣanikācanam(?) ||  
 1.28.39  kaṭuko dīpanīyaś ca viṣahā svastiko rase |
       
       kaṣāyamadhurā  cillī cuñcurmadhuraśītalaḥ ||  
 1.28.40  bhārṅgī māṣaś ca madhurau rasataḥ parikīrtitau |
       
       mudgaśākaṃ satiktaṃ tu sakṣāraś caiva vāstukaḥ ||  
 1.28.41  niṣpāvaśākaṃ madhuraṃ māṣaśākaṃ tathā smṛtam |
       
       candrākaśākamamlaṃ tu kaṣāyas tu gavedhukaḥ ||  
 1.28.42 tunnakaṃ prapunāṭaś ca jīvantī suniṣaṇṇakam |
       
       madhurāṇyalpadoṣāṇi tathaiva tu kuṭiñjakaḥ ||  
 1.28.43  piṇḍāluśākaṃ ca navaṃ tuṇḍikeraphalāni ca |
       
       madhurāṇyalpadoṣāṇi saṃsṛṣṭakaṭukāni ca ||  
 1.28.44  upodakā tu madhurā lavaṇenopasaṃhitā |
       
       ity etannirdiśecchākaṃ yadanyadapi tadvidham ||  
 1.28.45  ājaṃ gavyamathaurabhraṃ vārāhaṃ caiva yatsmṛtam |
       
       hastimāṃsaṃ ca madhuramuṣṭraṃ guru ca nirdiśet ||  
 1.28.46  vidyādevaṃguṇaṃ caiva sakaṣāyaṃ ca māhiṣam |
       
       khaḍgamāṃsamabhiṣyandi sasvādulavaṇaṃ rase ||  
 1.28.47  kutamāyurmayūraśca  gokarṇo gavayo guruḥ |
       
       sṛmaraścamaro nyaṅkurmadhurā guravaś ca te ||  
 1.28.48  ṛśyaś ca mṛgamātā ca tuṅgaś ca hariṇī mṛgaḥ |
       
 pārāvata  || iti bhele
      aṣṭāviṃśo ' dhyāyaḥ || iti bhelasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthānaṃ samāptam ||
      nidānasthānam  || dvitīyo ' dhyāyaḥ ||  
 
 
 
 
 
 
 2.2.1  urovighātāttasyātha jvaraḥ kāsaś ca jāyate |
       
       svaraḥ sīdati cāpy asya niṣṭhīvati saśoṇitam ||  
 2.2.2  athavāpyavaśo jantuḥ śaśvatsa parihīyate |
       
       ity etairlakṣaṇairvidyāt sāhasaprabhavaṃ kṣayam ||  
 2.2.3  yāvatsa balavāneva bṛṃhayet tāvadeva tam |
       
       yasmād balasamāveśaṃ puruṣasyeha  jīvitam ||  
 2.2.4  sa yadā gurumadhye vāpy athavā rājasaṃsadi |
       
       goṣṭhe strīdyūtamadhye vā hastipṛṣṭhe ' thavā rathe ||  
 2.2.5  bhayāt prasaṅgāc ca hriyā ghṛṇitvād vāpi mānavaḥ |
       
       prāptapātaṃ purīṣaṃ vā mūtraṃ vāpi ruṇaddhi yaḥ ||  
 2.2.6  tasya sandhāraṇādvāyurūrdhvabhāge samīritaḥ |
       
       uraḥśūlaṃ pārśvaśūlaṃ gulmaṃ ca janayatyatha ||  
 2.2.7  gulmajanmanimittaś ca jvaraḥ kāsaś ca jāyate |
       
 svaraḥ prabhidyate cāsya niṣṭhīvati sapūtikam ||  
 2.2.8  athavāpyavaśo jantuḥ śaśvatsa parihīyate |
       
       ity ebhir lakṣaṇair vidyāt sandhāraṇakṛtaṃ kṣayam ||  
 2.2.9  ātmārthaṃ lajjate janturgurorvā strījanasya ca |
       
       tasmād ātmārthameveha prāptaṃ vegaṃ na dhārayet ||  
 2.2.10  sa yadā durbalo jantuḥ svalpāhāraḥ kṛśo ' pi vā |
       
       rūkṣabhojī viśeṣeṇa striyo yaś cātisevate  ||  
 2.2.11  saraktaṃ kurute mūtraṃ jantuḥ śuklaparikṣayāt |
       
       retaḥsthānaṃ ca suṣiraṃ vāyurasya pradhāvati ||  
 2.2.12  tasya vātābhibhūtasya jvaraḥ kāsaś ca jāyate |
       
       svaraḥ sīdati cāpy asya niṣṭhīvati saśoṇitam ||  
 2.2.13  athavāpyavaśo jantuḥ śaśvatsa parihīyate |
       
       ity ebhir lakṣaśairvidyādatimaithunajaṃ kṣayam ||  
 2.2.14  ratimūlaṃ śarīraṃ hi śarīrasya ratiḥ phalam |
       
       tasmāt phalārthī mūlārthaṃ striyaḥ seveta yuktitaḥ ||  
 2.2.15  sa yadā durbalo jantuḥ sevate viṣamāśanam |
       
       bhuñjānasyāsya viṣamaṃ vaiṣamyaṃ yānti dhātavaḥ ||  
 2.2.16  tataḥ purīṣameveha vardhayatyasya bhojanam |
       
       nāvāpnoti rasaṃ dehe vikṛtasyeva dehinaḥ ||  
 2.2.17  rase nivṛtte tasyātha jvaraḥ kāsaś ca jāyate |
       
       svaraḥ sīdati cāpy asya niṣṭhīvati saśoṇitam ||  
 2.2.18  athavāpyavaśo jantuḥ śaśvatsa parihīyate |
       
       ity ebhir lakṣaṇairvidyādviṣamāśanajaṃ kṣayam ||  
 2.2.19 yasmādarthī śarīrārthaṃ rasabhojanamicchati |
       
       śarīrāpekṣayā tasmād āhāraṃ susamācaret ||  
 2.2.20  iti catvāri śoṣāṇāmuktānyāyatanāni me |
