 yāni buddhvā pariharedārogyārthī pumāniha |
       
       buddhau cārogyamāyattamidamuktaṃ maharṣiṇā || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ
      |
       
       iti bhele nidāne dvitīyo ' dhyāyaḥ || || tṛtīyo ' dhyāyaḥ || athāto
      gulmanidānaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 2.3.1  vātātpittātkaphāccaiva nicayādatha lohitāt |
       
       pañca gulmā bhavantīha teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam ||  
 2.3.2  sa yadā vātalo janturvātalaṃ bhajate ' śanam |
       
       dhāvati plavate vāpi rātrau jāgarti vā punaḥ ||  
 2.3.3 atibrūte ' tihasati striyo vātiniṣevate |
       
       udāvartayate vāpi karma cātiniṣevate ||  
 2.3.4  vṛkṣaprapatanādvāpi chardayatyathavā balāt |
       
       tasyaivaṃ kupito vāyur āmāśayamupāgataḥ ||  
 2.3.5  pārśvayor hṛdi kukṣau vā gulmaṃ saṃjanayatyatha |
       
       sa sakṛdbhavati sthūlaḥ punar bhavati vāpy aṇuḥ ||  
 2.3.6  todasphuraṇasaṃyukto vidhyate ca vidhāvati |
       
       vedanāṃ janayatyeṣa jvaraṃ sañjanayaty api ||  
 2.3.7  vastiśīrṣaṃ ca saṃgṛhya dārayanniva tiṣṭhati |
       
 viṣaṃ bhavati cāhāro mūrdhānaṃ pratipadyate ||  
 2.3.8  punaś ca dṛśyate vyaktaṃ punarnaśyati cāpy atha |
       
       karoti gāḍhaṃ duḥkhena purīṣaṃ vā saśoṇitam ||  
 2.3.9 kṛṣṇābhāsaś ca puruṣo vātagulmī sa dṛśyate |
       
       yassadā pittalo jantuḥ pittalaṃ bhajate ' śanam ||  
 2.3.10  apramāṇena durmedhāḥ sevate pānamīdṛśam |
       
       tasyaivaṃ kupitaṃ pittamāmāśayamupāgatam ||  
 2.3.11  pārśvayor hṛdi kukṣau vā gulmaṃ sañjanayatyatha |
       
       uṣyate dūyate cāpi dahyate dhūpyate tathā ||  
 2.3.12  nityaṃ taptaś ca raktaṃ ca svedaṃ
      muñcatyabhīkṣṇaśaḥ  |
       
       ayogolo yathā taptas tathā sthānagate dahet ||  
 2.3.13  tṛṣṇāṃ mūrcchāṃ ca janayetsthānād api visarpati |
       
       vedanā paramā caiva tasmin sthāne prajāyate ||  
 2.3.14  purā jātāni lomāni tasmād gulmaparigrahāt |
       
 cyavante na ca jāyante yāvadvyādhirna śāmyati ||  
 2.3.15  pittagulmena puruṣaḥ pītābhāsaś ca lakṣyate |
       
       yassadā śleṣmalo  jantuḥ śleṣmalaṃ bhajate ' śanam ||  
 2.3.16  apramāṇena durmedhā divāsvapnaratas tathā |
       
       tasyaivaṃ kupitaḥ śleṣmā hyāmāśayamupāgataḥ ||  
 2.3.17  pārśvayor hṛdi kukṣau vā gulmaṃ sañjanayatyatha |
       
       na cāsya svadate bhojyaṃ bhuktaṃ na ca vipacyate ||  
 2.3.18  śleṣmaṇā saha bhuktaṃ ca muhurūrdhvaṃ prapadyate |
       
       śuklamūtrapurīṣaś ca śuklābhāsas tathaiva ca ||  
 2.3.19  śuklanetraś ca bhavati gulme śleṣmasamudbhave |
       
       yassadā karśito janturvyādhinā bheṣajena vā ||  
 2.3.20  asañjātabalāgniś ca doṣalānyupasevate |
       
       tasya sannicitā doṣā gulmaṃ kurvanti dāruṇam ||  
 2.3.21  tatra sarvāṇi rūpāṇi dṛśyante sānnipātike |
       
       atha lohitagulmas tu strīṇām eva prajāyate ||  
 2.3.22 nāsau bhavati nṝṇāṃ tu tasya vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam |
       
       acirapracyute garbhe sūtikāyās tathā ' cirāt ||  
 2.3.23  atiprajananādvāpi tathā ' prajananena vā |
       
       sandhāraṇādvā bhārasya raktamādhmāpayet tataḥ ||  
 2.3.24 sā śoṇite sthite nārī garbhiṇī strīti manyate |
       
       samayādatha  śūlāni tasyāḥ kukṣau bhavatyatha ||  
 2.3.25  koṣṭhe gulmodaraṃ tac ca garbho ' yam iti manyate |
       
       garbho ' yam iti ca vyādhirvarṣamekaṃ bahūny api ||  
 2.3.26  dhārayatyatha nirbhedaṃ kathañcitsanniyacchati |
       
       athāsyāḥ kālaparyāyāt sakṣīrau bhavataḥ stanau ||  
 2.3.27  kṛśā bhavati sā pāṇḍurdohadaṃ cābhinandati |
       
       chardirniṣṭhīvikā caiva tandrā caivaṃ prabādhate ||  
 2.3.28  pādayoḥ śvayathuś ca syādraktagulme praduṣyati |
       
       eṣāṃ tu khalu pañcānāṃ gulmānāṃ samudāhṛtam |
       
 vidyādasādhyaṃ nicayaṃ yatnasādhyāṃstathetarān || ity āha
      bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele nidāne tṛtīyo ' dhyāyaḥ || || caturtho ' dhyāyaḥ || athātaḥ
      kāsanidānaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 2.4.1  vātātpittātkaphāccaiva kṣatādvātha kṣayād api |
       
       pañca kāsā bhavantīha teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam ||  
 2.4.2  yassadā vātalo janturasātmyaṃ vai niṣevate |
       
       rūkṣamaśnāti pibati rūkṣaṃ hi bahu khādati ||  
 2.4.3  tasya vātaḥ prakupito gṛhītvā hṛdayaṃ tataḥ |
       
       ūrdhvaṃ samprāpya dhamanīratha kāsāya kalpate ||  
 2.4.4  uraḥśūlaṃ pārśvaśūlaṃ pṛṣṭhastambhaśca  jāyate |
       
       āṭopyate ' syodaraṃ ca śiraś cāsyātimanthyate ||  
 2.4.5  uro ' bhighātātpārśve ca gṛhyete iva dehinaḥ |
       
 kaphaḥ prakāsamānasya sasaṃrambhaḥ pravartate |
       
 
 2.4.6  pratataṃ kāsamānasya mūtraṃ vāto ruṇaddhi hi |
       
       ity ebhir lakṣaṇairvidyādvātakāsaṃ śarīriṇām ||  
 2.4.7  yassadā pittalo janturasātmyaṃ vai niṣevate |
       
       amlamaśnāti pibati khādatyāsvādayaty api ||  
 2.4.8  tasya pittaṃ prakupitaṃ gṛhītvā hṛdayaṃ tataḥ |
       
       ūrdhvaṃ samprāpya dhamanīstataḥ kāsāya kalpate ||  
 2.4.9  uro vidahyate cāsya tathaivāpyabhitapyate  |
       
 soṣmanāsaś ca bhavati dahyete cākṣiṇī tataḥ ||  
 2.4.10  niṣṭhīvati sapittaṃ ca raktaṃ vā nā kadācana |
       
       mukhaṃ bhavati vā pītaṃ pittakāsena dehinaḥ ||  
 2.4.11  yassadā śleṣmalo jantuḥ śleṣmalaṃ bhajate ' śanam |
       
       pibatyaśnāti madhuraṃ madhuraṃ vāpi khādati ||  
 2.4.12  avyāyāma rataś cāpi divāsvapnaṃ ca sevate |
       
       tasya śleṣmā prakupito gṛhītvā hṛdayaṃ tataḥ ||  
 2.4.13  ūrdhvaṃ samprāpya dhamanīstataḥ kāsāya kalpate |
       
       grathitaṃ śleṣmaṇā kāsaṃ niṣṭhīvati sapūtikam ||  
 2.4.14  duṣṭaśleṣmapratiśyāyaḥ śleṣmakāsena jāyate |
       
       sāhasaṃ karma yaḥ kṛtvā vikṣataṃ khedayatyuraḥ ||  
 2.4.15  niṣṭhīvati saraktaṃ ca kāse kṣatasamudbhave |
       
       strīṣu saktaś ca yo jantus tasya śuklaparikṣayāt ||  
 2.4.16  liṅgaṃ vātābhibhūtatvāt sūcībhir iva tudyate |
       
       saraktaṃ kurute mūtraṃ tathā śuklaṃ ca lohitam ||  
 2.4.17  sarva ete samuddiṣṭāḥ kāsā lakṣaṇato mayā |
       
       tānavekṣya bhiṣag buddhyā tataḥ kuryāc cikitsitam  || ity āha bhagavān
      ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele nidāne caturtho ' dhyāyaḥ || || pañcamo ' dhyāyaḥ || athātaḥ
      kuṣṭhanidānaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 2.5.1  pippalīṃ kākamācīṃ  ca likucaṃ dadhisarpiṣā |
       
       vātāyuṃ  payasā sārdhaṃ guḍena saha mūlakam ||  
 2.5.2  anyadevaṃvidhaṃ yac ca viruddhaṃ tatsamaśnataḥ |
       
       chardiṃ pratighnataś cāpi mithyāsaṃsargasevanāt ||  
 2.5.3  anullikhya vidagdhaṃ ca vidāhi ca samaśnataḥ |
       
 pathi cārādviriktasya  śrāntasyodakasevanāt ||  
 2.5.4  matsyān payaś ca nimbūṃś ca tathaikadhyaṃ samaśnataḥ
      |
       
       jantossañjāyate kuṣṭhaṃ tadvidhānāṃ ca sevanāt ||  
 2.5.5  yassadā śleṣmalo jantuḥ śleṣmalaṃ bhajate ' śanam |
       
       sevate ca divāsvapnaṃ tasya śleṣmā pravardhate ||  
 2.5.6  sa vṛddho dūṣayatyasya māṃsaṃ tvagrudhiraṃ  tathā |
       
       utsādyate tvagdoṣeṇa svidyate tena cāpy atha ||  
 2.5.7  tatra kuṣṭhāni jāyante dadru sidhmāni vai punaḥ |
       
       maṇḍalāni ca citrāṇi teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam ||  
 2.5.8  maṇḍalāni ghanānīha piṭakābhāni sarvaśaḥ |
       
       sakaṇḍūni visarpīṇi dadrukuṣṭhāni nirdiśet ||  
 2.5.9  prasravanti yadā tāni doṣotsannāni dehinaḥ |
       
       tadāsya kīlaṃ koṣaṃ ca picchilaṃ saṃsravanti ca ||  
 2.5.10 saṃhatāni vipāṇḍūni paṅkiloṣṭhacitāni ca |
       
 tvagutthāni tu rūksāṇi maṇḍalāni tanūny api ||  
 2.5.11  sidhmakuṣṭhāni jānīyāt tathā tāni bhavanti vai |
       
       picchilaṃ madhuvarṇaṃ ca yadā doṣāḥ sravanti ca ||  
 2.5.12  maṇḍalāni ca śuklāni ghanotsannāni sarvaśaḥ |
       
       vidyānmaṇḍalakuṣṭhāni cirabhedīni dehinām ||  
 2.5.13  yadā tu tāni bhidyante tadā śvetaṃ sravanti hi |
       
       iti śleṣmasamutthāni trīṇi kuṣṭhāni nirdiśet ||  
 2.5.14  yassadā vātalo janturvātalaṃ bhajate ' śanam |
       
       vātātapau sevate ca tasya vātaḥ pravardhate ||  
 2.5.15  sa vṛddho dūṣayatyasya tvaṅmāṃsarudhiraṃ tathā |
       
 utsādyate tvagdoṣeṇa svidyate tena cāpy atha ||  
 2.5.16  kapālakuṣṭhaṃ tenāsya praduṣṭe māṃsaśoṇite |
       
       jantorvivṛddhavātasya tasya vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam ||  
 2.5.17  paruṣāṇyaruṇābhāni maṇḍalāni samāni ca |
       
       vidyāt kapālakuṣṭhāni cirabhedīni dehinām ||  
 2.5.18  yassadā pittalo jantuḥ pittalaṃ bhajate ' śanam |
       
       vātātapau sevate ca tasya pittaṃ prakupyati ||  
 2.5.19  tad vṛddhaṃ dūṣayatyasya tvaṅmāṃsarudhiraṃ tadā |
       
       utsādyate tvagdoṣeṇa svidyate tena cāpy atha ||  
 2.5.20  tataḥ kuṣṭhāni jāyante praduṣṭe māṃsaśoṇite |
       
       pittasya parikope vā teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam ||  
 2.5.21  pakvodumbaravarṇāni maṇḍalānīha yāni tu |
       
       vidyādaudumbarāṇyatra tānyasādhyāni dehinām ||  
 2.5.22  prāpnuvanti yadā bhedaṃ kuṣṭhāny audumbarāṇi ca |
       
       maṇḍalīkāni kuṣṭhāni tadā tāni bhavanti vai ||  
 2.5.23  maṇḍalāni ca yānīha puṇḍarīkanibhāni vai |
       
       puṇḍarīkāṇi sādhyāni tāni vidyādvicakṣaṇaḥ ||  
 2.5.24  prāpnuvanti yadā bhedaṃ puṇḍarīkāṇi yāni vai |
       
       ṛśyajihvāni kuṣṭhāni tadā tāni vinirdiśet ||  
 2.5.25  nīlotpalasavarṇāni maṇḍalānīha rūpataḥ |
       
       ṛśyajihvāni kuṣṭhāni tānyasādhyāni nirdiśet ||  
 2.5.26  prāpnuvanti yadā bhedamṛśyajihvānyaśeṣataḥ |
       
       kākaṇānīti matimāṃstadā tāni vinirdiśet ||  
 2.5.27 kākaṇantikavarṇāni maṇḍalānīha yāni tu |
       
       kākaṇānīti tānyāhuḥ pratyākhyeyāni dehinām ||  
 2.5.28  iti kuṣṭhanidānaṃ vai vyākhyātam anupūrvaśaḥ |
       
       tanniśamyeha matimān hitajīrṇāśano bhavet || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele nidāne pañcamo ' dhyāyaḥ || || ṣaṣṭho ' dhyāyaḥ || athātaḥ
      pramehanidānaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 2.6.1  prakṛtiprabhavaś caiva narasya svakṛtas tathā |
       
       jñeyaḥ prameho dvividhas tasya vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam ||  
 2.6.2  ślakṣṇāṅgā mṛdavaḥ snigdhā bhṛśaṃ śleṣmalamedurāḥ |
       
       jātapramehā nardanti matsyamāṃsocitā narāḥ ||  
 2.6.3  mātāpitṛbhyāmīdṛgbhyāṃ janito yas tu mānavaḥ |
       
       medaḥśithilanāttasya prakṛtyā sa tu mehati ||  
 2.6.4  anūpajānāṃ susnigdhairvividhaiś cāpi vārijaiḥ |
       
       gavyājaurabhramāṃsaiś ca sadyo dadhnā ghṛtena vā ||  
 2.6.5  guḍaprakāraiḥ payasā palalenaudakaiḥ khagaiḥ |
       
       avyāyāmāddivāsvapnātsukhaśayyāsanāttathā ||  
 2.6.6  ity ebhir īdṛśaiś cānyairmedaḥ  snigdhaiḥ
      pravardhate |
       
       medaḥ pravṛddhaṃ dehaṃ ca vastiṃ ca kledayaty api ||  
 2.6.7  yassadā medasā klinnaḥ śleṣmalaṃ bhajate ' śanam |
       
       tasya prakupitaḥ śleṣmā pramehān kurute daśa ||  
 2.6.8  tad yathodakamehaṃ ca piṣṭamehaṃ tathaiva ca |
       
       evamādīṃstathānyāṃś ca teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam ||  
 2.6.9  sphaṭikāmbunibhaṃ mūtramudamehī pramehati |
       
       śuklapiṣṭanibhaṃ cāpi piṣṭamehī pramehati ||  
 2.6.10 kāṇḍekṣurasamehī ca mehatīkṣurasopamam |
       
       mūtraṃ śuklopamaṃ cāpi śuklamehī tu mehati ||  
 2.6.11  ity etāṃścaturo mehāñ jānīyāt kevalātkaphāt |
       
       śleṣmaṇyanubale  pitte ye mehanti tu tāñchṛṇu ||  
 2.6.12  lavaṇāmbunibhaṃ mūtraṃ vidyāllavaṇamehinaḥ |
       
       pramehati tathā jantussurāmehī surākṛti || mūtraṃ sāndraṃ prasannaṃ tu
      dṛśyate  sāndramehinaḥ |
       
 
 iti bhele nidāne ṣaṣṭho '
      dhyāyaḥ || || saptamo ' dhyāyaḥ ||  ..
        .. gītāni bhajate nityaṃ 
      pittonmādanipīḍitaḥ  ||  
 
 
 2.7.1  yassadā śleṣmalo jantuḥ śleṣmalaṃ bhajate ' śanam |
       
       sevate ca divāsvapnaṃ tasya śleṣmā pravardhate ||  
 2.7.2  sa vṛddha ūrdhvaṃ hṛdayād gṛhītvā dhamanīrdaśa |
       
       ruddhvā cetovahaṃ mārgaṃ saṃjñāṃ bhraṃśayate tataḥ ||  
 2.7.3  sa bhraṣṭasaṃjñaḥ puruṣastāni tāni viceṣṭate |
       
       gāyannṛtyati caikatra hasatyatha ca roditi ||  
 2.7.4  ekatrāste vinā lokaṃ śete cāpi jaḍo yathā |
       
       janaṃ bhīṣayate cāpi śleṣmonmādī pumāniha ||  
 2.7.5  yas tv etat sarvamaśnāti yathoktaṃ doṣakopanam |
       
       sannipātāttathonmādaṃ sarvaliṅgaṃ sa ṛcchati ||  
 2.7.6  sa yadā dhananāśena maraṇena priyasya vā |
       
       atha cintayate, tasya saṃjñā bhraśyati cintayā ||  
 2.7.7  sa cintayati yān bhāvāṃstāneva pralapatyatha |
       
       āgantuṃ pañcamaṃ vidyādity unmādaṃ śarīriṇām ||  
 2.7.8  sarvān etān vijānīyādunmādānvai  cikitsitāt |
       
       duḥkhena saṃjñābhraṣṭo hi prakṛtiṃ punar ṛcchati ||  
 2.7.9  evaṃ śarīrajā doṣāḥ śarīre paryavasthitāḥ |
       
       śarīram eva hiṃsanti pāvakaḥ svamivāśrayam ||  
 2.7.10 na hi satvāni hiṃsanti na piśācā na rākṣasāḥ |
       
 devās tathā dharmaśīlāḥ madhyasthā manujānprati ||  
 2.7.11  vamane recane yukto nirūhe cānuvāsane |
       
       na jātu dāruṇān rogānunmādān prāpnuyān naraḥ || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele nidāne saptamo ' dhyāyaḥ || || aṣṭamo ' dhyāyaḥ || athāto '
      pasmāranidānaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 2.8.1  vātātpittātkaphāccaiva sannipātāttathaiva  ca |
       
       apasmārā bhavantīha teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam ||  
 2.8.2  yassadā vātalo janturvātalaṃ bhajate ' śanam |
       
       vyāyāmaṃ sevate cāpi tasya vātaḥ prakupyati ||  
 2.8.3  sa vṛddha ūrdhvaṃ hṛdayād gṛhītvā dhamanīrdaśa |
       
       ruddhvā cetovahaṃ mārgaṃ saṃjñāṃ bhraṃśayate tataḥ ||  
 2.8.4  sa bhraṣṭasaṃjñaḥ patati dantānkaṭakaṭāyate |
       
       utphālayati netre ca bhruvau prakṣipate tathā ||  
 2.8.5  sa cetpratyāgato brūyāt tamasaḥ parato gataḥ |
       
       pratibhāti ca me kṛṣṇā jagatī khaṇḍaśas tathā ||  
 2.8.6  tadordhvamevaṃ hṛdayaṃ vāyurvarcopadhāvati |
       
       ity etairlakṣaṇairvidyādapasmāraṃ tu vātajam ||  
 2.8.7  yassadā pittalo jantuḥ pittalaṃ bhajate ' śanam |
       
       agnyātapau sevate ca tasya pittaṃ pravardhate ||  
 2.8.8  tad vṛddhamūrdhvaṃ hṛdayād gṛhītvā dhamanīrdaśa |
       
       ruddhvā cetovahaṃ mārgaṃ saṃjñāṃ bhraṃśayate tataḥ ||  
 2.8.9  sa bhraṣṭasaṃjñaḥ patati dantānkaṭakaṭāyate |
       
       utphālayati netre ca bhruvāvutkṣipate tathā ||  
 2.8.10  sa cetpratyāgato brūyāt tamasaḥ parato gataḥ |
       
       pratibhāti ca me śuklā jagatī khaṇḍaśas tathā ||  
 2.8.11  tadordhvamevaṃ hṛdayaṃ kapho varcopadhāvati |
       
       ity etairlakṣaṇairvidyādapasmāraṃ kaphātmakam ||  
 2.8.12  yas tv etat sarvamaśnāti yathoktaṃ doṣakopanam |
       
       sannipātādapasmāraṃ sarvaliṅgaṃ sa ṛcchati ||  
 2.8.13  evaṃ rasairihāpathyairvivṛddheṣv anilādiṣu |
       
       nā ' pasmārayate prāṇī na satvair upahanyate ||  
 2.8.14  yadā yadābhivardhante doṣāḥ parvasvivodadhiḥ |
       
       tadā tadāpasmarati naiṣa kliśyati santatam ||  
 2.8.15  jvarasya śoṣagulmānāṃ kāsināmatha kuṣṭhinām |
       
       pramehonmādināṃ caiva tathāpasmāriṇām api ||  
 2.8.16  ity aṣṭau vai pradiṣṭāni nidānāni śarīriṇām |
       
       vimānāni pravakṣyāmi yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele aṣṭamo ' dhyāyaḥ || iti bhelasaṃhitāyāṃ nidānasthānaṃ samāptam ||
      || vimānasthānam || |
       
       |prathamo ' dhyāyaḥ || athāto rasavimānaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān
      ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 
 
 3.1.1  śarīraṃ dhārayantīha ṣaḍrasāḥ samamāhṛtāḥ |
       
       ato ' nyathā vikārāṃs tu janayanti śarīriṇām ||  
 3.1.2  rūkṣo laghuḥ sthiraśśītaḥ kaṣāyastikta eva ca |
       
       tīkṣṇoṣṇāvamlalavaṇau kaṭurvāpi vikāśyatha ||  
 3.1.3  śītaḥ snigdho gururbalyaḥ picchilo madhuro rasaḥ |
       
 kaṣāyatiktakaṭukaḥ śīto rūkṣo ' nilaḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
 3.1.4  rūkṣoṣṇamamlaṃ pittantu kaṭukaṃ ca pracakṣate |
       
       śleṣmā tu madhuraḥ snigdhaḥ śīto mandaḥ sthiro guruḥ ||  
 3.1.5  ity etān rasadoṣāṇāṃ sahotpannān guṇānviduḥ |
       
       tatra vāyuguṇaistulyān kaṣāyakaṭutiktakān ||  
 3.1.6  kaṭvamlalavaṇaistulyāṃs tathā pittaguṇānviduḥ |
       
       madhuraṃ lavaṇāmlau ca vidyāt kaphasamān rasān ||  
 3.1.7  tasmād abhyasyamānais taiḥ śleṣmā dehe pravardhate |
       
 atraikatra kṛto rāśirdvirmahatvamiharcchati ||  
 3.1.8  guṇasāmyādvivardhante yathāsvaṃ dhātavo nṛṇām |
       
       rasais tadviparītaiś ca yāntyete kṣayamāhṛtaiḥ ||  
 3.1.9  yathodakaṃ samāsādya śāntiṃ gacchati pāvakaḥ |
       
       kaṣāyatiktakaṭukai rūkṣo rūkṣairvivardhate ||  
 3.1.10  mārutaḥ snigdhabhāvaiś ca tato ' nyair upaśāmyati |
       
       kaṭvamlalavaṇaiḥ pittamuṣṇamuṣṇairvivardhate ||  
 3.1.11 śītaiśśāmyati śeṣais tu guṇānāṃ hi viśeṣataḥ
      |
       
       snigdhaḥ snigdhaiḥ kaphaś cāpi vardhate madhurādibhiḥ ||  
 3.1.12  rasaiḥ śāmyati rūkṣaiś ca kaṣāyakaṭutiktakaiḥ |
       
       ekaikamekasāmānyādvardhayanti trayastrayaḥ ||  
 3.1.13  ghnanti cānyaguṇatvena rasā doṣaṃ śarīriṇām |
       
       na vāyussaha tailena snehauṣṇyādvyapalīyate ||  
 3.1.14  śītatvānmadhuratvāc ca na pittaṃ saha sarpiṣā |
       
       raukṣyāt kaṣāyabhāvāc ca snigdho madhura eva ca ||  
 3.1.15  na śleṣmā madhunā sārdhaṃ dehe paryavatiṣṭhate |
       
       ānūpamāṃsajā vāpi vasā majjāna eva ca ||  
 3.1.16  tailavanmārutaṃ ghnanti snehauṣṇyagurubhāvataḥ |
       
       śākādaviṣkirāṇāṃ ca rasā majjāna eva ca ||  
 3.1.17 ghṛtavad ghnanti te
      pittaṃ śītamādhuryabhāvataḥ |
       
       kaṣāyatiktakaṭukaṃ yac ca kiñcidihauṣadham ||  
 3.1.18  madhuraṃ tatkaphaṃ hanti guṇānyatvena dehinām |
       
       atha nātyupayuñjīta pippalīṃ kṣāram eva ca ||  
 3.1.19  lavaṇaṃ caiva, bahvetad bhuktaṃ doṣāya kalpate |
       
       śleṣmāṇaṃ cyāvayitvā tu notsahetāpakarṣitum ||  
 3.1.20  pippalī pākamadhurā tasmāt tāṃ nātibhakṣayet |
       
       atyāhṛtā paceddehaṃ tīkṣṇoṣṇakaṭubhāvataḥ ||  
 3.1.21  kṣāraṃ ca lavaṇaṃ caiva bhoktuṃ neheta kevalam |
       
       mātrāvaduṣṇaṃ snigdhaṃ ca sātmyaṃ svādu ca bhojanam ||  
 3.1.22  avidāhi ca yat pāke jīrṇe tadupayojayet |
       
       balavarṇakaraṃ snigdhamuṣṇaṃ śleṣmānilāpaham ||  
 3.1.23  vidahyate na mātrā ca sātmyatāṃ ca karotyatha |
       
       svādu puṣṭikaraṃ jantoravidāhi prasādanam ||  
 3.1.24  nṛṇāmāyuṣkaraṃ caiva jīrṇe bhojanamiṣyate |
       
       na jalpanna hasaṃś cāpi na drutaṃ na vilambitam ||  
 3.1.25 bhuñjītābhyādṛtaḥ snigdhaṃ dehe nirvartate rasaḥ |
       
       yatheha vodyato vahniḥ pravarteta sudāruṇi ||  
 3.1.26  pacyamāne tathā bhukte rasādirupacīyate |
       
       jīvayanti paraṃ varṣā hemantaḥ pāyayaty api ||  
 3.1.27  grīṣmaḥ pacati cāpy enaṃ pariṇāma ivāparaḥ |
       
       bhṛśamauṣṇyāt kaṭurgrīṣmaḥ sarvadhātuviśoṣaṇaḥ ||  
 3.1.28  dhairyasthairyakaraṃ śītaṃ, varṣāmadyaba.... |
       
       |....... || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ || |tṛtīyo ' dhyāyaḥ ||  
 
 
 3.3.1  |.. |.. yasya bhuktaṃ vipacyate |
       
       bhuñjānasyāpi cānnāni balaṃ varṇaś ca hīyate ||  
 3.3.2  alpaṃ laghvapi yaccānnaṃ bhuktaṃ duḥkhena jīryati |
       
       nāpnoti balavarṇau ca durbalāgniḥ sa ucyate ||  
 3.3.3  kadācitpacyate bhuktaṃ kadācinna vipacyate |
       
       guru vā laghu vā yasya viṣamāgniḥ sa ucyate ||  
 3.3.4  mitaṃ pacyeta yasyānnamatibhuktaṃ na pacyate |
       
       samāgniṃ taṃ naraṃ vidyāt samapittakaphānilam ||  
 3.3.5  naro bhavati tīkṣṇāgniḥ prakṛtyā vātapaittikaḥ |
       
       vātiko viṣamāgniśca, mandāgniś ca kaphān naraḥ ||  
 3.3.6  yasya hīnādhikas tv agniḥ kṣipraṃ dehaṃ sa muñcati |
       
       samāgniś ca samātmā yaḥ sa dīrghāyuṣṭvamṛcchati ||  
 3.3.7  gavyamāhiṣavārāhaiḥ kulīrairmatsyakarkaṭaiḥ |
       
       māṃsaissapalalaiḥ snigdhairatyagniṃ pratibhojayet ||  
 3.3.8  godhāniṣkvathite kṣīre siddhaṃ bhuñjīta pāyasam |
       
       pibeddadhi sasarpiṣkaṃ māṣasūpena miśritam ||  
 3.3.9  tathā palalasammiśraṃ kacchapāṇḍarasaṃ pibet |
       
       guḍaṃ ca tailasammiśraṃ kuryād anyac ca taddhitam ||  
 3.3.10  snigdhasya viṣamāgnes tu vamanādīni kārayet |
       
 grahaṇīdūṣaṇīyoktaṃ mandāgnes tu cikitsitam ||  
 3.3.11  antarauṣadhapānāni bahirlepe ca yā kriyā |
       
       śastrakarmavidhānaṃ ca bheṣajaṃ trividhaṃ smṛtam ||  
 3.3.12  madhuro ' mlaḥ kaṭuś caiva paktimārgāstrayaḥ smṛtāḥ
      |
       
       kaṭur bhavati pakvasya pacyamānasya cetarau ||  
 3.3.13  ihānnapānaṃ bhojyaṃ ca madhurāmlaṃ pracakṣate |
       
       vātajeṣu vikāreṣu yadā vā tairna śāmyati ||  
 3.3.14  dadyādathāsmai snigdhāya bhiṣak snehavirecanam |
       
       vastibhir vā cikitseta hyadhobhāge ca mārutaḥ ||  
 3.3.15  tathā ca tiktamadhuraṃ pānamannaṃ pradāpayet |
       
       paittikeṣu vikāreṣu yadi vātanna śāmyati ||  
 3.3.16  tasya snigdhasya vamanaṃ śirasaś ca virecanam |
       
       kuryād yathābalaṃ śleṣmā hyūrdhvabhāgaprakīrtitaḥ ||  
 3.3.17  śakṛnmūtrānilāś caiva raktamāṃsādayaś ca ṣaṭ |
       
       vidyānnibandhanānīti tāni deheṣu dehinām ||  
 3.3.18  balaṃ vayaḥ śarīraṃ ca pratyekaṃ trividhaṃ smṛtam |
       
       uttamādhamamadhyaṃ tu bhedenātha niśāmayet ||  
 3.3.19  āhāraś ca vihāraś ca sevyamānau krameṇa tu |
       
       kālena prakṛtiṃ yātas tad āhuḥ sātmyalakṣaṇam ||
       
       ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ | iti bhele vimāne tṛtīyo ' dhyāyaḥ || || caturtho '
      dhyāyaḥ || athāto rogaprakṛtiviniścayaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān
      ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 3.4.1  pramṛśya dṛṣṭvā pṛṣṭvā ca parīkṣetāturaṃ bhiṣak |
       
       pūrvaṃ tu rogavijñānaṃ tataḥ paś cāccikitsitam ||  
 3.4.2  rūpaṃ chāyām upacayaṃ prāgvyādhervyādhitasya ca |
       
       dṛṣṭvā bhiṣak parīkṣeta prākṛtaṃ vaikṛtaṃ tathā ||  
 3.4.3  jvarasya sāmyaṃ vaiṣamyaṃ gātraṃ vā ślakṣṇakarkaśam |
       
       dṛṣṭvā spṛṣṭvāvagaccheddhi śaity amauṣṇyaṃ ca pāṇinā ||  
 3.4.4  mātāpitṛsamācāraṃ sātmyaṃ garbheṇa dauhṛdam |
       
       vyādhikālaparīṇāmaṃ śakṛnmūtravivarṇatām ||  
 3.4.5  pūrvarūpasamutthānaṃ śarīrāgnivayobalam |
       
       prakṛtiṃ janmadeśaṃ ca bhojanaṃ ca yathocitam ||  
 3.4.6  vyāyāmaniṣṭhāsātmyaṃ ca mātrāmātre ca bhojane |
       
       praśnoktāni vijānīyādyadanyadapi tadvidham ||  
 3.4.7  kecidicchanti munayo doṣamekamihādhikam |
       
       vikārasyāviśiṣṭatvād aniṣṭaṃ kāraṇaṃ ca tat ||  
 3.4.8  rūkṣāsaho naro yas tu sa vātaprakṛtiḥ smṛtaḥ |
       
       pettiko ' mbusahaś cāpi madhurāmlāsahaḥ kaphāt ||  
 3.4.9  svabhāvaprabhavo hyeṣa sahotpanno guṇāgamaḥ |
       
       prakṛtiṃ vai vijānīyāt tasya vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam ||  
 3.4.10  avyaktaṃ ca mahāṃś caiva mahābhūtāni pañca ca |
       
       parāḥ prakṛtayassapta svabhāvaḥ kāla eva ca ||  
 3.4.11 tebhyo bhavanti bhūtāni tānyeva pratiyānti ca |
       
       indriyāṇīndriyārthāś ca buddhayaḥ pañca tās tathā ||  
 3.4.12  ṛtukāle yadā nārī rūkṣāṇyannāni sevate |
       
       udāvarte tathāpīha karma cātiniṣevate ||  
 3.4.13  tadaivaṃ vātasanduṣṭaṃ raktaṃ garbhāśayasthitam |
       
       tadvidhenaiva śuklena yadā yogam upaiti vai ||  
 3.4.14  tadā vātapraduṣṭena śuklena rudhireṇa ca |
       
       vātaprakṛtitāmeti garbhaḥ prāgātmanaḥ sa vai ||  
 3.4.15  evam evartukāle vai bhajantyāḥ kaphapaittikam |
       
       ślaiṣmikī paittikī cāpi prakṛtirjāyate tataḥ ||  
 3.4.16  hrasvaḥ śīghraḥ kṛśaś cāṇuḥ pralāpī paruṣapriyaḥ |
       
 stabdhāṅgo viṣamaśliṣṭo gaṇarūpe gaṇe dhṛtiḥ ||  
 3.4.17  sahaḥ kleśasya visrambhī rūkṣatvaganavasthitaḥ |
       
       kharamūrdhajaromāṅgaḥ kṣipragrāhī tathā smṛtaḥ ||  
 3.4.18  svapneṣu coṣṭreṇāyāti viyaty api tu gacchati |
       
       yasyopaśete susnigdhaṃ sa vātaprakṛtirnaraḥ ||  
 3.4.19  śithilāṅgo ' garugandhaścaṇḍaḥ śīghro mahāśanaḥ |
       
       valīpalitakhālity aśīghrapākī tathākṣamaḥ ||  
 3.4.20 vṛttākṣaḥ krodhano yaś ca durbalo
      durbalendriyaḥ |
       
       nāmlāśaḥ śītaśītāśī duṣprajāḥ śītalapriyaḥ ||  
 3.4.21  ativarṇo ' timedhāvī svapne pāvakadṛk tathā |
       
       śīghramāvāti yaḥ snātaḥ paittikaprakṛtirnaraḥ ||  
 3.4.22  susnigdhaḥ ślakṣṇabaddhāṅgaḥ subhagaḥ priyadarśanaḥ |
       
       dṛḍhasmṛtiściragrāhī dṛḍhabhaktiparāyaṇaḥ ||  
 3.4.23 priyamāṃsoṣṇakaṭukaḥ priyayoṣidbahupradaḥ |
       
       kṣamāvān balavān dhanyaḥ śītāluraśanapriyaḥ ||  
 3.4.24  cirād dṛḍhavyādhiratho mitavāgalpabhuk smṛtaḥ |
       
       dīrghadarśī mahotsāho dhīraḥ kleśasahas tathā ||  
 3.4.25  romadantanakhaiḥ keśairbahulairyassubandhanaiḥ |
       
 cirādāvāti ca snātaḥ svapne paśyati codakam ||  
 3.4.26  yas tu rūkṣaṃ tu sahate sa śleṣmaprakṛtirnaraḥ |
       
       saṃsṛṣṭaprakṛtiṃ vidyāt saṃsṛṣṭaiś cāpi lakṣaṇaiḥ ||  
 3.4.27  nivṛttā prakṛtirdhanyā dvandvā bhavati madhyamā |
       
       sannipātātmikā yā tu jaghanyā sā prakīrtitā || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele caturtho ' dhyāyaḥ || || pañcamo ' dhyāyaḥ || athāto
      vyādhitarūpīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 3.5.1 guruvyādhirnaraḥ kaścinmūrtyā caiva balena ca |
       
 laghuvyādhiḥ naras tv anyaḥ sattvād ibhir ananvitaḥ ||  
 3.5.2  guruvyādhirivābhāti bhiṣak tatra pramuhyati |
       
       tatrālpamātraṃ bhaiṣajyaṃ sevitaṃ gururogiṇām ||  
 3.5.3  na nirdahatyataḥ sarvāndoṣānalpena tejasā |
       
       mūrchā chardistimitatā jṛmbhā ca gurugātratā ||  
 3.5.4 tṛṣṇā santatabhāvaś ca bhavanty etāni tasya tu |
       
       mustā kuṣṭhaṃ haridre dve pragrahātiviṣāmayāḥ ||  
 3.5.5  bhallātakaṃ vayasthā ca citrakaḥ suradāru ca |
       
       etairāsthāpanaṃ tac ca kuryād gomūtrasaṃyutaiḥ ||  
 3.5.6  pūrṇādiṣṭānadiṣṭāṃś ca tathā śāntiṃ niyacchati |
       
       āragvadhaṃ saptaparṇaṃ madanaṃ svādukaṇṭakam ||  
 3.5.7 śārṅgeṣṭāṃ kaṭukāṃ pāṭhāṃ naktamālaṃ savatsakam |
       
       etadāragvadhārthaṃ tu kuryād āsthāpanaṃ bhiṣak ||  
  || ṣaṣṭho ' dhyāyaḥ || athāta
      ṛtuvimānaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 3.6.1  ādity agativaiśeṣyādṛtūnāṃ parivartanāt |
       
       kṣayaṃ vṛddhiṃ ca gacchanti yathāsvaṃ dhātavo nṛṇām ||  
 3.6.2  bhūmibāṣpātpurovātād ghanacchāyāprasaṅgataḥ |
       
       mahīkaluṣasanduṣṭātpīyamānānnavodakāt ||  
 3.6.3  graiṣmikātkṛśabhāvāc ca prāṇe durbalatāṃ gate |
       
       varṣāsu dehināmagnirmṛdutvam upagacchati ||  
 3.6.4  tato viṣṭambhajo vāyuryasmāddhītaḥ prakupyati |
       
       tanna seveta varṣāsu kaṭvamlalavaṇān rasān ||  
 3.6.5  mudgayūṣeṇa vāśnīyāt purāṇān śāliṣaṣṭikān |
       
       athavā yavagodhūmaṃ sṛṣṭavāte hitaṃ smṛtam ||  
 3.6.6  paṭolāni ca takraṃ ca jāṅgalāṃś ca rasān laghūn |
       
       kaupaṃ divyaṃ jalaṃ siddhaṃ bhajedāsthāpanāni ca ||  
 3.6.7  asaṃsthitatvād varṣāsu jalamamlaṃ vipacyate |
       
       tasmād vivardhate pittaṃ yathāmlaiś ca tathāśanaiḥ ||  
 3.6.8  sūryopatāpātsahasā gatvā caivauṣadhīkṛtam |
       
       varṣāsu nicayaṃ pittaṃ kopaṃ śaradi gacchati ||  
 3.6.9  snānānulepanaṃ tasmācchītaṃ śaradi kārayet |
       
       vījayet tālavṛntaiś ca vigāheta sarassu ca ||  
 3.6.10  lājasaktuṃ pibec cāpi śarkarāmadhuvāribhiḥ |
       
       mudgayūṣeṇa cāśnīyāt purāṇān śāliṣāṣṭikān ||  
 3.6.11  rasān madhurakāṃś cāpi jāṅgalān sarpiṣā kṛtān |
       
       vidārīkṣurasaṃ drākṣāṃ sevetānyac ca tadvidham ||  
 3.6.12  gatapittapravegaś ca śaratkāle ghṛtaṃ pibet |
       
       tathāsyāpyāyyate dehaḥ śeṣā doṣāś ca yāntyadhaḥ ||  
 3.6.13  paścādvātasya rūkṣatvāc chītalatvād ṛtos tathā |
       
       hemantena nigacchanti kharatvaṃ dhātavo nṛṇām ||  
 3.6.14  tasmāt snehaṃ bahuvidhaṃ snānaṃ coṣṇena vāriṇā |
       
       bhajetkharatvapāruṣye tathābhyaṅgātpraśāmyati ||  
 3.6.15  śakunānaudakānmatsyān snehāmlalavaṇānvitān |
       
       ānūpāni ca māṃsāni sevetānyac ca tadvidham ||  
 3.6.16 kaṭurhi paścimo vāyuḥ śaity aṃ tīvraṃ
      ca vāriṇaḥ |
       
       atyarthaṃ rūkṣayed vāyuḥ śarīraṃ rūkṣabhojāt ||  
 3.6.17  guruprāvaraṇaś ca syādātapāgnī ca saṃśrayet |
       
       rūkṣe hi tejasā jantoḥ śarīrāddhriyate balam ||  
 3.6.18  āpo hi śītamadhurā hemante tu bhavantyatha |
       
       tasmāt kaphas tathā tābhiḥ snigdhairannaiś ca cīyate ||  
 3.6.19  śītalatvād ṛtoś cāpi na tāvatparibhidyate |
       
       tasmāt tailaguḍopetāṃ vāruṇīṃ śiśire pibet ||  
 3.6.20  vividhāni ca māṃsāni bhakṣayec ca prakārataḥ |
       
       evaṃ tu nicitaḥ śleṣmā śītatvād iha dehinām ||  
 3.6.21  dravatāmeti saṃspṛṣṭo vasante sūryatejasā |
       
       ravirhi madhyamāṃ kāṣṭhāṃ vasante pratipadyate ||  
 3.6.22  dahyatāmiva śailānāṃ nṛṇāmaṅge prakupyati |
       
       tataḥ śleṣmā dravībhūto hṛdayaṃ vyapalimpati ||  
 3.6.23 tasmācchardyavipākau ca dṛśyete śiśirātyaye |
       
       tasmād vasante śleṣmaghnaṃ madhumārdvīkamīritam ||  
  iti bhele ṣaṣṭho ' dhyāyaḥ || iti
      bhelasaṃhitāyāṃ vimānasthānaṃ samāptam || || śārīrasthāna || dvitīyo ' dhyāyaḥ
      || Bhṣ4.2.? ||  
  māno ' vatiṣṭhate |
       
       jātasya daśame māse nāmagotre namaskṛte || Bhṣ4.2.? |
       
       taruṇasya kumārasya vardhamāneṣu dhātuṣu |
       
       asthimajjasu pūrṇeṣu śukraṃ na pratipadyate ||  
 
 
 
 
 4.2.3  aṅgāṅgeṣu pravṛddheṣu pratimūleṣu dhātuṣu |
       
       śuklaṃ ca ṣoḍaśe varṣe suvyaktaṃ pratipadyate ||  
 4.2.4  tathā vṛddhasya jantoś ca parikṣīṇeṣu dhātuṣu |
       
 vivekā[ ma] na yathāpūrvaṃ vivicyante parikṣayāt ||  
 4.2.5  tato ' lparetā bhavati sujīrṇo durbalo ' thavā |
       
       na paśyati naraḥ śuklaṃ sarvadhātuparikṣayāt ||  
 4.2.6  raktaṃ māṃsaṃ vasāsthīni[ ca] majjā śuklaṃ
      tathānalaḥ |
       
       śakṛnmūtre ca tairmandaṃ vidyānnavatitaḥ param ||  
 4.2.7  iha narchati garbhaṃ strī vātenopahatā tathā |
       
 yonidoṣeṇa[ yā] cānnena na hi vandhyāsti nā ca na ||  
 4.2.8  vamanaṃ recanaṃ
      caiva vastimāsthāpanaṃ[ vastirā] tathā |
       
       tasmāt tatkārayetstrīṇāṃ prasiddhāḥ prasuvanti[ prasa] vai ||  
 4.2.9  athātra bhavati praśnaḥ kasmācchabdaṃ[ rasā
      chardiṃ] na nāsayā |
       
 gṛhṇāsyāsyena[ gṛhīṣvā] vā gandhaṃ tulyaṃ sarvatra khaṃ yadi ||  
 4.2.10 tvagbhāge[ tvadbhā] ca same kasmānna
      gṛhṇātyanyayā rasam |
       
       iti tadvacanaṃ śrutvā pratyuvāca punarvasuḥ ||  
 4.2.11  ghrāṇaṃ gandhaṃ ca bhaumaṃ hi rūpaṃ[ rūkṣaṃ]
      cakṣuś ca taijasam |saṃsparśaṃ sparśanaṃ vāyoḥ śrotraṃ
       śabdātmakhaṃ[ śabdātmakaṃ] tathā ||  
 4.2.12  rasanaṃ ca raso hy āpyaṃ[ vyā-] tasmād
      etairihendriyaiḥ |
       
       yathāsvaṃ tulyayogitvād viṣayagrahaṇaṃ smṛtam ||  
 4.2.13  svaṃ svaṃ hi viṣayaṃ dhātur vijānāty ātmanānvitaḥ |
       
       ātmendriyamanorthānāṃ bandhācceti[ bandhiśce] samādiśa || ity āha
      bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele dvitīyo ' dhyāyaḥ || tṛtīyo ' dhyāyaḥ |
       
       athāto ' samānagotrīyaṃ śārīraṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 4.3.1  ihāsamānagotrān tu[ vai] ṛtusnātāṃ striyaṃ
      vrajet |
       
       medhā vinamarogaṃ[ di-] sā putramevaṃ prasūyate ||  
 4.3.2  bījadoṣādyathā sasyaṃ na
      samyak viprarohati[ -rohiṇī] |
       
       mātāpitros tu doṣeṇa tathā garbhaḥ praṇaśyati[ prayaccha] ||  
 4.3.3  tasmāt samyagrasāhārā vṛtukāle[ dṛ-] ' tha
      dampatī |
       
       rahas saṃyogam eyātāṃ smarantau manasā vibhum ||  
 4.3.4  vikṛtāḥ syuragarbhā vai rasāpathyaniṣevaṇe |
       
       sandhāraṇādvā vegānāṃ yonidoṣeṇa vā punaḥ ||  
 4.3.5  yonau doṣopasṛṣṭāyāṃ[ doṣopavṛ-] na garbho hy
      avatiṣṭhate |
       
       tathaiva bāhyayonau[ brāhma]
      hi nirvāhiṇyāṃ[ nirvāhinyāṃ] ca sarvadā ||  
 4.3.6  gṛhṇāti vāyuryasyāṃ ca yonau śukram[ ruśraṃ]
       upāgatam[ upāgataḥ] |
       
       bibharti garbhaṇī garbhaṃ śuddhārtavasamanvitā ||  
 4.3.7  cyavate ca yadā cāsau tadā garbhaḥ praṇaśyati |
       
       vātodaraṃ striyāstadvai tasmā dūkṣāṇi[ dūpā] varjayet ||  
 4.3.8  bhavatyabhyadhike śukle puruṣaḥ śoṇite ' ṅganā |
       
       napuṃsakaṃ tayoḥ sāmye tasmācchuklaṃ vivardhayet ||  
 4.3.9  yadā tu kalalaṃ vāyustad dvidhā kurute balī |
       
       yamau tadā sambhavataḥ kṛṣṇātreyavaco yathā ||  
 4.3.10  tatra śuklottare bhāge pumān raktottare ' ṅganā |
       
       anenaiva ca kalpena yamakeṣv api nirdiśet ||  
 4.3.11  vāyus tv aśvavarāhāṇāṃ deheṣu valavān punaḥ |
       
       sa tatra kalalaṃ bhittvā karoti bahuputratām ||  
 4.3.12  nāpnoti ca yadā garbho rasaṃ duṣṭaiḥ sirāmukhaiḥ |
       
       asaṃpūrṇo vasannāgaḥ tathā varṣāṇi tiṣṭhati ||  
 4.3.13  sampūrṇagātro bhavati yadā sa rasabhāvitaḥ |
       
       tadā sūto[ prasautyathākāśaṃ] yathākālaṃ garbhaḥ
      strīkukṣivicyutaḥ ||  
 4.3.14  ye ca te viṃśatiḥ proktā yonidoṣāś
       cikitsakaiḥ[ cikitsite] |etaiś cānyaiś ca bahubhir garbho
      vyāpadyate striyāḥ ||  
 4.3.15  tasmād etāṃścikitset tu doṣān putracikīrṣayā |
       
 ibhāśvagarbhasārūpyaṃ[ ibhāśvā] prayogāddhi bhavec chuci ||  
 4.3.16  vāyvākāśartuyukto hi daivateṣv itareṣu tu |
       
       antarjāto jātavedāḥ prabhāvāyopakalpate ||  
 4.3.17  ṛtau yadā strīpuruṣau prasannamanasau rahaḥ |
       
       upeyātām atha tadā garbho bhavati sāttvikaḥ ||  
 4.3.18  ṛtau yadā strīpuruṣau vyāyastamanasau bhṛśam |
       
       upeyātām atha tadā garbho bhavati rājasaḥ ||  
 4.3.19  ṛtau yadā strīpuruṣau pradīnamanasau rahaḥ |
       
       upeyātām atha tadā garbho bhavati tāmasaḥ ||  
 4.3.20  lakṣaṇaṃ ca samutthānam ity etat samudāhṛtam |
       
       tisṛṇāṃ sattvayonīnāṃ, miśrāṃstenaiva[ mitrāntenaira] lakṣayet ||
      ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele śārīre tṛtīyo ' dhyāyaḥ || caturtho ' dhyāyaḥ || athātaḥ
      puruṣanicayaṃ śārīraṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 4.4.1  iha khalu bho ayam[ jaya]-annātpuruṣo bhavati
      |
       
 rasajanmāno ' sya[ rajja] vyādhayo bhavanti |
       
       tad yathā khalvayaṃ puruṣo rasajanmā rasajīvī rasajvalano rasasamādhiko
      rasajīvanaś ca bhavati |
       
       rasānāmasamyagupayogānmithyopayogāttadvikārānṛcchati |
       
       na kaścinmithyopayogādajīrṇāpathyabhojanātsvastho bhavati ||  
 4.4.2  athātra praśno bhavati |
       
       ko ' tra khalvasyāhāraṃ pacati vātaḥ pittaṃ śleṣmānupānaṃ veti |
       
       netyāha bhagavān punarvasurātreyaḥ |
       
       yadyete pākahetavaḥ syustarhi na kaścidiha durbalāgniḥ syādvātādīnāṃ
      sannihitatvāt , sānupānatvāc ca |
       
       athāsyoṣmā tejaś ca śarīrasthamāhāraṃ pacataḥ |
       
       te kāyāgnir  iti[ -agne] vidyāt ||  
 4.4.3  tatra bhela ātreyamidamuvāca---bhagavan |
       
       pañcadhā ye śārīrāḥ[ śārīrā] paṭhyante;
      ālocakarājakabhrājakasādhaka- pācakabhedena[ vā]; teṣāṃ katham
       idaṃ[ idāṃ] pañcābhidhāyināṃ pṛthaktvaṃ bhavatīti ||  
 4.4.4  atrovāca bhagavān ātreyaḥ tatrālocako nāma
      varṣaśītātapapravṛddhaḥ |
       
       sa dvividhaḥ |
       
       cakṣurvaiśeṣiko buddhivaiśeṣikaśceti |
       
       cakṣurvaiśeṣiko nāma ya ātmamanasossannikarṣajñānamudīrayitvā citte
      cittamapyādhāya saṃsvedajāṇḍajodbhijjajarāyujānāṃ caturṇāṃ bhūtagrāmāṇāṃ
      lakṣaṇasaṃsthānarūpavarṇasvarair uccāvacānāṃ puṣpaphalapatrāṇāṃ rūpanirvṛty
       arthamekaikasya[ arthamaikekaṃ dvau vā trayo vā] dvayostrayāṇāṃ
      sarveṣāṃ vā yugapatpraṇipatitānāṃ
      cakṣuṣā vaiśeṣyamutpādayatīti[ vaiṣamya] ||  
 4.4.5  buddhivaiśeṣiko nāma yo bhruvormadhye śṛṅgāṭakasthaḥ
      susūkṣmānarthān adhyātmakṛtān gṛhṇāti jñānena, jñeyaṃ jñānaṃ
      kṛtsnajñeyakaivalyārtheṣu darśayati |
       
       tasmād jñānajñeyaṃ jñātvā jñānaṃ gṛhṇāti |
       
       gṛhītaṃ dhārayati |
       
       dhāritaṃ pratyudāharati, atītaṃ smarati, pratyutpannaṃ kṛtvā ' nāgataṃ
      prārthayati, jātamātraś ca punaranupadiṣṭasvabhāvaṃ mātṛstanyamabhilaṣati |
       
       dhyāne pratyāhāre yojanāc ca buddhivaiśeṣyamutpādayatīti ||  
 4.4.6  tatra bhrājako nāma yo hyasya[ yasya] śarīraṃ
      lakṣaṇaṃ copagamayati, prādhānyaṃ pradarśayati,
      śiraḥpāṇipādapārśvapṛṣṭhodarajaṅghāsyanakhanayanakeśānāṃ ca
      pratibhāvṛddhiviśeṣānutpādayati, bhrājayatīti bhrājakaḥ ||  
 4.4.7  prabhaviṣṇutvendriyaprābalyād budhyavasthāhaṃkāreṇa
      vā- abhimatarthamarthebhya[ abhimate] ātmakṛtamādhate |
       
       cakṣuḥśrotraghrāṇarasanasparśanavākpāṇipādapāyūpasthebhyaḥ sarveṣāṃ
      viṣayārthānāṃ svabhāvoparaktānāṃ parasparebhyo rāgamutpādayatīti |
       
       antarmadhye ca pittasthānamantaraṃ praviśya rāgaṃ janayatīti
       rājakaḥ[ rājakam] ||  
 4.4.8  sādhako nāma yaḥ[ yā] śabdasparśagandhebhyo '
      rthakāmebhyaś ca devapitṝṣibhyaś ca iha cāmutrakāṇāṃ ca pādārthānāṃ
      viśreyasama?dhikṛtya sarvapadārthā nāpnoti[ nāṃ nūti] svayuktyā
      sādhayatīti sādhakaḥ ||  
 4.4.9  pācako nāma aśitapītalīḍhakhāditamāhārajātaṃ jātanīryaṃ
       pācayatīti[  - -ca] pācakaḥ |
       
       yaḥ svakaṃ kāmamevāgniṃ prapūrayati harṣayati ||  
 4.4.10  bhavanti cātra--- yo ' yaṃ nirdahati kṣipramāhāraṃ
      sarvadehinām |
       
       apānamadyanidanaḥ? kāyāgniḥ paripaṭhyate[ pariparyate] ||  
 4.4.11 prabhāvalakṣyassaṃyukto[ -lakṣyasati]
      jīvasyeha sanātanaḥ |
       
       nābhimadhye śarīrasya vijñeyaṃ somamaṇḍalam ||  
 4.4.12  somamaṇḍalamadhyasthaṃ vidyāt tat sūryamaṇḍalam |
       
       pradīpavac cāpi nṛṇāṃ tasya madhye hutāśanaḥ ||  
 4.4.13  dehinā bhojanaṃ bhuktaṃ nānāvyañjanasaṃskṛtam |
       
       sūryo divi yathā tiṣṭhan tejoyukto gabhastibhiḥ ||  
 4.4.14  viśoṣayati sarvāṇi palvalāni payāṃsi ca |
       
       tadvaccharīriṇāṃ vyaktaṃ[ bhuktaṃ] jāṭharo nābhisaṃsthitaḥ ||  
 4.4.15  mayūkhaiḥ kṣipramādatte sūryakānto maṇiryathā |
       
       kṣipraṃ samyak pradahati gomayaṃ kāṣṭham eva ca ||  
 4.4.16  sthūlakāyeṣu sattveṣu yavamātrapramāṇataḥ |
       
       hrasvakāyeṣu sattveṣu truṭimātrapramāṇataḥ ||  
 4.4.17  krimikīṭapataṅgeṣu vāyumātro ' vatiṣṭhati |
       
       yastaṃ cikitsetsīdantaṃ[ cikitsiddhantaṃ] vyādhinā cāpi dehinām
      ||  
 4.4.18  āyurvedābhiyogena sa vai kāyacikitsakaḥ |
       
       rasaṃ ca śoṇitaṃ caiva medo māṃsamathāpi ca ||  
 4.4.19  mahatyanaśane nẏṇāṃ sarvāṇy etāni khādati |
       
       agnīṣomātmakaṃ sarvaṃ jagatsthāvarajaṅgamam ||  
 4.4.20  agnīṣomātmakāḥ sarve dehinas tu caturvidhāḥ |
       
       sūryātmakāni sarvāṇi[ cāndrāṇi] tathā somātmakāni ca ||  
 4.4.21  mahatyanaśane nẏṇāṃ tenāntrāṇi sa[ na]
      khādati |
       
       jāṭharo jalasambhūtaḥ pāvakaḥ pavanaissaha ||  
 4.4.22  pradīpyate nṛṇāṃ koṣṭhe sati vendhanapūritaḥ |
       
 ikṣvākukośam[ śoka] āsthāya yathā dīpaḥ sthire ' mbhasi ||  
 4.4.23  tiṣṭhate timire sakto na tathā calite ' mbhasi |
       
       evaṃ śarīriṇāṃ koṣṭhe[ rūṣṭhe] vaikṛtena punaḥ punaḥ ||  
 4.4.24  agnirvaiṣamyamāpnoti pūryamāṇaḥ punaḥ punaḥ |
       
       sa ca yatnena vai rakṣyo vipanne[ vipanno] doṣadarśanāt |
       
 chardyate[ dviyarta] cātisāryeta vikāraṃ cāyamṛcchati ||  
 4.4.25 asāvasamprāptakālo[ śvāsaṃ] ya evaṃ mriyate,
      varṣaśataṃ hi puruṣāyustaccānāptuṃ jīrṇalaghupathyabhojanānuvartinā
      bhavitavyam iti ||  
 4.4.26  tatrāha kasmād 
       alasakaviṣūcikāvān[ -viṣūcikāvasādhyaye vāgavi] sadya evāgadī
      bhavati kaścinmriyata iti?
      atrāha---rūkṣasyādhyaśanena- utpīḍitā[ utpiti]
       vātapittaśleṣmāṇaḥ[ -śleṣmāṇi] ūrdhvamadho vā nānulomā bhavanti,
      udvṛttais tatra taiḥ sadya eva mriyate |
       
       snigdhasyādhyaśamotpīḍitā vātādayaḥ ūrdhvamadho
      vā+ anulomāḥ[ anulomāṃsvāṅgasāṃstu] svāṅgadeśāṃs tu pradadyante,
      tatra taiḥ sadya evāgadī bhavati ||  
 4.4.27  atha daśāntarguhāḥ[ -antahānta], daśa
      bahirguṇāḥ? |
       
       tad yathā---dvicakṣuṣī dvināsike dve śravasī
      kaṇṭhanāḍīgudameḍhravāyusrotāṃsīti[ srotasī kaṇṭhanābhi-] daśa
      antarguhāḥ |
       
       daśa dhamanyo hṛdaye[ hṛdayaṃ] nibaddhā bhavanti |
       
       tāḥ prabhave[ prabhavaṃ] caturaṃgulamātraṃ gatvā viṃśatirbhavanti
      |evam etā daśa dhamanyaḥ ṣaṣṭirbhavanti |
       
       tatra tu bhavanti[ bhavantutrī] trīṇi śatasahasrāṇi
       ṣaṣṭiriyaṃ[ ṣahtaṃśāli] jālāni sirāṇāṃ |
       
       tad yathā--- vṛkṣaḥ[ vṛkṣa] śākhāvṛtaḥ[ śākhāvṛta]
      phalapalāśairavatarati sarvatra |
       
       tad yathā vā hāgo[ hanyo]+ aśmabhir atataḥ[ aśmabhir
      ataraḥ]  tathāyaṃ[ tatāyaṃ] sirābhir avatataḥ |
       
       romakūpe romakūpe[ rūpakūpe] hy asya sirāmukhaṃ bhavati, yataḥ
       svedaḥ[ svetaḥ] kṣaratīti[ kṣiratīti] ||  
 4.4.28  tatrāha kasmād ayaṃ puruṣo na santatamapasmaratīti?
      atrocyate---yathā saritāṃ prādurbhāve vārijāni sattvāni prādurbhavanti hāse vā
      hasanti |
       
       yadā yadā rasavegaṃ prāpnuvanti tadā tadā apasmārayanti |
       
       tasmād dvyahāttryahāt pakṣānmāsāntarāccāpasmarante ||  
 4.4.29  kecidrakṣopahata ity āhuḥ, taccāyuktam |
       
       yadi hyevaṃ syād dṛśyeran puruṣaśarīre prahārādīni vā |
       
 tataśca[ tastaccha] naivam |
       
 vetālābhibhūta[ velāvabhūta] iti cetta cāpy anupapannam |
       
       puṇyāni
      hyeṣāṃ manāṃsi[ vanāṃsi] dhyāyanti[ dhyāyantye] |
       
       yadi caivaṃ kadācidbhavati |
       
       tasmāt tad eva pāṭhyaṃ rasopahatam iti cedevam eva |
       
       rasapravivekakāle tṛtīyakacaturthakāva pi[ va] dṛśyete jvarāvapi
      |neṣatrāṃ hy ananārthaḥ? ||  
 4.4.30  atrāha kiṃ khalvasya[ jalpa] garbhasya
      prathamaṃ sambhavati? hastau[ hastaṃ] pādāviti baḍiśaḥ
      tat pratiṣṭhitatvāt 
      [ pratiṣṭatāt] śarīrasya[ śaīraśva] |
       
       paścād guda iti śaunakaḥ tadāśritatvād vāyoḥ |
       
       nābhir iti khaṇḍakāpyaḥ tatra nāḍīnāṃ pratiṣṭhitatvāt [ pratiṣṭa]
      |
       
       hṛdayam iti parāśaraḥ vijñānamūlakānāṃ tanmūlatvāt |
       
       śira iti bharadvājaḥ śarīrasya tanmūlatvāt |
       
       cakṣuriti kāśyapaḥ |
       
       netyāha bhagavānpunarvasurātreyaḥ |
       
       tasmād arbudamevāsya prathamaṃ sambhavati |
       
       tatra sarve śarīrapradeśāssambhavanti arbudasnehotpannāḥ ||  
 4.4.31 
      atrāha---kiṃ nu[ tu] garbho[ garvo]
       māturudarastho ' śnāti[ māturastho] na veti |
       
       atrocyate nāśnāti |
       
       yadi hy aśnīyāt syād asya[ asyā puruṣa] purīṣamatītakālaṃ, na
       cedamasti[ cedasi] |
       
       kathaṃ tarhi? nābhyāṃ nāḍī pratiṣṭhitā tasyāmaparā māturhṛdayamāśritā tayā
      māturannaraso ' bhivahan garbhaṃ prīṇayatyabhivardhayati |
       
       tad yathā kulyāḥ kedāramabhisaṃśrayantyo bhāvayanti tadvat ||  
 4.4.32  tatrāha kathaṃ garbho māturudare tiṣṭhatīti |
       
       ūrdhvam iti śaunakaḥ |
       
       avākchirā iti bharadvājaḥ |
       
       nety āha bhagavānpunarvasurātreyaḥ |
       
       yady ūrdhvaṃ tiṣṭhet tarhi mātṛghātī syāt |
       
       yady avākchirāḥ svaghātī syāt |
       
       kathaṃ tarhi? tiryak sarvairayamaṅgapratyaṅgaiḥ pratibhugnaḥ śete
      || tasya tadananataraṃ tatprathamaṃ pratipadyate [ sandarbheṇānena
      pratipipādayiṣito ' rthaḥ na spaṣṭaḥ] |
       
       tasmāt tasya śiraḥ prathamaṃ punarvasurātreyaḥ pratipadyate |
       
       tadasya gurutaraṃ bhavatīti |
       
       atha khalu vṛkko medo gururiti saṃpravṛddhau parasparamabhivardhayanti ||  
 4.4.33  tatra ślokaḥ, ūṣmā rasastho dehe ' smiñjīvanaṃ gṛhya
      tiṣṭhati |
       
       rasodbhavaḥ pumāṃstasmād raso jīvanamucyate || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele śārīre caturtho ' dhyāyaḥ || || pañcamo ' dhyāyaḥ || athātaḥ
      śarīranicayaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 4.5.1  iha khalvojastejaḥ śarīre nity e ca[ va]
      bhavataḥ |
       
 tayoḥ[ teyo] sthānāni dvādaśa bhavanti |
       
       tad yathā--- tvakśoṇita[ vaśoṇīta]-māṃsamedo '
      sthimajjāśuklasvedapittaśleṣmamūtrapurīṣāṇīti |
       
       tānyavyāpannāni sukham ity ucyate |
       
 vyāpannaistu[ vyāpannestu] vātapittaśleṣmāṇaḥ praduṣṭā rasādiṣu
      vikārānupajanayanti ||  
 4.5.2  atha yonayaścatasro bhavanti |
       
       tad yathā---jarāyujāṇḍajodbhijjasvedajāśceti |
       
       tatra jarāyujā jarāyuyuktāssaṃbhavanti[ -yu] paśumṛgamanuṣyādayaḥ
      |
       
       śakuna- matsya[ macha]-kacchapa- sarpa[ sarva]-prabhṛtayoṇḍajāḥ
      |
       
       yūkāmat- kuṇa[ kupa]-pataṅgāśiviṣamakṣikādayaḥ svedajāḥ |
       
       udbhijjās tu tṛṇalatāvṛkṣavanaspataya iti ||  
 4.5.3  tatra puṣpaphalavanto vṛkṣāḥ |
       
       apuṣpaphalavanto vanaspatayaḥ |
       
       sapuṣpāḥ saphalāś cāpuṣpāś cāphalāś ca bīrudhaḥ |
       
       phalapākā latāścauṣadhayaḥ |
       
       tatra ye śvetakṣīrāḥ saumyāḥ, raktakṣīrāḥ kādrā vāruṇā vāligrahā? iti ||  
 4.5.4  iha khalu triṣu daśarātreṣu pumān rasena saṃyujyate |
       
       āsāṃ tu khalu catasṛṇāṃ yonīnāṃ ṛtukāle yadā rasāḥ samyak prāptiṃ vā
      gacchanti tadā garbhaḥ tiṣṭhaty[ tiṣṭe] avikṛtaḥ viparyaye
      viparyayaḥ ||  
 4.5.5 tryahantu[ -ha] khalu purāṇarudhiraṃ
      parivarjayet |
       
       kiñ ca tatpurāṇam? yadāditastryahaṃ parisravadṛtukāle tatpurāṇam |
       
       tasmin tryahe garbha- upakramaṇe[ upakrameṇa] na tiṣṭhati |
       
 avasthito[ avasthi vā] vā nāyuṣi samartho bhavati |
       
 nirgate[ nirgave] tu tryaheṇa purāṇe
      rudhire cāvasthite[ ṇa]
      śuddhasnātāyāścaturthaṣaṣṭha- aṣṭama[ aṣṭa]-daśama- dvādaśeṣu[ dvādaśamu]
      ahassu garbhovakramamāṇaḥ pumān bhavati |
       
       pañcamasaptama- navamaikādaśeṣu[ -navaikādaśu] strītvāyopakalpate
      |sa eṣa āsaptarātrātsarvasañcāro ' bhidadhatyataḥ paramasañcārovakṛtatvād 
      vālpāt? ||  
 4.5.6  strīṇāṃ khalu śoṇitaṃ śarīraṃ śoṣayati tasmānna tāḥ rajaḥ
      paśyanti |
       
       paripūrṇadhātuśarīrās tu yadā bhavanti tadā vivekajalalohitaṃ māse māse
      prativedayanti |
       
       pratigatapraveśaṃ ca tatpunarmāsena samāgacchatyārtavam ||  
 4.5.7  yadā tu tacchoṇitaṃ duṣṭaṃ mārgaṃ pratipadyate tadā
      strīṇāṃ pradaro bhavati |
       
       taṃ śarīraṃ śoṣayantaṃ[ śoṣaya] lohitapittabheṣajenopakrameta ||  
 4.5.8  garbhiṇyās tu tridhā kāye raso ' bhinirvartate,
       garbhatvāya[ garbhātpā] stanyatvāya rasatvāya ceti ||  
 4.5.9  iha khalu bhoḥ
       garbhātsthirādantaḥsthādāyatamudaraṃ[ -sthitāvasthātamā] bhavati
      madhye nāryāmantargatāyām |
       
       sthūlamūlasaṃsthitasaṃvṛttamacchidraṃ puruṣo ' ntargate |
       
 droṇīvodaraṃ[ droṇicodaraṃ] bhavatyubhayor antargatayoḥ |
       
       vāmaṃ pārśvamāyataṃ māturudarasthā strī, dakṣiṇe pumān, madhye napuṃsakam |
       
       vāmamakṣi hrasati nāryāmantargatāyām, puruṣe dakṣiṇam, ubhe napuṃsake |
       
       savyaṃ pādaṃ pūrvaṃ prakrāmati savyena cākṣṇā bhruvā ca pūrvaṃ prati kurute,
      ceṣṭate ca[ na] savyena[ sarvena] pārśvena prāyaḥ
       saṃviśati[ śaṃsate] strīsaṃjñāneṣu ca prāyaśo dauhṛdaṃ kurute
      nāryāmantargatāyām |
       
       viparyaye tadataḥ puruṣaṃ bibhartīti vidyāt ||  
 4.5.10  atha iha[ ye] khalu garbhasya ṣaḍbhyaḥ
      sthānebhyaḥ śarīramabhinirvartate |
       
       tad yathā---jalakāyād vāyukāyāt tejaḥkāyāt pṛthivīkāyād ākāśakāyād rasakāyāc
      ceti ||  
 4.5.11  ṣaḍdhātur evāyaṃ puruṣo bhavati |
       
       dhātavaḥ punaḥ pañca bhūtāni brahma yadavyaktam[ padavyaktam] ||  
 4.5.12  tatra yat kharakaṭhinam, tad
      yathā---dantakeśaroma- nakha[ mukha]-purīṣasnāyvasthi,
      gandhajñānaghrāṇasaṅghātagauravāṇīti |
       
       yad dravaṃ snigdhaṃ mṛdu vā tadaudakam ||  
 4.5.13 tadyadā[ tadyamu] sannipatitayor yatra
      puruṣaḥ  pūrvamarthaṃ[ sarvamardha] nandayati jaghanyaṃ strī tatra
       pumānihāṅgapratyaṅgaiḥ[ pumānipratyaṅgaiḥ] sadṛśo jāyate |
       
       yatra tu strī prathamamarthaṃ sādhayati jaghanyaṃ puruṣaḥ, tatra strī
      vāṅgapratyaṅgais sadṛśī[ sadṛśo] jāyate ||  
 4.5.14  atha strīpuruṣāvṛtukāle[ -nāle] rūkṣāṇi
       vātalānyannāni[ vātaśānyannāni] sevete, vegāṃś ca dhārayataḥ,
      tayor garbhaḥ śoṇitādiṣu vātasaṃdūṣiteṣu niḥsṛto[ viḥsṛto]
      bhavati, gadgadabādhiryaminmiṇatvamanyeṣāṃ ca vātapittavikārāṇāmanyatamaṃ
      prāpnoti |
       
       evam eva pittaśleṣmalānṛtukāle mātāpitroḥ sevamānayoḥ pittaśleṣmavidūṣito
      garbhaḥ sambhavati ||  
 4.5.15  atha khalu garbhaśarīraṃ catrudaśendriyakāyāḥ
      samanupraviśanti |
       
       vidhṛtāś cānupalabhyamānāś ca saptadivyāḥ saptamānuṣāḥ ||  
 4.5.16  tatra divyāḥ
       brahmadeva[ brahmadevataṃ]-varuṇagandharvapiśācāsuramahārajakāyā
      bhavanti |
       
       tān vyākhyāsyāmaḥ |
       
       tatra yaḥ satyārjavānṛśaṃsakṣamādam- adhyāna[ advāyāna]-sampanno
      'dhyātmatattvadarśī bhavati taṃ brahmakāyam iti vidyāt ||  
 4.5.17  yastādyaśīlopādānayadyatraiyavān? muditastaṃ deva kāyam
      iti vidyāt ||  
 4.5.18  yo yajñananditarāgadṛṣṭiḥ salilapriyaścirasnāyī piṅgākṣaḥ
      kapilakeśaḥ saṃbhavati taṃ varuṇakāyam iti vidyāt ||  
 4.5.19  yas tu priyanṛtyagītavāditraḥ strīvihāranity aḥ
      śucivastragandhamālyānulepanaratir bhavati taṃ gandharvakāyām iti vidyāt ||  
 4.5.20  yas tu priyamadyamāṃsamatsyas tathā gomahāśano bībhatso
      bālānāṃ bhīṣayitā nidrābahulaś ca bhavati taṃ piśācakāyam iti vidyāt ||  
 4.5.21 yas tvāt magurūṇāṃ[ -gu] mānayitā paścād
      dveṣī caṇḍaḥ krodhano jñātīnāṃ bhedako bhavati tamāsuraṃ kāyam iti vidyāt ||  
 4.5.22  yas tu dhīraḥ śūraḥ mahābhogo mahotsāho mahaiśvaryaś ca
      bhavati taṃ mahārājakāyam iti vidyāt ||  
 4.5.23  anurāgeṇa mānuṣās tu
      pratyātmadarśanaśravaṇasparśanarasanaghrāṇasukhaduḥkham iti tatpravidyāsahitāḥ
      kevalāś cāvatiṣṭhante kārtsnyena |tairanvito janturliṅgati nimiṣati ākuṃcati
      prasārayati vedyaṃ vedayate ||  
 4.5.24 sa[ na] yadā bhedaṃ gacchati
       tadāyamantataḥ[ tathāyaḥ antaḥ kāyam eva yānti] jalaṃ jalakāyam
      eva yāti, vāyurvāyukāyaṃ, tejaḥ tejaḥkāyaṃ, pṛthivī pṛthivīkāyaṃ,
      ākāśamākāśakāyam iti |
       
 yathākāyam[ dāyam]- indriyakāyaṃ[ -kālaṃ] bhajate ||  
 4.5.25  bhavati cātra--- vidyamāne śarīre vai dhāturdhātuṃ
      niyacchati |
       
       mano buddhiś ca sarveṣāṃ brahmaṇi pratitiṣṭhati || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele śārīre pañcamo ' dhyāyaḥ || || ṣaṣṭho ' dhyāyaḥ || athātaḥ
      khaḍḍikāṃ garbhāvakrāntiṃ śārīraṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 4.6.1  iha khalu bho mātṛjaś cāyaṃ garbhaḥ pitṛjaś cātmajaś ca
      sātmyajaś ca rasajaś ca |
       
       asti ca sattvam aupapādakam[ aupavādakam] ity ātreyavacanam |
       
       neti bharadvājaḥ |
       
       amātṛjaś cāyaṃ garbhaḥ apitṛjaś
      cānātmajaśca- asātmyajaś[ anātmajaś] cārasajaś ca |
       
       nāsti ca sattvam aupapādakam[ aupavādhikam] iti |
       
       yadi hi mātā putraṃ janyet bhūyiṣṭhaṃ hi strī putrakāmā maithunavargamabhis
      andhāya putraṃ janayet strīkāmā ca striyam ||  
 4.6.2 yadā[ -vi] jīven a saha sūkṣmāvagnimārutau
      garbhaṃ viśataḥ tadā[ -va] dvāvetāvaṅgapratyaṅgāni vikurutaḥ,tau
       ceṣṭayataḥ[ ceṣṭataḥ], tau vardhayataḥ, tāveva yadā śarīrād
      vyavakrāmataḥ tadā tadbhavati nirvāto nirūṣmā preto mṛta iti |
       
       netyāha bharadvājaḥ |
       
       mṛto ' pi jantuḥ vāyunādhmāṣyate, agninā śoṣyate |
       
       netyāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       saha vā tasyāgnimārutau jīvayataḥ, tayor  apakrāntayor 
      [ apakrāntayor vātya] bahyāgnimārutāvāviśata iti ||  
 4.6.3  yatpunarāḥ sati ca bhūtanānātve[ bhūtarnātve]
      kathamekaḥ syāditi? atrocyate |
       
       yatraitannānātvamāśritaṃ tadetadavyaktamasti pañcamahābhūtasaṃgraha iti ||  
 4.6.4  yatpunarāha yadyavyaktaṃ sarvaṃ syādavikāraḥ syād
      iti[ ya---sa vivasyādadhi], atrocyate |
       
       vātapittaśleṣmakṛtā rasasamutthā asya vyaktāḥ procyante vikārāḥ, avyakte
      hyukte  te[ rute] vyaktāḥ kathamavyaktaṃ srakṣyanti, kathaṃ
      tarhi śarīre tadvikriyate, unmādaḥ kathamavyaktaṃ
      manaḥ spṛśatīty[ spṛśatithena] etaccānupapannam |
       
       kiṃ tarhi yathādity assambhūto ' pi meghāntarito[ memāmtarito] na
      prakāśam upajanayati tathā[ ---] mano ' ntarhiteṣu vijñānasrotassu
      tamasā smṛtiṃ nopajanayatīti ||  
 4.6.5  yatpunarāḥ yadyayaṃ paralokād garbho '
      vakrāmennāsya[ garma ukta] kiñcittatrādṛṣṭaṃ syāditi, atrocyate |
       
       iha tāvadayaṃ cirotsṛṣṭāni vijñānāni vividhāni cāścaryabhūtāni na smarati kiṃ
      punardehāntarāṇi bhūtāni bhāvaviśeṣā- antarāṇi[ ---] ||  
 4.6.6  tatra ślokaḥ--- tamasā bhāvito yo vai saṃsmarenna sa
      mānavaḥ |
       
       saṃsmaretpūrvacaritaṃ sukṛte vedavad[ vedavidṛja] dvijaḥ || ity 
      āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele śārīre ṣaṣṭho ' dhyāyaḥ || || saptamo ' dhyāyaḥ || athātaḥ
      śarīrasaṃkhyāśārīraṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 4.7.1  iha khalu śarīre ṣaṭ tvaco bhavanti |
       
       udakadharā prathamā ' sṛgdharā
      dvitīyā, sidhmakilāsasaṃbhava[ maṃ] adhiṣṭhānā tṛtīyā,
      dadrukuṣṭhasambhavādhiṣṭhānā caturthī, alajīvidridhisambhavādhiṣṭhānā pañcamī,
      ṣaṣṭhī tu yasyāṃ chinnāyāmuttāmyati timiramivānupraviśati duṣṭāruṣkāṇi cāsya
      yāmāśrity a jāyante iti ||  
 4.7.2  asthigaṇanā---trīṇi saṣaṣṭīni[ saṣaṣṭhiṇi
      śavā] śatānyasthnāṃ tad yathā---dvātriṃśaddantāḥ, dvātriṃśaddantolūkhalāni,
       viṃśatirnakhāḥ[ paṇipādaśalānānyaṅgulyasthīni], ṣaṣṭiḥ
      pāṇipādāṅgulyasthīni, viṃśatiḥ pāṇipādaśalākāḥ, catvāri
      pāṇīpādaśalākādhiṣṭhānāni, dve pārṣṇyor asthinī[ pārṣorasthīni],
      catvāraḥ pādayoḥ gulphāḥ, dvau maṇikau, māṇike dve
      hastayoḥ, catvāryaratnyor asthīni[ catvāryaśayo], dve jaṅghayoḥ,
      dve jānunī, dve jānukapālike,
       dvāvūrunalakau[ dāvūrudvāvūrunaśaktau], dvāvaṃsau, dve
      aṃsaphalake, dvāvakṣakau, ekaṃ jatru, dve tālunī, dve cibuke, dve
      śroṇiphalake, ekaṃ bhagāsthi,
      pañcacatvāriṃśat pṛṣṭhagatānyasthīni[ pṛṣṭhagatau dhṛsthini],
      pañcadaśa grīvāyām, caturdaśorasi, caturviṃśatiḥ parśukāḥ pārśvayoḥ,
       tāvanti[ yāvanti] caiva sthālakāni, tāvanti caiva
      sthālakārbudakāni, ekaṃ hanvasthi, dve hanubandhane, ekaṃ
      nāsāsthi- hanu[ tathā hanu]-kūṭalalāṭam, catvāri śīrṣakapālāni ||  
 4.7.3  hṛdayamekaṃ cetanāyatanam |
       
       daśa prāṇāyatanāni tad yathā---mūrdhā kaṇṭho hṛdayaṃ gudo nābhir vastirojaḥ
      śauklaṃ śoṇitaṃ māṃsam iti ||  
 4.7.4  pañcadaśa koṣṭhāṅgāni[ koṣṭhāni] |
       
       tad yathā---nābhiś ca hṛdayaṃ ca kloma ca yakṛc ca plīhā ca vṛkkau ca vastiś
      ca purīṣādhānaṃ cāmāśayaścottaragudaś cādharagudaś ca kṣudrāntraṃ ca
      sthūlāntraṃ ca vapāvahanaṃ ceti ||  
 4.7.5  ṣaṭpañcāśatpratyaṅgāni tad yathā---dvau gulphau, dve
      nitambe, dve jaṅghe, dve piṇḍike, dve ūrupiṇḍike, dvau sphicau, dvau vṛṣaṇau,
      ekaṃ śephaḥ, dvau śaṅkhau, dvau baṅkṣṇau, dvau kukundarau, eko vastiḥ,
      śīrṣamekamudaramekam, dvau stanau, dvau bāhū, dvāṃvasakau, ekaṃ cubukaṃ,
      dvāvoṣṭhau, dve dantaveṣṭe, dve  sṛkvaṇī[ sṛkvaṇīti], ekaṃ tālu,
      galaśuṇḍikā ekā, dvau karṇau, dve karṇaśaṣkulike, dvau gaṇḍau, dve akṣikūṭe,
      catvāryakṣivartmāni, dve  akṣiṇī[ akṣiṇīti] iti ||  
 4.7.6  śarīradravyāṇī---daśodakasyāñjalayaḥ śarīre pracyavamānaṃ
      purīṣamanubadhvātyatiyoge, navāñjalayaḥ pūrvasyāhārapariṇāmadhātoryantaṃ rasa
      ity  ācakṣate[ ācakṣati] kuśalāḥ, aṣṭau śoṇitasya, sapta
      purīṣasya, catvāro mūtrasya, dvau medasaḥ, eko majjñaḥ, mastiṣkasyāñjaliḥ
      śuklasya ceti ||  
 4.7.7  athātra praśno bhavati---
      katamayaṃ jīvo[ devo] dehāddehāntaram upakramata iti? atrovāca
      bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       jalūkāyā ivāsya kecidgatiṃ bruvate |
       
       tanna yuktam |
       
       iha vyaktyantāmūrtaṃ yugapatsyādevāpare ' pyevamicchanti |
       
       sarvathāpi mumukṣorasyāyamantarātmā param upakramata iti sarvathāpyasmin
      parity akte paricaye tāvadasaṃprāptaṃ tarā syāt |
       
       avasthānatvāccettadiṣṭaṃ karmaṇopyevaṃ bhavati vaiyyarthyam api tu khalu
      pratiśrutyāpahitaḥ paratra gamanaṃ tasya vidyāt |
       
       athavā yathādity asya hṛdaye bhūmau raśmayaḥ pratitiṣṭhante |
       
       vilambitāvevamatasya tatra gamanamanupaścediti |
       
       |
       
 
 4.7.8  atha khalu puruṣe[ puruṣā] ṣoḍaśādhyātmadevatā
      bhavanti |
       
       tad yathā---agniś ca pṛthivī cāpaś cākāśaś ca vāyuś ca vidyuc ca parjanyaś ca
       indraśca[ -ga] gandharvaś ca mṛtyuś cādity aś ca candramāś ca
       tvaṣṭā[ tṛṣṇā] ca viṣṇuś ca prajāpatiś ca brahmā ceti |
       
       tāḥ karmabhir vidyādutpattitaś ca parimāṇataś ca vidyāt |
       
       ūṣmā hy atrāagneś[ -gniś] ca karma dehe |
       
       ghrāṇaṃ ca pṛthivyāḥ, sneho raso jñānaṃ codakasya, sparśanaṃ vāyoḥ, śrotraṃ
      cākāśasya, rūpādānaṃ parjanyasya saṃvegādānāni vidyutaḥ, balamindrasya, kāmo
      gandharvāṇāṃ, kopo mṛtyoḥ, cakṣurādity asya, prasādaścandramasaḥ, rūpaṃ
      tvaṣṭuḥ, ceṣṭā viṣṇoḥ, vyavāyaḥ prajāpateḥ, buddhirbrahmaṇa iti ||  
 4.7.9  tatra ślokaḥ--- viśuddhanetrāstapaso munayaḥ śāntakalmaṣāḥ
      |
       
       jagataścopapannāṃś ca sarvān[ svarbhā] paśyanti mānavān || ity 
      āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele śārīre saptamo ' dhyāyaḥ || || aṣṭamo ' dhyāyaḥ || athāto
      jātisūtrīyaṃ śārīraṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 4.8.1  iha khalu bhoḥ yāḥ striyaḥ pathyalaghubhojinyo '
      nudāvartanaśīlā apraduṣṭā yathāgarbhāśayāḥ suviśuddhasrotaso bhavanti, tā
      ācakṣate avandhyāḥ iti kuśalāḥ |
       
       tā iṣṭarūpaṃ medhāvi cāpatyaṃ janayanti, viparyaye viparyayaḥ ||  
 4.8.2  ṛtau ca garbho ' vatiṣṭhate |
       
       tad yathā---sukṛṣṭakṣetre bījaṃ prakṣiptaṃ tatra vrīhiḥ vrīhitvāya kalpate,
      yavo yavatvāya evam eva[ priya] indriyamṛtukāle
       visṛṣṭamaduṣṭāyāṃ[ -māmaṭṭa] yonau garbhāśayam upagacchati |
       
 tad yathā[ tad yathāya]---āvartagṛhītāḥ pratīpaṃ pratidhāvanti
      tadvat śuklaśoṇitaṃ garbhāśaye[ garbhāśaya astikaṃ] āsiktaṃ
      kṣīramiva |
       
 taccānekakanakamiva[ taṃ cānekanakamivo]-udumbareṇa
      niṣiktamekatvamāpannamṛddhiṃ labhate ||  
 4.8.3  sā ced evamākāṅkṣetaudvāhike[ evayā kāṃkṣā-]
      śivāvadātaputraṃ janayeyam[ janayanti] iti, yavānāṃ
       manthaṃ[ mandaṃ] sarpissamyuktaṃ saptarātramanupahataṃ bhuñjīta |
       
       tato dauhṛdinī[ dauhṛtdvi] śvetāyā goḥ sarūpavatsāyāḥ payasi
      pāyasaṃ pācayitvā tadevāśnīyāt [ -atmīyāt] |
       
       śukle ca vāsasī paridadhyāt [ parirabhyāt] |
       
       sarvaśvetaṃ cāsyāḥ saṃskṛtaṃ vimānaṃ kārayet |
       
 vṛṣabhamaśvaṃ[ vṛṣabhagaga] vāsyā darśayet |
       
       evamavadātaṃ putraṃ janayet |
       
       netyāha śaunakaḥ |
       
       paiṅgalyaṃ vā tato ' pyatreti |
       
       ātreya uvāca kiṃ syādāvādhakam, piṅgalāvayavayā āyuṣmanto nīrogāś ca
      bhavantīti ||  
 4.8.4  sā cedevam[ iti
      hā] āśāsīta[ āsita] śyāmaṃ lohitākṣaṃ
      putraṃ janayeyam[ jana yetre yāvat dvitīye māsapuṣpaṃ paśyet
      yamiti] iti eṣāmeva[ eṣāma] yavānāṃ manthaṃ[ mandaṃ]
      kārayet lohitakukkuṭaraktena saptarātraṃ raktaśālīnāmodanamanupahataṃ bhuñjīta
      |
       
       dauhṛde sā tāmreṇa ca vāsasā paridadhyāt |
       
       tāmre cāsyāḥ śayanāsane dadyād raktavṛṣamaśvaṃ[ -vṛṣamadaṃ] vāsyā
      darśayet |
       
       evaṃ śyāmaṃ lohitākṣaṃ putraṃ janayati ||  
 4.8.5 yā[ yāvad] vi dvitīyamāsi puṣpaṃ paśyenna
       vāsyā[ va] garbhastiṣṭhatīti vidyādajāta sārā[ nā] hi
      tadā garbhavatyo bhavanti |
       
 yasyāstu[ tasyāstu] khalu yoniḥ[ yoni] jātasāre
      puṣpam  āsravati[ āśraya] tasyāḥ
      patati vāpyatikālaṃ[ vāpity a-] vā ' vatiṣṭhate gabhaḥ
      pariśuṣkagātra iti ||  
 4.8.6  caturthe khalu māse prativihite kṣīre navanītaṃ prāśnīyāt
      |
       
       pañcame kṣīrayavāgūḥ, ṣaṣṭhe kṣīrasarpiḥ, saptame dadhyudaśvit, aṣṭame
      kṣīrasarpiḥ, navame tu khalu māse prativihite
       madhurauṣadhasiddhena[ kadambamāṣṭerāghataitānuvāsa]
      tailenānuvāsaḥ ||  
 4.8.7  evaṃ hy asyāḥ pratimāsaṃ[ pratisaṃvartamānāyā
      yacchatanmataṃ] vartamānāyāḥ kukṣīkaṭīpārśvapṛṣṭhaṃ mṛdūbhavati jīrṇapurīṣaṃ
      cādhaḥ travetsukhaṃ ca prajāyate ||  
 4.8.8  saptame tu khalu māse garbhaprapīḍitā
       vātapittaśleṣmāṇa[ -śleṣmāṇo] uraḥ prāpya
       savidāhaṃ[ vidahyamānāḥ] kaṇḍūṃ janayanti |tena kikkisāni jāyante
      strīṇām |
       
       triphalācūrṇaṃ śaśarudhireṇa piṣṭvā tenāsyāḥ tānyālepayet ||  
 4.8.9  aṣṭame tu khalu māse prativihite sati sūkikāgāraṃ samyak
      prāgdvāramudakdvāraṃ vā kārayet
      tinduka- palāśa[ phalāśa]-aśvatthaiḥ |
       
       | 
 4.8.10  athātra pūrvasaṃkalpitāḥ syuḥ dvau khalu bilvamayau
      paryaṅkau śūrpau ca dvau taṇḍulamusalau
      gaṇḍopadhānaṃ yavāgūḥ[ mayau] sarpiś ca tailaṃ ca sarṣapāśceti ||  
 4.8.11  athaināṃ prajanayiṣyatīti yavāgūṃ pāyayet |
       
       anāgatagarbhaved anāṃ caināmavahananaṃ ca kārayet |
       
       sā yadi jānīyādavabhraṣṭo me kukṣiḥ pravimukto me hṛdgarbhaḥ prasrutā me
      yoniriti, athainām
      upakārikalpitanakhāścatasra upajīvikāḥ[ upajīvā] pratidinam
      upatiṣṭheyuḥ |
       
       śanaiḥ pūrvaṃ pravāhetapaścād[ pravāhetatpaścād] balavattaram iti
      |na cāpy anāgatavegā vā bāliśatayā[ bābāhūhli(?)tatayādyā],
      anāgatavegā hi  duḥkhāyātmānaṃ[ tanā duḥkhā] prayacchati saha
      putreṇa ||  
 4.8.12  tasyāścet prajātāyā[ prajātāyāparānapra]
      aparā na prapadyate, tadaināṃ
      raktaśālīnāmakṣamātraṃ kalkamamlena[ kalpya]
       mūtreṇa[ mūtreṇa(?)] vā pāyayet |
       
       etenaiva kalpena dantīdravantīvṛścikālīvunarnavāvanaśīrṣākaṃ kārayet |
       
 tathā[ talau]-umākāla- sarpa[ sarva]-purāṇamālānām
      anyatamena dhūpayet |
       
       sā cedanena vidhinā na pravartate athaināṃ
      tīkṣṇaphala- tailena[ taire]-anuvāsayet  ||
      [ ayamadhyāyaḥ mātukāyāmardhe vicchinno dṛśyate |] |.. |.. |.. |.. |..
      |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. iti bhele
      śārīre ' ṣṭame ' dhyāyaḥ || iti bhelasaṃhitāyāṃ, śārīrasthānaṃ samāptam || ||
      indriyasthānaḥ || || prathamo ' dhyāyaḥ || -----------------------------------

 5.1.1  hrasvaikapakṣo vitato yas tu garbhas tu susvaraḥ |
       
       māsamekaṃ tu jīvitvā vināśāyopapadyate ||  
 5.1.2  piṇḍīśirā dīrghahanuranalpe saṃhate bhruvau |
       
       dvitīye māsi saṃprāpte mriyate garbha īdṛśaḥ ||  
 5.1.3  jātamātrasya garbhasya vyañjanaṃ yatra dṛśyate |
       
       tṛtīye māsi saṃprāpte mriyate garbha īdṛśaḥ ||  
 5.1.4  trikekaro ghaṭaśirā yas tu garbhas tu susvaraḥ |
       
       caturthe māsi saṃprāpte vināśam upagacchati ||  
 5.1.5  yasya ṣoḍaśavarśasya vyañjanaṃ tūpajāyate |
       
       śīghraṃ ca pañcadhātutvād alpāyuriha dṛśyate ||  
 5.1.6  yasya viṃśativarṣasya vyañjanaṃ tūpajāyate |
       
       sa dīrghamāyurāpnoti puruṣo nātra saṃśayaḥ ||  
 5.1.7  śarīrāpacayo ' buddhirapathyāni balaṃ tathā |
       
       bālasya yasya dṛśyante taṃ gatāyuṣamādiśet ||  
 5.1.8  yasya jātasya jāyete gulmakāstunakau tathā |
       
       aṣṭāviṃśe gate varṣe sarvaṃ taṃ hanti mānavam ||  
 5.1.9 pṛṣṭhe corasi cāvartassavyatho yas tu dṛśyate
      |
       
       catvāriṃśe gate varṣe maraṇāyopakalpate ||  
 5.1.10 āvarto yaś ca pṛṣṭhe tu sannatastriṣu dṛśyate
      |
       
       phalamasya tu vijñeyaṃ sthāpanaṃ na prasūyate ||  
 5.1.11  sthūlāsthūlāṅgulī pāṇī nakhā yasyāpi lohitāḥ |
       
 kalyāṇadeśapratyaṅgaḥ pañcāśadvarṣa eva ca ||  
 5.1.12  vyūṭhorasko dīrghabhujaḥ sthūlajānuś ca yo bhavet |
       
       dīrghāṅgulirdīrghanakhaḥ ṣaṣṭi varṣāṇi jīvati ||  
 5.1.13  utpīḍitasvaraṃ vāpi tuṅganāsakaconmukham |
       
       ūrukaṃ bhadrasampannaṃ vidyāt saptatikaṃ naraḥ ||  
 5.1.14  bhadraṃ puraś ca paś cāc ca ṛjukaṃ priyavādinam |
       
       aśītikaṃ naraṃ vidyāt kṛṣṇātreyavaco yathā ||  
 5.1.15  lalāṭaṃ nāsikā karṇau yasyaitāni pṛthak pṛthak |
       
       ṣaḍaṅgulapramāṇāni sa jīvati śataṃ samāḥ ||  
 5.1.16  yasyākuñcitam eva syājjānubhyāṃ samitaṃ śiraḥ |
       
       ūrdhvajānugatau karṇau pautraṃ paśyatyayaṃ naraḥ ||  
 5.1.17  mahāntau vipulau karṇau bhavetāṃ romaśau tathā |
       
       snigdhau bahulakeśaś ca sa ceha śatamṛcchati ||  
 5.1.18  dharmeṇa satyavākyena guruśuśrūṣaṇena ca |
       
       rasāyanopayogāc ca sa dīrghamanujīvati || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele indriye prathamo ' dhyāyaḥ || || dvitīyo ' dhyāyaḥ ||  
 
 
 5.2.1  mukhaṃ netre śarīraṃ ca pāṇipādaṃ tathaiva ca |
       
       saraktaṃ dṛśyate yasya sa vai svastho bhaviṣyati || 5| 
 2.2.  yasya gomayacūrṇābhaṃ narāṇāṃ mūrdhni dṛśyate |
       
       śirasi snihyamāne ca kaṇḍūssaṃjāyate dṛḍham ||  
 5.2.3  yasya keśāḥ pramucyante śīrṇamūlāḥ śarīriṇaḥ |
       
       yasyaitāni tu rūpāṇi sa vai svastho bhaviṣyati ||  
 5.2.4  nāsya dantāḥ prahṛṣyanti mukhaṃ ca na vilupyati |
       
       nābaddhaṃ bhāṣate cāpi sa vai svastho bhaviṣyati ||  
 5.2.5  na vikṣipati gātrāṇi svaro ' sya na vivartate |
       
       vastreṇa gūhate guhyaṃ sa vai svastho bhaviṣyati ||  
 5.2.6  na bhavatyunnato nābhir yathāvastho ' bhitiṣṭhati |
       
       sukhaṃ śvasiti rātrau ca sa vai svastho bhaviṣyati ||  
 5.2.7  na nakhāḥ karkaśābhāsā na śyāvā na ca niṣprabhāḥ |
       
       prasannāssuprabhāś caiva sa vai svastho bhaviṣyati || Bhṣ5.2.8? |
       
       ātapādhiṣṭhito yas tu na |.. prakāśace |
       
       na ca lohitasaṃyu 
  || tṛtīyo ' dhyāyaḥ ||  
  Bhṣ5.3.? |
       
       |...dhitasvapne tāṃ rātriṃ nātivartate ||  
 
 
 5.3.1  iyaṃ me śiṣṭaśibikā vaiḍūryamaṇiyantritā |
       
       evaṃ pralāpayeccārto gatāyuriti taṃ viduḥ ||  
 5.3.2  prajvalaty api yo dīpe tama evābhipaśyati |
       
       ( śabdānvipratibudhyeta cāpūrvāniva nāsti saḥ) ||  
 5.3.3  āvākśirāḥ pralambāmi nāma mā parivartaya |
       
 manujaḥ pralapannevaṃ saptāhaṃ nātivartate ||  
 5.3.4 marmāṇi dalitānīva yo ' bhīkṣṇaṃ cātisāryate |
       
       pravāhamāṇo durgandhi kuṇapaṃ pūtikaṃ tathā ||  
 5.3.5  tac ca lohitagandhaṃ vāpy athavā matsyagandhikam |
       
       kṛṣṇaṃ nīlaṃ vivarṇaṃ vā mumūrṣuś ca sa hocyate ||  
 5.3.6  madhumehī vasāmehī sarpirmehī ca yo naraḥ |
       
       bahumehī ca yo jantuḥ sa vai proktaḥ parāsukaḥ ||  
 5.3.7  prameheta yadā janturbinduṃ binduṃ savedanam |
       
       vāyunā bhinnavastiḥ syād durlabhaṃ tasya jīvitam ||  
 5.3.8  krimayo bahavo yasya nissaranti śarīriṇaḥ |
       
       āturasya śayānasya nauṣadhaṃ tasya sidhyati ||  
 5.3.9  ity etāni bhiṣak dṛṣṭvā lakṣaṇāni mumūrṣatām |
       
       na cikitsāṃ prayuñjīta yathāmārgaṃ cikīrṣakaḥ || ity āha bhagavān
      ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele indriye tṛtīyo ' dhyāyaḥ || || caturtho ' dhyāyaḥ ||  
 
 
 5.4.1  yadāturasya hṛdayaṃ vāyuḥ saṃgṛhya tiṣṭhati |
       
 dhamanīssaṃparīpīḍya sadyo jahyāt sa jīvitam |
       
 
 5.4.2  āturasya yadā vāyuḥ śarīramanupadyate |
       
       uttāne netraniṣyandaḥ sadyo jahyāt sa jīvitam ||  
 5.4.3  yasya koṣṭhagato vāyurupāvṛttaśśarīriṇaḥ |
       
       kṣīṇalohitamāṃsasya sadyo jahyāt sa jīvitam ||  
 5.4.4  yasyāturasyeha vātād vātāṣṭhīlā vivardhate |
       
       na saṃsarati cānyatra sadyaḥ prāṇān jahāti saḥ ||  
 5.4.5  yasyobhe piṇḍike stabdhe nāsā jihmā ca lakṣyate |
       
       vyāvṛtte cākṣiṇī yasya sadyaḥ prāṇān jahāti saḥ ||  
 5.4.6  āmāśayasamutthānā yasyaiva parikartikā |
       
       tṛṣṇā ca tīvrarāgaś ca sadyaḥ prāṇān jahāti saḥ ||  
 5.4.7  pakvāśayasamutthānā yasya syāt parikartikā |
       
       tṛṣṇā galagrahaścograḥ sadyo jahyāt sa jīvitam ||  
 5.4.8  śoṇitaṃ romakūpebhyo yasya kṣarati dehinaḥ |
       
       atīva mukhato bhedi sadyo jahyāt sa jīvitam ||  
 5.4.9  hṛdayasya tu saṃghātaṃ parikṣīṇasya dehinaḥ |
       
       atyarthaṃ pīḍayecchūlaṃ sadyaḥ prāṇān jahāti saḥ ||  
 5.4.10  yasya kṣīṇaśarīrasya saṃjñāṃ harati mārutaḥ |
       
       vyāhanti ca mahāsrotaḥ sadyaḥ prāṇān jahāti saḥ ||  
 5.4.11  hṛdayasya tu saṃghātaṃ parikṣīṇasya dehinaḥ |
       
       etair eva ṃvidhairliṅgairanyaiś cāpi tathāvidhaiḥ || prakṛtervikṛtiṃ
      prāptaṃ parīkṣetāturaṃ bhiṣak |
       
       ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele indriye caturtho ' dhyāyaḥ || || pañcamo ' dhyāyaḥ || athāto
      yasyaśyāvīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 5.5.1  yasya śyāve ume netre dṛśyete harite tathā |
       
       utpannaś ca śirorogaḥ phalitaṃ tasya jīvitam ||  
 5.5.2 haritāś ca sirā yasya romakūpāś ca lohitāḥ |
       
 bhuṅkte vānnāni sāmlāni tatraiva sa vinaśyati ||  
 5.5.3  yasyor dhvavātaḥ kopena jantorāmāśayaṃ gataḥ |
       
       hṛdayaṃ parigṛhṇāti paretaṃ tasya jīvitam ||  
 5.5.4  gātre ca pāṇipāde ca yasya śuṣyati śoṇitam |
       
       muhurmuhurnṛtyati ca paretaṃ tasya jīvitam ||  
 5.5.5  vṛṣaṇau pāṇipādau ca yasya śuṣkaṃ mukhaṃ tathā |
       
       chaviś ca śoṣam āyāti paretaṃ tasya jīvitam ||  
 5.5.6  hanū hastau ca pādau ca vṛṣaṇau liṅgam eva ca |
       
       dṛśyate dehino yasya paretaṃ tasya jīvitam ||  
 5.5.7  hṛdayaṃ dahyate yasya mumūrṣuṃ taṃ samādiśet |
       
       āturas tu sa yāto vai paretaṃ tasya jīvitam ||  
 5.5.8  apasmāraḥ kṣayaḥ kuṣṭhaṃ raktapittamathodaram |
       
       gulmaś ca madhumehaś ca dīrgharogā bhavanti te ||  
 5.5.9  balamāṃsakṣayo yasya dehino dīrgharogiṇaḥ |
       
       dṛśyeta svarahāniś ca paretaṃ tasya jīvitam ||  
 5.5.10  hṛdayaṃ dahyate yasya koṣṭhe śūlaṃ svarakṣayaḥ |
       
       abhīkṣṇaṃ dahyate cāpi paretaṃ tasya jīvitam ||  
 5.5.11 trāsābhitāpā jantūnāṃ koṣṭhe śūlāścaranti ca |
       
       hikkācchardiparītaś ca paretaṃ tasya jīvitam ||  
 5.5.12 vāpitaṃ jvalitaṃ martyaḥ, salilaṃ hi hutāśanam |
       
       bhāskaraṃ manyate somaṃ durlabhaṃ tasya jīvitam ||  
 5.5.13  yaś cāpi vimale sūrye meghān paśyati sarvaśaḥ |
       
       durdinaṃ sudinaṃ cāpi paretaṃ tasya jīvitam ||  
 5.5.14  yaṃ rasā nāvatiṣṭhante bheṣajaṃ cendriyāṇi tu |
       
       yasya vā viparītāni na ca jīvati tādṛśaḥ ||  
 5.5.15  vānaspatyaphalaṃ mūlaṃ rogaspṛṣṭasya yasya
      vai |
       
       bhaiṣajyārthaṃ na dṛśyeta na ca jīvati tādṛśaḥ ||  
 5.5.16  ity etāni bhiṣag dṛṣṭvā lakṣaṇāni mumūrṣatām |
       
 na cikitsāṃ prayuñjīta yaśomārgapratīkṣayā || ity āha bhagavān
      ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele indriye pañcamo ' dhyāyaḥ || || ṣaṣṭho ' dhyāyaḥ || athātaḥ
      pūrvarūpīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 5.6.1 antarlohitakāyas tu bahiḥ pāṇḍuḥ prakāśate |
       
       pūrvarūpaṃ tadācaṣṭe mānavasya mumūrṣataḥ ||  
 5.6.2  bahirlohitakāyas tu pāṇḍurantaḥ prakāśate |
       
       pūrvarūpamanuprāptaḥ sa mṛtyor ucyate naraḥ ||  
 5.6.3  antarglāno bahiḥ pīno bahirādhmāta eva ca |
       
 yaś cātyantasamādhmātaḥ sarve ' pyete parāsukāḥ ||  
 5.6.4  abhīkṣṇaṃ jvaryate yas tu nivātamabhinandati |
       
       anuṣaktapratiśyāyaḥ kṣipraṃ śvāsena hanyate ||  
 5.6.5 ninādī vā pralāpī vā hasatyatyartham eva ca |
       
       unmādena kṛśo jantuḥ pañcatvam upagacchati ||  
 5.6.6  ghanaṃ saśūlaṃ yo veda sadāhaṃ hṛdayaṃ naraḥ |
       
       hṛdrogeṇa kṛśo janturvināśam upagacchati ||  
 5.6.7  prasvidyate ca kaṇḍūmān yo viruddhaṃ ca sevate |
       
       avirecanaśīlaś ca kuṣṭhena sa vinaśyati ||  
 5.6.8  sukumāraś ca yo jantuḥ snehaṃ māṃsaṃ ca sevate |
       
       divā svapiti cābhīkṣṇaṃ sa pramehī vinaśyati ||  
 5.6.9  pariśūnaś ca yo jantuḥ svede ca paruṣacchaviḥ |
       
       bhinnaṃ yaścopaviśati so ' tisāreṇa hanyate ||  
 5.6.10  yasyāgniś ca balaṃ caiva nālpaṃ bhavati dehinaḥ |
       
       kṣīṇalohitamāṃsasya yathā pretas tathaiva saḥ ||  
 5.6.11  sadyo raktaṃ śiro yasya pītakaṃ vā pradṛśyate |
       
       kapilaṃ pluṣṭakeśaṃ vā yathā pretas tathaiva saḥ ||  
 5.6.12  yasya netre lalāṭaṃ ca mukhaṃ nāsāṃ bhruvau
      tathā |
       
       jihmāni kurute vāyuryathā pretas tathaiva saḥ ||  
 5.6.13  śyāvā kaṇṭakinī jihvā yasya śuṣkā pradṛśyate |
       
       śyāve netre nakhāś cāpi yathā pretas tathaiva saḥ ||  
 5.6.14  yasya nirbhidyate kaṇṭhaḥ tāmyatyuccaiśśarīriṇaḥ |
       
       bahirāyāmabhājastaṃ pratyācakṣīta paṇḍitaḥ ||  
 5.6.15  yasyor dhvakāye balavān navo rogas tu duṣkriyaḥ |
       
       pūrvarūpaṃ tathā vācyaṃ mānavasya mariṣyataḥ ||  
 5.6.16  yasya cucchundarīgandhaḥ puruṣasya bhavatyatha |
       
       sauvarṇānapi vṛkṣāṃś ca yo veda sa vinaśyati ||  
 5.6.17  ity ebhir īdṛśaiś cānyairvikārairvarṇitaṃ naraḥ |
       
       nopakrameta medhāvī ya icchedātmanaḥ sukham || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele indriye ṣaṣṭho ' dhyāyaḥ || || saptamo ' dhyāyaḥ || athāta
      indriyāṇīkamindriyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 5.7.1  indriyāṇi yathā jantoḥ parīkṣeta viśeṣataḥ |
       
       āyuḥpramāṇaṃ jijñāsurbhiṣak tanme nibodhata ||  
 5.7.2  annapānātparīkṣeta darśanādyaiś ca tattvataḥ |
       
       arthādivihitaṃ jñānamindriyāṇāmatīndriyam ||  
 5.7.3  svasthebhyo vikṛtaṃ yasya jñānamindriyasaṃśrayam |
       
       alakṣitaṃ nimittena lakṣaṇaṃ maraṇe hi tat ||  
 5.7.4  ity uktaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ samyagindriyeṣv aśubhodayam |
       
       tad eva tu punarbhūyo vistareṇa nibodha me ||  
 5.7.5  ghanībhūtamivākāśaṃ paśyaṃstamiva medinīm |
       
 vigītaṃ hyubhayaṃ hyetatpaśyanmaraṇamṛcchati ||  
 5.7.6  yasya darśanam āyāti māruto ' mbaragocaraḥ |
       
 agnirnāyāti vā dīptaḥ tasyāpi kṣayam ādiśet ||  
 5.7.7  jale ' pi nirmale jālamajālaṃ manute naraḥ |
       
 sthire gacchati vā dṛṣṭvā jīvitātparihīyate ||  
 5.7.8  jāgratpaśyati yaḥ pretān rakṣāṃsi vividhāni ca |
       
       anyadvāpyadbhutaṃ kiṃcinna sa jīvati tādṛśaḥ ||  
 5.7.9  yo ' gniṃ prakṛtivarṇasthaṃ nīlaṃ paśyati niṣprabham |
       
       kṛṣṇaṃ vā yadi vā śuklaṃ na sa jīvati mānavaḥ ||  
 5.7.10 marīcīnasato meghe meghānvāpyamalāmbare |
       
       vidyuto vā vinā meghānna sa jīvati mānavaḥ ||  
 5.7.11  mṛṇmayīmiva vā pātrīṃ kṛṣṇāṃ vāpi purīṣitām |
       
       ādity amardhacandraṃ vā kṣipraṃ dṛṣṭvā vinaśyati ||  
 5.7.12  naktaṃ sūryamahaścandramavahnau dhūmamutthitam |
       
       agniṃ vā niṣprabhaṃ dṛṣṭvā rātrau, maraṇamādiśet ||  
 5.7.13  prabhāvataḥ prabhāṃ hīnāṃ niṣprabhānvā prabhāvataḥ
      |
       
       narān viliṅgān paśyanti bhāvān bhāvajighāṃsavaḥ ||  
 5.7.14  vyākṛtīni ca varṇāni visaṃkhyopacitāni ca |
       
       nimittāni ca paśyanti rūpāṇyāyuḥparikṣayāt ||  
 5.7.15 yas tu paśyatyadṛśyaṃ vā dṛśyaṃ yas tu na paśyati |
       
       tāvubhau gacchataḥ kṣipraṃ yamakṣayamasaṃśayam ||  
 5.7.16  aśabdasya ca yaḥ śrotā śabdaṃ yaś ca na
      vindati |
       
       dvāvapy etau yathā pretau tathā jñeyau vijānatā ||  
 5.7.17  viparyayeṇa yo vidyād gandhānāṃ caiva nāma tam |
       
       na vā tat sarvato vidyād vidyāt taṃ vai gatāyuṣam ||  
 5.7.18  yo rasaṃ na vijānāti vipakvaṃ vā ca tattvataḥ |
       
 apakvaṃ dṛśyate, pakvaṃ tam āhuḥ kuśalā narāḥ ||  
 5.7.19  uṣṇān śītān kharān ślakṣṇān mṛdūnapi ca dāruṇān |
       
 spṛśyān spṛṣṭvā tato ' nyac ca mumūrṣusteṣu manyate ||  
 5.7.20  antareṇa tapastīvraṃ yogaṃ vā vidhipūrvakam |
       
       indriyairadhikaṃ paśyan pañcatvam upapadyate ||  
 5.7.21  indriyāṇāmṛte dṛṣṭerindriyārthānnadoṣajān |
       
       naraḥ paśyati yaḥ kaścidindriyairna sa jīvati ||  
 5.7.22  svasthāḥ prajñāviparyāsairindriyārtheṣu vaikṛtam |
       
       paśyanti ye tu bahuśaḥ teṣāṃ maraṇamādiśet ||  
 5.7.23  etad eva ca vijñānaṃ yassamyaganupaśyati |
       
       maraṇaṃ jīvitaṃ caiva sa bhiṣag jñātumarhati || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele indriye saptamo ' dhyāyaḥ || || aṣṭamo ' dhyāyaḥ || athāto
      dūtādhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 5.8.1  tṛṇānnakhānvā chindan vai bhiṣajaṃ paripṛcchati |
       
       āturasya yadā dūtaḥ pratyākhyeyastathāvidhaḥ ||  
 5.8.2  viplutaṃ bhāṣamāṇaś ca bhiṣajaṃ paripṛcchati |
       
       āturasya yadā dūtaḥ pratyākhyeyastathāvidhaḥ ||  
 5.8.3  bhinatti kāṣṭhaṃ kāṣṭhena loṣṭaṃ loṣṭhena vāpy adhaḥ |
       
       āturasya yadā dūtaḥ pratyākhyeyastathāvidhaḥ ||  
 5.8.4  spṛśannaṅgāni bālāṃś ca bhiṣajaṃ paripṛcchati |
       
       āturasya yadā dūtaḥ pratyākhyeyastathāvidhaḥ ||  
 5.8.5 pidhāya pāṇinā nābhiṃ bhiṣajaṃ paripṛcchati |
       
       āturasya yadā dūtaḥ pratyākhyeyastathāvidhaḥ ||  
 5.8.6  kapālikāṃ śarkarāṃ vā bhinattyaṅgārikām api |
       
       āturasya yadā dūtaḥ pratyākhyeyastathāvidhaḥ ||  
 5.8.7  āste bhūmau pariśrānto gṛhṇātyaṅgamatha bhraman |
       
       āturasya yadā dūtaḥ pratyākhyeyastathāvidhaḥ ||  
 5.8.8  naṣṭaṃ mṛtamatikrāntaṃ nānuśocanti paṇḍitāḥ |
       
       ity āturasya hi yadā vadeddūto na so ' sti vai ||  
 5.8.9  karaṃ kareṇa gṛhṇāti pāṇinā tāḍayetkaram |
       
       āturasya yadā dūtaḥ pratyākhyeyastathāvidhaḥ ||  
 5.8.10  khādedoṣṭhau ca jihvāṃ ca nakhān dantaiś ca kalpayet |
       
       āturasya yadā dūtaḥ pratyākhyeyastathāvidhaḥ ||  
 5.8.11  āturasya yadā gehe vaidye vai paryupasthite |
       
       chidyate bhidyate caiva pratyākhyeyastathāvidhaḥ ||  
 5.8.12 parāvartya ghaṭaṃ pūrṇaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ paripṛcchati |
       
       āturasya yadā dūtaḥ pratyākhyeyastathāvidhaḥ ||  
 5.8.13  gṛdhraḥ sṛgālaḥ kākaś cāpy ulūko vāyasas tathā |
       
       nadeyurdakṣiṇe pārśve rogiṇo yasya nāsti saḥ ||  
 5.8.14  kaṣāyavastro muṇḍo vā jaṭilo vātha nagnakaḥ |
       
       carmabhir vā parivṛto, mahānasyeva śāṭikaḥ ||  
 5.8.15  tailābhyaktaśchinnanāso vāgmī conmatta eva vā |
       
       bhagnauṣṭhaḥ kharavāṭo vā na dūtaḥ sampraśasyate ||  
 5.8.16  iti dūtasamācāro vyādhitānāṃ prakīrtitaḥ |
       
 ya evaṃ veda nipuṇaṃ siddhikāmaḥ sa vai bhiṣak || ity āha
      bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele indriye aṣṭamo ' dhyāyaḥ || || navamo ' dhyāyaḥ || athāto
      gomayacūrṇaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 5.9.1  cūrṇaṃ śirasi yasyaiva śuṣkagomayasannibham |
       
       snehino dṛśyate jantormāsāddehaṃ jahāti saḥ ||  
 5.9.2  kṛśasya kapharogeṇa yasya śleṣmaparikṣayaḥ |
       
       karṇau raktau mukhaṃ caiva dvau māsau nātivartate ||  
 5.9.3  yasya lohitakābhāsamambu tāluni dṛśyate |
       
       kṣīṇalohitamāṃsasya sa māsaṃ nātivartate ||  
 5.9.4  arundhatīṃ na paśyet tu sthitāṃ saptarṣisaṃsadi |
       
       sa māsādaṣṭamānmartyaḥ kṣipraṃ prāṇairvimucyate ||  
 5.9.5 aṇukābhiś ca kṛṣṇābhir āsyaṃ jihvā ca tāluke |
       
       sarvatassamanucchinnaṃ na sa jīvati tādṛśaḥ ||  
 5.9.6  śīrṣābhitāpino yasya  śleṣmarogavatas tathā |
       
       hikkā viniṣyandate vai nāyamastīti nirdiśet ||  
 5.9.7  yasya lomāni keśāś ca pluṣyantīva śarīriṇaḥ |
       
 saṃhṛṣṭānīva vā dehī na sa jīvati tādṛśaḥ ||  
 5.9.8  yasya kālāntare dantā dṛśyante raktasannibhāḥ |
       
       niṣprabhāś cānuliptā vā na sa jīvati tādṛśaḥ ||  
 5.9.9  kṣāreṇa vidhṛtaṃ gātraṃ dṛśyate yasya dehinaḥ |
       
       samamuṣṇe ca śīte ca na sa jīvati tādṛśaḥ ||  
 5.9.10  gātreṣu kharavarṇeṣu yasya vārilavaplavaḥ |
       
       anabhyakteṣu gātreṣu na sa jīvati tādṛśaḥ ||  
 5.9.11  śūlamaṅge bhavedyasya sphuṭitaṃ raktamāsravet |
       
       adho golakasaṃkāśaṃ paretaṃ tasya jīvitam ||  
 5.9.12  āpāṇḍu madhumehe tu yaś ca mehati mānavaḥ |
       
       abhyantareṇa pañcāhātsa pañcatvaṃ hi gacchati ||  
 5.9.13  aratiś cāvipākaś ca kārśyadaurbalyam eva ca |
       
       yasya saṃdṛśyate jantorna sa jīvati tādṛśaḥ ||  
 5.9.14  yas tu dīnamanātho vā balena parihīyate |
       
       bhidyāmārogamāpnoti yathā pretas tathaiva saḥ ||  
 5.9.15 anuvṛttau yathā jantuḥ pittena parimūrcchitaḥ |
       
       saṃmūḍhavākyo bhavati yathā pretas tathaiva saḥ ||  
 5.9.16  yas tv āsane ' tha śayane ratiṃ na labhate naraḥ |
       
       sa śīghraṃ kurute kālaṃ yaś ca sāśrūṇi khādati ||  
 5.9.17  āruhya vānaraṃ yas tu saṃkalpaṃ nāvabudhyate |
       
       tam āhuḥ paralokāya svapne tu kuśalā narāḥ ||  
 5.9.18  parisaṃvatsarādyasya jvaro nāpaiti dehinaḥ |
       
       uṣṇo vā yadi vā śīto yathā pretas tathaiva saḥ ||  
 5.9.19  yasya jātapramehasya piṭakā pāṇḍurā bhavet |
       
       sopadravā śatapadā yathā pretas tathaiva saḥ ||  
 5.9.20  yasyor dhvaṃ kramate vāyuḥ śrotraṃ vādhaḥ
      pravartate |
       
       sarvāṇi ca prabhidyante yathā pretas tathaiva saḥ ||  
 5.9.21  ity etairlakṣaṇairyuktaṃ bhiṣak dṛṣṭvaiva mānavam |
       
       nopakramettathā vīra rakṣannātmayaśaḥ sphuṭam || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele indriye navamo ' dhyāyaḥ || || daśamo ' dhyāyaḥ ||
      athātaśchāyādhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 5.10.1  anucchāyāthavā jantordṛḍhacchāyāthavā punaḥ |
       
       vicchinnā yasya vā chāyā na sa jīvati tādṛśaḥ ||  
 5.10.2  yo vidyutamivākāśe vyabhre paśyati mānavaḥ |
       
       dhūmāyate śiraśchāyā yasya nāstīti taṃ viduḥ ||  
 5.10.3  lākṣāraktaṃ yathā vastramevaṃ paśyati yo mahīm |
       
       athavā raktamākāśaṃ raktapittena hanyate ||  
 5.10.4  yo hṛṣṭaromā puruṣaḥ kāsena śleṣmaṇācitaḥ |
       
 kaṇṭhaś ca śūkānugato yasya nāstīti taṃ viduḥ ||  
 5.10.5  yasya śaṅkhāccyutaṃ māṃsaṃ śyāve netre tathaiva ca |
       
       cūrṇakaś ca mukhe jātaḥ paretaṃ tasya jīvitam ||  
 5.10.6  yasya hastāccyutaṃ māṃsaṃ jantordṛśyeta kuṣṭhinaḥ |
       
       athāviprayuktasya na sa jīvati mānavaḥ ||
