 5.10.7  avipakvaṃ vipakvaṃ vā bhuktaṃ bhuktaṃ yathā bhavet |
       
       kāśaśvāsajvaraiḥ spṛṣṭo nāsti tasya cikitsitam ||  
 5.10.8  hṛdayaṃ pūrvamāvāti yasya snātasya dehinaḥ |
       
       ardhamāsātparaṃ tasya jīvitaṃ nātivartate ||  
 5.10.9  ūrdhvaśvāsahato yas tu raktaṃ pracchardayen naraḥ |
       
       śūlaṃ vā bhinnakoṣṭhasya na sa jīvati mānavaḥ ||  
 5.10.10 antardāho ' dhiko yasya śītārtiś cāpi bāhyataḥ |
       
       ākāśaṃ paripūrṇaṃ vā vetti yo na sa jīvati ||  
 5.10.11  yasya pakvāvubhāvoṣṭhau nīlau jambūphalopamau |
       
       ucchūnaṃ yasya ca śiraḥ paretaṃ tasya jīvitam ||  
 5.10.12  yasyocchūnaṃ bhavenmadhyamubhāvaṃsau kṛśau tathā |
       
       viriktaḥ punarādhmāti yathā pretas tathaiva saḥ ||  
 5.10.13  etadindriyavijñānaṃ yassamyaganupaśyati |
       
       sa jīvitaṃ ca mṛtyuṃ ca nṛṇāṃ vidyādbhiṣagvaraḥ || ity āha bhagavān
      ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele indriye daśamo ' dhyāyaḥ || || ekadaśo ' dhyāyaḥ || athātaḥ
      puṣpīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 5.11.1  śirasyaṅge raktavarṇaṃ yo ' nilaṃ vāpi paśyati |
       
       ghaṭikāmekavarṇaṃ vā sa puṣpita ihocyate ||  
 5.11.2  aṣṭāpadaṃ vā sukṛtaṃ jagatīṃ yaḥ prapaśyati |
       
       sa dṛṣṭiparihīnatvāt puṣpitaḥ procyate naraḥ ||  
 5.11.3  suptaś ca saṃvṛte gehe paśyatyākāśam eva yaḥ |
       
       romanthayati dantaiś ca sa puṣpita ihocyate ||  
 5.11.4  dīpyamānamivākāśaṃ pṛthivīṃ ca vanāni ca |
       
       yo vetti romasaṃhṛṣṭaḥ puṣpitaḥ sa ihocyate ||  
 5.11.5  anullipto yathā dehī vāti cetkuṇapaṃ yathā |
       
       sevante makṣikāś caiva puṣpitaḥ sa ihocyate ||  
 5.11.6  avijñātā naraṃ nārī svapna eva nivāsinī |
       
       dakṣiṇāṃ diśamehīti yaṃ brūyānna sa jīvati ||  
 5.11.7  prakīrṇakeśo vikaraḥ svapne yo dakṣiṇāṃ diśam |
       
 pratipadyeta tatraiva na sa jīvati tādṛśaḥ ||  
 5.11.8  kuśair iva nirūḍhāṅgamātmānaṃ svapna īkṣate |
       
       khaṃ vā sadhūmaṃ yo vetti na sa jīvati tādṛśaḥ ||  
 5.11.9  yaḥ svapne vṛkṣamāruhya na rogī trāyate gṛhe |
       
       prakīrṇakeśo vikacaḥ yo ' gnimāruhya roditi ||  
 5.11.10  prāsādamekasthūṇaṃ tu svapne yaś cādhirohati |
       
       naro nṛtyati paṅke vā sa pumānna ca jīvati ||  
 5.11.11  svapne prāsādamāruhya mahāntaṃ kāñcanaṃ tathā |
       
       yo nṛttagītapānānnī na sa jīvati mānavaḥ ||  
 5.11.12  gajenoṣṭreṇa vā gacchan yaḥ paśyeddakṣiṇāṃ diśam |
       
       jīvet tu rogī saptāhaṃ, nīrogaḥ śaradāṃ śatam ||  
 5.11.13  yāti yo durdine vāpi svapne vā dakṣiṇāṃ diśam |
       
       pratibudhyeta tatraiva na sa jīvati tādṛśaḥ ||  
 5.11.14  bhāsairbarhivarāhaiś ca śvabhir mahiṣavājibhiḥ |
       
       samaṃ yo taddivā yone svapne yogaphalaṃ bhavet ||  
 5.11.15  yadā gaṇḍaṃ ca khaḍgaṃ ca svapne cāśnaṃś ca paśyati |
       
       prakīrṇakeśam api ca na sa jīvati tādṛśaḥ ||  
 5.11.16  yaḥ svapne puruṣaḥ kālaṃ pītaṃ vā vastramṛcchati |
       
       gāyannaceṣṭayanvāpi na sa jīvati tādṛśaḥ ||  
 5.11.17  yaḥ svapne vītakāmo ' pi pītāṃ pibati vāruṇīm |
       
       citrakaṇṭhaguṇo vāpi na sa jīvati tādṛśaḥ ||  
 5.11.18 ākulāpāṃ nadīṃ svapne yovagāheta mānavaḥ |
       
       jīvetsarogassaptāhaṃ, nīrogasśaradāṃ śatam ||  
 5.11.19  svapne snātānuliptasya bhraṃśedyasya tu varṇakaḥ |
       
       gātrasya puruṣasyeha sa śastreṇa vinaśyati ||  
 5.11.20  etadindriyavijñānaṃ yassamyaganupaśyati |
       
 jīvitaṃ caiva mṛtyuṃ ca nṛṇāṃ vidyādvicakṣaṇaḥ || ity āha bhagavān
      ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele indriye ekādaśo ' dhyāyaḥ || || dvādaśo ' dhyāyaḥ ||
      athāto+ avākcitīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 5.12.1  avākcitā vā jihmā vā yasya chāyālpikā bhāvet |
       
       netre ca viṣame syātāṃ paretaṃ tasya jīvitam || 5.1 
 5.12.2  yadi dīnāni pakṣmāṇi na nimīlanti dehinaḥ |
       
       dahyete nayane vāpi paretaṃ tasya jīvitam ||  
 5.12.3 namantyau yasya dṛśyete bhruvau mūrdhani bā
       sthite |
       
       jīvet tu sa tryahaṃ rogī ṣaṇmāsān vyādhivarjitaḥ ||  
 5.12.4 luñcyamāneṣu keśeṣu vedayannāti vedanām |
       
 nivṛttasukha duḥkhaḥ syāt paretaṃ tasya jīvitam ||  
 5.12.5  yasyāturasya piṭakā vyaṅgo vā dṛśyate mukhe |
       
       adṛṣṭapūrvaṃ prathamaṃ paretaṃ tasya jīvitam ||  
 5.12.6  śuṣyate nāsikāvaṃśaḥ pṛthutvaṃ yasya gacchati |
       
 aṃso ' nilāt kāsavataḥ paretaṃ tasya jīvitam ||  
 5.12.7  atyuṣṇaṃ vātiśītaṃ vā stabdhaṃ vā mṛdu vāpy atha |
       
       manyate pāṇipādaṃ ca paretaṃ tasya jībitam ||  
 5.12.8  yo ' vatīrya nadīṃ pūrṇāṃ toye paśyati jālakam |
       
       gātraṃ liptamathādbhiś ca yasya nāstīti taṃ viduḥ ||  
 5.12.9  vivartayati yaḥ śīrṣamatyarthaṃ ca nasā naraḥ |
       
       na svidyate lalāṭaṃ ca nāsti tasya cikitsitam ||  
 5.12.10  jvaryate kāsate vāpi tathocchavasiti vai dṛḍham |
       
       ākramyate tāmyate ca yathā pretas tathaiva saḥ ||  
 5.12.11  yasyodaraṃ samādhmātaṃ tadvartma ca vibhāvyate |
       
       bhinnaṃ purīṣaṃ tṛṣṇā ca yathā pretas tathaiva saḥ ||  
 5.12.12 anārataṃ gṛhe yasya kāṃsyaṃ bhidyeta dehinaḥ
      |
       
       candrastīkṣṇo mṛduścārko yasya syāt taṃ vivarjayet ||  
 5.12.13  apradhātuḥ pradhāturvā svastho vā yadi vā++āturaḥ
      |
       
       yaścandanamivāvāti na sa jīvati tādṛśaḥ ||  
 5.12.14  yūthikotpannagaṇḍaśca, vāti yaś cāpi vartmavat |
       
       abhaktaḥ tasimaṃ bālye yo vāti na sa jīvati ||  
 5.12.15  dviṣadbhiḥ kurute sakhyaṃ yaḥ priyairyāt i vipriyam |
       
       akasmātkupyate yas tu paretaṃ tasya jīvitam ||  
 5.12.16 ebhir evaṃvidhairliṅgairanyaiś cāpi yathāyatham |
       
       nopakrameta medhāvī bhiṣaganvitamāturam ||  
 5.12.17  etadbhiṣagariṣṭānāṃ yo jñānamanubudhyate |
       
       yathoktaṃ veda vedāyuḥ sa bhiṣak śāstrakovidaḥ || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele indriye dvādaśo ' dhyāyaḥ || iti bhelasaṃhitāyām indriyasthānaṃ
      samāptam || |
       
       |cikitsāsthānam || || prathamo ' dhyāyaḥ || athāta ekādaśasarpiṣkaṃ
      vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 
 
 6.1.1  akalpayan na yajñāṅgaṃ purā dakṣastriśūline |
       
       tasmāt praṇāśayāmāsa yajñaṃ dakṣasya śaṅkaraḥ ||  
 6.1.2  taṃ ca nāśayatā yajñaṃ devyāḥ priyacikīrṣayā |
       
       krodhenoṣṇaṃ viniśvasya tān lokān vyāpito jvaraḥ ||  
 6.1.3  sa eṣa santāpayati jagatsthāvarajaṅgamam |
       
       nidhane cāpi bhūtānāṃ nānyo heturvinā jvarāt ||  
 6.1.4  yāvanto ' nye samākhyātā vyādhayas tu śarīriṇām |
       
       saṃvatsareṇa te ghnanti sadyaḥ prāṇaharo jvaraḥ ||  
 6.1.5  rogānīkasya sarvasya jvaro rājā prakīrtitaḥ |
       
       jvarayatyeṣa bhūtāni tasmājjvara iti smṛtiḥ ||  
 6.1.6  śārīramānasānāṃ ca rogāṇāṃ pravaro jvaraḥ |
       
       tasmāt prathamatas tasya pravakṣyāmi cikitsitam ||  
 6.1.7  uktarūpasamutthānā jvarāś cāṣṭau prakīrtitāḥ |
       
       śītaścoṣṇaś ca niyataḥ samāsāt dvividho jvaraḥ ||  
 6.1.8  śītasyoṣṇāṃ kriyāṃ kuryād vātaśleṣmātmakasya  tu |
       
       uṣṇasyaikāntapittasya śītāṃ kuryāt kriyāṃ bhiṣak ||  
 6.1.9  vāyur āmāśayāt pūrvamūṣmāṇaṃ samudīrayet  |
       
       tvaggato roma cāpannaḥ saṃharṣayati mānavam ||  
 6.1.10  sa tu pittānubandhena tejasā paripācitaḥ |
       
       prāpnoti vilayaṃ śleṣmā sambandheneva toyadaḥ ||  
 6.1.11 śānte śīte punardāhaṃ pittātprāpnoti mānavaḥ |
       
       utpittamindhanībhūtaṃ vapurdahati pāvakaḥ ||  
 6.1.12 gatavegenilaḥ paścādūṣmaṇā paripācitaḥ |
       
       svam eva bhajate sthānamānulomyaṃ ca gacchati ||  
 6.1.13  evaṃ jvaramavāpnoti hyevam eva ca mucyate |
       
       etad buddhimatāṃ proktaṃ samāsena cikitsitam ||  
 6.1.14  durlabhā buddhimantas tu tasmād vakṣyāmi vistaram |
       
       ekādaśaprakāraṃ hi jvaritānāṃ cikitsitam ||  
 6.1.15  sarpiś caikādaśaṃ vidyāt tan me vistarataḥ śṛṇu |
       
 siddhās svedāḥ kaṣāyāś ca lehaḥ pācanakāni ca ||  
 6.1.16  cūrṇaḥ pradehāssekāś ca vaṭikā modakāḥ payaḥ |
       
       sarpiś caikādaśaṃ proktaṃ siddhamāmamathāpi ca ||  
 6.1.17  eṣāṃ prayogaṃ vakṣyāmi vīryāṇi ca pṛthak pṛthak |
       
       śleṣmāṇamanilaṃ caiva jitvā pittantu dehinām ||  
 6.1.18  karoti yasmādūṣmāṇaṃ tasmājjvarita  ucyate |
       
       vāyuḥ pittena saṃsṛṣṭaḥ śleṣmā vā pittamūrcchitaḥ ||  
 6.1.19  ūṣmāṇaṃ kurute yasmāttataḥ  pittamupācaret |
       
       tṛṣyate coṣṇasalilaṃ deyaṃ doṣavipācanam ||  
 6.1.20  jvaraghnaṃ dīpanīyaṃ ca kaphapittānilāpaham |
       
       srotasāṃ śodhanaṃ caiva rucisvedakaraṃ nṛṇām ||  
 6.1.21  dīpyamāne hi kāyāgnau śleṣmā vāyuś ca śāmyataḥ |
       
 tayoś cāpy anulomatvāt pittam apyupaśāmyati ||  
 6.1.22  tasmād uṣṇodakaṃ peyaṃ śreṣṭhamāhurnavajvare ||  
 6.1.23  śītaṃ hi salilaṃ pītaṃ kopayetkaphamārutau |
       
       kuryād bhūyo ' gnimṛdutāṃ staimity amaruciṃ tathā ||  
 6.1.24  kāmaṃ tu tiktakaissiddhaṃ hitaṃ kvathitaśītalam |
       
       teṣāṃ sāmiśṛtaṃ pānaṃ ye cāpy ekāntaśītalāḥ  ||  
 6.1.25  bhojanārthaṃ hi ṣaḍrātraṃ peyā deyā bubhukṣite |
       
       kṣutpipāsāpahā pathyā śakṛnmūtrānilāpahā ||  
 6.1.26  auṣṇyādvātakaphau hanyāt llaghutvāt param eva ca |
       
       hṛdvyathāṃ  vidhiyuktā tu sā hanyāt svedamāvahet ||  
 6.1.27  tasmājjvareṣu sarveṣu jvaramukte ca mānave |
       
 pāyayed vidhivatpeyāḥ yathāsvauṣadhasādhitāḥ ||  
 6.1.28  śītajjvaraharaṃ kṛtsnamuktamevaṃ cikitsitam |
       
 ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi bhojyābhojyaṃ savistaram ||  
 6.1.29  śālayaḥ ṣaṣṭikāś caiva nīvārāssapramodakāḥ |
       
       yavānnavikṛtiś cāpi bhojaneṣu hitāssadā ||  
 6.1.30  kapiñjalāssahariṇā vartakāḥ kālapucchakāḥ |
       
       eṇā vartīrakāś caiva jāṅgalā jvarite hitāḥ ||  
 6.1.31  mudgāḍhakīmasūrāṇāṃ satīnānāṃ tathaiva ca |
       
       siddhāssūpāḥ praśasyante yūṣāś ca jvaranāśanāḥ ||  
 6.1.32 uṣṇān vrīhīn sayavakān saktukāṃścitrakānapi |
       
       māṣāṃstilāṃścoṣṇavīryān jvaritaḥ parivarjayet ||  
 6.1.33 grāmyānūpaudakaṃ māṃsaṃ tathobhe gavyamāhiṣe
      |
       
       chāgaso  raṇavārāhaṃ dadhi śuktaṃ ca varjayet ||  
 6.1.34  piṣṭānnāni ca sarvāṇi śākāni vividhāni ca |
       
       vidāhīnyuṣṇavīryāṇi jvaritaḥ parivarjayet ||  
 6.1.35  barhiṇastittirikrauñcān kapotānatha  kukkuṭān |
       
       pañcaitānviṣkirānuṣṇān jvaritaḥ parivarjayet ||  
 6.1.36 vamane ca vireke ca snehane laṅghane tathā |
       
       proktā me jvariṇaḥ kālāḥ sūtrasthāne savistarāḥ ||  
 6.1.37  amātyāś cālayaś cāpi suhṛdaś cānuśāsinaḥ |
       
       chandajñā matisampannāḥ śāstrajñāneṣu kovidāḥ ||  
 6.1.38  te vadeyuḥ kathāścitrā dharmakāmārthasaṃhitāḥ |
       
       āturasya vinodārthaṃ tandrāśokavināśanāḥ ||  
 6.1.39 dāruṇāś cāmanojñāś ca na ca prītivivardhanāḥ
      |
       
       pittavyādhiparītānāṃ kathāś ca parivarjayet ||  
 6.1.40  utsāhameva  janayed āturasya cikitsakaḥ |
       
       udagrasya hi bhaiṣajyamamṛtatvāya kalpate ||  
 6.1.41  candrānanāḥ pīnakucāḥ sugandhāḥ śuklavāsasaḥ |
       
       rujāklamavināśārthamupāsīta  ca yoṣitaḥ ||  
 6.1.42  atyāśanamatisthānamaticaṅkramaṇāni ca |
       
       jvarito varjayennityaṃ prāṇān rakṣec ca sarvaśaḥ ||  
 6.1.43  krodhaṃ striyaṃ caṅkramaṇaṃ divāsvapnātibhāṣaṇam |
       
       gurūṇyadhvā viruddhāni vyāyāmo vegadhāraṇam ||  
 6.1.44  praduṣṭo mārutaḥ pānaṃ niśi jāgaraṇaṃ ca yat |
       
       kāraṇānyupaśāntasya jvarasya prabhave punaḥ ||  
 6.1.45  na cainaṃ snāpayejjātu  sahasā jvarakarśitam
      |
       
       saṃdūṣitāṃ  hy asya tanuṃ punarāvartate jvaraḥ ||  
 6.1.46 maheśvarakrodhabhavo jvaraḥ prokto maharṣibhiḥ |
       
       tasmājjvaravimokṣārthaṃ pūjayet ṛṣabhadhvajam ||  
 6.1.47  snānāni śāntayo homavratāni niyamo yamaḥ |
       
 śasyante ceṣṭayaḥ kāmyā vedoktā jvaranāśanāḥ ||  
 6.1.48  rogādhipatirugraujāḥ  vyādhīnāṃ prasavo jvaraḥ |
       
       sarvabhūtāntako ghoro hutāśātmā jvaraḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
 6.1.49 prasaṅgī duścikitsyaḥ syādbhiṣagbhiḥ pāpasambhavaḥ
      |
       
 tasmād vedoditairmantrairhomaiś ca vinivartayet ||  
 6.1.50 bhūtavidyāsamutpannaṃ caṇḍakarma jvarāpaham |
       
       tatkāryaṃ bhūtavaidyena tathā nāviśati  jvaraḥ ||  
 6.1.51  rudrabhaktena śucinā vaidyenātha tapasvinā |
       
       prayatena prayoktavyaṃ cirajvaracikitsitam || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ
      |
       
       iti bhele cikitsite prathamo ' dhyāyaḥ || || dvitīyo ' dhyāyaḥ || athāto
      viṣamajvaracikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 6.2.1  kecidvātātmakaṃ prāhurbhiṣajo viṣamajvaram |
       
       sannipātodbhavaṃ kecidapare pittasambhavam ||  
 6.2.2.  śleṣmajaṃ tvapare prāhurapare bhūtasambhavam |
       
       janmanakṣatrapīḍābhir apare devacintakāḥ ||  
 6.2.3 īdṛśaḥ śāstrakārāṇāṃ matayo ' tha pṛthagvidhāḥ |
       
       sannipātodbhavaṃ hyetadahaṃ vakṣyāmi hetubhiḥ ||  
 6.2.4  pakvāśayasthapavano hy asthimajjagatastathā 
      |(ṃadhukośa on ṃṇ2.38)) kupitaḥ kopayatyāśu śleṣmāṇaṃ pittam eva ca ||  
 6.2.5  sa gambhīrasamutpattisthānatantratrayo mahān |
       
       anyedyuṣkaikāntaritau  kuryād vāpi caturthakam ||  
 6.2.6  majjānamasthi medaś ca dūṣayetprathame ' hani |
       
       dvitīye ' hani samprāpte dūṣayenmāṃsaśoṇitam ||  
 6.2.7  tatastṛtīye divase dūṣayet kaphamārutau |
       
       abhigamya tataḥ pittaṃ dūṣayet tu caturthake ||  
 6.2.8  jvaro ' yaṃ prāṇināṃ dehe raudro māheśvaras tathā |
       
       prayateta praśāntau tu tasmād asya vicakṣaṇaḥ ||  
 6.2.9  gambhīrasthānasambhūto dhātusaṃkaradūṣitaḥ |
       
       tasmāc caturthako nāma duścikitsyatamo mataḥ ||  
 6.2.10  śoṣayatyeṣa bhūtāni dāruṇo viṣamajvaraḥ |
       
       tasmāc choṣopacāreṇa kuryāt tasya cikitsitam ||  
 6.2.11  triphalākvāthasiddhena ghṛtena matimān bhiṣak |
       
       snehayet taṃ yathānyāyaṃ yuktyā vṛṣaghṛtena vā ||  
 6.2.12  sraṃsayet tamadhobhāgaṃ yathāvyādhibalābalam |
       
       doṣeṣvāmāśayastheṣu kārayed vamanaṃ bhiṣak ||  
 6.2.13  āsthāpanaṃ ca kurvīta tathā  cāpy anuvāsanam |
       
       etanmahāpañcagavyaṃ vikhyātaṃ sarpiruttamam ||  
 6.2.14  caturthakaṃ mokṣayati mantrasiddhiyuto yathā |
       
       śvayathuṃ pāṇḍurogaṃ ca plīhānaṃ sabhagandaram ||  
 6.2.15  udarāṇi tathā gulmān kāmilāṃ cāpakarṣati ||  
 6.2.16  śakṛdrasaṃ payo mūtraṃ dadhi sarpiś ca pāyayet |
       
       tatpañcagavyaṃ śamayecchvayathuṃ pāṇḍutāṃ jvaram ||  
 6.2.17  samūlapatraśākhasya śataṃ kṛtvā vṛṣasya tu |
       
       jaladroṇe vipaktavyamaṣṭabhāgāvaśeṣitam ||  
 6.2.18  garbheṇa vṛṣapuṣpāṇāmāḍhakaṃ sarpiṣaḥ pacet ||
      tatsiddhaṃ pāyayed yuktyā madhupādasamanvitam ||  
 6.2.19  kāsaṃ śvāsaṃ pāṇḍurogaṃ tṛtīyakacaturthakau |
       
       raktapittaṃ kṣayaṃ caiva vṛṣasarpirniyacchati ||  
 6.2.20  nāgaraṃ saindhavaṃ
      cavyaṃ pippalīkṣāracitrakau  |
       
       eteṣāṃ palikairbhāgairghṛtaprasthaṃ vipācayet ||  
 6.2.21  kṣīraprasthena saṃyojya śanairmṛdvagninā pacet |
       
       etena gulmāḥ śāmyanti kuṣṭhāni jaṭharāṇi ca ||  
 6.2.22  jvare ca viṣame peyaṃ plīhaśvayathumehinām |
       
       śūle pāṇḍvāmaye caiva grahaṇīdīpaneṣu ca ||  
 6.2.23  ūrdhvavātāś ca ye kecitsarveṣāmauṣadhaṃ param |
       
       tryūṣaṇaṃ citrakaṃ hiṃsrāṃ vilaṅgāni harītakīm ||  
 6.2.24  vibhītakānyāmalakaṃ cirabilvatvacaṃ tathā |
       
       daśaitāni samāṃśāni ślakṣṇānyakṣasamāni ca ||  
 6.2.25  taiḥ pācayed dhṛtaprasthaṃ samyak payasi ṣaḍguṇe |
       
       grahaṇī dīpyate tena vātagulmaś ca śāmyati ||  
 6.2.26  arśasāṃ śamanaṃ caiva gudaśophe ca pūjitam |
       
       etad eva hi vai śreṣṭhamudāvarte ghṛtaṃ bhavet ||  
 6.2.27  darbhavetasamūlāni candanaṃ madhukaṃ balā |
       
       phenilā padmakośīramubhe ca kamalotpale ||  
 6.2.28  kiṃśukaśceti  bhāgāḥ syuḥ
      pṛthak pañcapalonmitāḥ |
       
       jaladroṇe vipaktavyaṃ caturbhāgāvaśeṣitam ||  
 6.2.29  jīvakarṣabhakau medāṃ lodhraṃ lāmajjakaṃ tathā |
       
       kāleyakaṃ sapriyakaṃ  dadyāt kesaram eva ca ||  
 6.2.30  tripuṇḍarīkaṃ lodhraṃ ca padmakaṃ padmakesaram |
       
       surabhiṃ kuṅkumaṃ caiva mañjiṣṭhāṃ madayantikām ||  
 6.2.31  mācipatraṃ ca tulyāni dviguṇaṃ kuṅkumaṃ bhavet |
       
       caturguṇāṃ ca mañjiṣṭhāṃ sauvīraṃ snehasammitam ||  
 6.2.32  tailaprasthaṃ pacettena kaṣāyeṇārdhapeṣitam |
       
       etadabhyañjanaṃ tailaṃ viṣamajvaranāśanam ||  
 6.2.33 mahāpadmakam ākhyātam etat sarvajvarāpaham |
       
       vātapittodbhavaṃ kṣipraṃ jvarametanniyacchati ||  
 6.2.34  trāyamāṇāṃ jayāṃ vīrāṃ nākulīṃ gandhanākulīm |
       
       kāyasthāṃ ca vayaḥsthāṃ ca jīrakaṃ sapalaṅkaṣam ||  
 6.2.35 chatrāticchatrajaṭilāṃ sūkarīṃ  karkaṭīṃ
      tathā |
       
 cāraṭīṃ pūtanāṃ keśīṃ vacāṃ kaṭukarohiṇīm ||  
 6.2.36  mahāpuruṣadantāṃ ca vṛścikālīṃ kaṭambharām |
       
 sthirāṃ ca piṣṭvā taissiddhaṃ caturthakavināśanam ||  
 6.2.37  mahāpaiśācikaṃ nāma sarpiretajjvarāpaham |
       
 bhūtagrahānapasmārānunmādāṃś cāpakarṣati ||  
 6.2.38  etair eva uṣadhagaṇaiḥ pradehaṃ kārayed bhiṣak |
       
       dhūpayejjvaritaṃ caiva tathā sampadyate sukhī ||  
 6.2.39  balayaḥ śāntikarmāṇi homasvastyayanāni ca |
       
       snānāni copavāsaś ca śamayanti caturthakam ||  
 6.2.40  sraṣṭāraṃ cāsya rogasya bhūtādhipatimacyutam |
       
 pūjayaṃś cābhigacchec ca śmaśāne vṛṣabhadhvajam ||  
 6.2.41  bhūtavidyāsamutpannairbandhanaissādhanair api |
       
       homairbalividhānaiś ca nāśayed viṣamajvaram || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele cikitsite dvitīyo ' dhyāyaḥ || || tṛtīyo ' dhyāyaḥ || athāto
      raktapittacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 6.3.1  ūrdhvaṃ cādhaś ca martyānāṃ raktapittaṃ pravartate |
       
       atas tu dvividhā proktā cikitsā raktapittinaḥ ||  
 6.3.2  atyamlalavaṇāhārāt satatātapasevanāt |
       
 upavāsād bhramāt trāsādviruddhādhyaśanādibhiḥ ||  
 6.3.3  tilapiṇyākāśākānāṃ tathā piṣṭakṛtasya ca |
       
       pittalānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ matsyādīnāṃ ca sevanāt ||  
 6.3.4  ūrdhvaṃ cādhaś ca kupitaṃ raktapittaṃ pravartate |
       
       ghrāṇakarṇākṣimukhataḥ pāyuto meḍhratas tathā ||  
 6.3.5  niṣṭhīvati saraktaṃ ca tiktamamlamathāpi vā |
       
       na ca tatpatitaṃ bhūmau bhakṣayanti pipīlikāḥ ||  
 6.3.6  makṣikā vāpi tiktatvāc chuṣkaṃ pittaṃ ca lakṣyate |
       
       sandahyate dūyate ca kaṇṭhastālu  ca śuṣyati ||  
 6.3.7  lohagandhi mukhaṃ cāsya kaṇṭho dhūmāyate tathā |
       
       etānyevaṃ tvadhobhāge lakṣaṇānyupalakṣayet ||  
 6.3.8  ūrdhvabhāgaṃ tu sādhyaṃ syādadho vai yāpyamucyate |
       
       sarvasrotaḥpravṛttaṃ tu raktapittaṃ na sidhyati || raktapittamadhobhāgaṃ 
 chardinaissamupācaret ||  
  || caturtho ' dhyāyaḥ ||  
 
 
 
 
 6.4.1  svapneṣu nityaṃ paśyanti śuṣkāndagdhāṃś ca pādapān |
       
 makṣikātṛṇakeśāś ca sampatantyasya bhojane ||  
 6.4.2  romāṇi mūrdhajāś cāsya vivardhante viśeṣataḥ |
       
       avaguṇṭhanaśīlaś ca rahaḥkāmotthakopanaḥ ||  
 6.4.3  jugupsāluramarṣī  ca strīkāmo durbalendriyaḥ |
       
       ucitā hīyate chāyā tāluśoṣś ca jāyate ||  
 6.4.4  nāsāsrāvaḥ pratiśyāyaḥ svarabhedaśśirorujā |
       
       ūrū ca svidyato ' tyarthaṃ hāniś ca balavarṇayoḥ ||  
 6.4.5  śirasaḥ paripūrṇatvaṃ hastapādaṃ ca dahyate |
       
       aruciś cāvipākaś ca mūrchā śvāso mṛdurjvaraḥ ||  
 6.4.6  kṣatoraskaś ca kāsena niṣṭhīvati saśoṇitam |
       
       etāni pūrvarūpāṇi yakṣmiṇāṃ kīrtitāni ca ||  
 6.4.7  ṣaṭ caikādaśarūpāṇi  śuṣyatastāni lakṣayet |
       
       ucchritopadravaṃ cainaṃ pūrvarūpairabhidrutam ||  
 6.4.8  prakṣīṇabalamāṃsaṃ ca na cikitsedviśoṣiṇam |
       
       alpopadravasaṃyuktamaciropadravotthitam ||  
 6.4.9  dravyavantaṃ vayaḥsthaṃ ca pratyākhyāyārabheta vai |
       
       athāsyānumataṃ pūrvaṃ pravakṣyāmi cikitsitam ||  
 6.4.10  yadadhītya bhiṣagyuktyā yaśaḥ svargam avāpnuyāt |
       
       śoṣī nity ajugupsāluḥ sukhaśīlaś ca mānavaḥ ||  
 6.4.11  lolo dveṣṭā nikṛṣṭānāṃ vaidyabhaiṣajyakutsakaḥ |
       
       tasmāt tasyānukūlena bhiṣajā++ āśvasanena ca ||  
 6.4.12  asaṃbhrāntena yuktena prayoktavyaṃ cikitsitam |
       
       śoṣiṇo ' tha balasthasya pañcakarma vidhīyate ||  
 6.4.13  tad eva kṣīṇamāṃsasya prayuktaṃ viṣamaṃ bhavet |
       
       tasya saṃśuddhākāyasya bhojanānyupakalpayet ||  
 6.4.14  kalamān dīrghaśūkāṃś ca raktaśāliṃ saṣaṣṭikān |
       
       yavānnavikṛtīś cāpi jāṅgalāṃś ca mṛgadvijān ||  
 6.4.15  bhojaneṣu praśaṃsanti mudgān sūpārtham eva ca |
       
       saṃvatsarasthitaṃ dhānyaṃ bhojane śoṣiṇāṃ hitam ||  
 6.4.16  taddhi vīryādahīnaṃ syānmāṃsaṃ sadyohataṃ ca yat |
       
       viśeṣataś ca māṃsāni kravyādabilavāsinām ||  
 6.4.17  śoṣī nityaṃ niṣeveta madyāni vividhāni ca |
       
       śleṣmā dehe vivṛddho ' pi vāyunā susamīritaḥ ||  
 6.4.18  pittaṃ raktaṃ ca sandūṣya srotāṃsyūrdhvaṃ ruṇaddhi
      hi |
       
       te parasparasaṃruddhā dhātavaḥ pavaneritāḥ ||  
 6.4.19  kaphapradhānā rundhanti sarvā rasavahāḥ sirāḥ |
       
 tadā tā rasavāhinyaḥ sirā hṛdayavāhikāḥ ||  
 6.4.20  rasamāhārajātānāṃ na vahanti yathā purā |
       
       tasya bhuktaṃ na raktāya na māṃsāya ca kalpate ||  
 6.4.21  na ca medo+ asthimajjabhyo na śuklatvāy dehinām |
       
       teṣāmavṛddhādhātūnāṃ baddhānāmayaneṣv atha ||  
 6.4.22  bhuñjānānām api sarogāṇi gātrāṇi dehinām |
       
       hetunā tena śuṣyanti śuṣyatāṃ śoṣavanti ca ||  
 6.4.23  etacchoṣasya śoṣatvaṃ mukhyamāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ |
       
       sattveṣv atipramāthitvaṃ vyālakarma yathā ++āpadi ||  
 6.4.24  māṃsāny api tathā teṣāṃ srotāṃsi vikasanty api |
       
 śodhayanti pramāthitvāt srotāṃsi grathitāny api ||  
 6.4.25  tasmāt kravyādamāṃsāni śoṣī śaktyāvaśīlayet |
       
       rahasyametadvaidyānām upadiṣṭaṃ cikitsakaiḥ ||  
 6.4.26  madyaṃ kravyādamāṃsaṃ ca śoṣiṇāmamṛtopamam |
       
       vṛkāḥ śṛgālā ṛkṣāḥ śvasiṃhavyāghrāssasūkarāḥ ||  
 6.4.27  eṇaśabdena dātavyā nānādravyābhisaṃskṛtāḥ |
       
       gṛdhrān sahaṃsānulūkānmaṇḍūkāñśyenavāyasān ||  
 6.4.28  dadyādbarhiṇaśabdena madyaṃ ca niyataṃ pibet |
       
       ākhumārjāralopākān  dvijihvāñśalyakānapi ||  
 6.4.29 nakulāṃstāmracūḍāṃś ca bhakṣayecca 
      susaṃskṛtān |
       
       anyamāṃsopadeśena māṃsāny etāni dāpayet ||  
 6.4.30  jugupsayā vamati vā pāde ' tyavahito  bhavet |
       
       tasmād rahasyasiddhāni māṃsāny etāni bhakṣayet ||  
 6.4.31  bileśayakravyabhujāṃ bhiṣaṅ māṃsāni lābhataḥ |
       
       toyadroṇeṣu daśasu tulāmatha vipācayet ||  
 6.4.32  aṣṭabhāgāvaśiṣṭantu rasaṃ visrāvayed bhiṣak |
       
       garbheṇa jīvanīyānāṃ sarpirdroṇaṃ vipācayet ||  
 6.4.33  tatpibenmātrataḥ sarpirmāṃsaṃ tenaiva sādhayet |
       
       kāsaṃ śvāsaṃ sahṛdrogaṃ jvaraṃ pārśvarujām api ||  
 6.4.34  śvayathuṃ svarabhedaṃ ca śoṣiṇāmapakarṣati |
       
       pañcamūlaṃ  mahaddhrasvaṃ golomīṃ madhukaṃ balām ||  
 6.4.35  vipācayejjaladroṇe caturbhāgāvaśeṣitam |
       
       tatkaṣāyaṃ jalaṃ pūtaṃ ghṛtaprasthaṃ vipācayet ||  
 6.4.36  caturguṇena payasā jīvanīyaiś ca peṣitaiḥ |
       
       vidāryāmalakānāṃ tu tathaivekṣo  rasasya ca ||  
 6.4.37  dadyād ghṛtasamān bhāgān tatpacenmṛdunā ' gninā ||
      rasāyanīyam iti tat khyātaṃ sarpirbalāvaham ||  
 6.4.38  hṛdrogakṣatakāsānāṃ kṣayāṇāṃ ca nivāraṇam |
       
       ataḥ sarpirguḍaṃ kuryāc charkarāmadhusaṃyutam ||  
 6.4.39  godhūmacūrṇena saha modakānvāpi kārayet |
       
       pūrvokteṣu vikāreṣu śoṣiṇāmamṛtopamam ||  
 6.4.40  kṣīrānupānaṃ bhakṣyāste modakā balavardhanāḥ |
       
       madyānupānāssevyāste śoṣaḥ śleṣmādhiko yadi ||  
 6.4.41  prasthārdhaṃ dhautaluñcitatilānāṃ 
      kalkapeṣitam |
       
       toyaprasthena saṃyojya ghṛtaprasthaṃ vipācayet ||  
 6.4.42  atha siddhaṃ ca pūtaṃ ca punastadvipaced ghṛtam |
       
       saha kravyādamāṃsena kṣīreṇeha ca sarvaśaḥ ||  
 6.4.43  bilvamātreṇa piṇḍena bhāvitena sadāmbunā |
       
       jāṅgalena ca māṃsena sukṛtena vidhānavit ||  
 6.4.44  atha siddhaṃ ca pūtaṃ ca punaragnāvadhiśrayet |
       
       prasthena payasā sārdhaṃ samyagikṣurasāḍhake ||  
 6.4.45  vidārīṃ mudgaparṇīṃ ca māṣaparṇīṃ kaserukam |
       
       śṛṅgāṭakamṛṇālāni padmabījaṃ sajīvakam ||  
 6.4.46  kṣīraśuklāṃ saṛṣabhāṃ medāṃ samadhukāṃ tathā |
       
       payasyāṃ kṣīrakākolīṃ kandaṃ nīlotpalasya ca ||  
 6.4.47  saha tālakadambena kalkāṃstānakṣasammitān |
       
       tasminnāloḍya tat sarvaṃ vipacenmṛdunāgninā ||  
 6.4.48  tatsiddhaṃ srāvayitvā tu nirvātaṃ syādyathāmṛtam |
       
       tataḥ prātarghanībhūtaṃ khajenābhipramanthayet ||  
 6.4.49  athātra śarkarācūrṇaṃ pañcāśatpalasammitam |
       
       mathyamānaṃ tato dadyāddattvā dattvā ca manthayet ||  
 6.4.50  gandhārthaṃ cātra deyaṃ syāccūrṇaṃ tvaṅnāgapuṣpayoḥ
      |
       
       ekībhūtaṃ tathā rātrimekāṃ  parivasedatha ||  
 6.4.51  akṣapramāṇasaṃsthānāḥ kāryās tu modakās tathā |
       
       yavagodhūmacūrṇābhyāṃ tugākṣīryā ca cūrṇitān  ||  
 6.4.52  bhakṣayenmodakān kāle kṣīrapānaṃ pibetpunaḥ |
       
       yakṣmāṇaṃ śamayantyete vṛkṣamindrāśaniryathā ||  
 6.4.53 asṛgdaraṃ kṣataṃ kṣīṇaṃ hṛdrogaṃ viṣamajvaram |
       
       unmāda raktapittaṃ ca kāsaṃ caitena sādhayet ||  
 6.4.54  aśvatthasyātha mūlāni śuṅgāni saphalāni ca |
       
       śatāvarīṃ pṛśniparṇīṃ bṛhatīṃ kaṇṭakārikām  ||  
 6.4.55  golomīṃ  śreyasīṃ kālāṃ śāribāṃ sapunarnavām |
       
       kṣīradroṇeṣu daśasu kuṭṭitāni vipācayet ||  
 6.4.56 tacchṛtaṃ śītalaṃ
      pūtaṃ khajenābhipramanthayet |
       
       yattatra sarpirjāyeta taduddhṛtya vipācayet ||  
 6.4.57  bhaiṣajyāni ca piṣṭāni tatremāni samācaret |
       
       madhukaṃ madhuliṃ drākṣāṃ medāṃ vṛṣabhajīrakau ||  
 6.4.58  tālamajjāṃ salāmajjaṃ tathā puṣkarabījakam |
       
       jīvanīṃ trāyamāṇāṃ ca madhukāni kaśerukam ||  
 6.4.59  nīlotpalaṃ puṇḍarīkaṃ vārtākānapi coccaṭām |
       
       kāśmaryāmalakekṣūṇāṃ vidāryāḥ svarasaṃ  ca vā ||  
 6.4.60  tatsiddhaṃ dāpayet pūtaṃ kalaśe rājate dṛḍhe |
       
       tulārdhaṃ śarkarāyāś ca dattvā caivābhimanthayet ||  
 6.4.61  prakṣipec ca tugākṣīryāḥ prasthaṃ prasthaṃ ca mākṣikāt |
       
       ātmaguptāphalasya  syād guḍasya maricasya ca ||  
 6.4.62  uccaṭīkṣurasābhyāṃ ca dvau prasthau tatra dāpayet |
       
       tvagelānāgapuṣpāṇāṃ cūrṇaṃ tatra pradāpayet ||  
 6.4.63  palikān modakān kṛtvā sthāpayenmṛṇmaye  nave |
       
       aśnīyāttatpalaṃ kalyaṃ sāyaṃ bhūyaḥ palaṃ naraḥ ||  
 6.4.64  śayanaṃ mṛdu seveta brahmacārī samāhitaḥ |
       
       karmaṇānena niyataṃ yakṣmāṇamapakarṣati ||  
 6.4.65  saṃbṛhayati śuṣkaṃ ca puruṣaṃ durbalendriyam
      |
       
       vājīkaraṇamapyetannarāṇāṃ kṣīṇaretasām ||  
 6.4.66  strībhir hatā bhārahatāḥ jīrṇāś cātītayauvanāḥ |
       
       kṣīṇamāṃsāḥ kṣīṇabalāḥ ye cātha kṣīṇaśoṇitāḥ ||  
 6.4.67  pittaroge raktapitte śoṣe doṣajvare tathā |
       
       hatendriyā naṣṭaśuklāḥ saktakaṇṭhāś ca ye smṛtāḥ ||  
 6.4.68  aśaktamandakā ye ca ratinaṣṭendriyā narāḥ |
       
       punarnavāṃstānkurute yogo ' yamamṛtopamaḥ ||  
 6.4.69  apasmārānathonmādān hṛdrogānapatantrakam  |
       
       tejo vāpahṛtaṃ yeṣāṃ bhūtadharmeṇa kenacit ||  
 6.4.70  kṣīrānupānāttanvanti sadyaḥ poṣaṃ hi modakāḥ |
       
 vyākulātyalpādhātūnāṃ śoṣiṇāṃ mandadehinām ||  
 6.4.71  api yogaśatenāpi duḥkham eva cikitsitam |
       
       tasmād rasāyanavidhiṃ vardhamāne kṣaye bhiṣak ||  
 6.4.72  saṃvatsaraṃ paramṛtumayanaṃ vā samācaret |
       
       pippalīvardhamānaṃ tu pañcapañcavivardhitam  ||  
 6.4.73 nasye cābhyañjane pāne praśastaṃ bastikarmaṇi |
       
       vātavyādhiṣu sarveṣu kṣatakṣīṇe śirograhe ||  
 6.4.74  pārśvaśūle pramehe ca gulme sārśobhagandare |
       
       cyutabhagnāṅgahīnānāṃ kāse śvāse ca hṛdgrahe ||  
 6.4.75  jvarātisāreṣv arucau varṇabhede svarakṣaye |
       
       sukumāram idaṃ tailaṃ bālavṛddhasukhāvaham ||  
 6.4.76  etaddhi vṛṣyaṃ balyaṃ ca māsānmāṃsavivardhanam |
       
       svaravarṇakaraṃ caiva śoṣiṇāmamṛtopamam ||  
 6.4.77 niṣpākaś cāsya tailasya samyak siddhasya yo bhavet
      |
       
       udaśvidiva dadhyarthaṃ so ' pi kṛtyakaro bhavet ||  
 6.4.78  ekādaśa ca ṣaṭ caiva śoṣajā ya upadravāḥ |
       
       sukumāraṃ praśamayenmedho ' gnīniva vṛṣṭimān ||  
 6.4.79  luñcitānāṃ tilānāṃ tu tailaprasthaṃ vipācayet |
       
       palaṃ tu madhukasyātra garbhaṃ kṣīraṃ caturguṇam ||  
 6.4.80 mṛdupākaṃ ca tatsiddhaṃ bhūya eva vipācayet |
       
       caturguṇena payasā madhukasya palena ca ||  
 6.4.81  etena vidhinā caiva madhukasya śataṃ pacet |
       
       śatakṛtvo vipakvantu śatapākam iti smṛtam ||  
 6.4.82  pānābhyañjananasyeṣu bastau vyañjanasādhane  |
       
       bhojane cāmṛtaprakhyaṃ narāṇāṃ rājayakṣmiṇām ||  
 6.4.83  hṛdrogaṃ tāluśoṣaṃ ca pārśvaśūlaṃ pratānakam |
       
       tṛṣṇāmunmādavīsarpaṃ kāsaṃ śvāsamasṛgdaram ||  
 6.4.84  raktapittaṃ pravṛddhaṃ ca sarvato bhāgamūrcchitam |
       
       kāmalāṃ pāṇḍurogaṃ ca pānādetanniyacchati ||  
 6.4.85 mukhapākākṣipākau  ca bādhiryaṃ karṇavedanām
      |
       
       naktāndhyaṃ timiraṃ  kācaṃ liṅganāśaṃ sirācayam ||  
 6.4.86  biḍālikāṃ pūtinasyaṃ śirorogaṃ śirograham |
       
 nastaḥ kṛtaṃ praṇudati khālity aṃ palitāni ca ||  
 6.4.87  adhobhāge raktapitte raktārśassu bhagandare |
       
       sarvagātragate vāte raktapittasamudbhave ||  
 6.4.88  aprajassu  ca nārīṣu puṃsāṃ naṣṭe ca retasi |
       
 jānutrikādikubjeṣu praśastaṃ bastikarmaṇi ||  
 6.4.89  bahūparodhāḥ strīnity āḥ teṣāṃ vṛṣyatamaṃ matam |
       
       prayogeṇa prayuktaṃ ca rasāyanamanuttamam ||  
 6.4.90  sahasrapākam ity etat kalpenaitena sādhayet |
       
       rasāyanamidaṃ prāhurnṛṇāṃ varṣasahasrakṛt  ||  
 6.4.91  aśvagandhā hy apāmārgo nākulī gaurasarṣapāḥ |
       
       tilā bilvaṃ ca kalkaṃ syāt tatra rakṣayonmardanaṃ param ||  
 6.4.92  maṅgalācārasaṃyukto bhavetsvastyayano naraḥ |
       
       snānāni śāntihomāṃś ca śoṣī nityaṃ samācarete ||  
 6.4.93  iṣṭayo vedavihitā nāśanā rājayakṣmaṇaḥ |
       
       tāś ca nityaṃ niṣeveta pūjayed vṛṣabhadhvajam ||  
 6.4.94  upadravāś ca ye śeṣe ṣaṭ caikādaśa coditāḥ |
       
       teṣāṃ cikitsitaṃ kuryād yathā sve sve cikitsite ||  
 6.4.95  ity evaṃ prayatenoktaṃ rājyakṣacikitsitam |
       
       yaśaḥsvargakaraṃ puṇyaṃ śiṣyāṇāmarthasiddhaye || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele cikitsite caturtho ' dhyāyaḥ || || pañcamo ' dhyāyaḥ || athāto
      gulmacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |  
 
 
 6.5.1  pañca gulmāḥ samuddiṣṭā nidāneṣu savistaram |
       
       gulmatvaṃ teṣu vakṣyāmi cikitsāṃ tu pṛthak pṛthak ||  
 6.5.2  mārutaḥ kupito dehe srotāṃsyunnahya sarvaśaḥ |
       
       abhyāgatya dūṣayati pūrvaṃ pittaṃ kaphaṃ tataḥ ||  
 6.5.3  dūṣayatyatha raktaṃ ca medo māṃsaṃ vidhāvati |
       
       sa saṅghātasthirībhūto gulmatvam upapadyate ||  
 6.5.4  duṣṭānāṃ hantukāmānāṃ paraṃ prāṇabhṛtāṃ yathā |
       
       hastyaśvarathayānānāṃ saṃghāto gulma iṣyate ||  
 6.5.5  evaṃ dehe rasādīnāṃ dhātūnāṃ viprakarṣaṇam |
       
       saṃsargo gulma ity uktaḥ saṃghāto gulma ucyate ||  
 6.5.6 stambinistambinīnāṃ  tu vallīnāṃ vīrudhām api
      |
       
       saṃghāto gahanaṃ gulmaḥ tadvad gulmas tu dehinām ||  
 6.5.7  amūrtatvād dhi vātasya saṃvittirnopajāyate |
       
 sandhāya pittaśleṣmāṇau māruto gulmatāṃ vrajet ||  
 6.5.8  madhūcchiṣṭamayaṃ piṇḍaṃ cinvanti bhramarā yathā |
       
       tathā koṣṭheṣu pavano dhātūṃstānvicinoty api ||  
 6.5.9  sthānāni tasya gulmasya śaṃmanti gurulāghavam |
       
       kukṣikastigato gulmo vātabhūyiṣṭha ucyate ||  
 6.5.10  sa vātagulmarūpāṇi kuryāt sthānavaśena tu |
       
       tathaiva pittasthānasthaḥ pittarūpāṇi darśayet ||  
 6.5.11  evaṃ śleṣmaṇi rakte ca sannipāte ca sarvaśaḥ |
       
       sarveṣāṃ sannipāte tu svaṃ svaṃ rūpaṃ nidarśanam ||  
 6.5.12  āganturdūṣayatyatra dhātuṃ sthānastha ulbaṇaḥ
      |
       
       cikitsitaṃ tu sthānasya sa hi tatra balādhikaḥ ||  
 6.5.13  yadi vastigataḥ pākaṃ vātagulmas tu gacchati |
       
 hṛnnābhyor antaraṃ gulmaḥ pākaṃ gacchati paittikaḥ ||  
 6.5.14  hṛdi ca śleṣmagulmas tu pākaṃ yāty ananuṣṭhitaḥ |
       
       pacyate sannipātāt tu gulmaśśoṇitajas tathā ||  
 6.5.15  doṣadvayena saṃsṛṣṭāḥ sarve gulmāḥ pramāthinaḥ |
       
 tasmāt teṣāṃ bhedanīyāḥ kriyāssarvāḥ prayojayet |
       
       atyarthaṃ snihyamāno ' pi gulmo vṛddhim avāpnuyāt ||  
 6.5.16  atas tu vātagulmasya pravakṣyāmi cikitsitam |
       
       prabhurhi sarvabhūtānāṃ vāyuḥ prāṇeśvaro balī ||  
 6.5.17 harītakī trikaṭukaṃ vacā kaṭukarohiṇī 
      |
       
       sauvarcalaṃ yavakṣāro viḍaṅgaṃ citrakas tathā ||  
 6.5.18  akṣapramāṇairetais tu ghṛtaprasthaṃ vipācayet |
       
 tasmiddhaṃ srāvayitvā tu pāyayet tu yathābalam ||  
 6.5.19  vātagulmaṃ krimiṃ kāsaṃ śvāsaṃ plīhānam eva ca |
       
       daśāṅgaṃ nāśayatyetadrogān vajramivāsurān ||  
 6.5.20 dvepañcamūlyau suṣavīmaśvagandhāṃ punarnavām |
       
       kālāṃ chinnaruhāṃ rāsnāṃ bhārṅgīṃ gokṣurakaṃ  balām ||  
 6.5.21  śaṭiṃ puṣkaramūlaṃ ca palāśaṃ gandhasaṃjñakam |
       
       eteṣāṃ dvipalān bhagān jaladroṇe vipācayet ||  
 6.5.22  kolānāṃ sakulutthānāṃ māṣāṇāṃ ca yavaissaha |
       
       prasthaṃ prasthaṃ pṛthak kṛtvā tasminn eva samāvapet ||  
 6.5.23  tena pādāvaśiṣṭena ghṛtaprasthaṃ vipācayet |
       
       dadhyādibhis samaṃ śuktamāranālaṃ tuṣodakam ||  
 6.5.24 dāḍimāmrātakarasaṃ mātuluṅgarasaṃ tathā |
       
       caturguṇaṃ cātra dadhi garbhe caiṣāṃ samāvapet ||  
 6.5.25  kāravīṃ tryūṣaṇaṃ dantīṃ trīṇyeva lavaṇāni ca |
       
       hiṃsrāṃ rāsnāṃ vacāṃ caiva yavānīmamlavetasam ||  
 6.5.26  viḍaṅgaṃ dāḍimaṃ hiṅgu nīlikāṃ trivṛtām api |
       
       dvau kṣārau cājamodāṃ ca pāṭhāṃ pāṣāṇabhedakam ||  
 6.5.27 ūṣakaṃ vṛṣakaṃ bhārṅgīṃ śvadaṃṣṭrāṃ hapuṣām api |
       
 trapusorvārubījāni śatavīryopakuñcike  ||  
 6.5.28  ajājīṃ citrakaṃ mūrvāṃ tumburuṃ gajapippalīm |
       
       dhānyakaṃ surasaṃ caiva dadyādakṣeṇa sammitam ||  
 6.5.29  garbheṇānena  tatsiddhaṃ pāyayetsarpiruttamam |
       
 raktagulmādṛte sarvān gulmānetatpraṇāśayet ||  
 6.5.30  ekāṅgage pakṣagate gṛdhrasyāṃ plīhni caiva hi |
       
       hṛdroge grahaṇīdoṣe vātagulme ca dāruṇe ||  
 6.5.31  dādhikaṃ nāma vikhyātaṃ sarpiretanmahāguṇam |
       
       unmādaṃ  koṣṭhaśūlāni cāpasmāraṃ ca nāśayet ||  
 6.5.32  yāvaśūkaṃ tathā kṣāraṃ saindhavaṃ hastipippalīm |
       
       pippalīṃ śṛṅgaberaṃ ca maricaṃ ca samāvapet ||  
 6.5.33  eṣāṃ ṣaṇṇāṃ ṣaḍeva syuḥ pṛthagbhāgāḥ palaṃ palam |
       
       eṣāmardhapalān bhāgān kaṣāyam upasādhayet ||  
 6.5.34  peṣyairardhapalīnais tu ghṛtaprasthaṃ vipācayet |
       
       snehatulyaṃ kaṣāyaṃ tu kṣīraṃ taddviguṇaṃ bhavet ||  
 6.5.35  ity etat ṣaṭpalaṃ nāma sarpirgulmavināśanam |
       
       plīhānamarśāṃsi tathā grahaṇīdoṣam eva ca ||  
 6.5.36  vastikuṇḍalavardhmāni  pānādevāpakarṣati |
       
       eṣāmanyatamaiḥ svehaiḥ snehitaṃ vātagulminam |
       
       virecanena snigdhena yuktyā saṃśodhayed bhiṣak ||  
 6.5.37  ghṛtaṃ ca saktuṃ ca tathā citrakaṃ saindhavaṃ vacām
      |
       
       pippalīṃ ca pacetkṣīraṃ praśastaṃ cāvatārayet ||  
 6.5.38  tato biḍālapadakaṃ pibeduṣṇena vāriṇā |
       
       ghṛtena payasā vāpi madyenoṣṇena vāriṇā ||  
 6.5.39  vātagulmaṃ nudatyeṣa gulmaśūlāni yāni ca |
       
       saplīhānamudāvartaṃ śleṣmagulmaṃ ca nāśayet ||  
 6.5.40  mahauṣadhaṃ devadāru vāsā kaṭukarohiṇī |
       
 citrakaḥ pippalīmūlaṃ pippalyo hastipippalī ||  
 6.5.41  kuṣṭhaṃ ca sarpagandhā ca pañcaiva lavaṇāni ca |
       
       dvau kṣārau trivṛtā dantī dravantī copakuñcikā ||  
 6.5.42  eṣāmardhapalān bhāgān lavaṇānāṃ palaṃ palam |
       
       cūrṇāni dadhnaḥ prasthārdhe  samāloḍya vipācayet ||  
 6.5.43  vasātailaghṛtānāṃ ca prasthaṃ prasthaṃ pradāpayet |
       
       pradīptaṃ ca yathāśāntamathainamavatārayet ||  
 6.5.44  tato biḍālapadakaṃ pibeduṣṇena vāriṇā |
       
       ghṛtena payasā vāpi madyenāmlena vā punaḥ ||  
 6.5.45  eṣa kṣārāgado nāma vātagulmavināśanaḥ |
       
       plīhānamarśaḥśūlāni vardhmodāvartakuṇḍalam ||  
 6.5.46  krimīn sagrahaṇīdoṣān viṣān vātāpatānakau |
       
       sarpamūṣakadaṃśāṃś ca granthitān gadayojitān ||  
 6.5.47  vātaśleṣmasamutthānaṃ  sannipātātmakaṃ  tathā
      |
       
       prasahya nāśayed gulmaṃ chinnābhrāṇīva mārutaḥ || vandhyā ca labhate garbhaṃ
      garānapi ca naśayet |
       
       apasmārānathonmādān 
 
  || ṣaṣṭho ' dhyāyaḥ ||  
 
 
 
 
 6.6.1  | pittaṃ bhṛśaṃ
      dehe prakupyati |
       
       tatpraduṣṭaṃ dūṣayati raktamāṃsamatholbaṇam ||  
 6.6.2  tatra kuṣṭhāni jāyante dehe bahuvidhāni tu |
       
       teṣāṃ rūpāṇi vakṣyāmi cikitsāṃ ca yathākramam ||  
 6.6.3  doṣāṇāṃ sañcitānāṃ tu tvaṅmāṃsācchāsracāriṇām |
       
       pradūṣaṇaṃ  hi sarveṣāṃ kuṣṭham ity abhidhīyate ||  
 6.6.4  viruddhamāhārayato+ apyajīrṇādhyaśanena ca |
       
       chardimūtrapurīṣāṇāṃ vegānāṃ ca vidhāraṇāt ||  
 6.6.5  grāmyānūpaudakaṃ māṃsaṃ śākaṃ haritakāni ca |
       
       madyamamlamathātyarthaṃ sevitvā yaḥ pibetpayaḥ ||  
 6.6.6  bhuktvā vāpy uṣṇamāhāraṃ madhu māṃsaṃ ca sevate |
       
       madyaṃ madhu ca yaḥ pītvāt yuṣṇamannaṃ ca sevate ||  
 6.6.7  vidagdhabhukto yaś cāpi grāmyadharma niṣevate |
       
       uṣṇātapāmyāṃ sahasā yaś cāpy apsu nimajjati ||  
 6.6.8 tasyoṣmā sanniruddhas tu prakopayati mārutam |
       
       udīrayati vāyus tu dūṣito doṣasaṃcayān  ||  
 6.6.9  doṣāśśirāḥ prapannāste rudhiraṃ dūṣayantyati |
       
       raktamāṃsaniruddhās tu vātapittakaphāstrayaḥ ||  
 6.6.10  janayanty āśu kuṣṭhāni nṛṇāmaṣṭādaśaiva tu |
       
       nidāneṣv api nirdiṣṭaṃ nidānaṃ sāptakuṣṭhikam ||  
 6.6.11  aṣṭādaśa tu kuṣṭhāni teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam |
       
       yatkuṣṭhamaruṇābhāsaṃ śyāmaṃ  rūkṣaṃ savedanam ||  
 6.6.12  pipīlikākīrṇamiva  karkaśaṃ cāpi vātikam |
       
       kṣipramuttiṣṭhate yas tu dūṣyate paridahyate ||  
 6.6.13  tāmraṃ śyāvaprakupitaṃ sajvaraṃ cāpi paittikam |
       
       samutpanneṣu vā teṣu stimitaṃ bahulaṃ guru ||  
 6.6.14  pāṇḍu snigdhaṃ ca guru ca yatkuṣṭhaṃ śleṣmasambhavam |
       
       sphuṭitaṃ srāvabahulaṃ dāharāgarujānvitam ||  
 6.6.15  tvagromanakhamāṃsaiś ca dīryadbhis sānnipātikam |
       
       prādurbhaviṣyatāṃ  caiva pūrvarūpāṇi me śṛṇu ||  
 6.6.16  tāni saṃlakṣya medhāvī cikitsitamupācaret |
       
       ūṣmāyaṇaṃ parītāpaḥ svedo raukṣyaṃ vivarṇatā ||  
 6.6.17  suptatvaṃ romaharṣaś ca gātrāṇāṃ gauravaṃ klamaḥ |
       
       rāgaḥ pipāsā daurbalyaṃ davathuḥ piṭakādayaḥ ||  
 6.6.18 tataḥ kuṣṭhāni jāyante teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam |
       
       svedanaṃ kākaṇābhāsaṃ  samuptannaṃ  savedanam ||  
 6.6.19  sphuṭitaṃ nīlaparyantaṃ kākaṇaṃ kuṣṭhamucyate |
       
       udumbaranibhairyat tu maṇḍalairbahubhiścitam ||  
 6.6.20  nirāsrāvaiḥ sravadbhir vā vidyādaudumbaraṃ tu tat |
       
       maṇḍalairbandhujīvābhair utsannaiś ca vidāhibhiḥ ||  
 6.6.21  vidyānmaṇḍalakuṣṭhaṃ tadvedanācoṣaṇānvitam |
       
       rśyajihvopamaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ ṛśyajihvaṃ vibhāvayet ||  
 6.6.22  puṇḍarīkadalābhāsaṃ puṇḍarīkaṃ tu tadviduḥ |
       
       alābupuṣpasadṛśaṃ sidhmaṃ kuṣṭhamudāhṛtam ||  
 6.6.23  kapālakuṣṭhaṃ kṛṣṇantu maṇḍalaiḥ paruṣaṃ tathā |
       
       carmakuṣṭhaṃ tu bahulaṃ hasticarmanibhaṃ kharam ||  
 6.6.24  sasphoṭakā sasantāpā pāmā kaṇḍūrujānvitā |
       
       dṛḍhaṃ punaḥ prasravati kaṇḍūrodhānvitaṃ ca yat ||  
 6.6.25  vartate ca samutpannaṃ kiṭibaṃ tatprakīrtitam |
       
       śyāvā raktā samutpannā praklinnā srāviṇī tathā ||  
 6.6.26  māṃsenopacitā yuktā vijñeyā sā vicarcikā |
       
       pariśuṣkāṇi rūkṣāṇi kaṇḍūrāṇi ghanāni ca ||  
 6.6.27  maṇḍalānyunnatāgrāṇi dudrukuṣṭhaṃ hi tatsmṛtam |
       
 aruḍbhiścīyamānaṃ tu nīlalohitakaiḥ kharaiḥ ||  
 6.6.28  bahubhiś ca sravadbhiś ca śatāruṣkantu tadviduḥ |
       
 śāliśūkapratīkāśairlomabhiḥ śuklalohitam ||  
 6.6.29  anyonyairmaṇḍalairviddhaṃ śvitraṃ tadupapādayet |
       
       mīnamūṣikakīṭānāṃ viṣavegena dūṣitam ||  
 6.6.30  sakaṇḍūrāgapiṭakaṃ viṣajaṃ śyāmam eva vā |
       
       pāṇipādatalāṅguṣṭhapārṣṇideśeṣu  jāyate ||  
 6.6.31  sphuṭitaṃ vedanādāhayuktaṃ vaipādikaṃ smṛtam |
       
       udumbarasavarṇaṃ tu samutpannaṃ savedanam ||  
 6.6.32 picchārāgavivarṇaṃ ca kuṣṭhaṃ sthūlāruruvyate |
       
       visarpaissaṃparikrāntaṃ vikūṇaṃ saparisravam ||  
 6.6.33  tad ekakuṣṭham ity uktam ekaṃ vīsarpasambhavam |
       
 etānyaṣṭādaśoktāni kuṣṭhānīha svalakṣaṇaiḥ ||  
 6.6.34 nava teṣāmasādhyāni cikitsyāni tathaiva ca |
       
       puṇḍarīkamatha śvitraṃ ṛṣyajihvaṃ sakākaṇam ||  
 6.6.35  udumbaraśatāruṣkaṃ carmakuṣṭhaṃ ca yatsmṛtam |
       
       ekakuṣṭhaṃ tu yatproktaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ vaipādikaṃ ca yat ||  
 6.6.36  etāni nava kuṣṭhāni na sidhyanti kadācana |
       
       sidhmaṃ vicarcikā pāmā dadruś ca kiṭikāni ca ||  
 6.6.37  kapālakuṣṭhaṃ sthūlārurmaṇḍalaṃ viṣajaṃ ca yat |
       
       etāni nava sādhyāni kuṣṭhānyāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ ||  
 6.6.38  karmajāni nava hyeṣāṃ doṣajāni navaiva tu |
       
       karmajāni na sidhyanti sidhyanti hītarāṇi tu ||  
 6.6.39  ātmavānmucyate tebhyaḥ kuśalena svanuṣṭhitaḥ |
       
 raktodbhavāni kuṣṭhāni sannipātodbhavāni ca ||  
 6.6.40  tasmāt teṣāṃ prathamataḥ sirākarma vidhīyate |
       
 kuṣṭhasyātyalpato nyāyyaṃ bahuśaḥ pracchanaṃ smṛtam ||  
 6.6.41  jalūkālābuśṛṅgair vā śoṇitaṃ tasya smṛtam |
       
       śṛṇu raktavikārāṃs tu pṛthagdhātusamāśritān ||  
 6.6.42  saphenamaruṇaṃ rūkṣaṃ vātikaṃ śoṇitaṃ tanu |
       
       nīlapītāsitaṃ taptaṃ raktaṃ pittānvitaṃ smṛtam ||  
 6.6.43  vijjalaṃ pāṇḍuraṃ snigdhaṃ tantumacca  kaphātmakam
      |
       
       sarveṣāṃ darśane  vidyācchoṇitaṃ sānnipātikam ||  
 6.6.44  indragopakasaṅkāśamaduṣṭaṃ raktamucyate |
       
       narasya muktaraktasya pratibhuktavatas tathā ||  
 6.6.45 siddhairghṛtaiḥ snehitasya kuryāt saṃśodhanaṃ tataḥ
      |
       
       vamanaṃ recanaṃ caiva tathā śīrṣavirecanam || āsthāpanaṃ ca kurvīta na
      cainamanuvāsayet ||  
 6.6.46  śālīna saṣṭaṣṭikāṃś caiva jāṅgalāṃś ca mṛgadvijān |
       
 yavānnavikṛtīś caiva kuṣṭhī nityaṃ samācaret ||  
 6.6.47 grāmyānūpaudakaṃ māṃsamikṣustilaghṛtaṃ surā |
       
       dadhi dugdhaṃ divāsvapnaḥ phalānyamlāni miathunam ||  
 6.6.48  mūlakaṃ piṣṭavikṛtirvasā haritakāni ca |
       
       kaphaṃ pittaṃ ca raktaṃ ca sarvametatprakopayet ||  
 6.6.49  evaṃvidhāni cānnāni hyabhiṣyandakarāṇi ca |
       
 ajīrṇādhyaśanaṃ caiva kuṣṭhī nityaṃ vivarjayet ||  
 6.6.50  dhānvantaraṃ pibetsarpiḥ svehanārhteṣu kuṣṭhitaḥ |
       
       mahadvai pañcagavyaṃ vā tailaṃ śairīṣam eva vā ||  
 6.6.51  pippalīvardhamānaṃ vā mākṣikeṇa samācaret |
       
       ariṣṭamabhayāriṣṭaṃ gaṇḍīrāriṣṭam eva vā ||  
 6.6.52  muṣṭiṃ khadirasārasya kuṭṭitaṃ pratibhojayet |
       
       tryahaṃ śṛtaṃ pibettac ca snāyādudvartayet tataḥ  ||  
 6.6.53  tena siddhaṃ ca bhuñjīta pānīyārthaṃ ca kārayet |
       
       pakṣaṃ māsamṛtuṃ  vāpi ṣaṇmāsānevamācaret ||  
 6.6.54  prasadya khadiro hanti kuṣṭhāni sugurūṇy api |
       
       saṃvṛddho lokaparyāye yugāntāgnirnagāniva ||  
 6.6.55 pañcābhayās tu savyoṣāḥ saguḍā vāpi cūrṇitāḥ |
       
 lihyāt pathyāśanaḥ kuṣṭhaśāntirvā nacirādbhavet ||  
 6.6.56  gomūtreṇa haridrāṃ tu rasāñjanamathāpi vā |
       
       prayogeṇa pibetkuṣṭhī tathā rogātpramucyate ||  
 6.6.57  drākṣā haridrā mañjiṣṭhā triphalā devadāru ca |
       
       nāgaraṃ pañcamūlyau dve mustā madhurasā tathā ||  
 6.6.58  saptaparṇo hy apāmārgaḥ picumandāṭarūṣakau  |
       
       viḍaṅgaṃ citrakaṃ dantī pippalyo maricāni ca ||  
 6.6.59  teṣāṃ tu samabhāgānāṃ kuṣṭhī cūrṇapalaṃ pibet |
       
       māsaṃ gomūtrasaṃyuktaṃ tathā kuṣṭhātpramucyate ||  
 6.6.60  uṣṭrīkṣīraṃ pibejjīrṇe kṣīravṛttirbhaven naraḥ  |
       
       jātakrimīṇi kuṣṭhāni cyutaromanakhāny api ||  
 6.6.61  api vā śīrṇamāṃsāni kṣīramauṣṭraṃ vināśayet |
       
       etās tv ābhyantarāḥ proktāḥ kriyāḥ kuṣṭhanibarhaṇāḥ ||  
 6.6.62  bāhyāṃ kriyāṃ pravakṣyāmi vistareṇa nibodha me |
       
 ālepanāni kurvīta muktaraktasya dehinaḥ ||  
 6.6.63  vighṛṣya śastraiḥ patrair vā gomayair api vā punaḥ |
       
       tataḥ kuṣṭhāni lepyāni pralepaiḥ kuṣṭhanāśanaiḥ ||  
 6.6.64  svarjakākuṣṭhatuthāni viḍaṅgamaricāni ca |
       
       manaḥśilā ca lodhraṃ ca lepaḥ kuṣṭhavināśanaḥ ||  
 6.6.65  avalgujaphalaṃ dantīṃ śyonākaṃ gajapippalīm |
       
       citrakau sarṣapau dvau tu haridre dve vipeṣayet ||  
 6.6.66  mātuluṅgarasainaitatsamāloḍya nikhānayet |
       
       saptarātrātparaṃ caiva kuṣṭhānāṃ lepanaṃ param ||  
 6.6.67 dadruṃ kapālakuṣṭāni kiṭikāni vicarcikām |
       
       sthūlāruṣkāṇi viṣajaṃ sidhmāni ca niyacchati ||  
 6.6.68  karavīro lāṅgalikī dantī hiṃsrā śukānanā |
       
       citrakārkastrikaṭukaṃ triphalā kaṭurohiṇī ||  
 6.6.69  kośātakī bhadramustā bṛhatī sarṣapā vacā |
       
       karañjabījaṃ sudhā ca svarṇakṣīrī nidigdhikā ||  
 6.6.70  picumandaś ca jātyāhvaḥ  pīlutilvakapallavam |
       
       saudhāmalakabījāni karṇikārohyavalgujaḥ || Bhṣ6.6.? |
       
       | bhallātakam  |
       
  || saptamo ' dhyāyaḥ ||  
 
 
 
 
 6.7.1 striyaṃ ca yuktyā seveta divāsvapnaṃ ca varjayet |
       
       kaṣāyasnānanity asya kaṣāyodakasevinaḥ ||  
 6.7.2  viśeṣataḥ śleṣmamehān tīkṣṇair eva samācaret |
       
       sakaṣāyaṃ ca tiktaṃ ca paittikeṣu prayojayet ||  
 6.7.3  asādhyavātajānmehāṃścaturaḥ parivarjayet |
       
 aruciś cāṅgamardaś ca tṛṣṇākāsau bhramastamaḥ ||  
 6.7.4  śūlāni piṭakā kaṇḍūḥ pramehāṇām upadravāḥ |
       
       akriyābhiḥ prameheṣu piṭakāsv apikārayet ||  
 6.7.5  upadravaiś ca yuktānāṃ piṭakābhis tathaiva ca |
       
       pramehiṇāmidaṃ proktaṃ mayā bhaiṣajyam uttamam ||  
 6.7.6  vyastairetaissamastaiś ca yo gais tu pravibhāgaśaḥ |
       
       cikitsāṃ kalpayed vaidyo yathādoṣaṃ yathābalam ||  
 6.7.7 viṃśatermūtrarogāṇāṃ lakṣaṇāni nirīkṣya tu |
       
       doṣasaṃsargahetūṃś ca tato yogān prakalpayet ||  
 6.7.8  uddeśamātraṃ teṣāṃ tu tasmād vakṣyāmi bheṣajam |
       
       bhūyo mūtrapraśāntyarthaṃ pravibhāgaṃ ca tacchṛṇu ||  
 6.7.9  śatāvarīmūlarasaḥ samāṃśo madhusarpiṣā |
       
 ikṣumehe tu pātavyaḥ kaphapittapraśāntaye ||  
 6.7.10  kirātatiktasvarasaḥ paṭolārukayos tathā |
       
       sakṣaudraḥ śamayenmehaṃ kvāthastūdakasaṃjñitam  ||  
 6.7.11  pippalī śṛṅgiberaṃ ca maricāni tathaiva ca |
       
       pibetsukhāmbunā hyetatsāndramehātpramucyate ||  
 6.7.12  cavyacitrakamūlāni pūtikasya tvacas tathā |
       
 khale yūṣeṣu saṃskṛtya bhuñjāno vai sukhī bhavet ||  
 6.7.13  kṣīrasiddhairyavairbhakṣyairyacchastaṃ hiṅgusaṃyutam |
       
       ghṛtaṃ prasaṅgena piban bhasmamehātpramucyate ||  
 6.7.14  kapitthaś cājamodā ca maricāni tathaiva ca |
       
       tato yutaṃ tairlavaṇaṃ kācaproktaṃ pradāpayet ||  
 6.7.15  pippalīkaṇasaṃyuktaṃ  madhuyuktaṃ saśarkaram |
       
       jayellavaṇamehantu pītaṃ śītena vāriṇā ||  
 6.7.16 mehayuktena bhoktavyaṃ sāndraprasravaṇena vā
      |
       
       etat tu vijayennityaṃ mehaṃ lavaṇasaṃbhavam ||  
 6.7.17  elāpravālakaṃ hiṅgu lavaṇaṃ ca samaṃ bhavet |
       
 madyenoṣṇena vā pītaṃ mehaṃ sasikataṃ jayet ||  
 6.7.18  tumburūṇi kapitthānāṃ niryāsaṃ kṣaudrasaṃyutam |
       
       śuklamehe praśaṃsanti yavānnasya ca sevanam ||  
 6.7.19  sakulutthāni yūṣāṇi sadravāṇi viśeṣataḥ |
       
       bhojyāni śuklameheṣu yavānnavikṛtis tathā ||  
 6.7.20  śvadaṃṣṭrādarbhamūlais tu kevalaṃ kvathitaṃ payaḥ |
       
       saśarkaraṃ pibejjantuḥ kṣāramehātpramucyate ||  
 6.7.21  drākṣāśṛtaṃ vāpi pibet tathā kṣīriśṛtaṃ naraḥ
      |
       
       pittamehātpramucyeta kṣāramehāc ca sarvaśaḥ ||  
 6.7.22 pītāmañjiṣṭhacūrṇau dvau mehanāc ca
      prayojayet |
       
       sakṣaudraṃ śītamehe tu yavānnopahitaṃ sadā ||  
 6.7.23  madayanty āś ca patrāṇāṃ kalkaṃ kṣaudrayutaṃ pibet |
       
       darbhamūlasya ca tathā raktamehī sukhī bhavet ||  
 6.7.24 pibet tu te sapayasī nīlamehātpramucyate |
       
       prarohaiḥ kṣīrivṛkṣāṇāṃ kṣīraṃ saṃkvathitaṃ pibet ||  
 6.7.25  saśarkareṇa mucyeta nīlamehāattu  paittikāt 
      |
       
       kumudotpaladaṇḍaiś ca sanālaiḥ kvathitais tathā ||  
 6.7.26  pibetprāyo yathāśakti vārimehātpramucyate |
       
       samāṃ kṣīrāśanaś cāpi yavānnamitabhojanaḥ ||  
 6.7.27  śarkarāsamabhāgaṃ tu kṣaudreṇa saha saṃsṛjet |
       
       śītena toyena pibannambumehātpramucyate ||  
 6.7.28  ity etat  ṣoḍaśānāṃ tu kaphapittaharaṃ pṛthak |
       
       cikitsitaṃ mayā proktaṃ pramehāṇāṃ vināśanam ||  
 6.7.29  asādhyā vātajāś caiva vijñeyā bhṛśadāruṇāḥ |
       
       avagādyātisūkṣmatvād dāyā prasravaṇaṃ śṛtam(?) ||  
 6.7.30  āsthāpanair vātaharaiḥ sukṛtaiś cānuvāsanaiḥ |
       
       majjapramehiṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā bahuśastamupācaret ||  
 6.7.31  prātaḥ prātaś ca seveta kevale madhusarpiṣī |
       
       koradūṣayavānnāni sthitāni ca viśeṣataḥ ||  
 6.7.32  hastimehaṃ jayed evaṃ vastisvedaiḥ prayatnataḥ |
       
       yatnavānvātamehaṃ hi bastamūtrāṇi vā caret ||  
 6.7.33  pāyayeccārayec cāpi gajamehaṃ bhayāvaham |
       
       kaṣāyaistiktakaṭukaiḥ rasairetaiḥ, pibetpayaḥ ||  
 6.7.34  śāstroktāmatha saṃprekṣya kriyāmetāṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ |
       
       yathāsvaṃ hi sampradhārya pramehān sādhayed bhiṣak ||  
 6.7.35  etatpramehikaṃ proktaṃ śiṣyāṇāmārthasiddhaye |
       
       cikitsitaṃ vistareṇa yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ ||  ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele cikitsite saptamo ' dhyāyaḥ || || aṣṭamo ' dhyāyaḥ || athāta 
      unmādacikitsitaṃ  vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 6.8.1  pañconmādās samākhyātā nidāneṣu savistarāḥ |
       
 saliṅgāssasamucthānāḥ śṛṇu teṣāṃ cikitsitam ||  
 6.8.2 cittabuddhīnriyāṇāṃ hi teṣām api viceṣṭitam |
       
       śirastālvantaragataṃ sarvendriyaparaṃ manaḥ ||  
 6.8.3  tatrasthaṃ taddhi viṣayānindriyāṇāṃ rasādikān |
       
       samīpasthān vijānāti trīn bhāvāṃś ca niyacchati ||  
 6.8.4 sumanaḥprabhavaṃ cāpi sarvendriyamayaṃ balam |
       
       kāraṇaṃ sarvabuddhīnāṃ cittaṃ hṛdayasaṃśritam ||  
 6.8.5  kriyāṇāṃ cetarāsāṃ  ca cittaṃ sarvatra 
      kāraṇam |
       
       sucittāssatpathaṃ yānti duścittās tu vimārgagāḥ ||  
 6.8.6 viditaṃ manasā cittamālabhya  prabhavet tataḥ
      |
       
       tato buddhiḥ prabhavati kāryākāryavicārikā ||  
 6.8.7  śubhāśubhaṃ hi kurvāṇā bodhanaṃ buddhiriṣyate |
       
       bodhanāc cāpi bodhyasya naro budha ihocyate ||  
 6.8.8  sā buddhiḥ paramātmā ca sa śarīre prakīrtitaḥ |
       
       yathā kṛtī karmakaraḥ kriyāṃ yojayate nṛṣu ||  
 6.8.9  manasaścittabuddhīnāṃ sthānāny etāni karma ca |
       
       sandūṣitānāṃ teṣāṃ tu śṛṇu hetumataḥ param ||  
 6.8.10  ūrdhvaṃ prakupitā doṣāḥ śirastālvantare sthitāḥ |
       
 manaḥ sandūṣayanty āśu tataścittaṃ vipadyate ||  
 6.8.11  citte vyāpadamāpanne buddhirnāśaṃ niyacchati |
       
       tatas tu buddhivyāpattau  kāryākāryaṃ na budhyate ||  
 6.8.12  evaṃ pravartate vyādhirunmādo nāma dāruṇaḥ |
       
       tasmād viśeṣaṃ vakṣyāmi hyunmādamadayor api ||  
 6.8.13  śokātkopāttathā harṣād dravyāṇāṃ ca vināśanāt |
       
       calite cittamanasi madamāśu niyacchati ||  
 6.8.14  pradhyāyati prasvipiti roditīhānimittataḥ |
       
       hasatyakasmānnidrāluralpavāṅ nityam utsukaḥ ||  
 6.8.15  trastaḥ śarīrī  krodhano nirapatrapaḥ  |
       
       purastādavalokī ca na yathāvṛtta eva ca ||  
 6.8.16  paruṣatvaṃ tathā lomnāmāvilaṃ cakṣuṣorapi |
       
       etāni yasya rūpāṇi sa mado nāma kīrtitaḥ ||  
 6.8.17  vivardhamānas tu mada unmādatvaṃ niyacchati |
       
       savātikāni rūpāṇi śleṣmapittodbhavāni ca ||  
 6.8.18 unmādastūcyate dhīraiḥ sannipātātmakāni ca |
       
       etallakṣaṇamuddiṣṭamunmādasya niruktitaḥ ||  
 6.8.19  nidāne pūrvamuddiṣṭaṃ śṛṇu teṣāṃ cikitsitam |
       
       snehitaṃ sveditaṃ caiva yojayetpañcakrmaṇā ||  
 6.8.20  dādhikaṃ vā pibetsarpistailaṃ śairīṣam eva vā |
       
       śatapākaṃ balātailaṃ mahāpaiśācikaṃ ghṛtam ||  
 6.8.21  dādhikaṃ ca mahākṣāramunmattaḥ śīlayet tathā |
       
 yac cikitsitam ākhyātam apasmāravināśanam ||  
 6.8.22  tad eva sarvaṃ nikhileṣūnmādeṣv avacārayet |
       
       ghātayet taṃ kaśābhiś ca vadhnīyāt tāḍayet tathā ||  
 6.8.23  gajenāpyathavāśvena trāsayetpannagena vā |
       
       punastṛṇāgninā vāpi sarvatassamavākiret ||  
 6.8.24  avakīryāthavāṅgāraiḥ pradīptaiḥ  pāribhadrakaiḥ |
       
       prayuktaṃ śītalenaiva jalenābhyukṣayetpunaḥ ||  
 6.8.25  prasārayed vā sariti  saraṇe vā nirodhayet |
       
       bubhukṣayā śoṣayed vā kūpe prakṣipya mānavaḥ ||  
 6.8.26  apūrvā bhīṣayeyustaṃ puruṣāḥ śastrapāṇayaḥ |
       
 vitrāsayeyurvaidyāstaṃ trāsanais tu pṛthagvidhaiḥ ||  
 6.8.27  trāsāstīvrā hi kurvanti cittasya vikṛtiṃ bhayāt |
       
       bhayam eva tu cittasya mānavānarthamucyate ||  
 6.8.28  prakṣiptacitto vicaret trāsyamāno ' pi 
      śastrataḥ  |
       
 kumārabṛndānugatastamasādhyaṃ  vinirdiśet ||  
 6.8.29 tāpanāñjananasyaiś ca kṣāraiḥ kṣārāgadair api |
       
       proktairapasmāraharair unmādaṃ samupācaret ||  
 6.8.30  purāṇaṃ pāyayeccainaṃ sarpirunmādanāśanam |
       
       sthitaṃ varṣaśataṃ śreṣṭhaṃ kumbhasarpistaducyate ||  
 6.8.31  pānābhyañjananasyeṣu hitamunmādināṃ sadā |
       
       kāñjikaṃ laśunaṃ caiva bastamūtreṇa peṣavet ||  
 6.8.32  unmādināṃ prayogo ' yaṃ purāṇaghṛtasaṃyutaḥ |
       
       etāḥ kriyāḥ prayuñjīta vaidyaḥ kāyacikitsakaḥ ||  
 6.8.33 śāntikarmāṇi homāṃś ca kuryād bhūtacikitsakaḥ |
       
       iṣṭayaḥ śāntikarmaṇi homāḥ svastyayanāni ca |
       
       vedoktāḥ karmavidhayaḥ kāryāśconmādanāśanāḥ || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele cikitsite aṣṭamo ' dhyāyaḥ || || navamo ' dhyāyaḥ || athāto '
      pasmāracikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 6.9.1  uktaṃ rūpaṃ samutthānamapasmārasya kṛtsnaśaḥ |
       
       nidāneṣu, cikitsāṃ tu vistareṇa nibodha me ||  
 6.9.2 gajāśvayānātpatanādabhighātāt  bhramād api |
       
       iṣṭadravyavināśāc ca cittaṃ vibhramamṛcchati ||  
 6.9.3  tasya citte paribhrānte hṛdayaṃ pariśuṣyati |
       
       ruṇaddhi vāyurūṣmāṇaṃ nāḍīṃ prāpya jalāvahām  ||  
 6.9.4  bhṛśaṃ tṛṣṇāparītaḥ  sa mohaṃ gacchatyapasmaran |
       
       apasmaratyapasmārī phenaṃ muñcati vepate ||  
 6.9.5  seveta  tailaṃ śairīṣaṃ ghṛtaṃ kalyāṇakaṃ tathā |
       
       mahāpaiśācikaṃ vāpi mahākṣāraṃ ca dādhikam ||  
 6.9.6  śaṇabījāni kaiḍaryaṃ |.. |.. cāpalūnakam |
       
       rūpasthā ca vayasthā ca pūtanā keśamāriṇī ||  
 6.9.7  triphalā tryūṣaṇaṃ mustā laśunaṃ pāpacelikā |
       
       etāni samabhāgāni vasātailaghṛtāni ca ||  
 6.9.8  ūrṇakaṃ ca tathaikadhyaṃ paced gomūtrasaṃyutam |
       
       yadā prajvalitaṃ śāntamathainamavatārayet ||  
 6.9.9  biḍālapadamātraṃ tu kṣārasyāsya sukhāmbunā |
       
       pibed apasmāraharam unmādasya ca nāśanam |
       
       arśāṃsi gulmānmehāṃś ca plīhānamudarāmayam  || 
 
  || daśamo ' dhyāyaḥ ||  
 
 
 6.10.0 
 
  bhayād vā yadi śokād vā yo ' tisāraḥ
      pravartate |
       
 
 6.10.1  atisāras tu bhūyiṣṭhaṃ sāma eva sa saṃbhavet |
       
       tasmāt sarvamatīsāraṃ laṅghanaissamupācaret ||  
 6.10.2 laṅghayed balavantaṃ ca, dīpanīyāni kārayet |
       
       durbalasya tu saṃsargīṃ kārayet tu viriktavat ||  
 6.10.3  stimitaṃ yasya guru ca paryādhmātamivodaram |
       
       dīpanīyopapapannaṃ tu bahudoṣaṃ tu dehinam  ||  
 6.10.4  stokaṃ stokaṃ sraṃsamānaṃ nigṛhītaṃ savedanam |
       
       dīpanīyasamāyuktaṃ pāyayetsraṃsanaṃ param ||  
 6.10.5 viśuddhasrotasas tasya doṣeṣu sraṃsiteṣu ca |
       
       sukhaṃ tadgrahaṇaṃ kartuṃ pācanaṃ stambha eva ca ||  
 6.10.6  harītakīṃ trikaṭukaṃ hiṅgu sauvarcalaṃ vacām |
       
       śuklāmativiṣāṃ caiva pāyayed uṣṇavāriṇā ||  
 6.10.7 niyataṃ janitādhmānamatisāraṃ savedanam |
       
       sthāpayatyatisaṃvṛddhaṃ veleva varuṇālayam ||  
 6.10.8  harītakī sātiviṣā hiṅgu sauvarcalaṃ vacā |
       
       saindhavaṃ ceti piṣṭāni pāyayed uṣṇavāriṇā ||  
 6.10.9  āmātisāre  yogo ' yaṃ vidhitas tu cikitsakaiḥ |
       
       yukte kvāthe prayoktavyo baidyenāpi yaśo ' rthinā ||  
 6.10.10  āmātisāro yo hyābhyāṃ yogābhyāṃ na nivartate |
       
       na sa sādhayituṃ śakyo hyanyairmārgaśatair api ||  
 6.10.11  bhūyiṣṭhamāmaprabhavaḥ kukṣirogaḥ kaphātmakaḥ |
       
       pravartate nṛṇāṃ tasya śṛṇu samyak cikitsitam ||  
 6.10.12  citrakaḥ pippalīmūlaṃ vacā kaṭukarohiṇī |
       
       pāṭhā vatsakabījāni harītakyo mahauṣadham ||  
 6.10.13  etadāmasamutthānamatisāraṃ savedanam |
       
       kaphātmakaṃ sapittaṃ ca varco badhnāti ca dhruvam ||  
 6.10.14  pāṭhā vacā trikaṭukaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ kaṭukarohiṇī |
       
       tat sādhupītāny etāni śleṣmātīsāranāśanam ||  
 6.10.15  bhallātakaṃ śakrayavāḥ pāṭhā kaṭukarohiṇī |
       
       yavānyajājīkuṣṭhaṃ  ca citrako ' tiviṣā ||  
 6.10.16 śaṭī puṣkaramūlaṃ ca tathā hiṅgu harītakī |
       
       sauvarcalaṃ śṛṅgaberaṃ gavāṃ mūtreṇa peṣayet ||  
 6.10.17  vaṭakānakṣamātrāṃstān chāyāśuṣkānnidhāpayet |
       
       teṣāmekaṃ pibed dvau vā sukhoṣṇenaiva  vāriṇā ||  
 6.10.18 etaddhyāmasamutthānamatisāraṃ savedanam |
       
 nudatyarśāṃsi ca tathā tamāṃsīva divākaraḥ ||  
 6.10.19  grahaṇīdīpanīyāś ca ye yogāḥ parikīrtitāḥ |
       
       śleṣmātisāre te kāryāḥ kṣāraḥ kṣāraguḍas tathā ||  
 6.10.20  etadāmātisārāṇāṃ śleṣmātīsāriṇām api |
       
       cikitsitaṃ samākhyātaṃ pittātīsāriṇāṃ śṛṇu ||  
 6.10.21  atisāras tu yaḥ pittāduttho  ' tisaratīha saḥ |
       
       pācitaṃ stambhayed enaṃ yathāvattannibodha me ||  
 6.10.22  biḍaṃ bilvaśalāṭūni tintriṇīkaṃ  sadāḍimam |
       
       sauvarcalaṃ dhātakī ca samaṅgā ceti tatsamam ||  
 6.10.23  kalkapiṣṭaṃ  bhavetpeyaṃ kālyamuṣṇena vāriṇā |
       
       pittātīsāraśūlārtaṃ naraṃ sadyaścikitsate ||  
 6.10.24  rasāñjanaṃ sātiviṣaṃ kuṭajasya phalaṃ tvacam |
       
       dhātakīṃ śṛṅgaberaṃ ca pāyayet taṇḍulāmbunā ||  
 6.10.25 mākṣīkayukto nudati pittātīsāramulbaṇam |
       
       mandaṃ dīpayate cāgniṃ śūlaṃ cāśu nivartayet ||  
 6.10.26 pāṭhā dāruharidrā ca pippalīmūlam eva ca |
       
 phalatvace vatsakasya śṛṅgaberaṃ tathaiva ca ||  
 6.10.27  etāni kalkapeṣyāṇi pāyayet taṇḍulāmbunā |
       
       ambaṣṭhakī śilodbhedaṃ dhātakī cāmlavetasam ||  
 6.10.28 uśīraṃ bālahrīberaṃ dāḍimatvaṅ mahauṣadham |
       
       jambūphalaṃ kapitthasya madhyaṃ bilvaśalāṭu ca ||  
 6.10.29  etāni caiva tulyāni pāyayet taṇḍulāmbunā |
       
       mākṣīkayuktaṃ nudati pittātīsāralakṣaṇam ||  
 6.10.30  savātāṃ  ca samūlāṃ ca nāśayetparikartikām |
       
       samaṅgā niculaṃ lodhraṃ dhātakī madhukaṃ tathā ||  
 6.10.31  vaṭalodhrapravālāś ca dāḍimasya phalaṃ tvacam |
       
       māṣaparṇīśilodbhedaṃ  sāmbaṣṭhākamathāpi ca ||  
 6.10.32 pittātisāre dātavyaṃ taṇḍulodakasaṃyutam |
       
       samaṅgā dhātakīpuṣpaṃ sāmbaṣṭhākamathāpi ca ||  
 6.10.33  pittātisāre padmaṃ ca taṇḍulādbhiḥ piben naraḥ |
       
       śaśasyaiṇasya vā raktaṃ madhukaṃ kṛṣṇamṛttikā ||  
 6.10.34  pittātisāre dātavyaṃ taṇḍulodakasaṃyutam |
       
 duṣṭaḥ pittātisārastu  gambhīrasthānamāśritaḥ ||  
 6.10.35  atīva sāryate raktamatisārassa raktajaḥ |
       
       nīlotpalaṃ bilvatilā madhukaṃ guḍaśarkarā ||  
 6.10.36  kesaraṃ puṇḍarīkasya kumudaṃ kṣaudram eva ca |
       
       ājena payasā pītaṃ raktātīsāranāśanam || nirvāhi |.. |.. |.. |..  
 6.10.37  athāsya varcojananīmanuyuktiṃ pradāpayet |
       
       dīptāgnikṣīṇamāṃsasya saśūlasyātisāriṇaḥ ||  
 6.10.38  ajasya mahato madhyādveśavāraṃ saśoṇitam |
       
       dadhnātha yāvake siddhaṃ guḍatrikaṭukānvitam ||  
 6.10.39  tena saṃbhojayet kāle  mṛdususvinnadehinam |
       
       kalpenaitena vārāhaṃ krauñcaṃ māṃsañ ca kārayet ||  
 6.10.40  etenaiva ca kalpena kārayeccaraṇāyudhān |
       
       tittirīn kacchapān lābhānmayūrānkrakarānapi  ||  
 6.10.41  vātātisāriṇāmetatsamākhyātaṃ cikitsitam |
       
 vātātisāre kartavyaṃ sarvamarśaścikitsitam ||  
 6.10.42  bhayādvā yadi vā śokādyo ' tisāraḥ pravartate |
       
       yaḥ kupyati tato doṣas tasya kuryāc cikitsitam ||  
 6.10.43  nityam āśvāsayeyustaṃ suhṛdaś ca vipaścitaḥ |
       
       manaḥ prahṛṣṭaṃ kuryāc ca, tadā sampadyate sukhī ||  
 6.10.44  sarvagātraparistabdho vivarṇaḥ stimitaś ca yaḥ |
       
       na ca duḥkhaṃ vijānīte parivarjyastathāvidhaḥ ||  
 6.10.45  yasya keśāḥ pralupyante balaṃ varṇaś ca hīyate |
       
 pariśuṣkamukho yaś ca na sa jīvati taddhidhaḥ  ||  
 6.10.46 viveṣṭamāno yaśśete sarvagātrāṇi vikṣipet |
       
       stabdhagātro na saṃcārī parivarjyastathāvidhaḥ ||  
 6.10.47  hanuṃ daśati yo ' bhīkṣṇaṃ na vedayati yo ' sukham
      |
       
       jihvāṃ khādati cātyarthaṃ gatāyuriti nirdiśet ||  
 6.10.48  saṃrakṣanvai yaśaḥ prājño na cainaṃ samupācaret |
       
       arthaghnaṃ ca yaśoghnaṃ ca na karma samupācaret ||  
 6.10.49  dṛṣṭvā sādhyamasādhyaṃ ca yaḥ karoti sa sidhyati |
       
       pūjāṃ ca labhate ' tyarthaṃ vidvatsu ca virājate ||  
 6.10.50  viṣūcyās tu pravakṣyāmi cikitsāṃ lakṣaṇāni ca |
       
 viruddhagurupiṣṭānnaśākarūkṣarasāśinām ||  
 6.10.51  ajīrṇabhojināṃ nityaṃ trayaḥ kupyanti dhātavaḥ |
       
       taddoṣabalamudbhūtamārutena vivardhitam ||  
 6.10.52  adhaścordhvaṃ ca tiryak ca srotāṃsi niruṇaddhyati |
       
       ruddhaiś ca mārute ruddhasrotāṃsi niruṇaddhi ca (?) ||  
 6.10.53  teṣu doṣaparīteṣu duṣṭenānnarasena ca |
       
       ūrdhvaṃ cādhaś ca vego ' sya kathaṃcitsaṃpravartate ||  
 6.10.54 tāṃ vilambīṃ vigarhanti viṣakalpāṃ viṣūcikām |
       
 yathāyathotpannaraso deheṣu viṣamāśritaḥ ||  
 6.10.55  nāḍīssa vyākulīkṛtya vardhayet tu  balāsakam
      |
       
       tasya kāso jvaro mūrchā bhaktadveṣo vivarṇatā |
       
 
 6.10.56  glāniścaivāvipākaś ca śleṣmasekaḥ pravāhikā
      |
       
       uroghātastathātyarthaṃ hṛdrogaś cāntrakūjanam ||  
 6.10.57 vibandho gātrahāniś ca so ' laso nāma dāruṇaḥ |
       
       utkleśo vepathuśchardirvidāho  veṣṭanaṃ jvaraḥ ||  
 6.10.58  śvāsādhmānaṃ śakṛdbhedo vidviṣṭāhāralakṣaṇam |
       
 śleṣmapracurakāsaś ca jṛmbhaṇaṃ hṛdayagrahaḥ ||  
 6.10.59  tathā śvāsaś ca kāsaś ca pārśvaśīrṣarujānvitaḥ |
       
       viṣūcyāḥ pūrvarūpāṇi svedo gātrasya śītatā ||  
 6.10.60  udgāro gurukoṣṭhatvaṃ mūtrānilaśakṛdgrahaḥ |
       
       etatpañcavidhaṃ proktamannavibhramalakṣaṇam ||  
 6.10.61  cikitsāṃ tatra kurvīta sarvāmāmātisāriṇām |
       
       upadravāś ca ye proktāḥ viṣūcyāmalase tathā ||  
 6.10.62 tāṃścikitsed bhiṣak samyagyathāsvaiś ca
      cikitsitaiḥ |
       
       etadviṣūcyāmākhyātaṃ samāsena cikitsitam ||  
 6.10.63  kūratvād asya rogasya bhūyo vakṣyāmi vistaram |
       
       viṣūcyāḥ pūrvarūpāṇi saṃniśamya cikitsakaḥ ||  
 6.10.64  vamanaṃ kārayetkṣipramuṣṇena lavaṇāmbunā |
       
       yāvatsa tiṣṭhettasya syānnānyaduddhāraṇātsukham ||  
 6.10.65  kārakaṃ ca kaṣāyaṃ syādathavārjunasādhitam  |
       
 pītaṃ kaṣāyaṃ vamanaṃ sadyo hanti viṣūcikām ||  
 6.10.66  tathā mustādikaḥ kalkaḥ pippalīkalkasaṃyutaḥ |
       
       pītaścoṣṇena toyena hanyāt kṣipraṃ viṣūcikām ||  
 6.10.67  viruddhā hi rasā bhuktā dūṣitāḥ pavanādibhiḥ |
       
       viṣībhavanti deheṣu pūrvavṛddhairmalāśaye  ||  
 6.10.68  tasmād viṣasamā hyāśu kriyāssarvāḥ prayojayet |
       
 dhūmān kaṣāyān vartīś ca pradehotsādanāni ca ||  
 6.10.69  avapīḍān pradhamanamagnikarmopanāhanam  |
       
 saṃsparśānyupacārāṃś ca viṣūcyāṃ kārayetkriyām ||  
 6.10.70  bhallātakaṃ  trikaṭukaṃ pūtikaṃ kṣavakaṃ balām |
       
 phaṇijjaṃ laśunaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ karañjasya phalāni ca ||  
 6.10.71  triphalāṃ ca yavānīṃ ca kuṭajasya phalāni ca |
       
       vartimetāṃ śivāṃ nāma bastamūtreṇa peṣayet || viṣūcalākṣākṣāraś ca
       jāyate(?)  |  | 
  |  |  |  |  |  |  | (Bhṣ6.10.2.1) |
       
       hanubhyāṃ nigṛhītābhyāmavyaktaṃ vyāharaty api |
       
       susaṃhatahanurvāpi na vyāharati kiṃcana || (Bhṣ6.10.2.2.) |
       
       snehapānāni nasyaṃ ca svedāḥ pathyāśanāni ca |
       
       upanāhāś ca śasyante vastayaś cārdite hitāḥ || (Bhṣ6.10.2.3) |
       
 dadhyāranālayor droṇe vasā lābhena cāḍhake |
       
       ānūpaudakanity ānāṃ māṃsāny api ca lābhataḥ || (Bhṣ6.10.2.4) |
       
       tilān kulutthānmāṣāṃś ca badarāṇi yavān balām |
       
       dve pañcamūlyau rāsnāṃ ca śatamūlāṃ śatāvarīm || (Bhṣ6.10.2.5) |
       
       etat sarvaṃ samāhṛtya sādhayenmṛdunāgninā |
       
       bāṣpeṇoccaratā  tena nāḍīsvedena svedayet || (Bhṣ6.10.2.6) |
       
       tailamebhiś ca vipacedabhyañjyāc ca pibec ca tat |
       
       etam eva ca sambhāram upanāhaṃ ca kārayet |
       
       |
       
       (Bhṣ6.10.2.7) |
       
       yac cikitsitam ākhyātaṃ vātavyādhivināśanam |
       
       tad eva sarvaṃ nikhilam arditeṣv api kārayet || (Bhṣ6.10.2.8) |
       
       mahāsnehaṃ balātailaṃ tailaṃ śairīṣam eva vā |
       
       pānābhyaṅgeṣu nasyeṣu vastau vāpi prayojayet || (Bhṣ6.10.2.9) |
       
       ānūpāni ca māṃsāni veśavāraṃ prakuṭṭayet |
       
       nātisnigdhena tenāsya kārayed upanāhanam || (Bhṣ6.10.2.10) |
       
       śleṣmaṇā samupastabdho yasyeha pavano bhavet |
       
       manyayor nmūrdhni gaṇḍe ca śoṣastasyopajāyate || (Bhṣ6.10.2.11) |
       
       mūko nidrāparītaś ca kaṇṭhaniśvasito bhṛśam |
       
       bhṛśaṃ lālāparītaś ca jihmajihvīkṛto naraḥ || (Bhṣ6.10.2.12) |
       
       śleṣmopaṣṭabdhametādṛgarditaṃ parikīrtitam |
       
 tasyānuvāsanaṃ kuryāt tathā  śīrṣavirecanam || (Bhṣ6.10.2.13) |
       
 tilvakena virektavyo bhaved bindughṛtena vā |
       
       purāṇaṃ vā pibetsarpirdhūmaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ pibettathā || (Bhṣ6.10.2.14) |
       
       śleṣmaṇyuparate tasya bṛṃhaṇaiḥ  samupakramaḥ |
       
       vātavyādhicikitsāṃ ca yathoktāṃ samupācaret || (Bhṣ6.10.2.15) |
       
 sthānasthas tatra ca kaphaḥ vāyurāgantur ucyate |
       
       tasmāt tayor gatiṃ dṛṣṭvā vātaghnīṃ kārayetkriyām || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ

 6.11.1  agnirvā++āyurmanuṣyāṇāṃ prāṇās tatra pratiṣṭhitāḥ |
       
       balamārogyamāyuś ca sukhaduḥkhaṃ tadāśrayam ||  
 6.11.2  mriyate hy upaśānte ' gnau yukte coṣmaṇi jīvati |
       
       tasmāt prāṇāyuṣī vidyādagnimūle śarīriṇām ||  
 6.11.3  so ' gnissamucitaṃ bhuktaṃ rasāya vitanotyadhaḥ |
       
       tenendriyabalaṃ puṣṭiṃ varṇañ ca labhate naraḥ ||  
 6.11.4  caturvidhaṃ pacatyagniḥ samaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ tathā mṛdu |
       
       viṣamaṃ ceti teṣāṃ tu yaḥ samo ' gniḥ sa śasyate ||  
 6.11.5  bhajatāṃ guru rūkṣaṃ ca divāsvapnaṃ ca nity aśaḥ |
       
       rātrau na vā saṃsvapatāṃ tathā vegavidhāriṇām ||  
 6.11.6  adhyaśnatāmajīrṇe  ' nne hy
      atisnehe virekiṇām |
       
 jvarānmadyaprasaṅgāc ca tathā ' sātmyaniṣevaṇāt ||  
 6.11.7  madhurakṣīranity ānāṃ tathā jalavihāriṇām |
       
       piṣṭānnadadhiśākānāmahṛdyānāṃ niṣevaṇāt ||  
 6.11.8  īdṛśairgrahaṇī jantordūṣyate ' ti niṣevitaiḥ |
       
       mandā tīkṣṇātiviṣamā trividhaṃ sā prakupyati ||  
 6.11.9  tathā rogāḥ pravartante grahaṇīdoṣajā nṛṇām |
       
       jvaraḥ kāsaḥ pāṇḍurogaḥ śvayathuḥ parikartikā ||  
 6.11.10  aruciś cāvipākaś ca gulmārśāṃsi bhagandaram |
       
       atisāraś ca kuṣṭhaṃ ca śūlānyalasako bhramaḥ ||  
 6.11.11  etāṃś cānyāṃś ca janayed rogānasyāmitāśinaḥ  |
       
       grahaṇī dūṣitā jantoḥ sāmā rogānnihanti vā ||  
 6.11.12  yasyākrānte hi kāyāgnau śleṣmaṇā madhurāśinaḥ |
       
       na pacyate ' nnaṃ kālena sa mandāgniriti smṛtaḥ ||  
 6.11.13  agnau mande kaphenāsya śīghraṃ bhuktaṃ na pacyate |
       
       sa bhūyo mṛdutāṃ yāti gurubhojanadūṣitaḥ ||  
 6.11.14  evaṃ rūpaś ca vṛddhaś ca kaphe
      tasya praśāmyati |
       
       evaṃ sa viṣamo nāma grahaṇīdoṣa ucyate ||  
 6.11.15  agnissomakṣayādyasya bhṛśaṃ dehe prakupyati |
       
       bhuktaṃ bhuktaṃ jarayate na ca varṇabalāya ca ||  
 6.11.16  bhukte bhukte kṣudhāpyasya jāyate na ca puṣyati |
       
       atyagniriti taṃ vidyāt sa ca duḥkhatamaḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
 6.11.17  ity eṣa rogastrividhaḥ grahaṇīsaṃśrito mayā |
       
       proktas tasya cikitsāṃ tu vistareṇa nibodha me ||  
 6.11.18  dhānvantaraṃ pibetsarpiḥ prājāpatyamathāpi vā |
       
       tato ' smai vamanaṃ dadyāt tataś cordhvaṃ virecanam ||  
 6.11.19  pippalīvardhamānaṃ vā pibetkṣārāgadānapi |
       
       takraṃ māsaṃ pibec cāpi gaṇḍīrāriṣṭam eva vā ||  
 6.11.20  dādhikaṃ ca pibetsarpistailaṃ śairīṣam eva vā |
       
       mahadyatpañcagavyaṃ vā  |  |  |  |  |  |  ||   |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  || dvādaśo ' dhyāyaḥ ||   |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
 
 
 6.12.1 tālapatrīkaṣāyaṃ  tu mūtrāghāteṣu dāpayet |
       
       bhojanaṃ krauñcamāṃsena mūtrāghāteṣu  śasyate ||  
 6.12.2  piṣṭvā tu tasya caivāsthi kṣīreṇa saha pāyayet |
       
       mūtrakṛcchrāṇi śamayed aśmarīṃ ca bhinatty api ||  
 6.12.3  ebhir yadi prayogais tu śarkarā nopaśāmyati |
       
       tāmuddharecchalyahartā dṛṣṭakarmā bahuśrutaḥ ||  
 6.12.4  pratīghātādindriyasya yasya kṛcchraṃ pravartate |
       
       anusannaṃ ca śūlaṃ ca śṛṇu tasya cikitsitam ||  
 6.12.5  balātailena svabhyaktamuṣṇāmbupariṣecitam |
       
       āsthāpayetpācanena mustādyena tu vastinā ||  
 6.12.6 pratyāgate nirūhe taṃ bhojayet siddhamodanam |
       
       tanunā mudgayūṣeṇa jāṅgalena rasena vā ||  
 6.12.7  tatas tu śuddhāmbarayā nāryā snātānuliptayā |
       
       iṣṭayā saṃviśetsārdhaṃ kalyāṇaguṇayuktayā ||  
 6.12.8  viśuddhe retaso mārge mārutaḥ praguṇī bhavet |
       
 svaṃ sthānaṃ mārute prāpte kṛcchraṃ tasya nivartate ||  
 6.12.9  aṣṭānāṃ mūtrakṛcchrāṇāmetaduktaṃ cikitsitam |
       
       rūpāṇi caiva sarveṣāṃ śiṣyāṇāmarthasiddhaye || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele dvādaśo ' dhyāyaḥ || || trayodaśo ' dhyāyaḥ || athāta
      udaracikitsāṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 6.13.1  bhārābhihatadehasya kaṭutiktopasevinaḥ |
       
       vāyussarvaśarīrastho duṣṭo vātahatāḥ sirāḥ ||  
 6.13.2  gatvā hi pūrayetkoṣṭhaṃ  tathādhmānaṃ karoti ca |
       
       dṛtivac ca samunnaddhamudaraṃ syāt samantataḥ ||  
 6.13.3 kṛṣṇarājivanaddhaṃ ca kṛṣṇaromācitaṃ tathā |
       
 etadvātodaraṃ vidyādetairliṅgaissamanvitam ||  
 6.13.4  uṣṇābhitapto yo janturvidāhīnyupasevate |
       
       vyāyāmoparataś caiva klānto yaścodakaṃ pibet ||  
 6.13.5  tasya dehe kapho duṣṭaḥ sirāḥ kaphavahā gataḥ |
       
       utsanno dūṣitaś cāpi koṣṭhamabhyantarāśritaḥ ||  
 6.13.6  sarvamādhmāpayetkoṣṭhaṃ vedanāṃ ca karoti saḥ |
       
       śuklarājivanaddhaṃ ca śuklaromācitaṃ tathā ||  
 6.13.7  tasya sīdanti gātrāṇi mukhasrāvaśca  jāyate |
       
       durgandhitāsyamālasyaṃ sakaphodarilakṣaṇam ||  
 6.13.8  samaśnataḥ sarvarasān mithyāhāravihāriṇaḥ |
       
 tasyānyārdhamivātyarthamudaraṃ  saṃprakāśate ||  
 6.13.9  nānārājivanaddhaṃ ca nānāromācitaṃ tathā |
       
       tathā nānāvedanāḍyamudaraṃ sānnipātikam ||  
 6.13.10  āmanantyudaraṃ nāryo garamātmodbhavaṃ yadā |
       
       karṇarodhakṛtaṃ cāpi śuklaṃ jihvāmalaṃ nakham ||  
 6.13.11  manuṣyamedoromāṇi strīṇāmārtavaśoṇitam |
       
       purīṣaṃ ca prayacchanti bhakta duṣṭodaraṃ bhavet ||  
 6.13.12  sarvavarṇasirānaddhaṃ nīlapītaprabhaṃ tathā |
       
 nṛṇāṃ dūṣyodaraṃ nāma jāyate sānnipātikam ||  
 6.13.13  tasyāṅgamardaḥ kāsaś ca śvāso hikkā ca jāyate |
       
       nidrā tandrā tathālasyaṃ dāhaś cāṅgagato bhavet ||  
 6.13.14  sadanaṃ sarvagātrāṇāṃ śoṣaṇaṃ pāṇḍuvarṇatā |
       
       viṣapīte ca yalliṅgaṃ tac ca tasyopajāyate ||  
 6.13.15  evaṃ dūṣyodaraṃ tvetairliṅgairmaraṇamṛcchati |
       
       abhuktvā yaḥ pibennityam udakaṃ prātarutthitaḥ ||  
 6.13.16  varṣāhemantakāleṣu pibedyaścodakaṃ bahu |
       
       tasyodare ' dhikā pīḍā cānyataḥ samprapadyate ||  
 6.13.17  sadanaṃ romaharṣaś ca śītāgnitvaṃ śirograhaḥ |
       
       tathā snigdhāvabhāsañ ca snigdharomācitaṃ ca yat ||  
 6.13.18  etairliṅgaissamastais tu nṛṇāṃ tadudakodaram |
       
       śaṅkunā snāyubhedena matsyānāṃ vātha kaṇṭakaiḥ ||  
 6.13.19  śakṛttṛṇāgrair vā bhuktairantraṃ yasya vibhidyate
      |
       
       tenānnapānaṃ chidreṇa sravettasyāntarodare ||  
 6.13.20  unnataṃ jāyate tasmād udaraṃ syāt samantataḥ |
       
 sirā++āyatā jāyate ca tvardhe jaṭharasannidhau  ||  
 6.13.21  saṃsrāviṇi ca jaṭhare lakṣaṇaṃ parikīrtitam |
       
       yaḥ plavellaṅghayed vāpi yaś ca vyāyacchate naraḥ ||  
 6.13.22 tenāsyāntrāṇi tudyante badhyante cāpy 
      athaikataḥ |
       
       tathā muñjaiś ca bālaiś ca bhuktairantraṃ niveṣṭyate ||  
 6.13.23  tena baddhaṃ gudaṃ nṝṇāṃ jāyate ' ntranipīḍanāt |
       
       utkṣiptakukṣir bhavati tathā saṃkṣiptamehanaḥ ||  
 6.13.24  śūnākṣaḥ śūnavṛṣaṇaḥ śūnahastas tathaiva ca |
       
       śūnapādagudaś caiva suptāṅgaś cāpi jāyate ||  
 6.13.25 natonnataḥ samaś cāpi naro baddhodarī bhavet |
       
       āmadhānyayavān yas tu naro bhuṅkte niṣevate ||  
 6.13.26  sakesaraṃ phalaṃ vāpi bhakṣayitvodakaṃ pibet |
       
       hastyaśvarathayānaṃ ca bhuktamātre  niṣevate ||  
 6.13.27 mahauṣadhaṃ samaricaṃ dvau kṣārau triphalā vacā |
       
       yavānī  kuñcikā hiṅgu tintriṇīkāmlavetasau  ||  
 6.13.28  dhānyājagandhe trāyantī dāḍimaṃ sayavāsakam  |
       
       kaṭukā kauṭajaṃ bījaṃ saindhavaṃ ca samān bhiṣak ||  
 6.13.29  trivṛtā saptalā dantī kampillaṃ nīlikā ' bhayā |
       
       suvarṇakṣīrī dviguṇaṃ sarvāṇy etāni cūrṇayet ||  
 6.13.30  āje gavye ' thavā mūtre saptāhaṃ paribhāvya tam |
       
       dviguṇaṃ śarkarāṃ cātra dāpayet tryaṅgulaṃ pibet ||  
 6.13.31  gomūtratriphalākṣārarasairmadyaiḥ  sukhāmbunā |
       
       suvarṇasamakaṃ cūrṇaṃ sarvarogārtibheṣajam ||  
 6.13.32  sarvodaraplīhaśoṣagulmahṛdroganāśnam |
       
       vātāṣṭhīlāmathānāhaṃ śvayathuṃ sarvagātrajam ||  
 6.13.33  halīmakāmilāpāṇḍupramehān  sajvarān jayet |
       
       jīvite saṃśayaṃ kṛtvā garalaṃ jaṭharī pibet ||  
 6.13.34  trapusorvārukaṃ vāpi mūlakaṃ vāpi daṃśayet |
       
       kruddhena kṛṣṇasarpeṇa jaṭharī tāni bhakṣayet ||  
 6.13.35 kukṣiṃ vipāṭya mānena chidramantrasya vīkṣya ca |
       
       tataḥ pipīlikādaṃśaṃ chidre tvantrsaya dāpayet ||  
 6.13.36  antracchidre saṃgṛhīte sīvyetkukṣiṃ tato bhiṣak |
       
       evaṃ chidrodaraṃ vaidyaḥ śalyakarturupācaret ||  
 6.13.37  tathā baddhagudaṃ caiva pāṭayecchalyaśāstravit |
       
       muñjān vālāṃstathoddhṛtya baddhaṃ sīvyettato bhiṣak ||  
 6.13.38 dakavanti hi sarvāṇi jaṭharāṇyakriyāvatām |
       
       vyathanaṃ teṣu kurvīta śalyakartuḥ prayogavit ||  
 6.13.39  vāme pārśve tvadhaḥ kukṣermuktvā ca
      caturaṅgulam  |
       
       nābhyāṃ vā praṇayecchastraṃ mātrāyuktaṃ cikitsakaḥ ||  
 6.13.40  visrāvayecca  jaṭharaṃ bhiṣagāmayapīḍitam  |
       
       mardayed udaraṃ cāsya veṣṭanena tu veṣṭayet ||  
 6.13.41  veṣṭitaṃ jaṭharaṃ cāsya nādhmāpayati mārutaḥ |
       
       pibedyavāgūṃ ca tato lavaṇasnehavarjitām ||  
 6.13.42  tataḥ paraṃ tu kṣīreṇa māsārdhaṃ samupācaret |
       
       tataḥ kṣīrayavāgūṃ ca, trīnmāsāṃs tu yavānbhiṣak ||  
 6.13.43  bhuñjītālavaṇaṃ tasmāt trīnmāsān laghu bhojanam |
       
       tataḥ salavaṇaṃ  bhojyamucyate tūdare ' pi ca ||  
 6.13.44  ke tūdarāṇāmicchanti lavaṇaṃ yogavāhataḥ  |
       
       kecit tu jaṭhare prāhuragnikarma cikitsakāḥ ||  
 6.13.45  ajātatoye jaṭhare pavanaśleṣmasambhave |
       
       plīhodaraṃ  hinastyagniḥ jayet tasmād viśeṣataḥ ||  
 6.13.46  nivṛttirvarṇitā, tatra salilodarakhedinaḥ |
       
       |.. |.. yāvatpeyā prakodaram(?) ||  
 6.13.47  maṇḍalaṃ nirmitaṃ yac ca śvayathuḥ sparśane mṛduḥ
      |
       
 ākoṭitamaśabdaṃ ca na ca rājisamākulam ||  
 6.13.48  ākramyamāṇaṃ  nābhyāntu mṛdureva hi sarpati
      |
       
 tataś ca salilodbhūtiṃ picchanaiś ca vinirdiśet |
       
       kriyāyatīś ca sarvāṇi sakriyāpiś ca dehinām(?) ||  
 6.13.49  bhallātakānāṃ pavanāhatānāṃ vṛntacyutānām iha cāṭhakaṃ
      syāt |
       
       tadiṣṭakācūrṇakaṇairvighṛṣya prakṣālayitvā visṛjet pravāte ||  
 6.13.50  śuṣkaṃ punastadvidalīkṛtaṃ ca vinikṣipedapsu caturguṇāsu
      |
       
       pādāvaśiṣṭaṃ paripūtaśītaṃ kṣīreṇa tulyena punaḥ paceta ||  
 6.13.51  tadardhayā śarkarayāvagāḍhaṃ lohābhayāvyoṣakacūrṇayuktam
      |
       
       etatsamaṃ śarkarapādayuktaṃ tataḥ khajenonmathitaṃ nidhāya ||  
 6.13.52  prasthadvayenāmalakīmadhūnāṃ śīte ' tha dhānyena
      punaḥ paceta |
       
       tatsaptarātrādupajātavīryaṃ sudhārasādapyadhikatvameti ||  
 6.13.53 prātarviśuddhīkṛtadehabhājāṃ mātrāṃ
       dadītātmaśarīrayogyām |
       
       na cānnapāne parihāryamasti na coṣṇavātādhvani maithune ca ||  
 6.13.54  janturnitāntaṃ narasiṃhavatsyād bhaven naraḥ
      kāñcanarāśisāraḥ |
       
       dantāś ca śīrṇāḥ punarudbhavanti keśāś ca śuklāḥ punareva  kṛṣṇāḥ ||  
 6.13.55  viśīrṇakarṇāṅgulināsiko  '
      pi kṛtāntadantāntagato ' pi kuṣṭhī |
       
       so ' pi krameṇāṅguligātraśākhastaruryathā rohati vārisiktaḥ || Bhṣ6.13.? |
       
       mahāmayūrāñjayati svareṇa balena nāgāṃsturagāñjavena |
       
       smṛmatibalamasatya(?)  |.. |.. |.. |.. |... || || caturdaśo ' dhyāyaḥ
