 6.14.1  vaṃśako naktamālaś ca mūrvā kaṭukarohiṇī |
       
       tarkārī pragrahaś caiva pīlūni niculāni ca ||  
 6.14.2  asanaḥ sptaparṇaś ca triphalā maricāni ca |
       
       etāni samabhāgāni kaṣāyam upapādayet ||  
 6.14.3  etānyeva ca cūrṇāni mākṣikeṇa piben naraḥ |
       
       anenaiva kaṣāyeṇa bhojayet siddhamodanam ||  
 6.14.4  picumandasya mūlāni citrako hastipippalī |
       
       tvakpatraphalamūlāni karañjātsarṣapās tathā ||  
 6.14.5  tulyāny etāni sarvāṇi valmīkasya ca mṛttikā |
       
       gavāṃ mūtreṇa piṣṭāni ślakṣṇānyudvartanaṃ varam ||  
 6.14.6  rāsnā vacā hy arkamūlaṃ hiṃsrā dantī tathaiva ca |
       
       śatapuṣpā ca kuṣṭhaṃ ca dve haridre punarnavā ||  
 6.14.7  aśvamūtre tvapāmārgaḥ  śārivā  naktamālikā |
       
       valmīkamṛttikā yuktametair udvartanaṃ varam ||  
 6.14.8  karajassuraso bilvaṃ devadāru vacārjunaḥ |
       
       tarkārī meṣaśṛṅgī ca śobhāñjanaka āraṇī  ||  
 6.14.9  ubhe bṛhatyau śyonākaḥ śbadaṃṣṭrā khadirāsanau |
       
 jale siddhairimaisttulyaiḥ  kaṣāyapariṣecanam ||  
 6.14.10  etair eva uṣadhaistulyaiḥ kṣīrapiṣṭaṃ pralepayet |
       
       anena vidhinā śīghramūrustambhaḥ praśāmyati ||  
 6.14.11  dve pañcamūlyau triphalā citrako devadāru ca |
       
       ekāṣṭhīlā tvapāmārgaḥ śreyasī vāyasī sudhā ||  
 6.14.12  kālā bhārṅgī pṛthakparṇī suvahā madayantikā |
       
       kāśmarī ca viśalyā ca hiṃsrā hemavidārikā ||  
 6.14.13  cirabilvo hy aśokaś ca balā cāṃśumatī tathā |
       
 vayasthā pīlaparṇī ca pāṭhā caiva śatāvarī ||  
 6.14.14  eṣāṃ paṃcapalān bhāgān jaladroṇeṣu saptasu |
       
       aṣṭabhāgāvaśeṣaṃ ca pacettailāḍhakaṃ śanaiḥ ||  
 6.14.15  kuṣṭhaṃ ca śatapuṣpā ca citrakastryūṣaṇaṃ tathā |
       
       devadārvagaru śreṣṭhaṃ viḍaṅgaṃ mustam eva ca ||  
 6.14.16  aśvagandhā ca pāṭhā ca mūrvā śyonāka eva ca |
       
       pippalyaḥ śṛṅgaberaṃ ca dantī hiṅgvamlavetasau ||  
 6.14.17  garbheṇānena vaidyas tu kaṣāyeṇa susādhayet |
       
       siddhaṃ pūtaṃ ca śītaṃ ca kṣaudrājyenānusaṃsṛjet ||  
 6.14.18  tadasya dadyāt pānārthaṃ tathaivābhyajjanādiṣu |
       
       ūrustambhaścirotpannastailenaitena śāmyati ||  
 6.14.19  ślīpadānyāṭhyavātaṃ  ca khuḍavātāṃś ca
      nāśayet |
       
       pippalīvardhamānaṃ vā mākṣikeṇa  jalena vā ||  
 6.14.20  ūrustambhe praśaṃsanti gaṇḍīrāriṣṭam eva vā |
       
       kṣārāḥ kṣārāgadāś caiva nirūhāś ca pṛthagvidhāḥ ||  
 6.14.21  harītakyāḥ prayogo vā hyūrustambhe praśasyate |
       
 vilekhyamāno hi yataḥ kṣīṇamāṃsabalo bhavet ||  
 6.14.22  śarīrarakṣaṇārthāya bhojayed bṛṃhayed api |
       
       bhuñjīta ṣaṣṭikān jīrṇān purāṇāṃś caiva śālikān ||  
 6.14.23  jāṅgalāni ca māṃsāni seveta mṛgapakṣiṇām |
       
       ūrustambhaparīto yo yadā vātādhiko bhavet ||  
 6.14.24  samyak proktam idaṃ sarvamūrustambhacikitsitam || ity 
      āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele caturdaśo ' dhyāyaḥ || || pañcadaśo ' dhyāyaḥ |
       
       |
       
       athāto visarpavātaśoṇitaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 6.15.1  vātātpittātkaphāccaiva sannipātād  dvayād api |
       
       visarpāḥ pañca nirdiṣṭās teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam ||  
 6.15.2  kaṣāyakaṭurūkṣāṃś ca yo nityam upasevate |
       
       tasya vāyuḥ prakupitaḥ tvagraktaṃ māṃsam eva ca ||  
 6.15.3  sirāś ca samadhiṣṭhāya visarpaṃ janayed balī  |
       
       pipīlikāṃ visarpantīṃ manyate tu, ghṛte ' pi ca (?) ||  
 6.15.4  jṛmbhikā tāluśoṣaś ca pārśvaśūlagrahajvarāḥ |
       
       ghoraś cāruṇavarṇābhaḥ śvayathuḥ kṛṣṇa eva ca ||  
 6.15.5  ity eṣa vātavīsarpaḥ tasya karmavidhiṃ śṛṇu |
       
       tasya nirvāpaṇaṃ kuryāt kṣīreṇa pariṣecanam ||  
 6.15.6  pītvā ca tailvakaṃ sarpirharītakyā virecanam |
       
       avidāhīni cānnāni bhojanārhtaṃ pradāpayet ||  
 6.15.7  kṣīraṃ ca yavacūrṇaṃ ca ghṛtaṃ caivātra sādhayet |
       
       yaṣṭīmadhukasaṃyuktametadālepanaṃ varam ||  
 6.15.8  gavāṃ mūtraṃ ca kṣīraṃ ca gośakṛdrasa eva vā |
       
       pañcamūlī ca tatsiddhaṃ jalaṃ seke praśasyate ||  
 6.15.9  rāsnāṃ ca madhukaṃ caiva peṣayed dadhimastunā |
       
       pradeho vātavīsarpe  ghṛtāktasya praśasyate ||  
 6.15.10  śṛṅgāṇi kṣīrivṛkṣāṇāṃ madhukaṃ nīlamutpalam |
       
       kṣīrasiddham idaṃ koṣṇaṃ vātavīsarpanāśanam ||  
 6.15.11  etair eva uṣadhaissarvaiḥ kṣīrapiṣṭaiḥ pralepayet |
       
       sukhoṣṇair vātavīsarpe  tathā  sampadyate sukhī ||  
 6.15.12  atha vā dadhimaṇḍena tailakṣīraghṛtena vā |
       
       secayanti sukhoṣṇena visarpe vātasambhave ||  
 6.15.13  kaṭvamlalavaṇakṣāratīkṣṇaṃ hyuṣṇāni cāśnataḥ |
       
       tasya pittaṃ prakupitaṃ śirāmāṃsatvagāśritam ||  
 6.15.14  raktena saha saṃsṛṣṭaṃ śarīre dehaveṣṭitam |
       
       jvalayitvā jvaraṃ pūrvaṃ jvalitāgniśikhopamam ||  
 6.15.15  visarpaṃ janayet tīvraṃ dāruṇaṃ pittasambhavam |
       
       sphoṭāstasyopajāyante vahnineva samīritāḥ ||  
 6.15.16  yatra yatra ca jāyante sphoṭās tatra vilīyate |
       
       hāridraṃ haritaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ koṣaṃ muñcatyabhīkṣṇaśaḥ ||  
 6.15.17  eṣo ' gnikalpo vīsarpaḥ paittiko dehanāśanaḥ |
       
       cikitsāṃ tatra kurvīta pratyākhyāya cikitsakaḥ ||  
 6.15.18  virecanaṃ snehayuktaṃ pāyayet taṃ cikitsakaḥ |
       
       pariṣekāṃś ca kurvīta kṣīrairikṣurasena vā ||  
 6.15.19  abhīkṣṇaṃ secayeccaiva himakalpena vāriṇā |
       
       kṣīrivṛkṣakaṣāyair vā kaṣāyairmadhukasya vā ||  
 6.15.20  pradehaṃ  tvasya kurvīta  śatadhaitena
      sarpiṣā |
       
       madhukotpalakalkais tu kṣīrapiṣṭaiḥ pralepayet ||  
 6.15.21  mañjiṣṭhā padmakaṃ padmaṃ candanaṃ nīlamutpalam |
       
       madhūkaṃ madhukaṃ drākṣā lāmajjakakaserukau ||  
 6.15.22  mṛṇālāni vidārī ca samudrāntā śatāvarī |
       
       sahasravīryā  naladaṃ balā dantī madhūlikā  ||  
 6.15.23  etāni samabhāgāni jaladroṇe vibhāvayet |
       
       etair eva kaṣāyaiś ca piṣṭaiś caiva vipācayet ||  
 6.15.24  ghṛtaṃ tasya hito ' bhyaṅgaḥ visarpe pittasambhave
      |
       
       nyagrodhodumbarāśvatthaplakṣavetasajās tathā ||  
 6.15.25  kalkāḥ pañca praśasyante kṣīrapiṣṭāḥ pralepane |
       
       śleṣmalānyannapānāni śleṣmalo yo niṣevate ||  
 6.15.26  tasya śleṣmā prakupito rakte tiṣṭhati dehinaḥ |
       
       tato ' sya śleṣmavīsarpo jāyate mandavedanaḥ ||  
 6.15.27 sphoṭāś ca tasya jāyante śvayathuḥ pāṇḍureva ca |
       
       tasya tandrā ca nidrā ca jvaraḥ kāsaḥ śirograhaḥ ||  
 6.15.28  cirāc ca pākaṃ vrajati visarpaḥ śleṣmasambhavaḥ |
       
       vamanaṃ recanaṃ caiva kuryāt tasya yathābalam ||  
 6.15.29  tailvakaṃ vā pibetsarpiḥ purāṇaṃ ghṛtam eva vā |
       
       sarjāśvakarṇau sustā ca sallakī somavalkalaḥ  ||  
 6.15.30  dvau karañjau kapitthatvak śirīṣośīrasāribāḥ |
       
       kṣīrivṛkṣapravālāni kuṭajatvagdhanajjayaḥ ||  
 6.15.31  dhavaḥ palāśaḥ syonākaḥ khadiro vetasāsanau |
       
       kaṣāyaṃ sādhayed etaṃ sukhoṣṇena ca secayet ||  
 6.15.32  ajākṣīreṇa piṣṭais tu kalkairetaiḥ pralepayet |
       
       tailaprasthaṃ pacedebhiḥ kaṣāyairatha peṣitaiḥ ||  
 6.15.33  abhyañjanena vīsarpaḥ  ślaiṣmikastena śāmyati |
       
       gomāṃsakhaṇḍair uṣṇaiś ca visarpam upanāhayet ||  
 6.15.34  majjabhir jāṅgalānāṃ ca tadabhyaṅgaṃ prakalpayet |
       
       māṃsopanāhaṃ kurvīta ślaiṣmike vātike ' pi vā ||  
 6.15.35  jāṅgalairgavyamāyūraiḥ kukkuṭaiśchāgalair api |
       
 yadā prakupitā  doṣās trayas tvaṅmāṃsamāśritāḥ ||  
 6.15.36  raktena saha saṃsṛṣṭāḥ śarīroddeśaceṣṭitāḥ |
       
       saṃśyāmaṃ  maṇḍalaṃ tatra jāyate kṛṣṇam eva ca ||  
 6.15.37  atha lohitaparyantaṃ visarpati savedanam |
       
       jvarastṛṣṇā ca dāhaś ca chardirmūrchā bhramas tathā ||  
 6.15.38  yadyac ca spṛśyate tena tatroṣmā na nivartate |
       
       dagdhe ca śoṇite gātraṃ śuṣkālābunibhaṃ bhavet ||  
 6.15.39  |.. |.. |.. |.. ||| yāṃ tatra kārayet |
       
       sukumāraṃ balātailaṃ tailaṃ śairīṣam eva vā |
       
       dhānvantaraṃ cāpi ghṛtaṃ pāyayed vātaśoṇite  ||  
 6.15.40  pippalīvardhamānaṃ vā takrāsavamathāpi vā |
       
       khādiraṃ vā niṣeveta vātaśoṇitapīḍitaḥ ||  
 6.15.41  nityam āsthāpayeccainaṃ mustādyena tu vastinā |
       
       pāyaye---ravastibhyām(?) athavā mādhutailikaiḥ ||  
 6.15.42  yac cikitsitam ākhyātaṃ visarpe vātasambhave |
       
       tadvātaśoṇite sarvaṃ kartavyaṃ śoṇitottare ||  
 6.15.43  yadi śoṇitamākrāntaṃ  gambhīre vātaśoṇite |
       
 vātavattaccikitseta snehapānānuvāsanaiḥ ||  
 6.15.44  mayūrakauñcalāvānāṃ vasā majjā ca lāmataḥ |
       
       pāne ' bhyaṅge ca vastau ca balātailaṃ praśasyate ||  
 6.15.45  akriyābhiḥ kriyābhir vā pakvaṃ yadvātaśoṇitam |
       
       pāṭanaṃ tatra kurvīta suvikalpya prayogavit || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ
      |
       
       iti bhele pañcadaśo ' dhyāyaḥ || || ṣoḍaśo ' dhyāyaḥ || athāto ' rśasāṃ
      cikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 6.16.1  vātātpittātkaphāccaiva  sannipātāttathaiva ca |
       
       sahajāni ca raktāc ca ṣoḍārśāṃsyatha dehinām ||  
 6.16.2  teṣāṃ nidānaṃ vakṣyāmi cikitsāṃ cānupūrvaśaḥ |
       
       adṛśyānāṃ ca yatproktaṃ dṛśyānāṃ ca yathākramam ||  
 6.16.3  vidāhigururūkṣāṇāmānūpaudakasevanāt |
       
       dadhidugdhaguḍādīnāṃ piśitānāṃ ca bhojinām ||  
 6.16.4  yavānāmudakānāṃ ca duṣṭānāmavacāraṇāt |
       
       nity ājīrṇabhujāṃ cāpi vegānāṃ ca vidhāraṇāt ||  
 6.16.5  pravāhaṇāccatimātraṃ maithunasyātisevanāt |
       
       duṣṭapānaprasaṅgāc ca kaṭhināt pṛṣṭhapīḍanāt ||  
 6.16.6  nirūhasyātiyogāc ca vastīnāṃ vibhramād api |
       
       snehapānāc ca vibhrāntānmadyadoṣācchramātkṣayāt  ||  
 6.16.7  ebhiḥ prakupitā doṣā vātapittakaphāstrayaḥ |
       
       ekaśassarvaśo vātha dvandvaśaḥ śoṇitena vā ||  
 6.16.8  gudābhiṣyandamevāśu karvanti gudamāśritāḥ |
       
       kīlās tatra prahohanti sūkṣmasarṣapasannibhāḥ ||  
 6.16.9  yavamudgādiniṣpāvakarkandhubadaropamāḥ |
       
       śarīrāṅguṣṭhamātrā vā tāmrā gostanasannibhāḥ ||  
 6.16.10  nirūḍhāste gude kīlāḥ stambhayanti gudaṃ bhṛśam |
       
       srotasāṃ gudamānahya  mūlaṃ badhnanti vāpy atha ||  
 6.16.11  nirodhātsrotasāṃ teṣāmūrdhvaṃ doṣāssamutthitāḥ |
       
       ekaikaṃ dūṣayitvā tu rogān  kurvanti cāśayān || 6.1 
 6.12.  purīṣabhedo  vaivarṇyaṃ śūlaṃ nirvāhikā  tathā
      |
       
       avadārastṛṣā dāho gudapṛṣṭhe medo jvaraḥ ||  
 6.16.13  aruciś cāvipākaś ca gātrakṣayabalakṣayau |
       
       paṇḍutvaṃ parvabhedaś ca śvayathuś cākṣikūṭayoḥ ||  
 6.16.14  glānirmaithunahāniś ca gudabhraṃśo gudagrahaḥ |
       
       arśasāṃ rūpasādṛśyaṃ pṛthaktvaṃ teṣu vakṣyate ||  
 6.16.15  kṛṣṇaṃ purīṣaṃ bhavati rūkṣaṃ kiṃcitsaphenilam |
       
       nityaṃ gāḍhapurīṣaś ca bhinnavarcāḥ punaḥ punaḥ ||  
 6.16.16  ūrupṛṣṭakaṭigrāho nity ānaddhasudurbalaḥ |
       
       jāyate parvabhedaś ca karṇaśūlastṛṣā bhramaḥ ||  
 6.16.17  arśo yakṛddhi pavano  jaṭharaṃ vāpi
      vardhayet |
       
       śūlāś cāsyopajāyanta ādhmānaṃ ca punaḥ punaḥ ||  
 6.16.18  grahaṇī dūṣitā cāsya vaivarṇyaṃ copajāyate |
       
       hṛtpārśvakoṣṭhaśūlāś ca durnāmnyanilasambhave ||  
 6.16.19  sajvaraṃ piṭakaṃ tṛṣṇā tīkṣṇavegaṃ saśoṇitam |
       
       uṣṇaṃ dravaṃ sadāhaṃ ca pittārśassūpaveśyate ||  
 6.16.20  pāṇḍuvarṇaś ca bhavati pītābhāsaś ca lakṣyate |
       
       dahyate ca gudo ' tyarthaḥ gudapākaś ca jāyate ||  
 6.16.21  śleṣmajeṣv api cārśassu picchilaṃ śuklasaṃplavam |
       
       purīṣaṃ sakaphaṃ yāti stokaṃ stokaṃ savedanam ||  
 6.16.22  upaviṣṭaściraṃ cāste niḥsvanaṃ copaveśyate |
       
 śūyate meḍhravṛṣaṇaṃ vastiś ca guda eva ca ||  
 6.16.23  aruciś cāvipākaś ca na ca pakvaṃ viricyate |
       
       śvayathuś ca viśatyenaṃ viśeṣeṇākṣikūṭayoḥ ||  
 6.16.24  etacchaleṣmasamutthānāmarśasāṃ rūpamucyate |
       
       sannipātasamutthānaṃ jānīyāt sarvalakṣaṇaiḥ ||  
 6.16.25  saṅghātaraktaṃ visraṃ vā bhinnaṃ vā pittamiśritam
      |
       
       cireṇa ca pravāho ' sya prasaktaṃ vā kadācana ||  
 6.16.26  abhiṣyaṇṇāni muñcanti raktārśāṃsyatha śoṇitam |
       
       vahanti dhārayā raktaṃ yathā viddhā sirā sthitā ||  
 6.16.27  rajasvaleva  yuvatī raktaṃ muñcantyabhīkṣṇaśaḥ |
       
       atīvamuḥ draṃ surāṃ(?) dantīṃ kakubhaṃ samayūrakam ||  
 6.16.28  gavāṃ ca mahiṣīṇāṃ ca mūtrāṇyatha samācaret |
       
       bhasmīkṛtya tu taṃ kṣāraṃ yuktyā madyena pāyayet ||  
 6.16.29  śleṣmārśāṃsi praśamayec chavayathuṃ pāṇḍutām api |
       
       arśasāṃ vātikānāṃ tu yaduktaṃ vai cikitsitam ||  
 6.16.30  tad eva ślaiṣmikāṇāṃ tu snehavarjaṃ samācaret |
       
       raktajeṣv api cārśassu kṣīramājaṃ praśasyate ||  
 6.16.31  ṛtuṃ vāpy ayanaṃ vāpi pibenmāsamathāpi vā |
       
       balābilvaśalāṭūni triphalā hastipippalī ||  
 6.16.32 karañjamadhupālāśamadhukotpalatindukaiḥ |
       
       kalkairakṣasamairetairghṛtaprasthaṃ vipācayet ||  
 6.16.33  ajākṣīre daśaguṇe tatsiddhaṃ mātrayā pibet |
       
       etadraktasamutthāni pittajāni hi yāni ca ||  
 6.16.34  arśāsi nāśayatyāśu chinnābhrāṇīva mārutaḥ |
       
       lodhraṃ dāruharidrā ca majjā baibhītakī tathā ||  
 6.16.35  taṇḍulodakapītāni madhunārśovināśanam |
       
       lākṣā haridrā mañjiṣṭhā madhukaṃ nīlamutpalam ||  
 6.16.36  ajākṣīreṇa pītāni raktajānāṃ vināśanam |
       
       śirīṣapuṣpaṃ puṣpaṃ ca kauṭajaṃ kakubhasya ca ||  
 6.16.37  dārvī haridrā lodhraṃ ca dhātakī kaṭphalaṃ vṛṣaḥ |
       
       eteṣāṃ pāyayetkalkānyuktitastaṇḍulāmbunā  ||  
 6.16.38  madhuyuktaḥ  praśamayed arśo vai
      raktapittajam  |
       
       madhukaṃ badaraṃ drākṣā mūlaṃ ca kuśakāśayoḥ ||  
 6.16.39  taṇḍulodakapītāni madhunārśovināśanam |
       
       nyagrodhodumbarāśvatthabadarīplakṣavetasāt  ||  
 6.16.40  pṛthak pravālānyārdrāṇi dvipalīnāni  saṃharet |
       
       avākpuṣpyāḥ palānyaṣṭavaṣṭau dārvyās tathaiva ca ||  
 6.16.41  śāliparṇīpṛśniparṇyoḥ pale dve dve samāvapet |
       
       dve rālaśākasya pale sarvametatsamāvapet ||  
 6.16.42  dvidroṇe salile sādhyamaṣṭabhāgāvaśeṣitam |
       
       ghṛtasya cāḍhakaḥ  sādhyaḥ sakaṣāyaḥ sukhāmbunā ||  
 6.16.43 cāṅgeryāmlikayā jātaḥ svarasaḥ snehasammitaḥ |
       
       devadārvabhayā mustā citrako bilvapeśikā ||  
 6.16.44  kaṭphalaṃ śṛṅgaberaṃ ca pippalī candanaṃ tathā |
       
       sauvīramañjanaṃ mūlaṃ pippalyāstiktarohiṇī ||  
 6.16.45 guḍapriyaṅgupuṣpaṃ ca śālmalīpicchasāhvayā 
      |
       
       vatsakasya ca bījāni tathaivātiviṣā vacā ||  
 6.16.46  etānakṣasamān bhāgān pṛthagdatvā vipācayet |
       
       etatsiddhaṃ ghṛtaṃ yuktyā raktārśo vai vināśayet ||  
 6.16.47  pittagulmamatīsāraṃ śūlaṃ jvaramarocakam |
       
       strīṇāmasṛgdaraṃ ghoraṃ raktapittaṃ pravāhikām ||  
 6.16.48  pāṇḍurogaṃ viṣaṃ kāsaṃ kṛmīṃścaivāpakarṣati |
       
       nāśanaṃ śleṣmajātānāṃ kāyāgnerdīpanaṃ param ||  
 6.16.49  garbhādhānaṃ ca vandhyānāṃ śoṣiṇāṃ cāmṛtopamam |
       
 cāṅgerīghṛtam ity etat khyātam arśovināśanam ||  
 6.16.50  balavarṇakaraṃ caiva raktagulmaharaṃ tathā |
       
       pittajeṣv api cārśassu hitaṃ tadraktajeṣv api ||  
 6.16.51  sannipātasamuttheṣu sarveṣveva ca pūjitam |
       
       arśasāṃ sahajānāntu yathāprakṛti cācaret ||  
 6.16.52  cikitsitaṃ svayaṃ buddhyā sampradhārya yathābalam |
       
       tripalaṃ śṛṅgaberasya caturthaṃ maricasya ca ||  
 6.16.53  pippalī kuḍavārdhaṃ ca cavyasya palam eva ca |
       
       tālīsapatrasya palaṃ palārdhaṃ kesarasya ca ||  
 6.16.54  dve pale pippalīmūlaṃ citrakasya palaṃ tathā |
       
       tathā tvakpatrayoḥ karṣau sūkṣmailākarṣam eva ca ||  
 6.16.55  triṃśadguḍapale śuddhe cūrṇāny etāni sādhayet |
       
       tato ' kṣamātrā vaṭikāḥ prāṇadā iti viśrutāḥ ||  
 6.16.56  tālīsapatravaṭakās ta eva parikīrtitāḥ |
       
       pūrvaṃ bhaktasya paścādvā bhakṣayet tu yathābalam ||  
 6.16.57  madyair māṃsarasair yūṣaiḥ kṣīraiś cāpy upabhojayet |
       
       etena hanti kaphajānyarśāṃsi sahajāni ca ||  
 6.16.58  vātapittasamutthāni raktajānītarāṇi ca |
       
       madātyaye mūtrakṛcchre pramehe hṛdayagrahe ||  
 6.16.59 viṣajvare pārśvaśūle kṣate kṣīṇe virecite |
       
       mandāgniviṣamāgnīnāṃ tathaiva kṛmikoṣṭhinām ||  
 6.16.60  śūlagulmaparītānāṃ chardyatīsāriṇām api |
       
       hṛdrogiṇāṃ kāmalināṃ śoṣiṇām ūrdhvavātinām ||  
 6.16.61  kāsaśvāsaparītānāṃ sevyāś ca vaṭakāḥ śubhāḥ |
       
       bhūyiṣṭhaṃ sahajānīha kṣapayanti śarīriṇam ||  
 6.16.62 tasmāc choṣopacāreṇa kuryāt tasya cikitsitam |
       
       rogānīkasya sarvasya paramarśaḥ sukīrtitam ||  
 6.16.63  tasmād arśo vistareṇa cikitset tu cikitsakaḥ |
       
       śastreṇa chedanaṃ teṣāṃ kṣāreṇa dahanaṃ tathā ||  
 6.16.64  śalyakartā prayuñjīta dṛṣṭakarmā cikitsitam |
       
       āyurvedavidā yat tu prayoktavyaṃ cikitsitam ||  
 6.16.65  ālepanābhyaṅgavidhiṃ svedakarma ca tacchṛṇu |
       
       abhyajya nābhiṃ kukṣiṃ ca vastimuṣkau gudaṃ tathā ||  
 6.16.66  amlaiḥ kṣīraiś ca mūtraiś ca sukhoṣṇaiḥ pariṣecayet |
       
       taruṇairmūlakaiḥ svinnais tathā gṛjjanakair api ||  
 6.16.67  sukhoṣṇaiḥ svedayed yuktyā piṇyākairgomayena vā |
       
 rāṭhameraṇḍamūlaṃ ca madhūkaṃ devadāru ca ||  
 6.16.68  yavacūrṇanayuktāni kṣīreṇāloḍya pāyayet |
       
       tenopanāhaṃ kurvīta svedayec ca punaḥ punaḥ ||  
 6.16.69 arśāṃsi śamamāyānti vedanā ca nivartate |
       
 vṛṣārkanaktamālānāṃ kāśmaryādaṇḍayos tathā ||  
 6.16.70 patrakvāthaiḥ  svedayet tu tatra
      caivopaveśayet |
       
 mahānimbaṃ śṛṅgaberaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ kāsīsam eva ca ||  
 6.16.71  saindhavaṃ citrakaṃ dantīṃ karavīraṃ  śilākaṇām |
       
       pūtikaṃ varuṇādvalkaṃ vidārīṃ lāṅgalāhvayām ||  
 6.16.72 viḍaṅgaṃ hemadugdhāṃ ca haritālaṃ ca peṣayet |
       
       garbheṇānena vipacet tailaṃ mūtracaturguṇe ||  
 6.16.73  snuhyarkakṣīrayoś cātra kuḍavaḥ kuḍavo bhavet |
       
       etadālepanaṃ yuktamarśasāṃ śamanaṃ param ||  
 6.16.74 kṣārakarmakaraṃ hyetanna ca dūṣayate gudam |
       
       kulīraśṛṅgī  hastyasthi balā lāṅgalikī tathā ||  
 6.16.75 hiṅgu kuṣṭhaṃ ca tutthaṃ ca bilvaṃ bhallātakāni ca
      |
       
       arśasāṃ lepanaṃ tena saptarātraṃ punaḥ punaḥ ||  
 6.16.76  śirīṣabījaṃ dvau kṣārau laṅgalī  saindhavaṃ tathā
      |
       
 snuhīkṣīreṇa piṣṭāni gavāṃ pittena bhāvayet ||  
 6.16.77  arṇāṃsi lepayet tena saptarātraṃ punaḥ punaḥ |
       
       etena liptānyarśāṃsi vinaśyanti na saṃśayaḥ ||  
 6.16.78  śigru |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |
       
       sarvamekatra saṃhṛtya snuhīkṣīreṇa peṣayet ||  
 6.16.79  karavīro ' navadyaś ca mālatī svarṇayūthikā |
       
 prakṣālanakaṣāyo ' yamarśasāṃ hita ucyate ||  
 6.16.80  sakṣaudraṃ navanītaṃ tu pralepo vraṇaropaṇaḥ |
       
       dahyate saptarātreṇa puṃstvaṃ ca na vinaśyati ||  
 6.16.81  saurmikābidadaṃ |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |
       
       |.. |.. rśātrikaṭukaṃ snuhīkṣīreṇa peṣayet ||  
 6.16.82  etadālepanaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ durnāmānaṃ vināśayet |
       
       svarṇakṣīrī tu |.. |.. |.. tsakam ||  
 6.16.83  kukkuṭsya purīṣaṃ ca snuhīkṣīreṇa peṣayet |
       
       etadālepanaṃ śreṣṭhamarśasāṃ kṣārasammitam ||  
 6.16.84 dahyante ' rśāṃsi saptāhāt puṃstvaṃ ca na
      vinaśyati |
       
       yavāssiddhārthakāś caiva bhallātakamatho vasā ||  
 6.16.85  dhūpanaṃ candanaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ śiṃsapāsāra eva ca |
       
 gavāṃ śakṛc ca vārāhaṃ patre vāriṣṭaśigruje ||  
 6.16.86  ghṛtamiśraṃ praśaṃsanti śreṣṭhaṃ dhūpanamarśasām |
       
       raktapittasamuttheṣu praśastāḥ kṣīravastayaḥ ||  
 6.16.87 tīkṣṇāḥ kaphasamuttheṣu vātikeṣv anuvāsanam |
       
 sannipātādasādhyāni cirotthānīha yāni tu |
       
 raktajāssahajā yāpyāḥ sādhyā anye trayo ' pi te || ity āha bhagavān
      ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele ṣoḍaśo ' dhyāyaḥ || || saptadaśo ' dhyāyaḥ || athātaḥ
      śvayathucikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 6.17.1  yaḥ kṣīṇamāṃso mandāgniḥ vyādhiyuktas sudurbalaḥ |
       
       gurūṇi sevate ' tyartham amlapittakarāṇi  ca ||  
 6.17.2  sadyo vānto virikto vā gurūṇyannāni sevate |
       
       upoṣitaś ca yo ' tyarthaṃ śākamūlaphalāśanaḥ ||  
 6.17.3  matsyān dadhi payo bhuṅkte divāsvapnaratiś ca yaḥ |
       
       apathyājīrṇabhojī ca naro vyāyāmasevitaḥ ||  
 6.17.4  yaś ca tiktakaṣāyāṇi kṣārāmlakaṭukāni ca |
       
       laghūni sevate ' tyarthaṃ rūkṣāṇi tu viśeṣataḥ ||  
 6.17.5  tasya vātaḥ prakupitaḥ śirā bāhyāḥ prapadyate |
       
       sa pittaṃ kopayatyāśu raktaṃ śleṣmāṇam eva ca ||  
 6.17.6  sirās tā  doṣasampūrṇāḥ saṃvisarpanti dāruṇāḥ
      |
       
       samupetyaikadeśe vā sarvagātreṣu vā punaḥ ||  
 6.17.7  evaṃ tacchvayathurnāma vyādhir bhavati dāruṇaḥ |
       
       doṣaiḥ pakvāśayasthais taiḥ so+ adhastāc chvayathur bhavet ||  
 6.17.8 pādapravṛttaḥ śvayathur narāṇāṃ nāśayaty asūn |
       
       yoṣitāṃ mukhasambhūta ubhayor api guhyajaḥ ||  
 6.17.9  bhūyiṣṭhamiha śophas tu doṣasaṅghātasaṃbhavaḥ |
       
       yas teṣāṃ tvadhiko hi syāt sa svarūpaṃ hi darśayet ||  
 6.17.10  śvayathurvātiko rūkṣaḥ kṛṣṇavarṇassavedanaḥ  |
       
       karoti pīḍito nimnamanimittaṃ ca naśyati ||  
 6.17.11 paittikaśvayathurnīlo lohitaḥ pīta eva vā |
       
       rujādāhaparītaś ca kṣiprapāko jvarānvitaḥ |
       
 
 6.17.12  śuklāvabhāso bahalaḥ  śvetapītaḥ sthiras tathā |
       
 ālambaś cāpy anāśaś ca bhṛśaṃ śophaḥ kaphātmakaḥ ||  
 6.17.13  vātapittakaphānāntu rūpaṃ syāt sānnipātike |
       
       asādhyaścopasargaś ca śvayathuḥ prasṛtaś ca yaḥ ||  
 6.17.14  nīlapītāruṇaṃ jyotirdṛśyate śvayathau yadi |
       
       kiñcitkṣaratyaslilaṃ tamasādhyaṃ vinirdiśet ||  
 6.17.15  śastradaṇḍaprahārābhyāṃ prāpātādasthibhaṅgataḥ |
       
       śvayathuḥ pañcamo dṛṣṭo bhūyiṣṭhaṃ sa tu raktajaḥ ||  
 6.17.16  abhighātāc ca jātānāṃ māṃsamasthi ca pīḍitam |
       
       sirāḥ sandūṣayatyāśu tato raktaṃ praduṣyati ||  
 6.17.17  sa dāharāgāhulo vardhate tīvravedanaḥ |
       
       kṣatavaisarpikīṃ tasya kriyāṃ kuryāc cikitsakaḥ ||  
 6.17.18  etallakṣaṇamuddiṣṭaṃ śvayathūnāṃ yathāvidhi |
       
       cikitsitaṃ pravakṣyāmi yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ ||  
 6.17.19  kalyāṇakaṃ pibetsarpirmahātiktamathāpi vā |
       
       mahadyatpañcagavyaṃ vā tatassaṃśodhayennaram  ||  
 6.17.20  harītakīṃ samadhukāṃ sakṣaudraṃ vāpi lehayet |
       
       mākṣikeṇa ca kṛṣṇāṃ ca lihyāt kṣīreṇa vā pibet ||  
 6.17.21  harītakī  śṛṅgaberaṃ devadāru ca tatsamam |
       
       etatsukhāmbunā pītaṃ śvayathūnāṃ nivāraṇam ||  
 6.17.22  ayor ajastrikaṭukaṃ trivṛtā tiktarohiṇī |
       
       triphalārasapītaṃ tacchvayathūnāṃ nivāraṇam ||  
 6.17.23  mahauṣadhaṃ devadāru sudhā varṣābhureva ca |
       
       etaiḥ kṣīraṃ samaiḥ siddhaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ śvayathunāśanam ||  
 6.17.24  gomūtrasya prayogo vā śreṣṭhaḥ śvayathunāśanaḥ |
       
       sakṣīraṃ vā pibenmūtraṃ māhiṣaṃ mūtram eva vā ||  
 6.17.25  auṣṭraṃ mūtraṃ pibeccaiva taduṣṭrīkṣīram eva vā |
       
       yathābalaṃ yathādoṣaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ śvayathunāśanam ||  
 6.17.26  mūlakāni ca siddhāni sānile bhakṣayen naraḥ |
       
       rasena mūlakānāṃ tu kurvīta pariṣecanam ||  
 6.17.27  naktamālārkamūlānāṃ vṛṣasyāragvadhasya ca |
       
       kaṣāyaṃ pariṣiktaṃ tu śvayathūnāṃ nivāraṇam ||  
 6.17.28  suvarcalā vyāghranakhaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ kaṭukarohiṇī |
       
       kākamāci  ṛṣabhako rāsnā mūrvā punarnavā ||  
 6.17.29  vārtākī niculaṃ mūlaṃ triphalā citrako vacā |
       
       kuṭherako haridre dve śyāmā mūṣakaparṇikā ||  
 6.17.30  viḍaṅgaṃ śigruvalkaṃ ca naktamālaṃ mahauṣadham |
       
       gomūtrapiṣṭaṃ śvayathau mukhyamudvartanaṃ bhavet ||  
 6.17.31  dantī viḍaṅgaṃ triphalā trayūṣaṇaṃ kaṭurohiṇī |
       
       citrakaṃ devakāṣṭhaṃ ca trivṛtā hastipippalī ||  
 6.17.32  cūrṇany etāni tulyāni dviguṇaṃ syādayor ajaḥ |
       
       kṣīreṇāloḍya pītāni śreṣṭhaṃ śvayathunāśanam ||  
 6.17.33  triphalāyās tu kuḍavaṃ pippalīkuḍavaṃ tathā |
       
       viḍaṅgamaricānāntu dve dve pale smṛte ||  
 6.17.34  palaṃ palaṃ ca kurvīta dantīcitrakayor api |
       
       palaṃ ca pippalīmūlaṃ tuṣṭebhyaś ca palaṃ tathā ||  
 6.17.35  śṛṅgaberapale dve ca gavyāt pañca palāni ca |
       
       śeṣāṇyardhapalīnāni  yāni tāni nibodha me ||  
 6.17.36  rāsnā balā gokṣurakaṃ madhukaṃ devadāru ca |
       
       vacā sātiviṣā pāṭhā mustā kaṭukarohiṇī ||  
 6.17.37  kaṭphalaṃ sāribe dve ca śyāmā bhallātakāni ca |
       
       punarnavā satejohvā tvak ca patraṃ śatāvarī ||  
 6.17.38  nidigdhikā vyāghranakhaṃ mañjiṣṭhā kuśaśambhalī |
       
       triphalā trivṛtā bhārṅgī kuṭajasya phalatvacaḥ ||  
 6.17.39  etadāhṛtya sambhāraṃ dvistāvatsyādayor ajaḥ |
       
       tadaikathyaṃ kṛtaṃ yuktyā lehayenmadhusarpiṣā ||  
 6.17.40  kṣīraṃ cānupibedyuktyā nirannakṣīrasevitā |
       
       ayor ajīyam ity etat khyātaṃ siddharasāyanam ||  
 6.17.41  saṃvatsaraprayogeṇa śatavarṣāṇi jīvati |
       
       varṣadvayena manujo dve jīveccharadāṃ śate ||  
 6.17.42  nihanyācchvayathuṃ ghoraṃ vṛkṣamindrāśaniryathā |
       
       pāṇḍurogamathārśāṃsi mandamagniṃ kṛmīnapi ||  
 6.17.43  bhagandaraṃ kāmilāṃ ca kuṣṭhāni jaṭharāṇi ca |
       
       saplīhānamapasmāraṃ śūlāni parikartikām ||  
 6.17.44  atisāraṃ pramehāṃś ca kṣatakāsaṃ kṣayaṃ tathā |
       
       yasminyasminvikāre tu yogo ' yaṃ samprayujyate ||  
 6.17.45  taṃ taṃ nihanti vai rogaṃ devārīn keśavo yathā |
       
       anuprayogo lājānāṃ saktavo madhunā saha ||  
 6.17.46  kṣīrānupānaṃ lehyo ' yaṃ divasān spta pañca vā |
       
       arśassvāmātisāreṣu vidhiḥ syāt parikartane ||  
 6.17.47 tathā kṣīṇeṣu kāseṣu jvareṣu viṣameṣu ca |
       
 varṣothito ' pi śvayathustasmānmāsena śāmyati ||  
 6.17.48  rasāyanaprayogāc ca pūrvoddiṣṭādyathāvidhi  |
       
       śālīn saṣaṣṭikāṃś caiva navānnavikṛtīs tathā ||  
 6.17.49  kṣārāmlalavaṇāṃś cāpi sadā dhūmaṃ vivarjayet |
       
       āgantuśvayathurvāpi yo vā syāddoṣasambhavaḥ ||  
 6.17.50  laṅganaiś ca vilepaiś ca raktasekaiḥ praśāmyati |
       
       avipāko jvaraśchardirdaurbalyaṃ parikartikā |
       
       śvāso ' tisāro hikkā ca śophasyopadravāḥ smṛtāḥ || ity āha bhagavān
      ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele saptadaśo ' dhyāyaḥ || || aṣṭādaśo ' dhyāyaḥ || athāta
      udāvartacikitsitaṃ vyākhayāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 6.18.1  prakṛtyā vātalo yas tu rūkṣāṇyannāni sevate |
       
       kaṣāyaṃ kaṭukānnityaṃ rasāṃstiktāṃś ca sevate ||  
 6.18.2  karkandhūni kapitthāni karīralikucāni ca |
       
       pārāvatāni bhavyāni yaccānyatphalamīdṛśam ||  
 6.18.3  śuktakāni ca vallūraṃ piṇyākaṃ kodravaudanam |
       
       abhiṣyandīni  kaṭukaṃ vetraśākaṃ ca sevate ||  
 6.18.4  vātamūtrpurīṣāṇāṃ vidhṛtyā maithunasya ca |
       
       etairanyaiś ca gurubhir hetubhiḥ kupito ' nilaḥ ||  
 6.18.5  nigṛhṇāti gudadvāraṃ śarīraṃ vyāpya sarvaśaḥ |
       
       sa śoṣayati tatrasthaḥ śarīraṃ śoṣayan bhṛśam ||  
 6.18.6  adhovahāni srotāṃsi pittaśleṣmavahāny api |
       
       mūtrānnamalavāhīni badhnāti pavano bhṛśam ||  
 6.18.7 vātasandūṣitāste tu dhāvanto
      hyūrdhvamāsthitāḥ |
       
 āmapakvāśayasthāna  unmādyanti  sudāruṇam ||  
 6.18.8  ūrdhvaṃ hyapānassamprāpya codānena samāgataḥ
      |
       
       udārvata iti proktaḥ śastrasarpaviṣopaḥ ||  
 6.18.9  atha śūlāni tīvrāṇi dāho mūrcchā vivarṇatā |
       
 śūyate vastimūlaṃ ca mūtravarvograhas tathā ||  
 6.18.10 vatāvatha ca kukṣau ca hṛdi pārśvodare tathā |
       
       devanābhiparītaś ca nissaṃjño vetate ' sakṛt ||  
 6.18.11 niśvasity atha tāmyaṃś ca tṛṣyaty api ca hikkate |
       
       upadravā udāvarte śṛṇu teṣāṃ cikitsitam ||  
 6.18.12  susnigdhamenamabhyajya tailena lavaṇena ca |
       
       saṃkare prastare svede droṇyāṃ vā svedayet tataḥ ||  
 6.18.13  tato ' sya gudamabhyajya nirūhaṃ sampradāpayet |
       
       ekaṃ dvau vā bhiṣak kṛtvā yāvadvā sādhu manyate ||  
 6.18.14  surirūḍhaṃ ca taṃ jñātvā sukhāmbupariṣecitam |
       
       uṣṇodakānupānaṃ ca bhojyenmṛdumodanam ||  
 6.18.15  snuhāyāḥ patraśākena trivṛcchākena vā punaḥ |
       
       tābhyāṃ yūṣeṇa bhuñjīta yaccānyadbhedanaṃ param ||  
 6.18.16  nityaṃ bhinnapurīṣais taṃ bhojanīyair upācaret |
       
       evaṃ tasya purīṣaṃ hi vāyurbhūyo na śoṣayet  || |.. |.. |.. |..
      |.. |.. |.. |.. |
       
       |ekonaviṃśo ' dhyāyaḥ || |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |..
      |.. |.. |.. |.. |..  
 
 
 6.19.1 sarvāṇy etāni liṅgāni dṛśyante marmarogiṇaḥ |
       
       sannipātasamuttho ' sau naiva sidhyati karmaṇā ||  
 6.19.2  nirbhidyate devanārtaṃ dahyate marma dūyate |
       
       bhaktadveṣo jvaro mūrcchā śvāsaś ca paritapyate ||  
 6.19.3  bhinnavarṇo ' tha dīnaś ca hṛdi kaṇḍūś ca jāyate |
       
       hṛdrogaḥ krimijaḥ proktaḥ pañcamassa tu durjayaḥ ||  
 6.19.4  sādhyāstrayas tu hṛdrogā vātapittakaphātmakāḥ |
       
 dvau cāsādhyau smṛtau tatra sādhyānāṃ śṛṇu bheṣajam ||  
 6.19.5  hṛdrogiṇaṃ snehayitvā śamayecchodhayet tathā |
       
       laṅghayed acirottyaṃ taṃ hṛdrogaṃ vātikādvinā ||  
 6.19.6  harītakī vacā rāsnā pippalyau viśvabheṣajam |
       
       śaṭhī puṣkaramūlaṃ ca cūrṇaṃ hṛdroganāśanam ||  
 6.19.7  pāṭhāvacāyavakṣārā abhayā cāmlavetasam |
       
       durālabhā citrakaṃ ca tryūṣaṇaṃ lavaṇatrayam ||  
 6.19.8  śaṭhī puṣkaramūlaṃ ca tintriṇīkaṃ sadāḍimam |
       
       mātuluṅgyāś ca bījāni sūkṣmacūrṇāni kārayet ||  
 6.19.9  sukhodakena madyair vā cūrṇāny etāni pāyayet |
       
       arśaḥ śūlaṃ sahṛdrogaṃ gulmaṃ cāpi vyapohati ||  
 6.19.10  sauvarcalaṃ śṛṅgaberaṃ dāḍimaṃ sāmlavetasam |
       
       śvāsahṛdrogaśamanam idaṃ syāddhiṅgupañcamam  ||  
 6.19.11 pañcāśadabhayākalkaṃ pale sauvarcalasya ca |
       
       caturguṇajale mukhyaṃ ghṛtaprasthaṃ vipācayet ||  
 6.19.12  etadvallabhakaṃ nāma prāṇināṃ sarpiruttamam |
       
       amṛtapratimaṃ sṛṣṭaṃ śvāsahṛdroganāśanam ||  
 6.19.13  pibetkalyāṇakaṃ sarpirdhānvantaramathāpi vā |
       
       mātuluṅgasya ca rasaṃ pibetkṣārāgadānapi ||  
 6.19.14  śatapākaṃ balātailaṃ śairīṣaṃ sukumārakam |
       
       tailāny etāni seveta sadā hṛdgadapīḍitaḥ ||  
 6.19.15  pibedrasāyanaṃ sarpiḥ kṣīrāṇi ca guḍānapi |
       
       pittahṛdrogaśamanā ye coktā ghṛtamodakāḥ ||  
 6.19.16  jīvakarṣabhakau drākṣā śarkarā śreyasī balā |
       
       dve mede dve ca kākolyau kharjūryasitamutpalam ||  
 6.19.17  ghṛtaprasthaṃ pacedebhiḥ tulyāṃśairmāhiṣaṃ bhiṣak |
       
       caturguṇena payasā pātavyaṃ yuktitaś ca tat ||  
 6.19.18  vātapittasamutthāne hṛdroge nāśanaṃ param |
       
       vasā lābhena majjā ca tulyaṃ tailaghṛtaṃ tathā ||  
 6.19.19  amūni lābhato dadyādatha cāpi caturguṇam |
       
       vacā trikaṭukaṃ rāsnā jīvantī jīvako balā ||  
 6.19.20  nidigdhikā cāṃśumatī nīlī bhārṅgīṃ punarnavā |
       
       siddhamebhir mahāsnehaṃ balamālokya pāyayet ||  
 6.19.21  hṛdrogaṃ vātikaṃ snehaḥ sadya eva cikitsati |
       
       vicārayetsvayaṃ buddhyā vaidyo hṛdrogabheṣajam ||  
 6.19.22  madhuraṃ pittahṛdroge snigdhamuṣṇaṃ ca vātike |
       
       trayas tu pariśeṣā ye tīkṣṇoṣṇaistānupācaret ||  
 6.19.23  kṣāraiḥ kṣārāgadaiś caiva vamanaissavirecanaiḥ |
       
       cikitsitaṃ vistareṇa yaduktaṃ kṛmikoṣṭhinām ||  
 6.19.24  tadeva  krimihṛdroge kartavyamanasūyayā |
       
       audakānūpamāṃsāni dadhi dugdhaṃ guḍo rasaḥ ||  
 6.19.25  abhiṣyandakaraṃ sarvaṃ vātahṛdroganāśanam |
       
       etānyeva tu śeṣeṣu hṛdrogeṣu vivarjayet |
       
       laghūni cānnapānāni śasyante teṣu sarvadā || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele ekonaviṃśo ' dhyāyaḥ || || viṃśo ' dhyāyaḥ || athātaḥ
      kāsacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 6.20.1  pañca kāsāḥ samuddiṣṭā vātapittakaphātmakāḥ |
       
       kṣatajaḥ kṣayajaśceti teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam ||  
 6.20.2  udāvartādabhīghātād vyāyāmāc cāpi karśanāt |
       
       saṃbhojanāddivāsvapnād  drutapānātpralambanāt ||  
 6.20.3  karśitānāṃ ca rogebhyo doṣāsātmyakṛtātkṣayāt  |
       
       tīkṣoṣṇagurusevābhir nṛṇāṃ kāsā bhavanti te ||  
 6.20.4  teṣāṃ rūpāṇi vakṣyāmi cikitsāṃ ca pṛthagvidhām |
       
       mārutātkāsate śuṣkaṃ śūkapūrṇagalo yathā ||  
 6.20.5  niṣṭhīvati ca śuṣkaṃ ca tatra mukte na kāsate |
       
 pratāmyetkāsamānasya hṛdayaṃ cāvakṛṣyate ||  
 6.20.6  pārśve ca rujato ' tyarthaṃ śvāsena ca vikūjati |
       
       śaṅkhayor jāyate śūlaṃ tāluśoṣas tathaiva ca ||  
 6.20.7  śyāve netre ca vīkṣyete svaro varṇaś
      ca bhidyate |
       
       viśeṣādriktakoṣṭhaś ca kāsate vātapīḍitaḥ ||  
 6.20.8 amlarūkṣānnapānādivyāyāmoṣṇaniṣevaṇāt |
       
 kaṭukakṣārarūkṣānnatīkṣṇamadyaniṣevaṇāt ||  
 6.20.9  sadāhaḥ sajvaraś caiva pittakāsaḥ pravartate |
       
 hāridraṃ kaṭukoṣṇaṃ ca pītaṃ ṣṭhīvati cāti saḥ ||  
 6.20.10  mukhasya kaṭukatvaṃ ca tṛṣṇā cāsyopajāyate |
       
 hāridre cakṣuṣī cāsya lakṣyete pittakāsinaḥ ||  
 6.20.11  abhiṣyandigurusnigdhaśītamedyānnasevinaḥ  |
       
       divāsvapnaprasaktasya  vegāṃś cāpi nirundhataḥ ||  
 6.20.12  kaphapraseko bahalaḥ kāsastasyopajāyate |
       
       gurutvaṃ śiraso ' tyarthaṃ mādhuryaṃ vadanasya ca ||  
 6.20.13 kaphāt styānaṃ ca hṛdayaṃ bhaktasyānabhinandanam |
       
       stambhaścaivāvipākaś ca kaphakāsasya lakṣaṇam ||  
 6.20.14  vyāyāmādbhāraharaṇānnigrahādaśvadantinām |
       
       nihanyate yasya vakṣaḥ kṣatakāsaḥ sa ucyate ||  
 6.20.15  saraktaṃ pūtipūyābhaṃ grathitaṃ doṣasañcayam |
       
       niṣṭhīvati sa kāsārto jvaryate cātisaryate ||  
 6.20.16  uro nirbhidyamānaṃ ca manyate praśvasity api |
       
       sa tāmyetkāsamānaś ca tṛṣṇā śoṣo mukhasya ca ||  
 6.20.17 muhurāśūyate kaṇṭhaḥ svarabhedaś ca jāyate |
       
       saghoṣaṃ kāsate cāpi vikṛtaṃ bhinnavisvaram ||  
 6.20.18  durgandhaṃ ca tathodgāraṃ kṣatakāse vimuñcati |
       
       sarveṣāṃ sannipātāc ca kṣayakāsaḥ pravartate ||  
 6.20.19  tasya jvaraḥ pārśvarujā hastapādaṃ ca dahyate |
       
       kāsamānaś ca niṣṭhīvet kaphapūrvaṃ sa śoṇitam ||  
 6.20.20  kṣīyete balavarṇau ca gātraṃ ca parihīyate |
       
       na cāsya svadate bhojyaṃ na bhuktaṃ ca vipacyate ||  
 6.20.21  atisāro jvaraśchardirmūrcchā cāsyopajāyate |
       
       kṣayakāsassamākhyātaḥ sa cāsādhyaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||  
 6.20.22  kṣatakāsas tu yāpyaḥ syāt sādhyānāṃ sādhanaṃ śṛṇu |
       
       balavantaṃ snehitaṃ ca śodhanaissamupācaret ||  
 6.20.23  śodhitaṃ bhojayeccainaṃ purāṇān śāliṣaṣṭikān |
       
       jāṅgalānāṃ ca māṃsāni niṣevenmṛgapakṣiṇām ||  
 6.20.24  audakānūpamāṃsāni gurūṇi ca vivarjayet |
       
       daśakalkopasiddhaṃ vā kalyaṇakamathāpi vā ||  
 6.20.25  rasayanaṃ ca seveta sarpiḥ sarpirguḍāni ca |
       
       sarpirmodakayogaṃ vā rasāyanavidhiṃ tathā ||  
 6.20.26  yaduktaṃ śoṇite pūrvaṃ tatkāseṣv api yojayet |
       
       pippalyāmalakaṃ drākṣā tugākṣīryatha śarkarā ||  
 6.20.27  lājā ghṛtaṃ mākṣikaṃ ca lehaḥ kāsavināśanaḥ |
       
       pippalyāmalakaṃ rāsnā leho mākṣikasaṃyutaḥ ||  
 6.20.28  harītakyāssapippalyāścūrṇaṃ mākṣikasaṃyutam |
       
       pralehaḥ syānmadhughṛtaṃ sakṣaudraṃ śarkarānvitam ||  
 6.20.29  tryūṣaṇaṃ triphalāṃ caiva padmakaṃ devadāru ca |
       
       rāsnāṃ balāṃ viḍaṅgāni  sūkṣmacūrṇāni kārayet ||  
 6.20.30  cūrṇaṃ śarkarayā yuktaṃ lehayenmadhusarpiṣā |
       
       eṣa lehaḥ praṇudati pañca kāsān samutthitān ||  
 6.20.31  yavakṣāraṃ viḍaṅgāni hiṅgu bhārṅgī mahauṣadham |
       
       saindhavaṃ  pippalī rāsnā tulyāny etāni cūrṇayet ||  
 6.20.32  ghṛtamātrāyutaṃ cūrṇaṃ pibetkāsavināśanam |
       
       mandāgnitāṃ tamaśvāsaṃ hikkāṃ caivāpakarṣati ||  
 6.20.33  samūlaphalaśākhāṃ tu kuṭṭayetkaṇṭakārikām |
       
       tāṃ pacetsaliladroṇe caturbhāgāvaśeṣitam ||  
 6.20.34  kaṣāyaṃ taṃ parisrāvya punaragnāvadhiśrayet |
       
       ghṛtaṃ ca yuktyā dātavyaṃ kalkāṃścemānpradāpayet ||  
 6.20.35  durālabhā chinnaruhā tryūṣaṇaṃ citrakaṃ tathā |
       
       rāsnā karkaṭakākhyā ca pippalīmūlam eva ca ||  
 6.20.36  etānyardhapalīnāni  tathā phāṇitaśarkarā |
       
       palāni viṃśatiṃ datvā taṃ lehaṃ sāndramuddharet ||  
 6.20.37  śīte dadyāt pippalīnāṃ cūrṇasya kuḍavaṃ mitam |
       
       tugākṣīryāś ca kuḍavaṃ madhunaḥ kuḍavaṃ tathā ||  
 6.20.38  taṃ lihyānmātrayā lehaṃ pañcakāsavināśanam |
       
       hṛdrogānatha hikkāṃ ca śvāsaṃ caivāpakarṣati ||  
 6.20.39  siddhaṃ mantraṃ yathā sarpo nātikrāmedudīritam |
       
       tathā lehamimaṃ kāso nātikrāmati dehinām ||  
 6.20.40  daśamūlīmapānārgaṃ śaṅkhapuṣpīṃ śaṭhīṃ vacām |
       
       citrakaṃ cātmaguptāṃ ca pippalīmūlam eva ca ||  
 6.20.41  balāṃ puṣkaramūlaṃ ca tathaiva gajapippalīm |
       
       dvipalīnān  pṛthag dadyāt pratyagraṃ cābhayāśatam ||  
 6.20.42 yavāḍhakaṃ sahaibhiś ca jalaṃ pañcāḍhakaṃ pacet |
       
       avatārya yavaissiddhair uddharet tu harītakīḥ ||  
 6.20.43  bhedanaṃ tāsu kartavyaṃ tato vaṃśaśalākayā || |.. |..
      |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. || ekaviṃśo ' dhyāyaḥ
      || |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |..
      |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |..
      |.. |..  etadālepanaṃ kāryaṃ śaṅkhakasya vināśanam |
       
       etānyeva tu sarvāṇi kaṣāyam upadhārayet ||  
 
 
 6.21.1  tena śītena kartavyaṃ bahuśaḥ pariṣecanam ||  
 6.21.2  nityaṃ vegapratīghātādajīrṇādhyaśanādapi  |
       
       raktaṃ vāyuś ca kupitau mastake pratitiṣṭhataḥ ||  
 6.21.3  sa mastakagato vāyuḥ raktaṃ caikatra mūrchitam |
       
       udaye ' rkasya saṃpātādādity akaradūṣitam ||  
 6.21.4  vedanāṃ janayet tīvrāṃ śaṅkhayor mūrdhni gaṇḍayoḥ |
       
       nighnanniva śiro ' tyarthaṃ muhurgṛhṇāti pāṇinā ||  
 6.21.5  niṣyandate hi mastiṣkamādity oṣmasamuddhatam 
      |
       
       vardhate vardhamāne tu sūrye śīrṣarujā hyataḥ ||  
 6.21.6  sa mastiṣkaśca  nirvāti divasasya parikṣayāt |
       
       sūryāvarta iti prāhurmunayo ' nena hetunā ||  
 6.21.7  kalyāṇakaṃ pibetsarpiḥ sūryāvartanipīḍitaḥ |
       
       virecanaṃ ca kāryaṃ syāt tatrarahā śīrṣavirecanam ||  
 6.21.8  nasyakarma tathā kuryāt snehaś cottarabhaktikaḥ |
       
       ghṛtatailavasābhis tu dhāryāḥ syuḥ śīrṣavastayaḥ ||  
 6.21.9  mayūrān kukkuṭān lāvān kṣīreṇa saha sādhayet |
       
       tatkṣīramanthanodbhūtaṃ  navanītamathoddharet ||  
 6.21.10 tatkṣīre ṣaḍguṇe sādhyaṃ jīvanīyaissahauṣadhaiḥ |
       
       tato ' sya nasyaṃ dātavyaṃ sūryāvartavināśanam ||  
 6.21.11  bilvamaṃśumatī rāsnā sahadevā punarnavā |
       
       kālā guḍūcī suṣavī padmakaṃ madhukaṃ balā ||  
 6.21.12  etānyājena dugdhena siddhāni pariṣecanam |
       
       etair eva uṣadhaissiddhaṃ sarpirājaṃ  vināśayet ||  
 6.21.13  jāṅgalāni ca māṃsāni kārayed upanāhanam |
       
       tenāsya śāmyati vyādhissūryāvartassudāruṇaḥ ||  
 6.21.14  palalaṃ dadhi matsyāṃś ca piṣṭānnavikṛtīḥ payaḥ |
       
 divāsvapnaṃ ca bhajatastrayaḥ kupyanti dhātavaḥ ||  
 6.21.15 manyāpāś cātyaghāṭāsu tīvrāṃ kurvanti vedanām |
       
       tataścaivotthitā  tīkṣṇā bhruvoś cākṣṇoś ca tiṣṭhati ||  
 6.21.16  spandayed gaṇḍapārśve ca hanū vāsthāya tiṣṭhati |
       
 netrayor āmayān kuryāc chaṅkhau cāsya pratodayet ||  
 6.21.17  anantavāta ity eṣa śīrṣavyādhiḥ sudāruṇaḥ |
       
       sannipātasamutthānas tasya vakṣyāmi bheṣajam ||  
 6.21.18 lalāṭasthasirāṃ vidhyet snehapānaṃ ca kārayet |
       
       kāyaṃ virecayed asya  śiraś cāpi virecayet ||  
 6.21.19  cikitsitaṃ yathākhyātaṃ sūryāvartaśirograhe |
       
       anantavāte tatkāryaṃ tadā sampadyate sukham ||  
 6.21.20  sambhojanāddivāsvapnācchardikṣavathunigrahāt |
       
       abhighātātpratāpāc ca vegasandhāraṇād api ||  
 6.21.21  śirovahāṃ bhṛśaṃ gṛhya tasyobhau kaphamārutau |
       
       śīrṣārdhaṃ śaṅkhamūlaṃ ca dārayantau ca tiṣṭhataḥ ||  
 6.21.22  śvayathurjāyate gaṇḍe cakṣuścaivaṃ virajyate |
       
       ardhāvabhedako nāma śīrṣavyādhiḥ sudustaraḥ ||  
 6.21.23  virecanaṃ ca śiraso nasyakarma ca kārayet |
       
       lābhataśca  vasā sarvā ghṛtaṃ tailaṃ ca yuktitaḥ  ||  
 6.21.24  tasyaiva mahatīṃ mātrāṃ pāyayet tena sidhyati |
       
       kārpāsabījaṃ māṣāṃś ca godhūmān sarṣapān yavān ||  
 6.21.25  pañcamūlyau tathā dve ca kṣīreṇa saha sādhayet |
       
 auṣṇyamudvahatā tena nāḍīsvedena svedayet ||  
 6.21.26  uṣṇaiś ca taiḥ kṣīrasiddhaiḥ kuryāt tasyopanāhanam |
       
       karañjaṃ śigrubījāni tvak patraṃ śarkarā tathā ||  
 6.21.27  sarveṣāṃ śīrṣarogāṇāmetacchīrṣavirecanam |
       
       śiraso ' nte lalāṭānte śaṅkhaparyanta eva ca ||  
 6.21.28  manyayoś cāpi pippalyā dahetkāṇḍena vā punaḥ |
       
       tathaivārdhāvabhedasya tenaiva vidhinā bhavet ||  
 6.21.29  vātike śīrṣaroge ca dahanaṃ ślaiṣmike ' pi ca |
       
       tasmād atipravṛddheṣu śīrṣarogeṣu buddhimān ||  
 6.21.30  āraṇyapippalībhir vā dahetkāṇḍena vā punaḥ |
       
       rūkṣānnasevināṃ nityaṃ tathodāvartinām api ||  
 6.21.31  ūrdhvamutkramya pavanaḥ śiraḥkampamudīrayet |
       
       taṃ pāyayenmṛdu snehaṃ balātailamathāpi vā ||  
 6.21.32  nasyakarma snehapānaṃ nityaṃ caivānuvāsanam |
       
       samaśnataḥ sarvarasānajīrṇādhyaśanādapi  ||  
 6.21.33  kurvanti mūrdhni śvayathuṃ trayo doṣāssamutthitāḥ |
       
       tasya pūrvaṃ śirāṃ vidhyet pibejjīrṇaghṛtaṃ tathā ||  
 6.21.34  viśodhanaṃ dhūmapānaṃ śirasaś ca virecanam |
       
       ity eṣa śīrṣarogāṇāṃ pradeśaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ||  
 6.21.35  antaḥkaṇṭhagatān rogān vakṣyāmi sacikitsitān |
       
       uccaiḥ pralāpātsaṃrambhādatīvādhyaśanādibhiḥ  ||  
 6.21.36  rūkṣānnapānasevābhir bhinatti pavanaḥ param |
       
       dhūmāyate galas tasya tathā dhumadhumāyate ||  
 6.21.37  dūyate hṛdayaṃ cāsya svarabhedaśca  mārutāt |
       
       nasyakarmāṇi pāne ca balātailaṃ praśasyate ||  
 6.21.38 kaphavātottare dhāryās tathaiva kabalagrahāḥ |
       
       pippalī pippalīmūlaṃ maricāni harītakī ||  
 6.21.39  śṛṅgaberaṃ yavakṣāro lodhraṃ tejovatī tathā |
       
       etāni samabhāgāni cūrṇāni madhunā saha ||  
 6.21.40  arocake śleṣmabhave pradhānaṃ mukhadhāvanam |
       
       pippalyo madhukaṃ mūrvā candanaṃ kamalotpalam ||  
 6.21.41  uśīraṃ padmakaṃ lodhramelā lāmajjakaṃ tathā |
       
       etāni smabhāgāni kṣaudreṇa saha sādhayet ||  
 6.21.42  dviguṇaṃ śarkarāṃ dattvā pittajāyāmathārucau |
       
       ajājyo maricaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ bilvaṃ sauvarcalaṃ tathā ||  
 6.21.43  madhukaṃ śarkarā tailaṃ vātike mukhadhāvanam |
       
       jambvāmrapallavaṃ lodhraṃ triphalā cavyaciktrakau ||  
 6.21.44  paṭolaṃ naktamālaṃ ca śirīṣaḥ khadirāsanau |
       
       dārvī haridrā mustā ca tejohvā madhukaṃ balā ||  
 6.21.45  etāni samabhāgāni kaṣāyam upasādhayet |
       
       ity eṣa kabalagrāhaḥ kartavyo madhusaṃyutaḥ ||  
 6.21.46 sārdrakaś ca kapittho vā
      savyoṣmadhuśarkaraḥ  |
       
       arocakeṣu sarveṣu praśasto dhāraṇo  mukhe ||  
 6.21.47  ajājyo maricaṃ drākṣā tintriṇīkaṃ sadāḍimam |
       
       sauvarcalaṃ kāravīṃ ca guḍamākṣikasaṃyutam ||  
 6.21.48  drākṣāghautakaya |.. |.. (?) mukhabiśodhanaḥ |
       
       arocakānāṃ sarveṣāṃ praśastaḥ  kabalottamaḥ ||  
 6.21.49  sambhavanti trayo doṣāḥ gale nāsaudaneriṇīm |
       
       galaśuṇḍīṃ vardhayanti ghorāṃ galavisāriṇīm ||  
 6.21.50  sirāvyadhaḥ snehapānaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ śīrṣavirecanam |
       
 śastrāvacāro dhūmaś ca nāśayed galaśuṇḍikām ||  
 6.21.51  vātikaḥ karṇaśūlaś ca karṇavātaś ca vātikaḥ |
       
       bādhiryaṃ ca samākhyātam vātaśleṣmasamudbhavam ||  
 6.21.52  snehapānāni nasyaṃ ca nāḍīsvedopanāhanam |
       
       ānūpāś ca vasā majjāḥ praśastāḥ karṇapūraṇe  ||  
 6.21.53  pippalyau bilvamūlaṃ ca kuṣṭhaṃ madhukam eva ca |
       
       lodhravyāghranakhaṃ māṃsī sūkṣmailā devadāru ca ||  
 6.21.54  garbheṇānena tailasya prasthaṃ mṛdvagninā pacet |
       
 mūlakasyārdrakasyāpi rasau snehasamau tathā ||  
 6.21.55  tena karṇe picuṃ dadyānnasyakarma ca kārayet |
       
       tenopaśāmyati kṣipraṃ karṇaśūlassudāruṇaḥ ||  
 6.21.56  śairīṣaṃ śatapākaṃ ca balātailaṃ ca miśrakam |
       
       āśu karṇagataṃ śūlaṃ bādhiryaṃ cāpakarṣati  ||  
 6.21.57 chāgasarpamayūrāṇāṃ nakraśalyakayor api |
       
       tulāṃ māṃsasya vipacet kṣīradroṇeṣu saptasu ||  
 6.21.58  pādabhāgāvaśiṣṭantu śītaṃ pūtaṃ vimanthayet |
       
       tatra yannavanītaṃ syāt tadebhir vipacetsamaiḥ ||  
 6.21.59  kṣavaḥ |.. phaṇijjako ||| saindhavaṃ balā |
       
       vacā vyāghranakho  māṃsī devadārvagarū tathā ||  
 6.21.60  jīvakarṣabhakau medā śṛṅgī karkaṭakasya ca |
       
       ātmaguptāphalaṃ drākṣā tvakpatramatha vālukam ||  
 6.21.61  tat sarvaṃ srāvayitvā tu svanuguptaṃ nidhāpayet |
       
 picumabhyañjanaṃ pānaṃ vastikarma ca kārayet ||  
 6.21.62  etena śīrṣarogāś ca karṇaśūlāni yāni ca |
       
       karṇasrāvāś ca śāmyanti rogā jatrugatāś ca ye ||  
 6.21.63  etadvātottare proktaṃ karṇaśūle cikitsitam |
       
 ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi raktajaṃ krimijaṃ ca yat ||  
 6.21.64  yadā duṣṭaṃ pittaraktaṃ karṇameva  pradhāvati |
       
       śvayathuś ca hi rāgaś ca karṇaśūlaś ca jāyate ||  
 6.21.65  vidhyetsirāṃ lalāṭasya dadyāccāsya virecanam |
       
       |.. mle śirapānaṃ (?) ca tathā śīrṣavirecanam ||  
 6.21.66  akriyābhiḥ kriyābhiś ca karṇe pākaṃ niyacchati |
       
       tasyopanāhaṃ kurvīta vraṇatailaṃ ca ropaṇam ||  
 6.21.67  tathā karṇaśalākābhiḥ karṇasrāvaṃ viśodhayet |
       
       trayūṣaṇaṃ saindhavaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ mañjiṣṭhā madhukaṃ tathā ||  
 6.21.68  rāsnā haridrā tejohvā varāṅgaṃ tilvakatvacaḥ  |
       
       lākṣā mūrvā rubūrkākakesarāsanavīraṇāḥ  ||  
 6.21.69  sūkṣmailā tagaraṃ patraṃ tvagvyāghranakham eva ca |
       
       āramālatilā māṣā bhūrjagranthirnidigdhikā ||  
 6.21.70  etaistulyakṛtairbhāgais tailaprasthaṃ vipācayet |
       
       bhoginaś ca vasāṃ dadyānmāṃsaṃ babhroḥ kharasya ca ||  
 6.21.71  etena pūrayetkarṇaṃ muhūrtāccāvanāmayet |
       
       karṇasrāvaṃ karṇaśūlaṃ bādhiryaṃ karṇavedanām ||  
 6.21.72  sarvāṃś caiva śirorogān tailametanniyacchati |
       
       karṇasrotassu ruddheṣu tāluke mastake tathā ||  
 6.21.73 vedanā jāyate tīvrā vidāhastodavibhramau |
       
       etani karṇaśūlasya kṛmijasya manīṣiṇaḥ ||  
 6.21.74  rūpāṇyāhuḥ  samastāni sa cāsādhya ihocyate |
       
       pataṅgaḥ śatapadyaś ca tathā kīṭapipīlikāḥ ||  
 6.21.75  praviśya karṇasroto vai bhṛśaṃ kurvanti vedanām |
       
 karṇau nistudyatas tasya tathā ghuraghurāyaṇam ||  
 6.21.76  kīṭe carati ruk tīvrā niṣpandena bhaved aruk |
       
 madhuśuktena payasā surayā vā++āsavena vā ||  
 6.21.77  uṣṇena pūrayetkarṇaṃ muhūrtāccāvanāmayet |
       
       srute kīṭe tu yadyasya karṇasrāvaḥ pravartate || yathoktaṃ tasya kurvīta
      karṇasrāvacikitsitam  |
       
       |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. || dvāviṃśo '
      dhyāyaḥ || |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |..
      
 
 
 6.22.1  ajīrṇe yaddivā bhuktaṃ na duṣyati yathā nṛṇām |
       
 vyuṣitaṃ dūṣyate vāpi tatra hetuṃ nibodha me ||  
 6.22.2.  vyāyacchato  vicarataḥ vyākṣiptamanasas tathā |
       
       mande rasapraseke ca divābhuktaṃ na duṣyati ||  
 6.22.3  kamalapratimaṃ prāhurhṛdayaṃ divasakṣayāt |
       
       saṃvṛtaṃ  vivṛtaṃ caiva bhavatyādity araśmibhiḥ ||  
 6.22.4  vibuddhe hṛdaye cāsya srotassu vivṛteṣu ca |
       
       hṛdayaprabhavāś cāsya srotobhir vivṛtairdivā ||  
 6.22.5  na kledam upagacchanti divā tenāsya dhātavaḥ |
       
       ajīrṇe prātarāśe tu tṛptasyāpi divā tatha ||  
 6.22.6  anena vidhinā bhūyaḥ sāyamāśo na duṣyati |
       
 vyuṣitaṃ dūṣyate cāpi rogān sañjanayaty api ||  
 6.22.7 saṃvṛteṣv ayaneṣvevaṃ vāyuś cāgniś ca dehinām |
       
       vyāyāminaṃ vinaiveha  tau hyannaṃ pacato niśi ||  
 6.22.8 mlāne tu hṛdaye rātrāvutkleśaikapadeṣu ca |
       
       saṃvṛteṣv api srotassu vyāyāmaṃ ca na sevate ||  
 6.22.9  yadannaśeṣaṃ hṛdaye tiṣṭhatyāmāśaye ' pi ca |
       
       tenāsyāmapralambena dehe paktimagacchatā ||  
 6.22.10  hṛdaye  vyādhite  ruddhe viṇmūtre ' sya
      niśātyaye |
       
       upasthite cānnarase pittaśleṣmasamudbhave  ||  
 6.22.11  annasaṃpuṭaruddhe ca mārute cordhvamāsthite |
       
       hṛdayagrahamutkleśaṃ  hṛllāsaṃ gurugātratām ||  
 6.22.12  tadannaśeṣaṃ janayenmūrchā parikinī(?) tṛṣām |
       
       jvaraṃ chardimatīsāraṃ hikkāṃ bhaktasya vārucim ||  
 6.22.13  ajīrṇe vyuṣitaṃ kuryād rogānetān viṣopamān |
       
       tasmād ajīrṇe vyuṣitaṃ bhojanaṃ pratiṣidhyate  || |.. |.. |.. |..
      |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |..
      |.. || trayoviṃśo ' dhyāyaḥ || |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |..
      |.. |.. |.. |..  
 
 
 6.23.1  nidrāṃ caivātinidrāṃ ca mūrchāṃ caiva nibodha me |
       
       tamasā hi samākrānte sattve divasasaṃkṣayāt ||  
 6.23.2  indriyāṇyasya karmabhyaḥ kramātpraviramantyatha  |
       
       bhukte ' nne pacyamāne ca śleṣmaṇā hṛdgatena tu ||  
 6.23.3  vivṛddhena niruddheṣu cakṣuḥśrotravaheṣu ca |
       
       karmakriyāsūryapādaiścheditā prāṇino divā ||  
 6.23.4  śārīramānasaiś caiva tais tair uktair upāhṛtā  |
       
       evaṃkriyānnasaṃjñāni tandrā viśati tāmasī ||  
 6.23.5  evaṃ sarveṣu bhūteṣu nidrā nāmopajāyate |
       
       cintāśokaśramaharī brahmaṇā vihitā purā ||  
 6.23.6 svapatas tasya dehe ' smin
      prāṇāpānau sahoṣmakau |
       
 jāgṛtaḥ jīvasaṃyuktastenāsau na vinaśyati ||  
 6.23.7  indriyāṇām uparame manassūparataṃ yadā |
       
       sevate gocaraṃ teṣāṃ viddhi taṃ svapnanāmakam ||  
 6.23.8  pitṛdevamanuṣyeṣu saṃbhāṣaṇam upaiti ca |
       
       paraṃ ca labhate svapnabhedassa  hi na vātmanaḥ ||  
 6.23.9  atinidrā tu jantūnāṃ śleṣmaṇyucchrāyamāgate |
       
       vātottarāṇāṃ niyataṃ nidrā nāśaṃ vrajaty api ||  
 6.23.10  vastayaḥ snehapānāni grāmyānūpaudakā rasāḥ |
       
       guḍadugdhasya pānaṃ ca nidrāsaṃjananaṃ param ||  
 6.23.11 abhyaṅgodvartanaṃ snānaṃ madyaṃ ghṛtaṃ tathā |
       
       manaḥprasādo  nirvāṇaṃ naṣṭanidrasya bheṣajam ||  
 6.23.12  dhūmapānaṃ virekaś ca kāyasya śirasas tathā |
       
       pracchardanaṃ laṅghanaṃ ca nidrāsaṅgaṃ  nivartayet ||  
 6.23.13 ayānayānaṃ vyāyāmo gūḍhārthaparicintanam |
       
       yavānnanity asevātha nidrāsaṅgaṃ  nivartayet ||  
 6.23.14  indriyāṇāṃ prasannatvaṃ manastālvantarāśritam |
       
       hṛdi santiṣṭhate cittaṃ buddhisarvendriyāśrayam ||  
 6.23.15  sannipatya ca raktaṃ ca trayo doṣāś ca dūṣitāḥ |
       
       sampīḍayantīha nṛṇāṃ hṛdayaṃ śoṣayanty api ||  
 6.23.16  āśuṣyamāṇaṃ hṛdayaṃ pramādāddhi vimuhyati |
       
       saṃpīḍitaṃ ca hṛdayaṃ manaścittaṃ ca mohayet |
       
       sadanāccittamanasoḥ samprāpnoti visaṃjñatām |
