 6.24.1 hanugrahaṃ pādaharṣaṃ pārśvaśūlaṃ jvaraṃ kṣayam |
       
       vardhmakuṇḍalikṛcchrāṇi hṛdgrahaṃ gātrajaṃ klamam ||  
 6.24.2  aśītiṃ  vātikān rogān tailametadvyapohati |
       
       sannipātasamutthāṃś ca saṃsṛṣṭāṃś caikajāṃstathā  ||  
 6.24.3  yonivyāpattivandhyātvaṃ pravṛddhaṃ yadasṛgdaram |
       
       balavarṇakaraṃ caiva kāsakṣayanirbahaṇam ||  
 6.24.4  balāmūlātpalaśataṃ daśamūlācchataṃ tathā |
       
       śatāvaryā guḍūcyāś ca rāsnāmadhukadāruṇaḥ ||  
 6.24.5  kuryād daśapalānbhāgān kulutthān badarān yavān |
       
       māṣāṃś ca kuḍavāṃśena  jaladroṇeṣu pañcasu ||  
 6.24.6  kvāthaṃ droṇāvaśiṣṭantu tailāḍhakasamāyutam |
       
       ghṛtaprasthena vipacet kṣīradroṇena cāpy atha ||  
 6.24.7 peṣyān pradadyādvaidyo vai tagarośīravālakam |
       
       kuṣṭhadhānyakamustailā vacāñcāgurucandanam ||  
 6.24.8  paripelavakālīyaṃ  māṃsīṃ śrīveṣṭakaṃ rasam |
       
       kunduruṣkaṃ ca takkolaṃ  saralaṃ  nalikāṃ nakham ||  
 6.24.9  spṛkkākuṃkumakarpūraṃ jātitindukayoḥ phalam |
       
       patraṃ corakanāgāhvaṃ  śatāhvāṃ sahareṇukām  ||  
 6.24.10 saturuṣkaṃ jīvanīyaṃ 
      priyaṃguṃ hapuṣāṃ tathā |
       
       sthauṇeyakamuśīrāṇi śaileyaṃ ca samaṃ ghṛtam ||  
 6.24.11  kalkapiṣṭaiḥ pacettailametadvātāmayāpaham |
       
       pāne cābhyañjane nasye vastau cāpi prayojayet ||  
 6.24.12  sarvadehāśrayā vātāḥ saṃsṛṣṭāś caikajāś ca ye |
       
       teṣāṃ nigrahaṇe yuktam ity uvāca punarvasuḥ ||  
 6.24.13  tailenānena satataṃ vidhivattarpitaṃ naram |
       
       sarvāmayā varjayanti sihmāvāsaṃ yathā mṛgāḥ ||  
 6.24.14  balāyā jātasārāyāstulāṃ kuryāt sukuṭṭitām |
       
       pacettoye caturdroṇe caturbhāgāvaśeṣitam ||  
 6.24.15  palāni daśa piṣṭāni balāyās tatra dāpayet |
       
       luñcitānāṃ tilānāntu dadyāt tailāḍhakadvayam ||  
 6.24.16  caturguṇena payasā pacettanmṛdunāgninā |
       
       vātavyādhiṣu sarveṣu raktapitte  kṣatakṣaye ||  
 6.24.17  vyāpannāsu ca yonīṣu śastaṃ naṣṭe ca retasi |
       
       tāluśoṣaṃ tṛṣāṃ dāhaṃ pārśvaśūlamasṛgdaram ||  
 6.24.18  hanti śoṣamapasmāraṃ visarpaṃ saśirograham |
       
       āyurvarṇakaraṃ proktaṃ balātailaṃ prajākaram ||  
 6.24.19  rāsnāmūlasya kurvīta dve śate ca balāśatam |
       
       śatāvarīguḍcībhyāṃ varaṇāc ca śataṃ śatam ||  
 6.24.20  āḍhakīśigrukairaṇḍaśirīṣāragvadhād api |
       
 śvadaṃṣṭrābhūtikābhyāṃ ca pṛthak pañcapalaṃ kṣipet ||  
 6.24.21  toyadroṇeṣu daśasu sādhayetsūkṣmakuṭṭitam |
       
 droṇāvaśeṣe tasmiṃs tu tailasyārdharmaṇaṃ pacet ||  
 6.24.22  droṇān daśa ca dugdhasya ghṛtasyārdhaḍhakaṃ tathā |
       
       tadaikadhyaṃ vipaktavyaṃ garbhe cātra vipācayet ||  
 6.24.23  madhukaṃ mālatīpuṣpaṃ mañjiṣṭhāṃ madayantikām |
       
 kāśmaryāmajamodāṃ ca śṛṅgīṃ kapilamustakam ||  
 6.24.24  ātmaguptāḍhakīmūrvāvārtākāni madhūlikām |
       
       sahadevāmathairaṇḍāṃ  rohiṣaṃ navamālikām ||  
 6.24.25  phaṇijjakaṃ madhūkāni vīrānīrakadambakam |
       
       phalaṃ ca pīlupālāśaṃ kumāryaśvatthataindukam ||  
 6.24.26  hrīberaṃ pippalīkuṣṭhaṃ drākṣāṃ kaṭukarohiṇīm |
       
       kāyasthāṃ ca vayasthāṃ ca madhuparṇīṃ sacitrakām ||  
 6.24.27  mahāpuruṣadantāṃ ca modakīṃ sallakīm api |
       
       devadārvaguru śreṣṭhaṃ candanaṃ paripelavam ||  
 6.24.28  nīlotpalamuśīrāṇi mṛdvīkāṃ sāmlavetasām |
       
       etaiḥ palasamaiḥ piṣṭaissamaṃ tailaṃ vipācayet ||  
 6.24.29  bhojane ' bhyañjane pāne vastau nasye ca śasyate |
       
       vātavyādhiṣu sarveṣu kṣatakṣīṇe śirograhe ||  
 6.24.30  svarakṣaye raktapitte hikkāśvāseṣv asṛgdare |
       
       mārute pittasaṃsṛṣṭe saṃsṛṣṭe śoṇitena ca ||  
 6.24.31 viṣamajvarahṛdroge gātrakampe tathaiva ca |
       
       apasmāre raktagulme puṃsāṃ naṣṭe ca retasi ||  
 6.24.32  rāsnātailam idaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ balamāṃsavivardhanam |
       
       samūlapatraśākhasya śataṃ sahacarasya ca ||  
 6.24.33  caturṣu  toyadroṇeṣu sādhayetsūkṣmakuṭṭitam |
       
       droṇāvaśeṣapūte ca pacettailāḍhakaṃ śanaiḥ ||  
 6.24.34 ambujānūpamāṃsaiś ca śirastasyopanāhayet |
       
 nasyakarma ca kurvīta picuṃ mūrdhni ca dāpayet ||  
 6.24.35  mukhaṃ vighaṭayet tasya sandaṃśena yathāsukham |
       
       bhṛṅgāreṇa prayacchec ca snehamāṃsarasaṃ tathā ||  
 6.24.36  avyādadānasya tathā dantānuddhāṭya  saṃhatān |
       
       āmāśayagate vāte snehairnopacared bhiṣak ||  
 6.24.37  laṅghanaṃ tasya kurvīta tathā saṃśodhanāni ca |
       
       āmapralepasambhūtaḥ śleṣmasthānagato ' nilaḥ ||  
 6.24.38  snehairmāṃsarasaiś caiva snehyamāno vivardhate |
       
       tasmāt tasya virūkṣāṇi bhojanāni kaṭūni ca ||  
 6.24.39  āhāre cauṣadhārthe ca vidadhyācśāstrakovidaḥ |
       
       āmāśayasthe vamanaṃ kṣārāḥ kṣāraguḍās tathā ||  
 6.24.40  ariṣṭāśśīdhavaś caiva hitaṃ māṃsaṃ ca jāṅgalam |
       
       śyāmākāḥ koradūṣāś ca mudgā lohitaśālayaḥ ||  
 6.24.41  svedo yavānnaṃ ca hitamāmāśayagate ' nile |
       
       yadā pakvāśayagato rūpāṇi kurute ' nilaḥ ||  
 6.24.42  sirāsu sarvagātreṣu majjasvasthigato ' pi vā |
       
 nirūpya rūpamuktasya tasya kuryāc cikitsitam ||  
 6.24.43  kṛtsnaṃ yadupadiṣṭaṃ tu vātavyādhicikitsitam |
       
       raktasthānagate vāyau pūrvamuktaṃ cikitsitam ||  
 6.24.44  vātaśoṇitake tat tu kuryād raktagate ' nile |
       
       samutthitāyāṃ gṛdhrasyāṃ balātailaṃ praśasyate ||  
 6.24.45  śreṣṭhaṃ mūlakatailaṃ vā tailaṃ sahacarasya vā |
       
       vastayaḥ snehapānāni snehaśconmardanani ca ||  
 6.24.46  gṛdhrasyāṃ tu praśasyante śoṇitasya ca mokṣaṇam |
       
       aśītirvātajā rogāḥ ye ye pūrvaṃ prakīrtitāḥ ||  
 6.24.47  teṣāmeṣā cikitsā tu vāyoḥ sthāneṣu saptasu |
       
       sādhyā ye cāpy asādhyās tu rogā mārutasambhavāḥ ||  
 6.24.48  utpatantyatha tiṣṭhanti vāyoḥ sthāneṣu saptasu |
       
       asthimajjāgato  bhaṅgaṃ kampanaṃ gātraśoṣaṇam ||  
 6.24.49  pakṣagrahamapasmāramunmādam api cārditam |
       
       hanugrahaṃ kuṇiṃ kubjaṃ pāṅgulyaṃ sandhivicyutim ||  
 6.24.50 karoti māruto ' nye ca vātarogā bhavanty api |
       
 sādhyān sthānavaśādeva tāṃścikitsedyathākramam ||  
 6.24.51  itīyaṃ vistareṇoktā cikitsā vātarogiṇām |
       
       vāto hi jīvite hetuḥ prāṇināṃ ca tathātyaye ||  
 6.24.52  santatyā gamayennityaṃ sūryaṃ candramasaṃ tathā |
       
       varṣaṇaṃ vāyunā loke tathaiva ca nivāraṇam ||  
 6.24.53  vahate ca vimānāni sarvaśaḥ svargavāsinām |
       
       sāgare kurute velāṃ vāyurmeghān sṛjaty api ||  
 6.24.54  vigatirvāyunā megho vidyudbhavati vāyunā |
       
       trailokyadhārī pavanassarvaṃ vātātpravartate ||  
 6.24.55 nirvartayetpuṣpaphalaṃ vāyurdhārayate jalam |
       
       ulkāpātān mahīkampān dharaṇīdhāraṇāni ca ||  
 6.24.56  ākāśe  dhārayed gaṅgāṃ vāyus tv atibalānvitaḥ |
       
 etāś cānyāś ca bahavo vāyor guṇavibhāvanāḥ  ||  
 6.24.57  tasmāt prayatnatas tasya cikitsāṃ bhiṣajāṃ varaḥ |
       
       kuryāc chāstrānusāreṇa tathā siddhim avāpnuyāt || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele caturviṃśo ' dhyāyaḥ || || pañcaviṃśo ' dhyāyaḥ || athātaḥ
       plīhahalīmakacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 6.25.1  abhiṣyandīni bhojyāni bhuñjītātīva yo naraḥ |
       
       laṅghito vā virikto vā vyāyāmam upasevate ||  
 6.25.2  bhuktvā pītodako yas tu sahasā saṃpradhāvati |
       
       pṛṣṭhayānād drutāc cāpi plavanātsnehavibhramāt ||  
 6.25.3  rogairanyaiś ca klinnānāṃ kurbalānāṃ ca dehinām |
       
       plīhā sthānātpravardheta  tasya rūpāṇi me śṛṇu ||  
 6.25.4  karotyagnermārdavaṃ ca śūlaṃ kaṭhina eva ca |
       
       mahāparigrahaścaiṣa plīhā vātasamudbhavaḥ ||  
 6.25.5  sajvaraḥ sapipāsaś ca svedanastīvravedanaḥ |
       
       pītakaḥ stabdhagātraś ca plīhā pittātmako bhavet ||  
 6.25.6  nity ānāhitakoṣṭhaś ca nity odāvartapīḍitaḥ |
       
       vedanābhiparītaś ca plīhā śleṣmātmako  mataḥ ||  
 6.25.7  trayāṇāṃ yatra rūpāṇi doṣāṇāṃ lakṣayed bhiṣak |
       
       asādhyam iti taṃ vidyāt plīhānaṃ sānnipātikam ||  
 6.25.8  muṣṭimātrassusādhyas tu paramastamupācaret |
       
       atipramāṇavṛddhas tu na sidhyati kathañcana ||  
 6.25.9  sarveṣu teṣu daurbalyamānāho gātrasādanam |
       
       aruciś cāvipākaś ca varcomūtragraho jvaraḥ || 
 
 6.25.10  mārdvīkaṃ ca pibedyuktyā gaṇḍīrāriṣṭam eva vā |
       
       candraprabhaṃ śārkaraṃ vā pāyayet tu halīmake ||  
 6.25.11  ayor ajīyaṃ kṣīreṇa pāyayet tu rasāyanam |
       
       agastyābhayalehaṃ vā seveta prayataḥ śuciḥ || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ || iti
      bhele pañcaviṃśo ' dhyāyaḥ || || ṣaḍviṃśo ' dhyāyaḥ || athāto '
      patantrakacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 6.26.1  rūkṣānnapānasevābhir vegasandhāraṇena ca |
       
       karśitasyātimātrantu  ceṣṭitasya tathaiva ca ||  
 6.26.2  viriktayuktanasyasya vastinā karśitasya ca |
       
       apatantritabhaktasya bhaktasyāpyatisevinaḥ ||  
 6.26.3  śuddhaḥ pakvāśayagato vāyurvṛddhaḥ prapadyate |
       
       sa pīḍayitvā hṛdayaṃ dhamanīrdaśa saṃsthitaḥ ||  
 6.26.4  ūrdhvamāpūrya srotāṃsi śiraśśaṅkhau ca dhāvati |
       
 ākṣepāttasya gātrāṇi nāmyante  ca dhanuryathā ||  
 6.26.5  nimīlitākṣaḥ stabdho vā nirucchavāso viceṣṭate |
       
 kṛcchrācchavasiti sarpīva kūjaty api kapotavat ||  
 6.26.6  mukte ca hṛdi vātena punaḥ svāsthyaṃ niyacchati |
       
       bhūyas tu śete srastākṣo muhyatyaprayato yathā ||  
 6.26.7  ghorassa vātiko rogo dhamanīhṛdayāśritaḥ |
       
       sannirodhāc ca nāḍīnāṃ yantritānāṃ ca vegataḥ ||  
 6.26.8  srotasāṃ vyākulībhāvānnityaṃ syādapatantrakaḥ |
       
       na cainaṃ vāmayed dhīro na cāpy enaṃ virecayet ||  
 6.26.9  na cāsyāsthāpanaṃ dadyānna cainamapatarpayet |
       
       pippalyo ' tha viḍaṅgāni śigrūṇi maricani ca ||  
 6.26.10  etāni sūkṣmapiṣṭāni kuryāc chīrṣavirecanam |
       
       śvasato yasya saṃvṛddhiḥ śleṣmaṇo mārutasya ca ||  
 6.26.11  tasya śleṣmaṇyupahate saṃjñā samupajāyate |
       
       sauvarcalaṃ dāḍimaṃ ca tathā hiṃgvamlavetasam || 6.2 
 6.26.12  mahauṣadhaṃ ca pītāni nāśayantyapatantrakam |
       
       hiṅgu puṣkaramūlaṃ ca tumburūṇi harītakī ||  
 6.26.13 yavakvāthodakenaitaddātavyaṃ lavaṇaistribhiḥ |
       
       hṛdrogaṃ pārśvaśūlaṃ ca pravṛddhaṃ cāpatantrakam ||  
 6.26.14  yogo ' yaṃ śamayatyāśu śūlaṃ gulmaṃ ca vātikam |
       
       vibhītakaṃ cātiviṣāṃ  bhadramustāṃ sapippalīm ||  
 6.26.15  bhārṅgīṃ saśṛṅgaberāṃ ca sūkṣmacūrṇāni kārayet |
       
       tāni cūrṇāni madyena pītānyuṣṇodakena vā ||  
 6.26.16  nāśayanti nṛṇāṃ kṣipraṃ śvāsakāsapatānakam |
       
       harītakī vacā rāsnā saindhavaṃ sāmlavetasam ||  
 6.26.17  ghṛtamātrāsamāyuktaṃ nāśayatyapatānakam |
       
       śukanāsā mahāvallī dve bṛhatyau mahauṣadham ||  
 6.26.18  niculaś caiva bhārṅgī ca |.. |.. kālikā |
       
       punarnavā ceti samairakṣamātraiḥ pacedbhiṣak ||  
 6.26.19  toyāḍhake ghṛtaprasthaṃ tatsiddhaṃ cāpi pāyayet |
       
       śvāsakāsā mahāhikkā hṛdrogaś cāpatantrakaḥ  ||  
 6.26.20  nātikrāmed idaṃ sarpiḥ velāmiva mahodadhiḥ |
       
       kākādanī balālambā  dve bṛhatyau mahauṣadham ||  
 6.26.21  kadambapuṣpī kālā ca candravallī tathā vṛṣā |
       
       ādārī ca vidārī ca suvahā keśavaty api ||  
 6.26.22  eteṣāṃ dvipalān bhāgān jaladroṇe vipācayet |
       
       etairevākṣamātraiś ca ghṛtaprasthaṃ vipācayet ||  
 6.26.23  dviguṇena kaṣāyeṇa tatsiddhaṃ yuktiyaḥ pibet |
       
 asādhyāṃ mahatīṃ hikkāṃ śvāsaṃ caivāpakarṣati ||  
 6.26.24  harītakyāś ca pañcād dve ca sauvarcalātpale  |
       
       vipācayed ghṛtaprasthaṃ dviguṇakṣīrasaṃyutam ||  
 6.26.25  apatānaṃ sahṛdrogametasarpirvyapohati |
       
       hikkāśvāsau  ca saṃvṛddhau sadya eva cikitsati ||  
 6.26.26  atapānakanāśārthametaduktaṃ cikitsitam |
       
       athārditānāṃ vakṣyāmi cikitsāṃ lakṣaṇāni ca ||  
 6.26.27  śastrakāṣṭhaprahārācca  grāmyadharmātisevanāt |
       
       chardanānmadyapānāc ca dhanuṣaś ca vikarṣaṇāt ||  
 6.26.28  nityaṃ vyāyāmaśīlānāṃ patanāllaṅghanād api |
       
 avatantritabhaktasya vyādhinā karśitasya ca ||  
 6.26.29  narasya kupito vāyurūrdhvam eva prapadyate |
       
       hanumūlaṃ śiraś cāpi grīvāṃ caivārdayaty api ||  
 6.26.30  sa jihmaṃ kutute tasya vadanaṃ cakṣureva ca |
       
       kampate ' sya śirogrīvaṃ nāsā vakrībhavaty api ||  
 6.26.31 tasyākṣiṇī nimīlyete niṣpande viṣame tathā |
       
       ūrdhvaṃ viprekṣate ' tyarthaṃ tiryagākekarekṣaṇaḥ ||  
 6.26.32  oṣṭhau śvayathumantau  ca cibukaṃ ca vināmyate |
       
       ṣṭhīvatyathātimātraṃ  hi kalā sajjati cāsya vāk  || |.. |.. |..
      |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. || saptaviṃśo ' dhyāyaḥ || |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |..
      |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. ||| nāṃ vraṇanāśanāḥ |
       
 
 
 
 6.27.1  vraṇasya kāle sampaśyan tataḥ kuryād upakramam |
       
       bhedanaṃ pācanaṃ caiva stambhanaṃ śoṣaṇaṃ tathā ||  
 6.27.2  srāvaṇaṃ ropaṇaṃ caiva vraṇe kuryād upakramam |
       
       uditā karṇamoṭaśca  rāsnā mūlakaparṇikā ||  
 6.27.3  śukanāsā sugandhā ca samaṅgā  caiva kuṣṭhakam |
       
       kāleyakaṃ balā dantī pāṭhā  śatapadī  sthirā ||  
 6.27.4 pīḍanīyaḥ  praleyo ' yaṃ vraṇaśvayathunāśanaḥ
      |
       
       udumbaraḥ  śirīṣaś ca madhukaṃ candanaṃ tilāḥ ||  
 6.27.5 indukāntaṃ samudrāntā tathaiva ca śatāvarī |
       
       nīlotpalaṃ padmakaṃ ca tvacā dve cāpi sāribe ||  
 6.27.6  eṣa pralepo gāraṃ ca vraṇānāṃ tu vināśayet |
       
       tilakalkassamadhukaḥ  picumandasya  kalkavān ||  
 6.27.7 pūrvābhyāṃ sarpiṣā yukto vraṇeṣu vraṇaropaṇaḥ |
       
       triphalā dhātakī lodhraṃ samaṅgā madhukaṃ balā ||  
 6.27.8  dve bṛhatyau samudrāntā tathaiva ca śatāvarī |
       
       nīlotpalaṃ kaṭphalaṃ ca mālatī svarṇayūthikā ||  
 6.27.9  eṣāṃ kalkaissamaissiddhaṃ tailaṃ syād vraṇaropaṇam |
       
 nimbvāmrāmalakīnāṃ ca pallavaṃ madhukaṃ balā ||  
 6.27.10  etaiśśakṛdrasesiddhaṃ  tailaṃ vraṇanibarhaṇam |
       
       nyagrodhodumbarāśvatthaplakṣapāṭhāvarārjunāḥ  ||  
 6.27.11  śamībadaryā eteṣāṃ kaṣāyā vraṇadhāvanāḥ |
       
       yavānnaṃ śālikā raktā mudgā nīvāraṣaṣṭikāḥ ||  
 6.27.12  jāṅgalāni ca māṃsāni vraṇitaśśīlayetsadā  |
       
       amlaṃ dadhi ca śākaṃ ca māṃsaṃ cānūpavārijam ||  
 6.27.13  kṣīraṃ gurūṇi cānnāni vraṇitaḥ parivarjayet |
       
       etanupakramān kuryād vraṇe kāyacikitsakaḥ ||  
 6.27.14  śalyakṛc cāpi kurvīta vraṇe śeṣānupakramān |
       
       chedyaṃ bhedyaṃ ca lekhyaṃ ca sīvyaṃ pracchanam eva ca ||  
 6.27.15  pācanaṃ yac ca tastulyaṃ bhaved anyac ca kiṃcana |
       
       dvādaśa vraṇadoṣāśca  parīkṣā caiva ṣaḍvidhā ||  
 6.27.16 upakramāś ca ṣaṭtriṃśanniyatāḥ śalyahetuke |
       
       uddeśataḥ kriyāś caitāḥ kuryāt kāyacikitsakaḥ ||  
 6.27.17  triphalā madhukaṃ lodhraṃ mañjiṣṭhā bilvaśuṇṭhikā |
       
       samaṅgā dhātakī lākṣā viryāsaḥ śālmalerapi ||  
 6.27.18  pālāśasya ca niryāso niryāsaḥ kakubhasya ca |
       
       sūkṣmāny etāni cūrṇāni vraṇānāṃ ropaṇaṃ param ||  
 6.27.19  gugguloḥ sallakīnāṃ ca sarjasya tiniśasya ca |
       
       niryāsā ropaṇāḥ poktāḥ samastāḥ pṛthageva vā ||  
 6.27.20  vraṇe dhūmakramā ye ca pratyutpattau ca yā kriyā |
       
       etaccheṣaṃ śalyakṛtā kartavyaṃ dṛṣṭakarmaṇā || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele saptaviṃśo ' dhyāyaḥ || || aṣṭāviṃśo ' dhyāyaḥ
      || athātaḥ pānātyayacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān
      ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 6.28.1 sarve lavaṇavarjyās tu rasā madye pratiṣṭhitāḥ |
       
       tīkṣṇaṃ coṣṇaṃ tathā sūkṣmamāśukāri  vyavāyi ca ||  
 6.28.2 dīpanīyaṃ ca hṛdyaṃ ca sarvabhūtahitaṃ laghu |
       
       cintāśorkaklamaharaṃ ratiprītivivardhanam ||  
 6.28.3  harṣasthāne harṣakaraṃ bhayasthāne bhayāpaham |
       
       rativihārajananaṃ dyutiśauryakaraṃ param ||  
 6.28.4  śarīrāvayavān sarvānanugacchatyaṇūnapi |
       
 taikṣṇyān mohayate cittam auṣṇyāt pittakaraṃ ca tat ||  
 6.28.5  hṛdyaṃ vaiśadyabhāvāc ca raukṣyānmārutakopanam |
       
       śleṣmaghnaṃ tīkṣṇabhāvac ca harṣaṇād vṛṣyamucyate ||  
 6.28.6  madyāvacāraṇāttasya kupitau pittamārutau |
       
       śoṣayetāṃ rasavahāḥ sirāḥ kloma ca tālu ca ||  
 6.28.7 tṛṣāparītasso ' tyarthaṃ pānamevābhinandati |
       
       pītaṃ pītaṃ śoṣayato dehe tasyāgnimārutau ||  
 6.28.8  gacchatyāśu jarāṃ dehe sikatāyāmivodakam |
       
       tasmād ahorātram api pibataḥ pānasevinaḥ ||  
 6.28.9  tṛṣṇā nopaśamaṃ yāti pānaṃ jīryati cāśu ca |
       
       bhrāmitasya tu madyena pittaṃ vāyuś ca dehinaḥ ||  
 6.28.10  vihīne cittamanasi buddhiṃ pīḍayatastataḥ |
       
 sa roditi praharati visṛjatyati dhāvati ||  
 6.28.11  patatyutpatate hanti bahvabaddhaṃ ca bhāṣate |
       
       gacchatyagamyāmanyāṃ  ca kāryākārye na budhyate ||  
 6.28.12 tathā śvabhre ca patati śete ca mṛtaśāyikām
      |
       
       nagno viśedvicaitanyaṃ vicareddhi vicetanaḥ ||  
 6.28.13 īdṛśo ' pi bhavenmattaḥ pānenonmathitendriyaḥ |
       
       pramāṇena pibenmadyaṃ nātiseveta paṇḍitaḥ ||  
 6.28.14  yuktyā tu sevyamānaṃ tatpānaṃ cāmṛtamucyate |
       
       pānaṃ tadbhojane ' tyarthaṃ rucimantaṃ  karoti ca ||  
 6.28.15  harṣaṃ janayate strīṣu tajjarogaṃ cikitsakaḥ |
       
       pānenaiva praśamayennānyattasya cikitsitam ||  
 6.28.16  tasmānmadyaṃ niṣeveta śubhrāṇi vacanāni ca |
       
       bhajellaghūni cānnāni jāṅgalānna mṛgadvijān ||  
 6.28.17  snānaṃ sugandhaiḥ snānīyaiḥ kṛtvā tvaganulepanam |
       
       śabdān manojñān śṛṇvaṃś ca manojñaissaha bandhubhiḥ ||  
 6.28.18  gṛhe ' tyantasukhe hyetat kuryāt prasthottarottaram |
       
       kāntāssumadhyavayasaḥ tanumadhyāśśucismitāḥ ||  
 6.28.19 candrapādānmanohṛṣṭāścitramālyāmbarasrajaḥ |
       
       caturāḥ  kṣaumavasanā muktāmaṇivibhūṣitāḥ  ||  
 6.28.20  raktacandanadigdhāṅgā manojñā maṇimekhalāḥ |
       
       tāḥ samāliṅgya śayane śayītāpratimāḥ striyaḥ ||  
 6.28.21  yoṣito vai pradhānā vai śītasparśāḥ 
      svabhāvataḥ  |
       
       nṛṇāṃ svabhāvataś caiva nāryo harṣavivardhanāḥ ||  
 6.28.22  somo hi śiśiro dhāturhṛdi harṣāt
      pravardhate  |
       
 tasmād ālāpasaṃlāpaissaṃvāhanavinodanaiḥ ||  
 6.28.23  nārīṃ praharṣajananīṃ sevetāśu madātyaye |
       
 gītatūryasvanās tatra suhṛdaś ca madotkaṭāḥ ||  
 6.28.24  priyānuvarti gāyanto harṣaṃ kuryurmadātyaye |
       
       nirdoṣāṇi ca madyāni yuktāni śiśirairjalaiḥ ||  
 6.28.25  tāni tāni śubhairmāsaiḥ sopadaṃśāni pāyayet |
       
       pānakāni ca mukhyāni ṣāḍavāṃstarpaṇāni ca ||  
 6.28.26 tavakṣīrīṃ  sacukrīṃ  ca sevetāsau
       madātyaye |
       
       takraṃ drākṣārasassīdhustaittirīko raso madhu ||  
 6.28.27  āranālaṃ ca śukraṃ ca koladāḍimayo rasau |
       
 lājāḥ santarpaṇāś caiva sūkṣmāś ca yavatarpaṇāḥ ||  
 6.28.28  sauvarcalamajājyaś ca saindhavaṃ lavaṇaṃ tathā |
       
       śiśireṇa jalenaitattarpaṇaṃ pānavatpibet ||  
 6.28.29  mātuluṅgopadaṃśaṃ ca hanyāt pānātyayaṃ nṛṇām |
       
       lākṣārasastaittirīko dāḍimasya raso madhu ||  
 6.28.30  pūrvakalpena pātavyaṃ sampanne pānavibhrame |
       
       karkandhubadarāṇāṃ ca prasthaṃ kuryāt sukuṭṭitam ||  
 6.28.31 dviprasthe gālayaṃstoye saptakṛtvaḥ punaḥ punaḥ |
       
       mṛṇmaye tatra vai bhāṇḍe svanuguptaṃ nidhāpayet ||  
 6.28.32  dve ca dadyād guḍapale śarkarāyāḥ palaṃ tathā |
       
       sūkṣmaṃ ca maricātkarṣaṃ caturthaṃ kesarasya ca ||  
 6.28.33  tvakpatradharaṇe dve ca sūkṣmailākarṣam eva ca |
       
       amṛṇālārdhakarṣaṃ ca sūkṣmacūrṇāni kārayet ||  
 6.28.34  jātīvāsanayopetaṃ  pānakaṃ pānavibhrame |
       
       nāśayatyāśu pānena chinnābhrāṇīva mārutaḥ ||  
 6.28.35  etacchardiṃ tṛṣāṃ dāhamatisāraṃ pravāhikām |
       
       aruciṃ mūtrakṛcchraṃ ca hanyāt pānātyayaṃ nṛṇām ||  
 6.28.36  kāśmaryaṃ dāḍimaṃ drākṣāṃ madhukaṃ saparūṣakam |
       
       kuṭajāni ca saṃkṣudya prakṣipettajjalāḍhake ||  
 6.28.37  sūkṣmailāmadhukaṃ lodhraṃ mañjiṣṭhā pippalī tathā |
       
       etāni sūkṣmacūrṇāni dadyānmānaṃ  ca yuktitaḥ ||  
 6.28.38  kesaraṃ cātra dātavyaṃ puṣpaṃ nīlotpalasya ca |
       
       etatpānātyaye deyaṃ tṛṣācchardinivāraṇam ||  
 6.28.39  dve guḍūcī pale dve ca balā dvipalam eva ca |
       
       lāmajjakamṛṇālābhyāṃ dve pale madhukotpalam ||  
 6.28.40  etānyāpothya deyāni nave bhāṇḍe jalāḍhake |
       
       guḍasya ca palānyaṣṭau dadyānnīlotpalaṃ tathā ||  
 6.28.41  etatpānātyaye deyaṃ pānakaṃ kesarairyutam |
       
       jvaradāhatṛṣāśvāsacchardihikkāśca  nāśayet ||  
 6.28.42  yadi saṃśamanairetairna śāmyetpānavibhramaḥ |
       
       pāyayet taṃ trivṛccūrṇaṃ yuktyā madyena saṃyutam ||  
 6.28.43  pibedvirecanaṃ cūrṇaṃ mahātarpaṇam eva vā |
       
       pūrvoktānmodakāṃś cāpi bhakṣayitvā pibetsurām ||  
 6.28.44  vamanīyaṃ yadā vidyāt tadainaṃ vāmayed bhiṣak |
       
       vamanairmadyasaṃyuktaiścūrṇaiḥ pācanakair api ||  
 6.28.45  yavakṣāraiś ca saṃsargīṃ  tasya kuryāc cikitsakaḥ
      |
       
       na hi peyāḥ praśasyante manuṣyāṇāṃ madātyaye ||  
 6.28.46  madātyaye na śasyante yavāgvo doṣanāśanāḥ |
       
       jāṣyāt pānasya pītasya vegaṃ janayate punaḥ ||  
 6.28.47 tanmadyaśeṣaṃ saṃvṛddhaṃ kurvād ghorānupadravān |
       
       tasmāt pānātyaye ' pathyāḥ snehāḥ  peyā yavāgvapi ||  
 6.28.48  sūkṣmāṇi dehasrotāṃsi madyaṃ samanudhāvati |
       
       tiṣṭhatyavayavaiś cānyasrotassu viṣameṣv api ||  
 6.28.49 viṣvagdhṛtāṃs tu koṣṭhasthān kopayatyānilādikān |
       
       dhātavaste kharībhūtā vivṛddhāḥ pānadūṣitāḥ ||  
 6.28.50  pānena saha saṃsṛṣṭā janayanty āmayān bahūn |
       
       vyavāyi  madyamuddiṣṭaṃ viśeṣeṇa manīṣibhiḥ ||  
 6.28.51  ye tu sūkṣmādiviṣayā madyādīnanuyānti vai |
       
       na hi tānviṣayānanyo rasaśśakto vidhāritum  ||  
 6.28.52  tasmāt pānātyayārtānāṃ  madyamevauṣadhaṃ param |
       
       svā hi yoniś ca tatpānaṃ pralīnaṃ koṣṭhamāśritam ||  
 6.28.53  vaśībhūtaṃ prayatnena mahāsrotaḥ prapadyate |
       
       ārtasya madyasaṃyuktāny auṣadhāny api sarvaśaḥ ||  
 6.28.54  madyātyaye prakurvīta kriyāḥ śītāś ca sarvaśaḥ |
       
       ataś ca madyasaṃyuktāstarpaṇāḥ khalu dehinaḥ ||  
 6.28.55  deyāś cātiviriktāya  srotasāṃ śodhanāya ca |
       
       auṣṇyāt taikṣṇyādvikāsitvād vyavāyitvāc ca raukṣyataḥ ||  
 6.28.56  tulyaṃ hi rasavīryābhyāṃ viṣaṃ madyaṃ ca kīrtitam |
       
       tasmāt tattatkriyāssarvā viṣavatsamupācaret ||  
 6.28.57  kledanaṃ tīkṣṇamuṣṇaṃ ca vidāhyañjananāvanam  |
       
       tasmād uṣṇodakaṃ svedaṃ dhūmaṃ pānaṃ ca sarpiṣaḥ ||  
 6.28.58  jvālānalaṃ tu sarveṣāṃ yavāgūśca  vivarjayet |
       
       dadhi dugdhaṃ ca śākaṃ ca grāmyānūpaudakāni ca ||  
 6.28.59 tilapiṣṭakṛtaṃ caiva pānarogī vivarjayet |
       
       śālīn saṣaṣṭikān  mudgān jāṅgalānmṛgapakṣiṇaḥ ||  
 6.28.60  pānātyaye praśaṃsanti bhojaneṣu cikitsakāḥ |
       
       sameṣu dhātukopeṣu vivikteṣu ca me śṛṇu ||  
 6.28.61  atimātraṃ yadā pānaṃ pītaṃ kopayate ' nilam |
       
 saṃdṛśya vātikaṃ rūpaṃ tasya kuryāc cikitsitam ||  
 6.28.62  sauvarcalavyoṣayutaṃ madyaṃ mākṣikasaṃyutam |
       
       cukraṃ dāḍimasaṃyuktaṃ vātapānātyaye hitam ||  
 6.28.63 toyaṃ madyaṃ ca śuktaṃ ca dadhi tvamlaṃ ca
      kāñjikam |
       
       samākṣikastarpaṇo ' yaṃ vātapānātyaye hitaḥ  ||  
 6.28.64  abhyaṅgo mardanaṃ snānaṃ pānānyardhodakāni ca |
       
       vyaktāmlavyoṣasaṃyuktān rasān vrīhīṃś ca śīlayet ||  
 6.28.65  chāgalaṃ taittiraṃ  krauñcaṃ
      kaukkuṭaṃ bārhiṇaṃ tathā |
       
       vātapānātyayārtānāṃ bhojanārthaṃ hitaṃ nṛṇām ||  
 6.28.66  āmramāmrātakaṃ bhavyaṃ kapitthaṃ karamardakam |
       
       pūrvakalpena pātavyaṃ pānakaṃ vātarogiṇām ||  
 6.28.67 cavyaṃ sauvarcalaṃ hiṅgu mātuluṅgamahauṣadham |
       
       tathājamodacūrṇaṃ ca madyena saha pāyayet ||  
 6.28.68  pānātyaye pittakṛte pānakaṃ śarkarāyutam |
       
       pibenmākṣikasaṃyuktamardhatoyapariplutam ||  
 6.28.69  kecitpānaṃ tu garhanti pittapānātyaye nṛṇām |
       
       tanmadyānna  hi cecchakyaṃ vinā cānyaiścikitsitum ||  
 6.28.70  saṃyuktaṃ taddhi pittaghnairmadyamevāpi  sevyate |
       
       vidāryāmalakānāṃ ca rasairikṣurasena vā ||  
 6.28.71  madhūkamadhukāśmaryakharjūraṃ nīlamutpalam |
       
       pānakaṃ madyasaṃyuktaṃ pūrvakalpena sādhayet ||  
 6.28.72  ārdrakṣaumaparicchannā muktāmaṇivibhūṣitāḥ |
       
       śyāmāścandanadigdhāṅgāḥ  svapyādāśliṣya yoṣitaḥ ||  
 6.28.73  madyaṃ kharjūrakalkena pibed ikṣurasena vā |
       
       pakvaṃ pīlurasaṃ vāpi vārtākīrasam eva vā ||  
 6.28.74  raso drākṣāvidārībhyāṃ madyamikṣuraso madhu |
       
 pittapānātyayārtānāmetatpānaṃ  hitaṃ nṛṇām ||  
 6.28.75  dṛtiṃ himāmbusampūrṇāṃ gandhamālyasamucchritām  |
       
       svapyāt pariṣvajya gṛhe pittapānātyayārditaḥ ||  
 6.28.76  sarāṃsi vanarājiś ca nalinī phullapaṅkajā  |
       
       bhavetpaṅkajapatraiś ca śayanaṃ candanokṣitam ||  
 6.28.77  upagūhya mṛṇālāni kalhārakusumāni ca |
       
 śayīta jalasaṃsṛṣṭavyajanair upavījitaḥ ||  
 6.28.78  pānātyaye pittakṛte śastrāśaniviṣopame |
       
 jāṅgalairghṛtasaṃyuktairbhojayed raktaśālikān ||  
 6.28.79  mudgayūṣeṇa vā śītaṃ bhojanmṛdulaudanam  |
       
       triphalāyāḥ kaṣāyaṃ vā pibenmadyena saṃyutam ||  
 6.28.80  kṣaudreṇa rasamikṣorvā trivṛtkalkena vā punaḥ |
       
       triphalātvaṅmadhūkāni padmakaṃ padmakesaram ||  
 6.28.81  nīlotpalaṃ mṛṇālāni naladaṃ candanaṃ balām |
       
       siddhaṃ kaṣāyaṃ śītaṃ taiḥ śarkarāmadhusaṃyutam ||  
 6.28.82  kiṃcinmadyena saṃyuktaṃ pittapānātyaye hitam |
       
       drākṣā pīlūni pakvāni kharjūrāṇi parūṣakam ||  
 6.28.83  bhavyaṃ panasamajjā ca majjā tālaphalasya ca |
       
       āpothya tāni sarvāṇi palāṃśāni jalāḍhake ||  
 6.28.84  caturbhāgāvaśeṣaṃ  tu nave kumbhe samāvapet |
       
       datvā sitāpalānyaṣṭau palaṃ nīlotpalasya tu ||  
 6.28.85  tatpibetpānakaṃ  yuktyā pittapānātyayārditaḥ |
       
 ślaiṣmike pānaroge ca madyena vamanaṃ hitam ||  
 6.28.86  paṭolaṃ picumandaṃ ca madanasya ca pallavam |
       
       guḍūcī cāṭarūṣaś ca triphalā pāribhadrakaḥ ||  
 6.28.87  kaṣāyaṃ pāyayed etaṃ śītaṃ mākṣikasaṃyutam |
       
       nityaṃ seveta tiktāni kaṣāyakaṭukāni ca ||  
 6.28.88  jāṅgalāni ca māṃāni seveta mṛgapakṣiṇām |
       
       pibetkuṭannaṭācūrṇaṃ triphalārasasaṃyutam ||  
 6.28.89  dīpanīyāṃś ca seveta yogān pānena nity aśaḥ |
       
       vikāre śleṣmaṇi  hitaṃ madyaṃ bhūyiṣṭham eva hi ||  
 6.28.90  tasmāt pānātyaye madyaṃ ślaiṣmike paricakṣmahe |
       
       eṣā vimānataḥ proktā śleṣmapānātyaye kriyā ||  
 6.28.91  sarvataḥ sannipāte tu sadā kuryāc cikitsitam |
       
       ahāni sapta cāṣṭau vā nṛṇāṃ pānātyaye smṛtam ||  
 6.28.92  pānaṃ hi bhajate jīrṇamata ūrdhvaṃ vimārgataḥ |
       
       anena kālayogena yo rogo na nivartate ||  
 6.28.93  kṛtvānupūrvyā pānasya  kuryāt tasya cikitsitam |
       
       hikkāśvāsādayo rogā ye ca sarve samutthitāḥ ||  
 6.28.94  teṣāṃ cikitsitaṃ kuryād yathā sve sve cikitsite |
       
       iti pānātyayārtānāṃ vistareṇa cikitsitam ||  
 6.28.95  prajāhitam idaṃ proktaṃ śiṣyāṇāmarthasiddhaye || ity āha
      bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
       iti bhele aṣṭāviṃśo ' dhyāyaḥ ||  iti bhelasaṃhitāyāṃ
      cikitsāsthānaṃ samāptam || || kalpasthānam || || prathamo ' dhyāyaḥ ||
      athāto madanakalpaṃ vyākhyāsyāma it ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
       
 
 
 
 
 
 7.1.1  piṇḍītakāni tu trīṇi saṃgrahoktāni me śṛṇu |
        
 kṛṣṇaṃ śvetamubhe tac ca tritayaṃ madanaṃ smṛtam ||  
 7.1.2  phalānāntveva sarveṣāṃ madanaṃ sarvaśodhanam |
        
        vamanāsthāpane yojyaṃ tathaivāpy anuvāsane ||  
 7.1.3  yadā na paripūrṇān paripakvāni tāni ca |
        
        bhavanti rasapūrṇāni tatastānyuddhared bhiṣak ||  
 7.1.4  yavapalle  tathaitāni tuṣapalle  tathā punaḥ
       |
        
        saptarātraṃ vāsayitvā saṃkuñcitaphalatvacā  ||  
 7.1.5  subhāvitāni vijñāya mṛdubhūtāni śāstravit |
        
        dvidhā tridhā śodhayitvā samyak saṃśodhya cāvapet ||  
 7.1.6 dhānyeṣu māsaṃ saṃsthāpya mṛdā caivāvalepayet |
        
        nidhūme ca nivāte ca kapāṭapihite gṛhe ||  
 7.1.7  vaihāyase sthāpayec ca yathā svedo na saṃbhavet |
        
        eteṣāṃ phalamajjānāṃ sanakhaṃ muṣṭimāharet ||  
 7.1.8  jarjarīkṛtya dṛṣadi pātre  cāpy adhivāsayet |
        
        madhukasya kaṣāyeṇa rātrimekāṃ nidhāpayet ||  
 7.1.9  atha cotthāya pūrvāhṇe hastau prakṣālya mardayet |
        
        parisrutaṃ salavaṇaṃ madhuyuktaṃ pratāpya ca ||  
 7.1.10  pāyayed āturaṃ snigdhaṃ chardayet tena sādhu nā |
        
        etenaiva ca kalpena jīmūtakaphalair api ||  
 7.1.11  ikṣvākukuṭajābhyāṃ ca lavaṇaiś cāpi kārayet |
        
 kṛtavedhairhastiparṇaiḥ  dhāmārgavaphalair api ||  
 7.1.12  kaṣāyaṃ kārayed ebhiḥ phalabījāni bhāvayet |
        
        anena kalpena bhiṣak pāyayet tu yathābalam ||  
 7.1.13  madanasya phalānyeva punaruddhārayed bhiṣak |
        
        yathā syurnātipāṇḍūni tathaiva haritāny api ||  
 7.1.14  paripūrṇāni pakvāni tathā jātarasāni ca |
        
        sūcyā vā kaṇṭakair vātha vyadhayitvā samantataḥ ||  
 7.1.15  madanānāṃ kaṣāyeṇa trirātraṃ bhāvayed bhiṣak |
        
        etenaiva ca kalpena jīmūtakaphalair api ||  
 7.1.16  ikṣvākukuṭajānāṃ tu dhāmārgavaphalair api |
        
 kṛtavedhairhāstiparṇaiśchardayet tena sādhu nā ||  
 7.1.17  sa khalvetena kalpena kuśānāṃ varuṇasya ca |
        
        kākodumbarikāyāś ca kuṣṭhākhyāyās tathaiva ca || ekaikasya kaṣāyeṇa
       susnigdhaṃ pāyayed bhiṣak |
        
        balābalamavekṣya  |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |..
       |.. |.. ||  || tṛtīyo ' dhyāyaḥ || |.. |.. |.. ha smāha bhagavān
       ātreyaḥ |
        
 
 
 
 7.3.1  ikṣvākūṇyuddhareddhīmān vasante ' tha śarady api |
        
        yadā prayuṣpitāni syurmadhugandhīni vānti ca ||  
 7.3.2  teṣāṃ kriyāṃ pravakṣyāma  ikṣvākūṇāṃ yathā vidhiḥ
       |
        
        ikṣvākubhiḥ payassiddhaṃ tenaivaṃ vāmayed bhiṣak ||  
 7.3.3  payasā dadhi kṛtvā vā pāyayet tu yathābalam |
        
        nirmathya vāmayeccainaṃ navanītena vā naram ||  
 7.3.4  vihitā cekṣvākuṣveṣā samākhyātā  kriyā mayā |
        
        vṛntānyārdrāṇi cādāya sthāpayetphāṇitodare ||  
 7.3.5  ekarātrasthitānyatra hastau prakṣālya mardayet |
        
        parisrutaṃ salavaṇaṃ madhuyuktaṃ pratāpya ca ||  
 7.3.6  pāyayed āturaṃ snigdhaṃ charayet tena sādhu saḥ |
        
        etenaiva ca kalpena ikṣudarbhekṣuvārikaiḥ ||  
 7.3.7  tathā poṭagalekṣośca  kārayet tu rasāplutam |
        
        athavā kovidārasya patraissammiśritāni tu ||  
 7.3.8  ikṣvākūṇāṃ pallavāni svedayed gomayāgninā |
        
        tāni svinnāni coddhṛtya kṣodayitvā hyulūkhale ||  
 7.3.9  tataḥ phalakaṣāyeṇa svabhyāsicya samasya ca |
        
        ekarātraṃ kaṣāye ' smin svanuguptaṃ nidhāpayet ||  
 7.3.10  pūrvakalpavidhānena vāmayet taṃ yathābalam |
        
        ikṣvākūṇāṃ prasṛtaṃ ca sūkṣmaṃ cūrṇāni kārayet ||  
 7.3.11  kovidārakaṣāyeṇa gulikāḥ  kārayed bhiṣak |
        
        etenaiva kaṣāyeṇa vinīya gulikāntu tām ||  
 7.3.12  yathābalaṃ pāyayet tu chardayet tena sādhu saḥ |
        
 etena khalu kalpena kuśānāṃ tagarasya ca ||  
 7.3.13  etaikasya kaṣāyeṇa susnigdhaṃ vāmayed bhiṣak |
        
        yathābalaṃ yathoddiṣṭaṃ chardayet tena sādhu saḥ ||  
 7.3.14  ikṣvākubhiḥ payassiddhaṃ pāyayet tu yathābalam |
        
        ikṣvākūṇāmayaṃ kalpo vamanārthāya kīrtitaḥ ||  
 7.3.15  mṛdurabhyāsatassiddhaḥ  prayojyo deśakālataḥ ||
       ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
        
        iti bhele kalpasthāne tṛtīyo ' dhyāyaḥ || || caturtho ' dhyāyaḥ || athāto
       dhāmārgavakalpaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
        
 
 
 
 7.4.1  dhāmārgavānyuddhareta  vasante vā śarady api |
        
 yadā prapuṣpitāni syuḥ madhugandhīni bhānti ca ||  
 7.4.2  same bhūmipradeśe ' smin kuśarohiṣasaṃskṛte |
        
        kṛṣṇamṛtsnāprabhe vāpi hyathavā svarṇamṛttike ||  
 7.4.3  vyātape na nadītīre śvabhravalmīkayos tathā |
        
        paripūrṇāni pakvāni  tathā jātarasāni ca ||  
 7.4.4  bhiṣaguddhṛtya matimān yavapalle  nidhāpayet |
        
        vusapalle  ' tha vā dhīraḥ saptarātraṃ nidhāpayet ||  
 7.4.5  subhāvitāni vijñāya mṛdubhūtāni śāstravit |
        
        jarjarīkṛtya dṛṣadi pātreṣvāsicya  nirharet ||  
 7.4.6  kovidārakaṣāyeṇa rātrimekāṃ nidhāpayet |
        
        atha cotthāya pūrvāhṇe hastau prakṣālya mardayet ||  
 7.4.7  parisrutaṃ salavaṇaṃ madhuyuktaṃ pratāpya ca |
        
        pāyayed āturaṃ snigdhaṃ chardayet tena sādhu saḥ ||  
 7.4.8  dhāmārgavāṇāmeteṣāṃ muṣṭiṃ saṃgṛhya sannakham |
        
        jarjarīkṛtya dṛṣadi pātreṣv abhyavahārayet ||  
 7.4.9  kovidārakaṣāyeṇa rātrimekāṃ nidhāpayet |
        
        pūrvoktenaiva kalpena vāmayet tu yathābalam ||  
 7.4.10  naladasya kaṣāyeṇa tālīsaśatapuṣpayoḥ |
        
        kuṣṭhasya mūrvāpāṭhāyāḥ pūrvakalpena chardayet ||  
 7.4.11  dhāmārgavāñjaliṃ pūrṇaṃ sūkṣmacūrṇāni kārayet |
        
        śyāmākaṣāye prakṣipya caikarātraṃ yathāvidhi ||  
 7.4.12  tathā phalakaṣāye ' sminnikṣvākukṛtavedhane  |
        
        jīmūtake hastiparṇe kaṣāye  paribhāvayet ||  
 7.4.13  tata uddhṛtya saṃśoṣya sūkṣmacūrṇāni kārayet |
        
        kṛsarāṃ tena saṃyuktāṃ  nātyuṣṇāṃ pāyayennaram  ||  
 7.4.14  utpalaṃ puṇḍarīkaṃ ca naladaṃ kumudaṃ tathā |
        
        tena cūrṇena saṃspṛśya ghrātumasmai pradāpayet ||  
 7.4.15  sirāhṛdayamāpnoti yāvattatkila miśrakam |
        
        tvaritaṃ tāni puṣpāṇi ghrātumasmai pradāpayet ||  
 7.4.16  ghrātuṃ  punaḥ punarmadhyaṃ  cūrṇayitvā
       muhurmuhuḥ |
        
        anenaiva ca kalpena sukhaṃ vamati mānavaḥ ||  
 7.4.17  dhāmārgavāñjaliṃ pūrṇaṃ sūkṣmacūrṇāni kārayet |
        
        tridhā vibhajya matimān svanuguptaṃ nidhāpayet ||  
 7.4.18  atha bilvakaṣāyeṇa dvau bhāgau ścyotayed bhiṣak |
        
 cyute kaṣāye vimale svanuguptaṃ nidhāpayet ||  
 7.4.19  bhāgaṃ tu gulikāḥ kāryāḥ kolakarkandhusammitāḥ |
        
        kovidārakaṣāyeṇa pūrvakalpena chardayet ||  
 7.4.20  karkandhūbadarāṇāṃ ca kolānāṃ vāpi sīdhunā |
        
        gulikāṃ vinīya vidhivacchardayet tena sādhu saḥ ||  
 7.4.21  rohitasya ca matsyasya tathā karkaṭakasya ca |
        
        pakṣiṇāmaudakānāṃ ca rasena tu vametsukham ||  
 7.4.22 etena khalu kalpena cāmlaiś
       ca madhusīdhubhiḥ |
        
        gulikāṃ vinīya vidhivat pāyayet tāṃ  yathābalam || ity āha
       bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
        
        iti bhele caturtho ' dhyāyaḥ || || pañcamo ' dhyāyaḥ || athātaḥ
       kuṭajakalpaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
        
 
 
 
 7.5.1  vasante vā śaradi vā kuṭajāny uddhared bhiṣak |
        
        śuciśśuddhaśśiraḥsnātaḥ puṣyeṇāśvayujena vā ||  
 7.5.2  pratūṭhāni śucau deśe kuśarohiṣasaṃskṛte |
        
        kṛṣṇamṛtsnāprabhe vāpi tathā vā svarṇamṛttike ||  
 7.5.3  vyātape na nadītīre śvabhravalmīkayos tathā |
        
        paripūrṇāni pakvāni tathā jātarasāni ca ||  
 7.5.4  kuṭajānāmathaiteṣāṃ muṣṭiṃ saṅgṛhya sannakham |
        
        kovidārakaṣāyeṇa rātrimekāṃ nidhāpayet ||  
 7.5.5  atha cotthāya pūrvāhṇe hastau prakṣālya mardayet |
        
        parisrutaṃ salavaṇaṃ madhuyuktaṃ pratāpya ca ||  
 7.5.6  pāyayed āturaṃ snigdhaṃ chardayet tena sādhu saḥ |
        
        anenaiva ca kalpena kaṣāyaṃ kārayed bhiṣak ||  
 7.5.7  kovidārasya  bījaiś ca nīpasya vidulasya ca
       |
        
        gulūcyāśca  suṣvyāś ca paṭolapicumandayoḥ ||  
 7.5.8  kṛtvā madhūlikāyāś ca kaṣāyaṃ tena chardayet |
        
        eṣām eva phalānāntu muṣṭiṃ saṃgṛhya sannakham ||  
 7.5.9  madhukasya kaṣāyeṇa taccūrṇaṃ parimardayet ||  
 7.5.10  gulikāḥ kārayet tena karkandhubadaropamāḥ |
        
        kovidārakaṣāyeṇa pūrvakaloena chardayet ||  
 7.5.11  yathābalaṃ yathoddiṣṭaṃ chardayet tena sādhu saḥ |
        
 kṛtavedhanakalpo ' yamukto vamanavistare ||  
 7.5.12  ya evaṃ samprajānāti sa rājñāṃ kartumarhati || ity āha
       bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
        
        iti bhele kalpasthāne pañcamo ' dhyāyaḥ || || ṣaṣṭho ' dhyāyaḥ ||
       athātaścaturaṅgulīyaṃ kalpaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
        
 
 
 
 7.6.1  manojñadeśajātas tu yo bhavec caturaṅgulaḥ |
        
        phalamuṣṭiṃ samāhṛtya tataścūrṇāni kārayet ||  
 7.6.2  taccūrṇitaṃ tridhākṛtya bhāgamekaṃ nidhāpayet |
        
        dvau bhāgau ca śucissamyak kṛtvā manthanam eva tu ||  
 7.6.3  ścyotayitvā parisrutya suprasannamanāvilam  |
        
 paribhāgaṃ samāvāpya sādhayed gomayāgninā ||  
 7.6.4 tasmiṃs tathā sicyamāne sūkṣmāṇīmāni dāpayet |
        
        harītakīmāmalakaṃ vibhītakaphalāni ca ||  
 7.6.5  madhūkabhāgamāvāpya tadvilepanamāharet |
        
        tataḥ pāṇitalaṃ cūrṇaṃ lehyaṃ tena viricyate ||  
 7.6.6  etenaiva ca kalpena kaṇṭakāryāḥ phalair api |
        
        ścyotayitvā lehajātaṃ paritaḥ sāsavaṃ pibet ||  
 7.6.7  caturaṅgulasiddhā  vā peyā yojyā susaṃskṛtā 
       |
        
        viricyate tena sādhu nāyogo nātiyogitā  ||  
 7.6.8  dhātrīphalarasadroṇe śarkarārdhatulāṃ pacet |
        
        ghṛtaṃ catuṣpalaṃ pakvaṃ pṛthagardhapalaṃ kṣipet ||  
 7.6.9  nataṃ vellaṃ caturjātaṃ yaṣṭisaindhavajīrakam |
        
        palāśaṃ viśvamaricaṃ mṛdvīkāyāścatuṣpalam ||  
 7.6.10  prasthaṃ kaṇātrivṛtayor madhunaś ca nihanti tat |
        
 tatkhaṇḍāmalakaṃ nāma pāṇḍuśvayathukāmilām ||  
 7.6.11  śirobhramaṇamunmādamamlapittavikārajit ||  
 7.6.12.  bhallātakānāṃ pavanāhatānāṃ vṛntacyutānāmiha cāṭhakaṃ
       syāt |
        
        tadiṣṭakācūrṇakaṇairvighṛṣya prakṣālayitvā visṛjetpravāte ||  
 7.6.13  śuṣkaṃ punastadvidalīkṛtaṃ ca vinikṣipedapsu
       caturguṇāsu |
        
        pādāvaśiṣṭaṃ paripūtaśītaṃ kṣīreṇa tulyena punaḥ paceta ||  
 7.6.14  tatpādaśiṣṭaṃ punareva śītaṃ ghṛtena tulyena punaḥ
       paceta |
        
        tadardhayā śarkarayāvagāṭhaṃ lohābhayāvyoṣakacūrṇayuktam  ||  
 7.6.15  etatsamaṃ śārkarapādayuktaṃ tataḥ
       khajenonmathitaṃ nidhāya |
        
        prasthadvayenāmalakīmadhūnāṃ  śīte  ' tha dhānyena punaḥ paceta
       ||  
 7.6.16  tatsaptarātrādupajātavīryaṃ sudhārasādapyadhikatvameti
       |
        
 prātarviśuddhīkṛtadehabhājāṃ 
       mātrāṃ dadītātmaśarīrayogyām  ||  
 7.6.17  na cānnapāne parihāryamāste na coṣṇavātādhvani maithune
       ca |
        
        janturnitāntaṃ  narasihmavatsyādbhaven naraḥ kāñcanarāśigauraḥ ||  
 7.6.18  dantāś ca śīrṇāḥ punarudbhavanti keśāś ca śuklāḥ
       punareva  kṛṣṇāḥ |
        
 viśīrṇakarṇāṅgulināsiko ' pi kṛmyardito bhinnagalo  ' pi kuṣṭhī
       ||  
 7.6.19  so ' pi krameṇāṅguligātraśākhastaruryathā rohati
       vārisiktaḥ |
        
        mahāmayūrāñjayati svareṇa balena nāgāṃsturagān javena ||  
 7.6.20  |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. sudhākṣīreṇa bhāvayet |
        
        tatpibet tu yathotsāhaṃ tena sādhu viricyate ||  
 7.6.21 dantyakṣatā tu tejohvā tarkārī sudurālabhā
       |
        
        kaṣāyakvātha ity etatsudhākṣīreṇa miśrayet ||  
 7.6.22  tatpibet tu yathotsāhaṃ tena sādhu viricyate |
        
        sudhākṣīreṇa gokṣīramekasthamabhisaṃsṛjet ||  
 7.6.23  tatpibet tu yathotsāhaṃ tena sādhu viricyate |
        
        kṛtamūtrapurīṣasya vāte cāpy anulomite ||  
 7.6.24  prathamaṃ snigdhakoṣṭhasya svinnasya ca yathāvidhi |
        
        sandhyāvelāmatikramya vimale ca divākare |
        
        maitre muhūrte vyakte tu yogānetān prayojayet || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ
       || iti bhele kalpasthāne ṣaṣṭho ' dhyāyaḥ || || saptamo ' dhyāyaḥ
       || athāto dantīphalakalpaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ
       |
        
        |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |..  
 
 
 7.7.1  tridhā vibhajya matimān svanuguptaṃ nidhāpayet |
        
        rasenāmalakasyāpi dvau bhāgau ścyotayed bhiṣak ||  
 7.7.2  cyutaṃ kaṣāyaṃ vimalaṃ pariyogamadhiśrayet |
        
 tasmiṃs tathā pacyamāne taccūrṇamabhisaṃsṛjet ||  
 7.7.3  tanmātraṃ triphalācūrṇamāvapenmadhusaṃyutam |
        
        lehabhūtaṃ viditvainamathainamavatārayet ||  
 7.7.4  tasya pāṇitalaṃ cūrṇaṃ lehyaṃ tena viricyate |
        
        eteṣāṃ caiva mūlānāṃ kṛtvā cūrṇāni sūkṣmaśaḥ ||  
 7.7.5  śyāmākaṣāyeṇāloḍya ghṛtaṃ siddhaṃ vipācayet |
        
        jānīyāt tad yadā  siddham athainam avatārayet ||  
 7.7.6 tad dṛḍhe madhulipte tu nave kumbhe samāvapet |
        
        mṛtsnābhiḥ  svanulipte tu svanuguptaṃ nidhāpayet ||  
 7.7.7  prasṛtaṃ pāyayet tatra tena sādhu viricyate |
        
        eteṣāṃ caiva mūlānāṃ kṛtvā cūrṇāni sarvaśaḥ ||  
 7.7.8  bṛhatīrasasammiśraiḥ gulikāṃ kārayet tu taiḥ |
        
        gulikāṃ kārayitvā tu karkandhubadaropamām ||  
 7.7.9  śyāmākaṣāyeṇāloḍya dve vā tisro ' pi vā tataḥ |
        
        pāyayet tu yathotsāhaṃ taṃ snigdhasveditaṃ naram ||  
 7.7.10  viricyate tena sādhu nāyogo nātiyogitā |
        
        snehādi snehamūlaṃ tu pracchardanavirecanam |
        
 nāparisnigdhakoṣṭhasya prasidhyati viśodhanam || ity āha
       bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
        
        iti bhele kalpasthāne saptamo ' dhyāyaḥ || || aṣṭhamo ' dhyāyaḥ || athātaḥ
       śaṅkhinīkalpaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
        
 
 
 
 7.8.1  phalāni paripakvāni śaṅkhinyāstūddharedbhiṣak |
        
        antarā  caitravaiśākhamavyagro  yavasaṃgrahe ||  
 7.8.2  anūṣare niruddhāre kṣetre sūryapratāpite |
        
        kṛṣṇamṛtsnāprabhe vāpi tathā ca svarṇamṛttike ||  
 7.8.3  na vyagre na ca valmīke na cāpi tṛṇachādite |
        
        susame bhūpradeśe tu yā jātā śaṅkhinī bhavet ||  
 7.8.4 tasyā droṇaṃ samāvāpya tadbhāṇḍaṃ siddhabandhanam
       |
        
        yavaparṇoṣitaṃ cāpi samuddhṛtya nidhāpayet ||  
 7.8.5  saptarātraṃ vārdhamāsaṃ samācchādya samantataḥ |
        
        ātape pariśuṣkāṇi sūkṣmacūrṇāni kārayet ||  
 7.8.6  phalānāmatha caiteṣāṃ dvau bhāgau kārayed bhiṣak |
        
        tilaṃ tṛtīyakaṃ kṛtvā kṣodayitvā hyulūkhale ||  
 7.8.7  samyag dṛṣadi niṣpiṣya 
       tailamuddhārayet tataḥ |
        
        śaṅkhinyā hy akṣamātraṃ tu trivṛtkalkamathāpi vā ||  
 7.8.8  tasmiṃstaile payaś caiva bhiṣagdadyāccaturguṇam |
        
        etat sarvaṃ samāloḍya pācayenmṛdunāgninā ||  
 7.8.9  pakvamāhṛtya visrāvya svanuguptaṃ nidhāpayet |
        
        tasyāñjaliṃ prakuñcaṃ vā prasṛtaṃ vāpi pāyayet ||  
 7.8.10  viricyate tena sādhu nāyogo nātiyogitā |
        
        susūkṣmasyātha śaṅkhinyāścūrṇasya prasṛtaṃ śṛtam ||  
 7.8.11  kṣīrapātreṇa saṃyojya pariyogamadhiśrayet 
       |
        
        tathā vipācya visrāvya śītīkṛtyābhimanthayet  ||  
 7.8.12  tatra yannavanītaṃ syāt tad uddhṛtya vipācayet |
        
        śaṅkhinīphalakalkena kṣīreṇa salilena ca ||  
 7.8.13  sa pibettad yathotsāhaṃ tena sādhu viricyate |
        
        śaṅkhinīphalakalkantu samyak dṛṣadi peṣayet ||  
 7.8.14  gokṣīreṇa samāloḍya pibettena viricyate |
        
        etenaiva ca kalpena hyuṣṭrīkṣīreṇa pāyayet ||  
 7.8.15  ajākṣīre  ' vikākṣīre  māhiṣe vātha vā
       punaḥ |
        
        gomūtreṇoṣṭramūtreṇa cāvimūtreṇa vā punaḥ ||  
 7.8.16  athavā hastimūtreṇa pibettena viricyate |
        
 āmṛdgannatha mṛdvīkāṃ dāpayetphāṇitodake ||  
 7.8.17  bhṛṣṭvā tu śaṅkhinītaile pariyogamadhiśrayet |
        
 ardhaṃ cūrṇāni pippalyā harītakyāś ca dāpayet ||  
 7.8.18  ataḥ pāṇitalaṃ prāśya tena sādhu viricyate |
        
        śaṅkhinīphalamadhyāni dātavyaṃ lavaṇaṃ tathā ||  
 7.8.19  śaṅkhinītailabhṛṣṭāni phāṇitenātha saṃsṛjet |
        
 godhūmājyena saṃsṛjya modakān kārayed bhiṣak ||  
 7.8.20  tāṃstrīn dvau vātha saṃbhakṣya tatassādhu viricyate |
        
        surāṃ sauvīrakaṃ takraṃ dadhimas tu tuṣodakam ||  
 7.8.21 kaṭvaraṃ kolasīdhuṃ vā
       dadhi pakvarasaṃ tathā |
        
        karkandhubadarāṇāṃ vā sīdhuṃ pīlupriyālayoḥ ||  
 7.8.22  bhavyapārāvatānāṃ ca mṛdvīkāmadyam eva vā |
        
        bilvaśigrukapitthānāṃ rasānvā saha pāyayet ||  
 7.8.23  ayaṃ hi śaṅkhinīkalpo mayā tu samudāhṛtaḥ |
        
        ya evaṃ samprajānāti sa rājñāṃ kartumarhati || ity āha bhagavān
       ātreyaḥ |
        
        iti bhele kalpasthāne ' ṣṭamo ' dhyāyaḥ || || navamo ' dhyāyaḥ || athātaḥ
       śyāmātrivṛtkalpaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
        
 
 
 
 7.9.1  śyāmāyāstrivṛtayāś ca mūlānyuddhārayed bhiṣak |
        
        kalyāṇadeśajātāyāḥ kuśarohiṣasaṃskṛte ||  
 7.9.2  kṛṣṇamṛtsnāprame vāpi hyathavā svarṇamṛttike |
        
        mūlāny etāni saṃgṛhya sūkṣmacūrṇāni kārayet ||  
 7.9.3  sthirākaṣāye  saṃsṛjya pāyayet tu yathābalam |
        
        viricyate tena sādhu nāyogo nātiyogitā ||  
 7.9.4  triphalārasamātreṇa drākṣāpīlurasena vā |
        
        āloḍya vāpi payasā sarpiṣā  vāpi pāyayet ||  
 7.9.5  hariṇasaya rasaṃ dadyānnyaṅkoś ca mahiṣasya ca |
        
        khaḍgasya kalaviṅkasya tittirerlāvukasya ca ||  
 7.9.6  rasamanyatamaṃ teṣāṃ trivṛcchyāmāprayojitam |
        
        yathābalaṃ pāyayet tu susnigdhaṃ sveditaṃ naram ||  
 7.9.7  śyāmāyāstrivṛtāyāś ca kṛtvā cūrṇāni sūkṣmaśaḥ |
        
        tridhā vibhajya tatraikaṃ svayaṃ guptaṃ nidhāpayet ||  
 7.9.8  rasena tu priyaṅgūṇāṃ dvau bhāgau ścyotayed bhiṣak
       |
        
        bhājane tu parisrāvya suprasannamanāvilam ||  
 7.9.9  pariyogamadhiśrity a pācayenmṛdunāgninā |
        
 tasmiṃs tathā pacyamāne cūrṇāny etāni dhāpayet ||  
 7.9.10 priyaṅguṃ tagaraṃ caiva tālīsaṃ naladaṃ tathā |
        
        hīberaṃ caiva mustāṃ ca balāṃ kālānusāribām ||  
 7.9.11  aśokapuṣpacūrṇāni padmasaugandhikāni ca |
        
        nalinaṃ puṇḍarīkaṃ ca pippalīmūlam eva ca ||  
 7.9.12  madhunā saha saṃsṛjya lihyāt pāṇitalonmitam  |
        
        susnigdho jīrṇabhaktaś ca yathāśāstraṃ yathābalam ||  
 7.9.13  viricyate tena sādhu nāyogo  nātiyogitā  |
        
        candanaṃ padmakaṃ nīpaṃ sālaṃ saptacchadaṃ tathā ||  
 7.9.14  punarnavāṃ  tu palalaṃ kirātaṃ tiktam eva
       vā |
        
        ye cānye tiktamadhurā rasāḥ pūrvaṃ prakīrtitāḥ ||  
 7.9.15  teṣāṃ kaṣāyairyojyaṃ syāt paittikānāṃ virecanam |
        
        pārāvatān kapotāṃś ca krauñcabarhiṇakukkuṭān ||  
 7.9.16  kuraṅgān hariṇāneṇān haritān kālapucchakān |
        
        vartakān tittirīṃścaiva  śaśalāvakapiñjalān ||  
 7.9.17  rasais tair upayuñjīta paittikasya virecanam |
        
        sārāḥ phalāni cūrṇāni patrāṇi ca payāṃsi ca ||  
 7.9.18  ya uktāḥ sthāvarāḥ pūrvaṃ tathaiva mṛgapakṣiṇaḥ |
        
        pānāni phalaniṣkvāthakaṣāyādidravān rasān ||  
 7.9.19 lehān bhakṣyāṃś ca sānnādīn tebhyaḥ
       samabhikalpayet |
        
        parūṣakasya drākṣāyā rasaṃ samadhuśarkaram  ||  
 7.9.20  trivṛdakṣasamāyuktaṃ pītvā sādhu viricyate |
        
        sādhayeccharkarāyuktaṃ sahaiva madhunā bhiṣak ||  
 7.9.21 śīte tasmiṃstrivṛccūrṇaṃ yathākoṣṭhaṃ samāvapet |
        
        tataḥ kampillakāccūrṇaṃ  dve ca te tindukasya ca ||  
 7.9.22 āragvadhaphalānmadhyabhāgāś
       cākṣasamāstathā  |
        
        trivṛccūrṇasya dharaṇaṃ śarkarā madhukaṃ madhu ||  
 7.9.23  maricaṃ nāgapuṣpaṃ ca tvakpatraṃ ca sucūrṇitam |
        
        etat sarvaṃ samāyojya modakaṃ kārayed bhiṣak ||  
 7.9.24  atha vā kārayellehaṃ tena sādhu viricyate |
        
        drākṣārasasya kuḍavaṃ parūṣakarasasya ca ||  
 7.9.25  madhunaḥ kuḍavārdhaṃ ca śarkarāpalam eva ca
       |
        
        trivṛccūrṇakṛto lehastena sādhu viricyate ||  
 7.9.26 etadutsannadoṣāṇāmīśvarāṇāṃ virecanam |
        
        śarkarāmodakaṃ vāpi guḍakaṃ māṣapūrakam ||  
 7.9.27  anena vidhinā kuryāt paittikānāṃ virecanam |
        
        trivṛccūrṇāni pippalyāḥ phalānyāragvadhasya ca ||  
 7.9.28  kalkānakṣasamānetān pibeddhīro virecanam |
        
        trivṛccūrṇasya dharaṇaṃ śarkarā madhukaṃ madhu ||  
 7.9.29  etadakṣasamāyuktaṃ pītvā sādhu viricyate |
        
        trivṛccūrṇāni pippalyo yavakṣāro mahauṣadham ||  
 7.9.30  śleṣmakopaśamārthāya  lihyāt tena viricyate |
        
        avimūtramajāmūtramuṣṭrasya mahiṣasya ca ||  
 7.9.31  mṛgasya mūtraṃ gomūtraṃ gardabhasya dvipasya ca |
        
        etānyaṣṭau prayuñjīta pṛthagvā yadi vā saha ||  
 7.9.32  trivṛccūrṇavimiśrāṇi vilihyānmadhunāpi vā |
        
        ajātāni ca madyāni tīkṣṇāni niśi tāni ca ||  
 7.9.33  trivṛccūrṇavimiśrāṇi pītvā sādhu viricyate |
        
        trivṛccūrṇaṃ yathākoṣṭhaṃ ślaiṣmikaḥ pātumarhati ||  
 7.9.34  trivṛtāyāḥ kaṣāyeṇa sakṣaudraṃ sāmlavetasam |
        
        atha vā dadhimaṇḍena kolakānāṃ rasena vā ||  
 7.9.35  kulutthamudgayūṣair vā  satīnaciribilvayoḥ |
        
        yavakolakayūṣeṇa pibetkaulatthameva  vā ||  
 7.9.36  yuktaṃ vā taintraṇīkena sāmlavetasadāḍimam |
        
        yūṣeṇa śigrukolāhvāmūlakānāṃ rasena vā ||  
 7.9.37 rasenāmalakānāṃ vā bījapūrārjakasya  vā |
        
        kapittharasamaṇḍena karamardarasena vā ||  
 7.9.38  yaccānyadapi vā kiñcitphalamamlam iti smṛtam |
        
        pibettatsvarasair vāpi pañcamūlīrasena vā ||  
 7.9.39  kaṭukalkavimiśraṃ vā yavakṣāreṇa saṃyutam |
        
        mṛdvīkāphalakalkena lehārtham upakalpayet ||  
 7.9.40  pratyekasya phalānāṃ ca pūrvoktānāṃ cikitsakaḥ |
        
        sujātānāṃ supakvānāṃ pratyagraṃ grāhayed rasam ||  
 7.9.41  tatrāmlalvaṇībhūte viripyāt saindhave bhavet(?) |
        
        lehe ' smin trivṛtaścūrṇaṃ  yathākoṣṭhaṃ samāvapet ||  
 7.9.42  sakṣaudraṃ saguḍaṃ vāpi lihyāt sakaṭukaṃ tathā |
        
        etena vidhinā kuryānmodakān ṣāḍabānrasān ||  
 7.9.43  pānāni ca phalāmlāni bhakṣyaṃ bhojyaṃ ca saṃskṛtam |
        
        etad rājñāṃ samākhyātam īśvarāṇāṃ virecanam ||  
 7.9.44  vidhimevaṃ prayuñjīta tvimaṃ cānyaṃ cikitsakaḥ |
        
        śāṇamāmalakānāṃ ca vibhītakaphalāni ca ||  
 7.9.45 tilvakassaptalā dantī śaṅkhinī
       caturaṅgulaḥ  |
        
        harītakīnāmekaṃ ca yavakṣāro vacaiva hi ||  
 7.9.46  pippalīnāṃ ca śāṇassyādviḍaṅgācchāṇa  eva
       ca |
        
        trivṛccūrṇasya triśśāṇāstat sarvamavacūrṇayet ||  
 7.9.47  tāni cūrṇāni madhunā sarpiṣā vā guḍena vā |
        
        lehaṃ vā vidhinā  |.. |.. |.. |.. || || siddhisthānam ||
       || prathamo ' dhyāyaḥ |
