        |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |..  
 
 
 
 
 8.1.1  riktakoṣṭhasya vamane mārutaḥ  samprakupyati |
        
        plīhā pracalati sthānāttasmād doṣānnihantyasūn ||  
 8.1.2  peyāṃ maṇḍaṃ pibettasmāt susnigdhaṃ lavaṇānvitam |
        
        saumye tithau muhūrte ca nakṣatre karaṇe śubhe ||  
 8.1.3  śuklavastraḥ śucirbhūtvā hyarcayitvā dvijanmanaḥ |
        
        tato ' smai vamanaṃ deyaṃ pūjayitvā bhiṣagvarān ||  
 8.1.4  prāṅmukhena tu pātavyaṃ nivāte śaraṇe śubhe |
        
        na cāsya kuryād āyāsaṃ  maṇḍaṃ bhojyaṃ praśasyate ||  
 8.1.5  vidhireṣa  bhavetkāryo vamane ca virecane |
        
        niṣkvāthasya  trayaḥ prasthāḥ māgadhās tu kanīyasi ||  
 8.1.6  jyeṣṭhe tu puruṣe jyeṣṭhaṃ vamanaṃ  na kanīyasi |
        
        catuḥprasthaṃ tu madhyaṃ syājjyeṣṭhaṃ prasthās tu te nava ||  
 8.1.7 kanīyo madhyamaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ trividhāni pṛthak pṛthak
       |
        
 apītapūrvaṃ vamanaṃ vireko vāpi yena tu ||  
 8.1.8  kanīyasā pramāṇena parīkṣeta ca buddhimān |
        
 tripalaṃ śreṣṭham ākhyātaṃ kanīyas tu palaṃ bhavet ||  
 8.1.9  madhyaṃ dve pale vidyāditi me niścitā matiḥ |
        
        viṣakuṣṭhahatā ye tu kāsaśvāsaprapīḍitāḥ ||  
 8.1.10  taruṇā balavantaś ca vāmayed uttamena tān |
        
        madhyame prāṇavayasi madhyamaṃ tatra kārayet ||  
 8.1.11  kanīyasi kanīys tu tathā prāṇe kanīyasi |
        
        viparītaṃ prayuñjāno na rogānvijayiṣyati ||  
 8.1.12  upadravānvā janayed āturaṃ vā vināśayet |
        
        aṅkolasyātha nimbasya niṣkvāthaṃ sādhu yojayet ||  
 8.1.13  sarpiṣā bheṣajaiścemaiḥ sukhoṣṇaṃ śītam eva vā |
        
        madanasya phalaṃ piṣṭvā devadālīphalaissaha ||  
 8.1.14  nimbapatrāṇi sārdrāṇi saindhavaṃ maricāni ca |
        
        saindhavena samāyuktaṃ takramaṇḍena  vā punaḥ ||  
 8.1.15  bandhujīvo ' tha pippalyo madanaṃ sarpireva ca |
        
        tatkaṣāyeṇa saṃyuktaṃ pradhānaṃ vamanauṣadham ||  
 8.1.16  madanaṃ bandhujīvaś ca śatapuṣpā śukānanā  |
        
        saindhavena samāyuktaṃ pradhānaṃ vamanauṣadham ||  
 8.1.17  madanasya ca patrāṇi puṣpāṇi saphalāni ca |
        
        saindhavaṃ bandhujīvaś ca rājakośātakāni ca ||  
 8.1.18 evaṃ pracchardano yogaḥ pradhānaṃ vamanauṣadham |
        
        śreṣṭhaś ca viṣayukteṣu kāsaśvāse tu pūjitaḥ ||  
 8.1.19  yadā tu vamanaṃ pītaṃ na chardayati mānavam |
        
        kiṃ tatra bheṣajaṃ kuryāt kathaṃ vaidyaḥ samācaret ||  
 8.1.20  darśayet tasya tu bhiṣak pālitāni  pṛthak
       pṛthak |
        
 makṣikākeśacūrṇāni tac ca maṇḍe niyojayet ||  
 8.1.21  etena tu prayogeṇa kṣipraṃ chardayate naraḥ |
        
        eṣā kriyā samākhyātā durbalānāṃ viśeṣataḥ ||  
 8.1.22  hṛdayaṃ pṛṣṭhadeśaṃ ca vigṛhya ca vamen naraḥ |
        
 tathāsya calati sthānātpītaṃ hy asminnupakrame ||  
 8.1.23  kaphaṃ hi pūrvaṃ vamati tataḥ pittamanantaram |
        
        pittasthānte bhavedvātaḥ tato vamati śoṇitam ||  
 8.1.24  lakṣaṇāni tu vakṣyāmi samyagvāntasya dehinaḥ |
        
        laghurāmāśaye śuddhirhṛcchuddhiś cāpy atandritā ||  
 8.1.25  kṣutpipāse yathākālaṃ srotaḥśuddhiryathāgnitā |
        
        ślaiṣmikāṇāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ vyādhīnāṃ vinivartanam ||  
 8.1.26  na ca vairasyamāsyasya samyagvāntasya lakṣaṇam |
        
        hṛllāso ' tha sirāharṣo manyā kaṇṭhaś ca dīryate ||  
 8.1.27  atyudgārastamaḥ kāso hikkā śvāsaḥ svarakṣayaḥ |
        
        vātajvaraḥ śuṣkavamistṛṣṇā śūlo hy anidratā ||  
 8.1.28  āsyahṛcchoṣaṇaṃ caiva kṣatāc ca rudhirāgamaḥ |
        
        indriyāṇyuparudhyante mūrcchā cāsyopajāyate ||  
 8.1.29  hanustambhaś ca kampaś ca hyativānte pravartate |
        
 ūrdhvaraktī pramehī ca gulmī cārśobhagandarī  ||  
 8.1.30  udarī pāṇḍurogī ca hṛdrogī kṛmikoṣṭhakaḥ |
        
        apasmārī viṣārtaś ca śophastambhaś ca vātikaḥ ||  
 8.1.31  viṣamajvaravīsarpī  vātaśoṇitikaś ca yaḥ |
        
        arśo ' tiviṣamāgniś ca kuṣṭhaśvayathupīḍitaḥ ||  
 8.1.32  udāvartī tathonmādī pipluvyaṅganipīḍitaḥ |
        
        pittaśleṣmasamutthānā vyākulā ye ca dhātavaḥ ||  
 8.1.33  sannipātasamutthāś ca yoniduṣṭāś ca yāḥ striyaḥ |
        
        śūlārtā raktagulminyo yāś ca saumyena pīḍitāḥ ||  
 8.1.34 asnigdhāraktatāṅgānāṃ lāghavaṃ gātramārdavam |
        
        hṛdayodgāramūtrāṇāṃ śuddhirvātānulomataḥ ||  
 8.1.35  prasannasvaravarṇatvaṃ bubhukṣā vyādhinigrahaḥ |
        
 śleṣmaṇā ca svayaṃ sthānaṃ suviriktasya laksaṇam ||  
 8.1.36  udaraṃ vātasampūrṇaṃ kaṇḍūmaṇḍalasambhavaḥ |
        
        piṭakājanma gātreṣu bhramaṇaṃ jvarasamplavaḥ ||  
 8.1.37  hṛdayāveṣṭanaṃ vahneḥ sādassyāt kukṣigauravam |
        
        kṛcchraviṇmūtravātatvaṃ durviriktasya lakṣaṇam ||  
 8.1.38 pārśvaśūlaṃ gudabhraṃśaḥ śākhāsaṃkocasambhramaḥ |
        
        vātavṛddhirvisaṃjñatvaṃ gudaśūlastṛṣā klamaḥ ||  
 8.1.39  śūnyatā jarjarībhāvastataścimacimāyanam |
        
        rūpāṇyativiriktānāṃ śūlaḥ śophaś ca jāyate ||  
 8.1.40  gaurave durviriktasya yadajīrṇaṃ tadullikhet |
        
        sātmyaṃ tu peyaṃ bhaiṣajyaṃ nirūho gāḍhavarcasām ||  
 8.1.41 rūpāṇyativiriktasya haretkṣīraghṛtādibhiḥ |
        
        snehaiścaivopanāhaiś ca sābhyaṅgaiś ca bhiṣagjayet  || |.. |..
       |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. || dvitīyo ' dhyāyaḥ || |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |..
       |.. |..  
 
 
 8.2.1  avapīḍānuvāsāś ca dhūmāḥ pradhamanāni ca |
        
        caturvidhaṃ nasyam āhuḥ pṛthaktvena tu me śṛṇu || 8| 
 8.2.2 galagraho rohiṇikā  śaṅkhako '
       rdhāvabhedakaḥ |
        
        pratiśyāyaś ca kāsaś ca śvāso hikkā biḍālikā ||  
 8.2.3  mukharogo  hy apasmāro dantatālukavidradhī |
        
        dantapuppuṭakaś caiva pūtināsāmukhaṃ tathā ||  
 8.2.4  abhiṣyandāś ca catvārastandrā ye netrasaṃbhavāḥ |
        
        sārbudāś cāpy adhīmanthāḥ  nāsārśaś ca bhagandarāḥ ||  
 8.2.5  upajihvā galagranthiḥ kaṇṭhaśālūka eva ca |
        
        galaśuṇṭhikālasake kāryaṃ śīrṣavirecanam ||  
 8.2.6  maricāni vilaṅgāni pippalyo ' tha phaṇirjakaḥ |
        
        kṣavako  yavanaś caiva śigrubījaṃ mayūrakaḥ  ||  
 8.2.7  hiṅgu sauvarcalaṃ bhārṅgī naktamālaphalāni ca |
        
        jyotiṣmatī  śṛṅgiberaṃ śairīṣaṃ bījam eva ca ||  
 8.2.8  etacchīrṣavirekārthamuktavyādhiṣu yojayet |
        
        avapīḍe ' tha dhūme vā dvandvaśaḥ sarvaśo ' pi vā ||  
 8.2.9  etair eva uṣadhagaṇais tailaṃ dhīro  vipācayet |
        
        avimūtreṇa saṃyuktaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ śīrṣavirecanam ||  
 8.2.10  dhūmaṃ ca sarvagandhānāṃ natakuṣṭhavivarjitam |
        
        dhūmavartiṃ pibettāvacchreṣṭhaṃ śīrṣavirecanam ||  
 8.2.11  śirasas tu virekeṇa karṇajihvākṣināsikāḥ |
        
        viśudhyante yathādoṣaṃ mukhanāsāvaheṣu ca ||  
 8.2.12 vivṛtiḥ kheṣu viśadā na ca śleṣmā prasicyate |
        
        samyak śirasi saṃśuddhe vedanā copaśāmyati ||  
 8.2.13  vyādhau ca bhaṅgacūrṇatvaṃ(?) srotasāṃ 
       suviśuddhatā |
        
        tathaivātiviśuddheṣu srotassvāyasyate śiraḥ ||  
 8.2.14  dantacāle hanustambhe manyāstambhe śirograhe |
        
        vādhirye karṇaśūle ca karṇamūlāc ca bhedane ||  
 8.2.15  apatantre keśasāde  ' prabodhe dṛṣṭivibhrame |
        
 hikkānetramukhāsrāve svarabhede ' tha vāggrahe ||  
 8.2.16  gaṇḍoṣṭhamukhacāleṣu kāceṣu timireṣu ca |
        
        daurgandhye  mukhanāsābhyāṃ pālity e vāpy akālaje ||  
 8.2.17  ūrdhvajatrugatā ye ca rogāssamparikīrtitāḥ |
        
        nasyakarma hitaṃ teṣāṃ tailaṃ vā sarpireva vā ||  
 8.2.18  jīvakarṣabhakau  drākṣā pippalyo madhukaṃ balā |
        
        prapauṇḍarīkaṃ medā ca śarkarā nīlamutpalam ||  
 8.2.19  nidigdhikā cāṃśumatī nīlikā saindhavaṃ vacā |
        
        rāsnā śvadaṃṣṭrā mañjiṣṭhā bṛhatī sapunarnavā ||  
 8.2.20  ebhiḥ palasamaiḥ siddhaṃ tailaṃ vā yadi
       vā ghṛtam |
        
        caturguṇena payasā nasyaṃ tatparamucyate ||  
 8.2.21  nasyataḥ snehapānena kṛṣṇaromā dṛḍhendriyaḥ |
        
 avalīpalitavyaṅgaḥ cakṣuṣmāñjāyate naraḥ ||  
 8.2.22  karṇākṣināsāvaktrāṇāṃ snehenāvṛtya tarpaṇam |
        
        indriyāṇāṃ vimuktatvaṃ prasādaḥ svaravarṇayoḥ ||  
 8.2.23  srotasāṃ vimalatvaṃ ca jñeyaṃ saṃsnigdhalakṣaṇam
       |
        
        asnigdhaliṅgaṃ rūkṣatvaṃ srotasāṃ riktatā tathā ||  
 8.2.24  śiraso guruduḥkhatvaṃ srotasāṃ snehapūrṇatā |
        
 karṇatālūpadehaśca  nasyātisnigdhalakṣaṇam ||  
 8.2.25  nājīrṇe nārdraśirasi panthānaṃ gantumicchataḥ |
        
        na pītamātre pānīye jvaritasya na dāpayet ||  
 8.2.26  na maithunaṃ gatavataḥ madyapītasya naiva ca |
        
 nātibhuktasya nāsnigdhasvinnasyānirvṛtes tathā || 
 
 8.2.27  samyaṅ nirūḍhasya narugujā samyak
       praśāmyati |
        
        yato mūtrapurīṣāmyāṃ vāto hy asya nivartate ||  
 8.2.28  nirūḍhaṃ  taṃ bhiṣagvidyādanirūḍhasya 
       lakṣaṇam |
        
        tathaiva vyādhirādhmānaṃ  śūlaṃ viṇmūtranigrahaḥ ||  
 8.2.29  pūrṇakukṣitvamānāho durnirūḍhasya  lakṣaṇam |
        
        nirūḍhasya punaryasya śoṇitaṃ sampraduṣyati ||  
 8.2.30  atīva tu nirūḍhasya niṣpurīṣasya  mārutaḥ |
        
        śūlenāveṣṭyamanasya sarvagātrāṇi pīḍayet ||  
 8.2.31  iti pañcavidhaṃ coktaṃ vyākhyātaṃ samupācaret |
        
        pañcakarmavidhānajño rājārho bhiṣagucyate || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
        
        iti bhele dvitīyo ' dhyāyaḥ || || caturtho ' dhyāyaḥ || athāto
       daśavyāpadīyāṃ vamanavirecanasiddhiṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān
       ātreyaḥ |
        
 
 
 
 8.4.1  adhobhāgordhvabhāgāni bheṣajāni prayatnataḥ |
        
        kalpayenmatimānvaidyo viṣaśastranibhāni tu ||  
 8.4.2  kaṭutiktakaṣāyāṇi vidāhīnītarāṇi ca |
        
        sūkṣmāṇyuṣṇāni tīkṣṇāni viṣyandīni gurūṇi ca ||  
 8.4.3  tāni samprāpya hṛdayaṃ dhamanīḥ
       pratipadya hi |
        
        tiryagūrdhvamadhaś caiva doṣānniṣyandayantyapi  ||  
 8.4.4 sūkṣmāñcharīrāvayavān  saukṣmyādanusarinti
       ca |
        
        visrāvayanti  dhātūṃś ca vimārgaurapi dehinām ||  
 8.4.5  ānayantīva hṛdayaṃ doṣāṃstānatimūrcchitān |
        
        āmāśayaṃ pūriyitvāhyūrdhvabhāgabhavāṃs tathā ||  
 8.4.6 evam eva ca biṣyandīnyāpūryāmāśayaṃ punaḥ |
        
        adhobhāge pravartante vikāreṣv iha  dehinām ||  
 8.4.7  viṣyandayanti  doṣāṃś ca yāvattiṣṭhanti dehinām |
        
        saṃśodhayantyataḥ  paścādūrdhvaṃ vā yadi vāpy adhaḥ ||  
 8.4.8  teṣāṃ tu duṣprayuktānāṃ vibhrāntānāṃ vidhāvatām |
        
        ayogāccātiyogācca  jāyante vyāpado daśa ||  
 8.4.9  parisrāvastathādhmānaṃ vibandho gudaniḥsravaḥ |
        
        hṛdrogaś caiva śūlaṃ ca tathaiva parikartikā ||  
 8.4.10  jīvādānaṃ śirorogo  daśamī ca pravāhikā |
        
        tāsāmekaikatassiddhiṃ vyāpadāṃ tu nibodha me ||  
 8.4.11 athaiti pītaṃ vamanaṃ tac ca tīkṣṇataraṃ
       pibet |
        
        anupānānna siddhiś ca saṃśodhyāsthāpayennaram ||  
 8.4.12  asidhyati vireke  ' pi bhūyastamanuvāsayet |
        
        asminnapi jarāṃ yāti tryahādūrdhvaṃ pibed ghṛtam ||  
 8.4.13  snehasvedopapannaś ca laghu ca pratibhojitaḥ |
        
        virecanaṃ ca vamanaṃ narastīkṣṇataraṃ pibet ||  
 8.4.14  yadā virecanaṃ pītaṃ vamanāyopapadyate |  prayoga
       evaṃ  vamane vireke ' pi ca yaḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
 8.4.15  snehasvedavimuktaṃ ca krūrakoṣṭhaṃ ca dehinam |
        
 ajīrṇe cauṣadhaṃ pītamādhyāpayati mānavam ||  
 8.4.16  laṅghitasya subhaktasya rūkṣasyānaśanasya ca |
        
        parikartaḥ parisrāvaḥ pralepo ' sveditasya ca ||  
 8.4.17  snehasvedavimuktasya mṛdukoṣṭhasya dehinaḥ |
        
 doṣāstathāvaśiṣṭās tu janayanti pravāhikām ||  
 8.4.18  atiraukṣyādatisvehādauṣadhānāṃ ca sambhramāt |
        
        nṛṇāṃ śūlaṃ prabhavati gudasraṃsaś ca dāruṇaḥ ||  
 8.4.19  vamane recane vāpi pīte vegavidhārite |
        
        vātapittakaphāḥ kruddhāḥ kurvanti hṛdayagraham ||  
 8.4.20  tasya gātrāṇi sīdanti klamaḥ śūlaś ca dāruṇaḥ |
        
        śirograhaś ca koṣṭhārtirvisaṃjñaś ca bhavaty api ||  
 8.4.21  svinnasya mṛdukoṣṭhasya snehitasya virecanam |
        
        atimātrauṣadhaṃ pītaṃ jīvādānāya kalpate  ||  
 8.4.22 sṛjecchuklaṃ sa śakṛtā kṛṣṇaṃ vā raktam eva vā |
        
        lodhrapuṣpasavarṇaṃ vā bhaṇḍipuṣpanibhaṃ tathā ||  
 8.4.23  pravirikto yadā śītāṃ kriyāṃ samupasevate |
        
        śaraṇāni ca śītāni vāri śītaṃ ca sevate ||  
 8.4.24  srotāṃsi kupito vāyus tasya cāvṛtya tiṣṭhati |
        
        kharībhavati tenāsya  doṣāḥ skandanti dehinaḥ ||  
 8.4.25  vātamūtrapurīṣāṇāmapravṛttistṛṣā jvaraḥ |
        
        vibandha eṣa vyākhyāto bhiṣajāṃ buddhivibhramāt ||  
 8.4.26  asnigdhaṃ tu yadā rūkṣamauṣadhaṃ pāyayed bhiṣak |
        
        gṛhṇāti kupitas tasya sarvagātrāṇi mārutaḥ ||  
 8.4.27  kaṭipṛṣṭhaśirogrīvāhṛdayaṃ ca yadānilaḥ |
        
        prapadyate tadā mohaṃ cittanāśaṃ ca gacchati ||  
 8.4.28  daśaitā vyāpadaḥ proktā rūpairnānāvidhaiḥ pṛthak |
        
        cikitsāṃ tāsu kurvīta yathātreyasya śāsanam ||  
 8.4.29  tatrāyoginamabhyajya  tailena lavaṇena ca |
        
 saṅkaraprastarasvedairnāḍīsvedairathapi vā ||  
 8.4.30  samyaṅ nirūḍhaṃ viśrāntaṃ pariṣicya sukhāmbunā |
        
        jāṅgalena rasenaiva bhojayenmṛdumodanam  ||  
 8.4.31  phalatailena koṣṇena tatastamanuvāsayet |
        
        ādhmānaṃ parikartaśca  parisrāvaś ca śāmyati ||  
 8.4.32  sālo rubūkastriphalā dantī citraka eva ca |
        
        sarpirebhir vipakvaṃ  ca pāyayec ca yathābalam ||  
 8.4.33  tatsnehapītaṃ susnigdhaṃ svedakarmopapāditam |
        
        vamanaṃ recanaṃ vāpi pāyayet tīkṣṇamauṣadham ||  
 8.4.34  hṛdrogo gātraharṣaś ca śīrṣaskandhagrahas tathā |
        
        vibandhaḥ parikartaśca  śūlaś cānena śāmyati ||  
 8.4.35  parikartaḥ parisrāvo  yathātattvena śāmyati |
        
        kaṣāyavastiṃ praṇayetpicchāvastimathāpi vā ||  
 8.4.36 śṛtaṃ madhu ghṛtaṃ vāpi kṣīravastiṃ
       pradāpayet |
        
        jīvanīyopasiddhena sarpiṣā cānuvāsayet ||  
 8.4.37  eraṇḍamūlaṃ triphalā drākṣā kāśmaryameva  ca |
        
        ebhiḥ śṛtaṃ payo dadyādvividhair api miśrayet ||  
 8.4.38  yāvaśūko bhavetkṣāraḥ saindhavaṃ sāmlavetasam |
        
        hiṅgu dāḍimasāraś ca pippalyo viśvabheṣajam ||  
 8.4.39  sarpiṣā payasā vāpi madyenoṣṇodakena vā |
        
 pītaṃ nivartayecchūlaṃ  tīvraṃ ca parikartikām ||  
 8.4.40  devadāru  sabilvaṃ ca rāsnā karkaṭakāhvayā 
       |
        
 eraṇḍo ' pyatha pūtiśca  tailamebhir vipācayet   ||  
 8.4.41  tenānuvāsayeccainaṃ tadā sampadyate sukham |
        
        gātrastambhaś ca śūlaś ca parikartaś ca śāmyati ||  
 8.4.42  upadravāṇām eteṣāṃ śāntir yadi na vidyate |
        
        teṣāṃ cikitsitaṃ kuryād yathāsvaṃ svaṃ cikitsitam ||  
 8.4.43  evaṃ cikitsitaṃ  proktam ayoge vistareṇa me |
        
        atiyoge tu vakṣyāmi vyāpadāṃ  yac cikitsitam ||  
 8.4.44  atipravṛttau vamane virecanam upācaret |
        
        virecane cātiyukte vamanaṃ pāyayed bhiṣak ||  
 8.4.45  vamane cātiyukte tu kāryam āsthāpanaṃ bhavet |
        
        ubhayor atiyoge tu stambhanaṃ hitamucyate ||  
 8.4.46 ullikhetkṣaudrayuktena sa narastaṇḍulāmbunā |
        
        pādau ca secayed dhastau tathā vāpy avagāhayet ||  
 8.4.47  lāmajjakamṛṇālaiś ca candanaiś ca sapadmakaiḥ |
        
        sandihyāt sarvagātrāṇi kaṣāyaiś cāvasecayet ||  
 8.4.48  dhātakī madhukaṃ lodhraṃ padmaṃ mocarasas tathā |
        
        nīlotpalaṃ samaṅgā ca kaṭphalaṃ padmakesaram ||  
 8.4.49  etairlohitaśālīnāṃ siddhāṃ peyāṃ suśītalām |
        
        pibenmākṣikasaṃyuktaṃ tadasya sthāpanaṃ param ||  
 8.4.50  lākṣā lodhrassamaṅgā ca mākṣikaṃ kamalotpalam |
        
        ājena payasā pītaṃ raktastambhanamucyate ||  
 8.4.51  rasaṃ kapitthapatrasya pāyayenmadhusaṃyutam |
        
        payasā bādaraṃ drākṣāṃ madhunā ca piben naraḥ ||  
 8.4.52  rasāś ca jāṅgalā deyā vyaktā dāḍimasārakaiḥ |
        
        ghṛtadāḍimasaṃyuktā deyāḥ syuḥ kṣīravastayaḥ ||  
 8.4.53  atipravṛtte rakte tu raktam evānuvāsayet |
        
        śāśaṃ mārgamathaurabhraṃ chāgaṃ māhiṣam eva vā ||  
 8.4.54  odanaṃ payasā++āmṛdya paripūtaṃ samākṣikam |
        
        pibed ikṣurasair vāpi parimardyaudanaṃ punaḥ ||  
 8.4.55  nyagrodhodumbaraplakṣavetasāśvatthajais tathā  |
        
        śṛṅgairathaiṣāṃ kṣīreṇa yavāgūḥ sthāpanaṃ param ||  
 8.4.56  padmaṃ śālmaliniryāsaḥ  samaṅgā dhātakī tathā |
        
        jambvāmrasāro madhukaḥ  lājā lākṣā priyaṅgavaḥ ||  
 8.4.57 etaiḥ śṛtaṃ payaḥ peyaṃ yavāgūṃ cāpi
       pāyayet |
        
        taṇḍulodakayuktāni pibedvā madhunā saha ||  
 8.4.58  odanaḥ koradūṣāṇāṃ madhunā sasyasaṃbhṛtaḥ  |
        
 palaṅkaṣāsamāyuktaś cātisāraṃ nivartayet ||  
 8.4.59  saṃyuktaṃ tilatailena saptarātrasthitaṃ dadhi |
        
 koradūṣaudanopetamatisārapraṇāśanam ||  
 8.4.60  saptarātraṃ sthite takre mūlakaṃ sādhayed bhiṣak |
        
        koradūṣaudano yojyaḥ tenātīsāranāśanaḥ ||  
 8.4.61  vaṭāṅkuro mocaraso lodhramāmrāsthikandakaḥ |
        
        taruṇāni ca bilvāni dhātakīkusumāni ca ||  
 8.4.62  pañcarātrasthite takre yūṣamebhis tu kārayet |
        
        koradūṣaudano yojyaḥ tathātīsāranāśanaḥ ||  
 8.4.63  nīlotpalaṃ nīlatilāḥ samaṅgā lodhram eva ca |
        
        kṣīraṃ vipācayed ebhir atīsāravināśanam ||  
 8.4.64  tilatailaṃ tathā lodhramājaṃ kṣīraṃ vipācayet |
        
        pravāhikā gudabhraṃśaḥ sarvametena śāmyati ||  
 8.4.65  balā cātibalā bilvameraṇḍaścorakas tathā |
        
        ebhir vipācayet kṣīraṃ kaphapittapraṇāśanam ||  
 8.4.66  hanustambhe ca pātavyamarśaḥśūle ca dāruṇe |
        
        anenaiva ca kalkena  kuryād ācchāditaṃ śiraḥ ||  
 8.4.67  tena mūrcchā bhramaś caiva praśāmyati śarīriṇām |
        
        upadravāś ca ye ' pyanye teṣāṃ tattaccikitsitam ||  
 8.4.68  śarkarāpadmakośīranyagrodhodumbarāstathā  |
        
        ebhir vipācayet kṣīraṃ  tṛṣṇādāhapraṇāśanam ||  
 8.4.69  kṣīravastiṃ vidadyāc ca picchāvastimathāpi vā |
        
        atiyoge praśasyante śītāś ca ghṛtavastayaḥ ||  
 8.4.70  jīvādānacikitsāyāṃ yatpūrvaṃ parikīrtitam |
        
        tatkartavyaṃ gudabhraṃśe tathā sampadyate sukham ||  
 8.4.71  vātaśūle tu sañjāte saṅkaraprastarādikān  |
        
        svedāṃścaivopadehāṃśca svabhyaktānāṃ prayojayet ||  
 8.4.72 vacāṃ śvadaṃṣṭrāṃ pūtīkāṃ pañcamūlīṃ ca sādhitām
       |
        
 yadi vā++āsthāpanaṃ dadyāt sukhoṣṇaṃ cānuvāsanam  ||  
 8.4.73 kṣāraiḥ kṣāraghṛtaiś cāpi śūlaghnaissamupācaret |
        
 dādhikaṃ ṣaṭpalaṃ vāpi pāyayenmātrayā ghṛtam ||  
 8.4.74  evam eva vibandhe ' pi vidhiṃ kuryāc cikitsakaḥ |
        
 yāś ca vyāpattayaḥ paścādvamane ca virecane ||  
 8.4.75  tāścikitseta matimān yathā sve sve cikitsite |
        
        grāmyān  paudakaṃ māṃsaṃ snehito  yo ' pi sevate ||  
 8.4.76 kaphe pravṛddhe tasyāśu vireko vamanaṃ 
       bhavet |
        
        ajīrṇe cauṣadhaṃ pītamalpaṃ vā yadi vā bahu ||  
 8.4.77 utkleśe cordhvavāte ca duryukte vāpi bheṣaje |
        
        evaṃ virecanaṃ pītaṃ vamanāyopapadyate ||  
 8.4.78 karśite rūkṣite vāpi sukumāre sudāruṇe |
        
        asaṃjātakaphasyaiva na ca snigdhasya dehinaḥ ||  
 8.4.79  chardanaṃ vā sthitaṃ kṣubdhaṃ virekāyopapādayet |
        
        tatrānupānamevāhuḥ kecitkecittvasāmpratam ||  
 8.4.80  bheṣajaṃ hy atimātraṃ tu jīvādānāya kalpate |
        
        ūrdhvaṃ daśāhātparataḥ snehasvedopapāditam  ||  
 8.4.81  pāyayet tīkṣṇamevaitaṃ bheṣajaṃ kalpakalpitam |
        
        siddhirvirecanasyaiṣā  vamanasya ca kīrtitā |
        
        vyāpadaś ca cikitsā yā yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ || ity āha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
        
        iti bhele siddhisthāne caturtho ' dhyāyaḥ || || pañcamo ' dhyāyaḥ ||
       athāto vastimātrīyāṃ siddhiṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān
       ātreyaḥ |
        
 
 
 
 8.5.1  saṃsṛṣṭabhakte  śaṃsanti vastikarma cikitsakāḥ |
        
 virikteṣv apare vaidyā nirūḍhe  tvapare janāḥ ||  
 8.5.2  trīṇyetānyavarāṇyāhuḥ na śaṃsanti viśāradāḥ |
        
        mataṃ teṣāmahaṃ samyag vyāhaniṣyāmi hetubhiḥ ||  
 8.5.3 satatantu viriktasya śītībhavati pāvakaḥ |
        
 hṛdāśrayāṇi srotāṃsi gudakoṣṭhāśrayāṇi ca ||  
 8.5.4  pravṛddho mārutastasya pakvādhānaṃ pradhavati |
        
        śītīkaroti kāyāgniṃ balaṃ cāsyāpakarṣati ||  
 8.5.5  srotassu śuddhāśuddheṣu yadi vastiḥ pradīyate |
        
        sa gambhīro gataḥ kāye sarvaśo na nivartate ||  
 8.5.6  chardiṃ pipāsāṃ hṛdrogaṃ pāṇḍutvaṃ śvayathuṃ tathā |
        
        janayed iha tasmād dhi viriktaṃ nānuvāsayet ||  
 8.5.7  saṃsṛṣṭabhaktasya punaḥ jātadoṣasya dehinaḥ |
        
        srotassu malalipteṣu bhavetsneho nirarthakaḥ ||  
 8.5.8  tīkṣṇetaranirūheṇa nirūḍhasya śarīriṇaḥ |
        
 samutkliṣṭeṣu doṣeṣu snehavastirna śasyate ||  
 8.5.9  kecic cāpi śarīrasya rātriparyuṣitasya ca |
        
        praśāntā doṣasaṃjñānaḥ(?) praśaṃsantyanuvāsanam ||  
 8.5.10  vastikarmavidhānaṃ tu śṛṇu me nirupadravam |
        
        snehitasya yathānyāyaṃ viriktasya ca kalpaśaḥ  ||  
 8.5.11 saṃsṛṣṭabhaktasya tathā punaś ca snehitasya ca |
        
        pañcarātrātparaṃ  tasya kārayed anuvāsanam ||  
 8.5.12 noparyasnigdhakoṣṭhasya kartavyamanuvāsanam |
        
        vāto hyūrīkṛtas tasya hṛdaye paritiṣṭhati ||  
 8.5.13 ucitādbhaktamānādapyardhamātraṃ tu bhojayet |
        
        tanunā mudgayūṣeṇa jāṅgalena rasena vā ||  
 8.5.14 bhuktvā kṛtasamāśvāsaḥ śakṛnmūtre  visṛjya
       ca |
        
 savyena pārśvena naraḥ saṃviśecchayane same ||  
 8.5.15  saṃkocayed dakṣiṇaṃ  ca sakthi vāmaṃ prasārayet |
        
        vāmopadhānaṃ kurvīta śirasyupahitaṃ naraḥ ||  
 8.5.16 athāsya praṇayed vastiṃ pṛṣṭhavaṃśānugaṃ sukham |
        
 yathākarmabalaṃ caiva na drutaṃ na vilambitam ||  
 8.5.17  nirvyalīko mṛdurvastirvyapanītānilastathā  |
        
 gāḍhānilānubandho ' syāpraśasto vastikarmaṇi ||  
 8.5.18 netraṃ vastimukhe dhṛtvā samyagekena pāṇinā |
        
        prapīḍayeccāpareṇa hastau cāpi na kampayet ||  
 8.5.19  pūrvaṃ ca gudamabhyajya yantraṃ hastau ca
       mānavaḥ  |
        
        pravartayed athottānaṃ pādau vāsya prasārayet ||  
 8.5.20 muhūrtānna nigṛhṇīyāddatte  vastau
       yathāsukham |
        
        tataḥ paramato vegānāgatānna vidhārayet ||  
 8.5.21  avibandhassavātaśca  sapurīṣassa  sidhyati
       |
        
        dattamātre punaryasya tailavastirnivartate ||  
 8.5.22  na sa karyakaraḥ proktastasyānyaṃ  praṇidhāpayet
       |
        
        tṛṣitassa  tathā rātriṃ kālyamuṣṇodakaṃ pibet ||  
 8.5.23  ekāntare ca dātavyo bastirna satataṃ nṛṇām |
        
        abhyaṅgonmardanaṃ caiva koṣṇatoyāvasecanam ||  
 8.5.24  uṣṇodakānupānaṃ ca vastikarmaṇi śasyate |
        
        caturṣu triṣu vā vaidyo yāvadvā snigdhatā punaḥ ||  
 8.5.25  snehavastiṣu datteṣu kuryād āsthāpanaṃ tataḥ |
        
        ārdrīkṛteṣu srotassu snehena vihitena  ca ||  
 8.5.26  śuddhaye srotasāṃ dadyānnirūhānyuktitaḥ  sukham |
        
 aśuddhe maline koṣṭhe snehavastiḥ prayojitaḥ ||  
 8.5.27  pradarśayati vaiśiṣyaṃ śukle parvavyayīkṛtam |(?)
       virecanopacāraśca  kartavyo vastikarmaṇi ||  
 8.5.28  yavāgūpratipānaṃ ca bastikarmaṇi varjayet |
        
        caturviṃśatisaṅkhyātāḥ  nirūhāssānuvāsanāḥ ||  
 8.5.29  etatkarmeti nirdiṣṭamūrdhvavāte pradāpayet |
        
        mṛdumadhyamatīkṣṇeṣu  rogeṣu kuśalo bhiṣak ||  
 8.5.30  mṛdumadhyamatīkṣṇaṃ ca vastikarma ca kārayet |
        
        grāmyānūpaudakaṃ māṃsaṃ piṣṭānnaṃ palalaṃ dadhi ||  
 8.5.31  amlaśākavikārāṃś ca bhakṣyāṇi vividhāni ca |
        
        śītodakasya pānaṃ ca tathā śītāvagāhanam ||  
 8.5.32  gurūṇi cānnapānāni vastikarmaṇi varjayet |
        
        śāliṣaṣṭikamudgāṃś ca bhojanārthaṃ pradāpayet ||  
 8.5.33  vyañjanārthaṃ pradeyāḥ syuḥ śaśatittirilāvukāḥ |
        
 jñānavānsumitāhāro vaidyaśuśrūṣureva  ca |
        
        yaś ca vastimupāsīta sa jīveccharadāṃ śatam || ity āha bhagavān
       ātreyaḥ |
        
        iti bhele siddhisthāne pañcamo ' dhyāyaḥ || || ṣaṣṭo ' dhyāyaḥ ||
       athāta  upakalpasiddhiṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
        
 
 
 
 8.6.1  upakalpamato  vasternetraṃ snehaṃ ca sarvaśaḥ |
        
        teṣāṃ prayogayuktiṃ  ca kriyāṃ karma ca me śṛṇu ||  
 8.6.2  bālānāmatha vṛddhānāṃ yuvamadhyamayostathā  |
        
        svasthānāmāturāṇāṃ ca vastikarma praśasyate ||  
 8.6.3  sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ tāmraṃ
       kāṃsyaṃ trapujamāyasam |
        
 śṛṅgavaṃśāsthivaṃśāgrāṇyāhurnetrāṇi paṇḍitāḥ ||  
 8.6.4 yathākramamathaitāni pradhānānītarāṇi ca |
        
        uttamādhamamadhyeṣu manuṣyeṣu prayojayet ||  
 8.6.5  gulikāsyaṃ  tu netraṃ
       syādanūnadvādaśāṅgulam  |
        
        aṅgule  karṇikāvāsaḥ  tāṃ ca na kramayed gude ||  
 8.6.6  tatra gopucchasaṃsthānaṃ suślakṣṇaṃ sukhakarṇikam |
        
        pradeśinīparīṇāhaṃ dānaṃ tena praśasyate ||  
 8.6.7  tatra mātrāśataṃ sthitvā svenaiva vinivartate |
        
        yadyakāle navasneho madyamāṃsaprakalpitaḥ ||  
 8.6.8  nyūnakālanivṛttaśca  śīghratvānna nirūhati |
        
        tatas tu madhyamaḥ kiñcinnivarteta śataistribhiḥ ||  
 8.6.9  evaṃ kālagatikrānto yo vastirna nivartate |
        
 tīkṣṇenāsthāpanenaivaṃ kṣipraṃ pratinivartate ||  
 8.6.10  tasmāt tīkṣṇataraṃ vastiṃ pūrvamevopakalpayet |
        
 prāṇasaṃdhāraṇe hyuccairvibandho na praśasyate ||  
 8.6.11  tasmāt kālaṃ ca yo vyādhiṃ nirūhāṇāṃ balābalam |
        
 pūrṇarūpaṃ ca yo vetti sa mohaṃ na nigacchati ||  
 8.6.12.  na tathā hy anyato hanyānnāśanirna hutāśanaḥ |
        
 duṣprayukto yathā vastiḥ prāṇaissadyo viyojayet ||  
 8.6.13 śastaḥ prāṇihito  vastissadyo rogaharas
       tathā |
        
        samyaṅ nivṛtto, rogaughairhyanivṛttas tu prāṇahā ||  
 8.6.14  sa nivṛttas tu vegena doṣān gambhīramāsthitān |
        
        unmārgasthānnayenmārgaṃ mārgasthāṃś cānulomayet ||  
 8.6.15  vastivego ' nilaṃ hanti parjanyaṃ ca yathānilaḥ |
        
        kaphapittavikārāhi  sarve vātavaśānugāḥ ||  
 8.6.16  aśītirvātikā rogāścatvāriṃśat tu pittajāḥ |
        
        viṃśatiḥ ślaiṣmikāś cāpi saṃsṛṣṭānāmasaṃgrahāt ||  
 8.6.17  sarveṣām eva caiteṣāṃ rogāṇāṃ saṃgrahaissadā  |
        
        arditānāṃ hi bhūtānāṃ vastiragryaṃ  parāyaṇam ||  
 8.6.18  anilaprabhavā hyete sarve vastivaśānugāḥ |
        
        tasmād ardhaṃ cikitsāyāḥ sarvaṃ vā vastir ucyate ||  
 8.6.19  yas tu vastiṃ niṣeveta cāturmāsyaṃ sadā naraḥ |
        
        rogāssaṃvarjayeyustaṃ siṃhāvāsaṃ yathā gajāḥ ||  
 8.6.20  ete guṇaviśeṣāś ca vyākhyātā vastikarmaṇi |
        
 nirūhasyāsya sāmarthyam upacāraṃ ca me śṛṇu ||  
 8.6.21  svinne paryuṣite jīrṇe tvatyantaṃ ca nirūhayet |
        
        so ' sya mūtraṃ purīṣaṃ ca śleṣmāṇaṃ cāpakarṣati ||  
 8.6.22  vātānulomyaṃ kurute balaṃ sañjanayaty api |
        
        viṣasthiraṃ doṣabalaṃ yac ca nāḍīṣu saṃsthitam ||  
 8.6.23  viśodhayati tat sarvaṃ nirūhaḥ sa prayojitaḥ |
        
        rogānīkasya sarvasya paro nāsti hi tatsamaḥ ||  
 8.6.24  vyākulānāṃ ca keśānāṃ sīmantakaraṇaṃ yathā |
        
        tathā bhṛśaṃ vyākulānāṃ doṣāṇāṃ syānnirūhataḥ ||  
 8.6.25  nirūho hi samāyuktassamyagvīryassamairguṇaiḥ  |
        
        vyādhīnathoddharetkṣipraṃ puṇyaṃ yuktaṃ naraṃ yathā ||  
 8.6.26  kṛcchramūtrapurīṣāṇāṃ śūlināṃ vātagulminām |
        
        virecanādyudāvarte  hṛdroge pārśvaśūlini ||  
 8.6.27  udareṣu prameheṣu kuṣṭheṣu kṛmikoṣṭhiṣu |
        
        śleṣmaṇā saha saṃsṛṣṭe śoṇitena ca dūṣite ||  
 8.6.28  saṃsṛṣṭeṣu ca sarveṣu sannipātodbhaveṣu ca |
        
        gambhīrā dhātugā ye ca teṣāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ nirūhaṇam ||  
 8.6.29  yadā kaphaṃ viricyeta śaṅkhasphaṭikasannibham |
        
        ṛte mūtrapurīṣābhyāṃ tannirūhasya lakṣaṇam ||  
 8.6.30 suśodhitaṃ nirūheṇa nātiparyuṣitaṃ tathā |
        
        sukhoṣitaṃ samāśvastaṃ  bhojitaṃ cānuvāsayet ||  
 8.6.31  ekato vastikarmāṇi hyekato  ' nyaccikitsitam |
        
 amṛtārthaṃ vastikarma kurute suprayojitam ||  
 8.6.32 śuklaṃ bahvavarodhasya na kṣayaṃ yāti
       dehinaḥ |
        
        strīṣu pradharṣaṇaṃ kuryānnarāṇāṃ kṣīṇaretasām ||  
 8.6.33  vastiprayogāt  ṣaṇḍo ' pi pumān bhavati sarvaśaḥ
       |
        
 kṛśānām api martyānāṃ māṃsasaṃjananaṃ smṛtam || ity āha
       bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
        
 iti bhele siddhisthāne ṣaṣṭho ' dhyāyaḥ || || saptamo ' dhyāyaḥ |
        
        |
        
        athātaḥ phalamātrāsiddhiṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ
       |
        
 
 
 
 8.7.1 phalamātraṃ nirūheṣu śreṣṭham āhur manīṣiṇaḥ |
        
        teṣāṃ tu madanaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ pravadanti cikitsakāḥ ||  
 8.7.2  jīmūtakaṃ praśaṃsanti keciddhāmārgavaṃ tathā |
        
        kṛtavedhanam ity eke kuṭajaṃ prāhurapyatha  ||  
 8.7.3  garhitā ssarva evaite vādāḥ pratyekaśaḥ smṛtāḥ  |
        
        bheṣajānāṃ ca saṅghāto nirūheṣu praśasyate ||  
 8.7.4  vātapittakaphagnāṃstu  nirūhāṃś cānupūrvaśaḥ |
        
        vyākhyāsyāmo yathānyāyaṃ sannipātahitāś ca ye ||  
 8.7.5  dvai pañcamūlyau kolāni naladaśśuṣkamūlakam |
        
 dvipalīnāni sarvāṇi jaladroṇe vipācayet ||  
 8.7.6  aṣṭabhāgāvaśeṣaṃ tu kaṣāyamavatārayet |
        
 kalkapeṣyāṇi cemāni bheṣajāni samāvapet ||  
 8.7.7  nikuñcikāṃ kharapuṣpāṃ pippalīṃ  saindhavaṃ vacām
       |
        
        trapusorvārubījāni śatapuṣpāṃ yavānikām ||  
 8.7.8  kuṣṭhaṃ ca tagaraṃ caiva yaṣṭīmadhukam eva ca |
        
        sakṣīrassakaṣāyaś ca sagomūtraśca  kīrtitaḥ ||  
 8.7.9  satailaś ca nirūhaḥ syādvātarogavināśanaḥ |
        
        paṭolapatramūlaṃ ca picumandaṃ śatāvarīm ||  
 8.7.10  trāyamāṇāṃ balāṃ rāsnāṃ bṛhatīṃ kaṇṭakārikām |
        
        guḍūcīṃ triphalāṃ śyāmāṃ sāribāṃ vaṃśakatvacam ||  
 8.7.11  dvipalīnān  pṛthagbhāgān pūrvakalpena sādhayet |
        
        madhukaṃ vaṃśakaphalaṃ śatapuṣpāṃ durālabhām ||  
 8.7.12  mahāsahāmaṃśumatīṃ kalkaṃ kuryāt pṛthak pṛthak |
        
        kṣīreṇātha kaṣāyeṇa ghṛtena madhunā tathā ||  
 8.7.13  kalpamiśraḥ sumathito nirūhaḥ pittanāśanaḥ |
        
        daśamūlī karañjau dvau dantī citrakam eva ca ||  
 8.7.14  ekāṣṭhīlā turaṅgī ca triphalā devadāru ca |
        
        pūtikaṃ rauhiṣaṃ śyāmā  mūrvā rājatṛṇāni ca ||  
 8.7.15  pṛthak pañcapalānetān 
       sādhayetsarvakalpavit  |
        
 adhobhāgordhvabhāgdravyaissādhayetsādhu yojitaiḥ  ||  
 8.7.16  mūtratailayutaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ nirūhaḥ śleṣmanāśanaḥ |
        
        aśvagandhāṃ balāṃ rāsnāṃ śvadaṃṣṭrāṃ  sapunarnavām ||  
 8.7.17  paṭolapañcamūlyau ca bhārṅgīṃ śyāmāṃ śatāvarīm |
        
        guḍūcīṃ triphalāṃ śigruṃ karṇikāyāḥ phalāni ca ||  
 8.7.18  uśīraṃ rajanīpatraṃ pūtikaṃ kattṛṇāni ca |
        
        pṛthak pañcapalānetān  khaṇḍaśaśchedayed bhiṣak ||  
 8.7.19  jaladroṇe vipaktavyamaṣṭabhāgāvaśeṣitam |
        
        madhukaṃ śatapuṣpāṃ ca saindhavaṃ sarṣapān guḍam ||  
 8.7.20  hapuṣāmajamodāṃ ca madanasya phalāni ca |
        
        vacāmaśokabījāni pippalīkuṣṭham eva ca ||  
 8.7.21  etāni kalkapeṣyāṇi bheṣajāni pṛthak pṛthak |
        
        kṣīratailasamāyukto ghṛtamūtrasamanvitaḥ ||  
 8.7.22  khajena mathitaḥ pūtaḥ sa nirūhaḥ  praśasyate |
        
        ekena yadi vā dvābhyāṃ tribhir vātipramāṇataḥ ||  
 8.7.23 kiṃcinnyūnātiriktaṃ  vā jñātvā
       vyādhibalābalam |
        
        kuryāt  , viṃśativarṣāṇāṃ tatra prasthapramāṇataḥ ||  
 8.7.24  atha dvādaśavarṣāṇāmardhaprasthaṃ prayojayet |
        
        kaṣāyakuḍavaṃ cātra ṣaḍvarṣāṇāṃ prayojayet ||  
 8.7.25  yuktaṃ lavaṇatailabhyāṃ kṣīreṇa madhunā tathā |
        
        kaṣāyavastiṃ kurvīta svehād dviprasṛtaṃ bhiṣak ||  
 8.7.26  prasṛtaṃ madhyame  kuryāt prasṛtārdhaṃ
       kanīyasi  |
        
        nātiśītaṃ na vātyuṣṇaṃ kaṣāyam upakalpayet ||  
 8.7.27  vāyuḥ kupyati śītatvād atyuṣṇaṃ tu gudaṃ dahet |
        
        atisāndrātigrathito doṣeṇa sa hi mūrchati ||  
 8.7.28  madapravego  bhavati vyāpaccāsyopajāyate |
        
        athavāpi tanuryasya kaṣāyo yojito bhavet ||  
 8.7.29  so ' lpaṃ harati doṣaṃ ca na ca saṃśodhayed gudam |
        
        parikartaṃ  ca śūlaṃ ca janayec ca pravāhikām ||  
 8.7.30  atyarthamadhuro datto vidagdhaḥ  stambhaved
       anām  |
        
        grahaṇīṃ raktamarśāṃsi pāṇḍurogaṃ bhagandaram ||  
 8.7.31  atitīkṣṇas tu duryuktaḥ kṣipraṃ pratinivartate |
        
        na nirharati doṣāṃś ca jvaraṃ mūrchāṃ karoti ca ||  
 8.7.32  jvaritaṃ dahyamānaṃ ca mūrchamānaṃ ca mānavam |
        
        śītairmadhurasaṃyuktairyojayetkṣīravastibhiḥ ||  
 8.7.33  yasyātha lavaṇaḥ koṣṭhe nirūhaḥ paittikīṃ rujām |
        
        janayet tatra peṣyaṃ syānmadhureṇa nirūhaṇam ||  
 8.7.34  nirūho madhuro yasya śleṣmāṇaṃ parikopayet |
        
        kaṭukaiś ca kaṣāyais taṃ  nirūhedyasya mārutaḥ ||  
 8.7.35 prakupyedadhikaṃ tatra mārutaghnaṃ nirūhaṇam |
        
        tasmāllavaṇayuktāni dravyāṇi madhurāṇi ca ||  
 8.7.36 bhiṣagdadyānna śītāni tathoṣṇāni vivecayet
       |
        
        pitte śīto nirūhaḥ syāduṣṇas tu kaphavātayoḥ  ||  
 8.7.37  praśleṣmaṇi pravāte vā pyuṣṇamāsthāpanaṃ bhavet |
        
        madanasya phalaṃ piṣṭvā tailenācchena sādhayet ||  
 8.7.38  tannirūhe  praṇaṃsanti phalatailaṃ cikitsakāḥ |
        
        gomūtrayuktametat tu phalatailanirūhaṇam ||  
 8.7.39  nirūhaṃ lavaṇaṃ kuryāc chreṣṭhamānāhabhedanam |
        
        bilvairaṇḍaphalaṃ vāpi paced dviprasthasammitam ||  
 8.7.40 amlaṃ salavaṇaṃ sādhyamaṣṭabhāgāvaśeṣitam |
        
        kaṣāye tatra pīlūni kalkapeṣyāṇi yojayet ||  
 8.7.41  phalatailayuto vastirdeya  ānāhabhedanaḥ |
        
        eṣa sarvānudāvartān śophagulmān bhinatty api ||  
 8.7.42  athaiva vastirādhmānamudāvartaṃ vināśayet |
        
        oṣṭhajihvaṃ pṛṣṭhaccūrṇaṃ(?) bṛhatīṃ  kaṇṭakārikām ||  
 8.7.43  candanaṃ padmakaṃ caiva vṛntaṃ puṣpaṃ
       ca śālmaleḥ |
        
        khaṇḍitānāṃ yavānāntu kuḍavaṃ tatra yojayet ||  
 8.7.44  tadaikadhyaṃ pacet sarvaṃ jale cāṣṭaguṇe bhiṣak |
        
        ghṛtena madhunā caiva picchāṃ saṃyojya śaktitaḥ ||  
 8.7.45  nirvāhikāyāṃ śaṃsanti picchāvastim imaṃ budhāḥ |
        
        atas tu ṣoḍaśī  caiva pale dve ca punarnave ||  
 8.7.46  kaṭāhake pañcamūlīṃ  yavaiḥ saha vipācayet |
        
        upodakāyāḥ kṣuṇṇāyāḥ svarasaṃ ca supīḍitam ||  
 8.7.47  yuktaṃ tena kaṣāyeṇa ghṛtena saha yojayet |
        
        mākṣikeṇa ca saṃyukto vastis tu yavamūrcchitaḥ ||  
 8.7.48  picchāvastir iti khyātaḥ  śūle nirvāhikāsu ca |
        
        taruṇaṃ śiṃśupāpatraṃ  karbudārasya pallavam ||  
 8.7.49  kṣuṇṇaissaha yavaissiddhaiḥ saṃpiṣṭo
       ghṛtasaṃyutaḥ  |
        
        mākṣikakṣīrasaṃyuktaḥ sa vastir yavamūrcchitaḥ ||  
 8.7.50  nirvāhikāṃ vātaśūlaṃ  kṣatakṣīṇasya nāśayet |
        
        ete nirūhā vyākhyātāḥ sarvarogavināśanāḥ |
        
        vyākuleṣu vikārais tu tān bhiṣak saṃprayojayet || ity āha bhagavān
       ātreyaḥ |
        
        iti bhele saptamo ' dhyāyaḥ || |
        
        |aṣṭamo ' dhyāyaḥ || athāto daśavyāpadāmāsthāpanānuvāsanasiddhiṃ 
       vyākhyāsyāma iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ |
        
 
 
 
 8.8.1  snehavastirnirūhaś ca dvividhaṃ yāti vibhramam |
        
        na yujyate vā duryukto yukto vāpy atipūryate ||  
 8.8.2  teṣāṃ vipratipannānāṃ  vastīnāṃ vyāpado daśa |
        
        tāsāṃ rūpaṃ cikitsāṃ ca pravakṣyāmyanupūrvaśaḥ ||  
 8.8.3 na māti vā gude yukto vātādigadapīḍite |
        
        purīṣeṇāvṛte vāpi sa na gāḍhaṃ prapīḍitaḥ ||  
 8.8.4 arśasā pratisaṃruddhaḥ śleṣmaṇā pihite gude
       |
        
 guruyantrayuto vāpi netre vā jīrṇasarpite ||  
 8.8.5  na gacchati gude vastirvibhrānteṣu ca dhātuṣu |
        
        tam ayogam iti brūyādatiyogaṃ nibodha me ||  
 8.8.6  vātābhibhūtapitte vā śleṣmaṇā vā  ' hitaśinaḥ |
        
        purīṣeṇābhibhūtaś ca dūraṃ cātiprapīḍitaḥ ||  
 8.8.7  na pratyāyātyadho vastirbhītasyonmathitasya
       vā |
        
 gudavalyāṃ tṛtīyāyāmarśobhir vā nivāritaḥ ||  
 8.8.8  virecitasya vāntasya madyaśokākulasya ca |
        
        na pratyāyāty adho vastirūrdhvaṃ vātipravartate ||  
 8.8.9  teṣām upadravā ghorā jāyante vastivibhramāt |
        
        jīvādānaṃ  tṛṣācchardiḥ hṛdrogaḥ śvayathus tathā ||  
 8.8.10  śūlamarśāṃsi pāṇḍutvaṃ śvāso ' tha parikartikā |
        
        eṣāṃ pratyekaśo rūpaṃ cikitsāṃ ca nibodha me ||  
 8.8.11  gurukoṣṭhasya rūkṣasya bahudoṣasya dehinaḥ |
        
        asnigdhasya guruvyādheryadi vastiḥ pradīyate ||  
 8.8.12  atyalpo vātha rūkṣo vā śītavīryauṣadhastathā  |
        
        lavaṇasneharikto  vā tanussāndro ' tha vā bhṛśam ||  
 8.8.13 sambaddhabahudoṣasya doṣān utkleśayaty api
       |
        
 tatrasthā yatra sarpanti doṣāste pīḍitā bhṛśam ||  
 8.8.14  kaṭāvasthyūrujaṅghe ca pādapṛṣṭhodare tathā |
        
 prasyandante bhavec cāsya  saśūlamudakodaram ||  
 8.8.15  vastiśūlamudāvarto  gudaśoṣo jvaras tathā |
        
        niṣṭhīvakāsahṛllāsā  bhaktadveṣo vivarṇatā ||  
 8.8.16  snigdhasya tasya svinnasya saṃkaraprastarādibhiḥ
       |
        
        nirūhaṃ kārayet tīkṣṇamamoghāprativāraṇam ||  
 8.8.17  bilvāgnimanthasyonākakāśmaryāśca  sapāṭalāḥ |
        
        rāsnā balāgokṣurakayavakolakulutthakāḥ ||  
 8.8.18  etat sarvaṃ samāhṛtya jaladroṇe vipācayet |
        
        caturbhāgāvaśiṣṭaṃ taṃ kaṣāyamavatārayet  ||  
 8.8.19  kalkena sarṣapāṇāṃ ca pīlūnāṃ madanasya ca |
        
        sayavāsakaṣāyaṃ tu tattailalavaṇena ca ||  
 8.8.20  mūtrāṇi ca yathālābhamatha samyaṅ nirūpayet |
        
        yathā tṛtibalā |.. |.. |.. |.. ||  
 8.8.21  tatra vāditraśabdāṃś ca śreyasaś ca
       svanānapi |
        
        śāntiṃ puṇyāhaghoṣāṃś ca kuryāc cāpi pradakṣiṇam  ||  
 8.8.22  taṃ nidhāya śubhe kumbhe vastiṃ dadyāt pramāṇataḥ
       |
        
        devaprasādato vastirarditānāṃ mahāguṇaḥ ||  
 8.8.23  sarvarogaharo vṛṣyaḥ kṣatakṣīṇarujāpahaḥ  |
        
        vātapittasamutthānā rogā ye parikīrtitāḥ ||  
 8.8.24 kāsadāhajvarādyāṃstānnāśayed aviśaṅkitaḥ |
        
        tribhāgamākṣiko hyeṣa valīpalitanāśanaḥ ||  
 8.8.25  rūpavarṇakaraḥ puṃsāṃ balamāṃsavivardhanaḥ  |
        
        śatāvarīṃ sahacaraṃ rāsnāṃ gokṣurakaṃ balām ||  
 8.8.26  śataṃ śataṃ kalpayitvā toyadroṇaśate pacet |
        
        droṇāvaśeṣitaṃ tac ca paripūtaṃ nidhāpayet ||  
 8.8.27  barhikukkuṭahaṃsānāṃ māṃsāny api pṛthak pṛthak |
        
        vasā māhiṣavārāhameṣāṇāṃ  prasthasammitam ||  
 8.8.28  vidāryāmalakekṣūṇāṃ rasaprasthāḥ  pṛthak pṛthak |
        
        tatra tailaghṛtaprasthau  kṣīramaṣṭaguṇaṃ bhavet ||  
 8.8.29  tadgomayāgninā yuktyā kalkenānena sādhayet |
        
        tugākṣīryāmalakyau ca drākṣāmadhukacandanaiḥ ||  
 8.8.30  madhūlikāpaṭolābhyāṃ patraṃ nīlotpalasya ca |
        
        viśālāṃ ca mṛṇālaṃ  ca kapikacchuphalāni ca ||  
 8.8.31 kharjūraudanapākyau ca śītapākīṃ 
       nidigdhikām |
        
 salāmajjatvacaṃ patraṃ hvīberaṃ samahāsaham ||  
 8.8.32  jīvakarṣabhakau medāṃ pippalīś cāpi saṃharet |
        
        tatsiddhaṃ śītalīkṛtya kṣaudraprasthe niyojayet ||  
 8.8.33  tatra vāditraśabdāṃś ca kuryāt svastyayanāni ca |
        
        gajaskandhaṃ samāropya śvetacchatrānupālitam  ||  
 8.8.34 celāvṛtaṃ ca kurvīta sādhuśabdāṃś ca sarvaśaḥ |
        
        tato ' smin dāpayed vastiṃ puṇye ' hani rasāyanam ||  
 8.8.35  vastinānena dattena gacchennārīśataṃ naraḥ |
        
        na vātra yantraṇā kāciduktā nārīvihāragā ||  
 8.8.36  vṛṣyo balakaro vastirāpta āyurvivardhanaḥ |
        
 valīpalitakhālity aṃ  sevamāno niyacchati ||  
 8.8.37  ṣaṇḍāṃś ca puruṣān kuryāllakṣaṇāḍhyān  guṇānvitān
       |
        
        kṣīṇān kṣatānnaṣṭaśuklān viṣamajvarapīḍitān ||  
 8.8.38  yonīnāṃ vyāpado  vandhyāṃ vastireṣa 
       niyacchati |
        
        guḍūcīsvarasaprasthaṃ grāhayed yantrapīḍitam ||  
 8.8.39  śatāvarīrasaprasthaṃ tadvatsahacarasya ca |
        
        vidāryāmalakekṣūṇāṃ drākṣākharjūrayor api ||  
 8.8.40  pṛthak kuryād rasaprasthaṃ prasthau dvau
       tailasarpiṣoḥ |
        
        ājamāhiṣagavyāni kṣīrāṇi dviguṇāni ca ||  
 8.8.41 kṣuṇṇapiṣṭāni cemāni peṣayitvā vipācayet |
        
        vadhūṭikāmuccaṭāṃ ca madhukaṃ pippalīm api ||  
 8.8.42  śṛṅgāṭakaṃ puṣkarikāṃ kāṇḍaṃ nīlotpalasya ca |
        
        jīvakarṣabhakau medāṃ balāṃ nīlotpalāni  ca ||  
 8.8.43  tugākṣīrīṃ mahāmedāṃ puṇḍarīkasya kesaram |
        
        vṛṣameṣacakorāṇāṃ haṃsakukkuṭayor iha  ||  
 8.8.44 jīvañjīvakamattākṣakurarīkrauñcabarhiṇām  |
        
        vasā majjā ca sattvānāṃ meṣamāṃsarasaissaha ||  
 8.8.45  tribhāgaṃ mākṣikaṃ caiva yuñjyāt samyagvipācite |
        
        śaṅkhabherīninādaiś ca paṭahair vā murīsvanaiḥ ||  
 8.8.46  āropayed gajaskandhe śvetacchatradhvajāyutam  |
        
        siddhānāṃ paramaṃ devaṃ maharṣigaṇasevitam ||  
 8.8.47  śaraṇaṃ sarvabhūtānāmarcayed vṛṣabhadhvajam |
        
 āśīrbhir maṅgalāśaṃsistutibhir devatārcanaiḥ ||  
 8.8.48  rasāyanāni sidhyanti viparītāni cānyathā |
        
        taṃ snehaṃ gamayed vastiṃ rāsāyanikam uttamam ||  
 8.8.49  athāhāravihāreṣu  na cainaṃ yantrayed
       bhiṣak |
        
        vyāpannayonayo vandhyā raktagulminya eva ca ||  
 8.8.50  yā vā ' patyaṃ mṛtaṃ sūte yāś ca naṣṭārtavās
       tathā |
        
 naṣṭaśuklakṣatakṣīṇā viṣamajvarapīḍitāḥ ||  
 8.8.51 prakṣīṇamāṃsarudhirā valīpalitapīḍitāḥ |
        
        āśu praśamayed rogān tānāyurmāṃsavardhanam ||  
 8.8.52  rasāyanam idaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ narāṇāmamṛtopamam |
        
        rasāyanavidhānāni proktāny etāni yāni ca ||  
 8.8.53  sahasraśatapākāni kāryāṇi vibhave sati |
        
        madhukaṃ saindhavaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ śatapuṣpā  hareṇavaḥ ||  
 8.8.54  madanāni ca rāsnā ca bhārṅgī, nīparakajvalam(?) |
        
        mari |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. ||  
 8.8.55 māyūraṃ kaukkuṭaṃ vāpi
       veśavāraṃ sukuṭṭitam |
        
        sahitaṃ daśamūlyā tu jaladroṇe vipācayet ||  
 8.8.56  rasasya tasya pūtasya prasthārdhaṃ
       ca pradāpayet |
        
        vasātailaghṛtānāṃ tu madhunaḥ prasṛtadvayam ||  
 8.8.57 hapuṣāśatapuṣpāṇāṃ mustānāṃ cāpi kārṣikam |
        
 kalkapeṣyaṃ punardadyādvastiṃ  salavaṇaṃ sukham ||  
 8.8.58  pādagulphorujaṅghāsu trikavaṅkṣaṇabastiṣu |
        
        śiśne vṛṣaṇayoś caiva vātarogaṃ niyacchati ||  
 8.8.59  mṛgāṇāṃ tittirāṇāṃ ca tathaiva bilavāsinām  |
        
        ānūpānāṃ khagānāṃ ca kalpamevaṃ prayojayet ||  
 8.8.60  tulyaṃ madhu ca tailaṃ ca tasmād uṣṇodakaṃ samam |
        
        dvau karṣau śatapuṣpāṇāṃ karṣaś ca lavaṇottamaḥ ||  
 8.8.61  eṣa rāsāyano vastirdīpanīyo ' tha bṛṃhaṇaḥ |
        
        balavarṇakaro vṛṣyo yāpano nirupadravaḥ ||  
 8.8.62 gulmodavartitādhmānapramehakṛmikoṣṭhinām |
        
        nityaṃ gāḍhapurīṣāṇāṃ vastireṣa hitaḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
 8.8.63  ghṛtaṃ madhu ca tailaṃ ca teṣāṃ mānaṃ samaṃ
       bhavet |
        
        pūrvakalkena  deyāni sa vastirbalavarṇakṛt ||  
 8.8.64  vastau meḍhragate doṣe vastyasātmyacikitsite |
        
        paittike mūtrakṛcchre ca pittavyādhiṣu cottamaḥ ||  
 8.8.65 tulyaṃ ghṛtamatha kṣaudraṃ tayor māṃsarasassamaḥ
       |
        
        akṣamātraṃ ca mustānāṃ sa vastiḥ pūrvakalpavat  ||  
 8.8.66 gulphorujānupṛṣṭheṣu sarvataḥ stambhiteṣu ca |
        
        balāsapādaharṣeṣu vastiḥ praśamanaḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
 8.8.67 vastau vṛṣaṇameḍhreṣu śūlamāśu niyacchati |
        
        trikajānūrupṛṣṭhādivedanāṃ cāpakarṣati ||  
 8.8.68 
       mṛdutvānna nivatante kṣubhyante vastayaś ca vā |
        
 tīkṣṇairāsthāpanaṃ kāryaṃ kṣipraṃ pratinivartayet ||  
 8.8.69  mṛdutvād yāpanānāṃ tu kecidvibhramabhīravaḥ |
        
 dīpanānāṃ kaṣāyeṇa yojayanti cikitsakāḥ ||  
 8.8.70  evamanyeṣu  vibhrāntau  sanirūheṣu vā punaḥ
       |
        
        vastayaḥ kalpadṛṣṭā hi yathā kāle sukhāvahāḥ ||  
 8.8.71  kṣīṇātiriktā dūṣyante tasmād yogaṃ samāharet |
        
        nityaṃ nārīvihārāṇāṃ kṣīṇānāmalparetasām ||  
 8.8.72  evam eva vidhānaṃ ca retobalavivardhanam |
        
 svecchāvihārān vakṣyāmi vastīn śuklavivardhanān  ||  
 8.8.73  rasaḥ karkaṭakānāṃ tu śarkarāmastusaṃyutaḥ |
        
        ghṛtasaubarcalayuto vastirvṛṣyatamaḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
 8.8.74  haṃsasārasalāvānāṃ tittirikrauñcabarhiṇām |
        
        kalpenānena kartavyā vājīkaraṇavastayaḥ ||  
 8.8.75  payaḥ kukkuṭamāṃsena vipakvaṃ madhusaṃyutam |
        
        caṭakāṇḍarasaś caiva  kukkuṭāṇḍarasastathā  ||  
 8.8.76  ghṛtamākṣikasaṃyuktaḥ śarkarāsaindhavairyutaḥ |
        
        eṣa vastiḥ smṛto vṛṣyaḥ māṃsaśuklavivardhanaḥ ||  
 8.8.77 yataś śataṃ vā ṣaṣṭiṃ vā nārīr gacchati mānavaḥ |
        
        eṣa varṇabalotsāhaḥ sthavire ' pi pradṛśyate ||  
 8.8.78  timiṅgile vā makare pāṭhīne nakramīnayoḥ |
        
 dugdhaṃ kūrme+ athakumbhīre kalpayecchiśumāravat ||  
 8.8.79  vārāhabastavṛṣaṇau vṛṣaṇau govṛṣasya ca |
        
        caṭakarkaṭakāṃś caiva kṣīreṇa saha sādhayet ||  
 8.8.80  tannirūhaṃ tu śukreṇa bastānāmatha miśrayet |
        
 uccaṭekṣurakaṃ  cātra kalkapeṣyaṃ samāvapet ||  
 8.8.81  ghṛtamākṣikasaṃyuktaṃ praṇītaḥ śarkarāyutaḥ |
        
        kiṃcillavaṇito  vastir gamayet strīśatāny api ||  
 8.8.82  eṣa nārīvihārāṇāṃ bahvantaḥ puravāsinām |
        
        retobalakaraḥ śreṣṭhaḥ krīḍāvastiranuttamaḥ ||  
 8.8.83  ātmaguptāphalaiḥ  kṣīram
       uccaṭekṣurakaiḥ śṛtam |
        
 bhojane vānupāne vā vṛṣyārthaṃ samprayojayet ||  
 8.8.84  rasāyanā vastayas tu ye mayā pūrvadarśitāḥ |
        
        tān etair māṃsaniryūhair yojayet kalpakalpitān  ||  
 8.8.85  babhrusūkarakhaḍgāś ca chāgagomahiṣās tathā |
        
        krauñcakāraṇḍavāḥ  krauñcacakravākabakāstathā  ||  
 8.8.86  nirūhameṣāṃ saṃhṛtya lābhatassādhu yojayet |
        
        kṣīraṃ panasabījāni kapikacchūphalāni ca ||  
 8.8.87  uccaṭekṣurabījāni madhukaṃ tālamastakam |
        
        pippalyaśśāribā  drākṣā kharjūro madanāny api ||  
 8.8.88  jīvakarṣabhakau medā bījaṃ nīlotpalasya ca |
        
 garbheṇānena saṃsiddhaṃ caṭakāṇḍarasāyutam || Bhṣ8.8.? |
        
        śarkarāmadhusaṃyuktaṃ  |.. |.. |.. |.. |.. ||
